*oṃ awighnamāstu*

<sragdharā>:1.
– – –| – ⏑ –| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – –| ⏑ – –| ⏑ – ⏓ = 21

siṅgiḥ dhyakṣa iŋ kalaṅwan saŋ aṅawaki laṅö mūṙtti saŋ hyaŋ manobhū,
pūjān riŋ puṣpa muṅgwiŋ sarasija gĕlarĕn muṣṭi niŋ kāmatantra,
maṅke caṇḍyā nira iŋ  bhāṣa saphalakĕna yan dèwa niŋ kūŋ winimba,
Āpan riŋ niṣkala anaṅga kawuwusan ira n saŋ maṅö wri ŋ palambaŋ*

hyaŋ-hyaŋ niŋ kāṙttika aṅambĕki kawi kakawin riŋ pasiṙ paṙwwata arūm,
līla adandan ghana apiṇḍa karas ira lĕṅö lwiṙ nika syuḥ kilatnya,
tansaḥ taŋ ciṇḍaga mrik tanaḥ ira n alaṅö maṙṇnana ŋ laṅwa-laṅwan,
gĕntĕṙ lagy-a aṅatag bhāwa nira n aṅikĕti ŋ twas niŋ onĕŋ tinambaŋ*

maṅgalyā ni ṅhulun dhꜽṙyya sahaja makĕdö mrākrĕtā ŋ bhomakāwya,
de niŋ siṅgiḥ mataŋnya n panulada kakawin ndān adoḥ yan paniṙwwa,
himpĕṙ wintaŋ lawan sūṙyya kĕta gati niki n taṇḍiṅĕn kāwidagdhan,
Āpan taṇḍiŋ laṅö dūra n amalika karas yan kadohan tanaḥnya*

hyaŋ wiṣṇw-aṅjanma riŋ madhyapada makadadin śrī mahārāja krĕṣṇa,
mwaŋ saŋ hyaŋ bāsukī maṅkana dadi baladewa agraja śrī narendra,
kapwa agöŋ riŋ kaśaktin prabhawa nira dudug trus tĕka iŋ swaṙggaloka,
sākṣād āditya kĕmbaṙ sira taya dumĕlö de ni göŋ niŋ pratāpa*

sakweḥ niŋ śatru kāṅśādi saha bala hilaŋ de nira alaḥ wiśīṙṇna,
swastha ŋ rāt ṅkā n subhikṣa ahayu sahana nikāŋ āśrama atiṅkaḥ akram,
sājñā saŋ mānu hetunya n apagĕḥ irikaŋ śāsana iŋ mānawādi,
māry-ambĕk crol ikaŋ duṣṭa sumiliḥ aharĕp muṅsira iŋ dhaṙmmayukti*

maṅgĕḥ göŋ niŋ kaśaktin ri haji sama-sama mwaŋ mahāmeru riŋ twas,
kadya aḍaṅhan mara ikaŋ tribhuwana winawa iŋ hasta de śrī narendra,
towin sampūṙṇna śakti i sira matika dumeḥ wīṙyya lumra aniwāṙyya,
Āpan taŋ wīṙyya riŋ nīti sira kadi catussāgara alaṅghanīya*

ramya atyanta ahalĕp rājya nira ṅaran ika iŋ dwārawaty-a atiśobha,
antuk niŋ hyaŋ paḍa bwat puji wijaḥ aturun kabwatan-tan hana asor,
bapranya ama as lawan gopura maṇik inukiṙ prāṇa pūṙwwa apura ago,
hetunya n swaṙgga riŋ meru linĕwiḥ ahajöŋ tan katon ṅke ri loka*

denya kweḥ niŋ karaŋ ratna saphala pakirim hyaŋ samudra i narendra,
prastāwanya n maṇik rāmya racana niŋ umaḥ mās parĕmpw-i i hatĕpnya,
sambandhanya praśasta iŋ bhuwana halĕp ikaŋ rājya ya atyanta riŋ śrī,
Āpan saŋ hyaŋ dhanendra aṅhudani ya rajaṭa aṅkĕn pituŋ lek hudan mās*

riŋ kastrī-hajyan akweḥ grĕha kanaka kinoṙyyan maṇik padmarāga,
söŋ-söŋ nīŋ oṣadhi byakta lumarap ahulap bhāswara aṅĕṇḍĕp-ĕṇḍĕp,
towi iki n teja niŋ ratna patiga sumĕnö nitya kīṙṇna i nataṙnya,
hetunya n tan pĕtĕŋ riŋ wĕṅi sumaji jugā pañjut iŋ kāla sore*

lāwan tāmanya makweḥ tuwu-tuwuhan ika apādapa akambaŋ awwaḥ,
wwaḥ riŋ māsa anurun rūm lĕṅĕŋ amisan apan tan hana aganti-ganti,
nitya aṅjraḥ paṅkajanya iŋ  talaga pinatiga iŋ candrakānta pradīpta,
wyaṙtha ikaŋ paṙwwata mwaŋ pasiṙ i hana nika n wāḥ laṅö rob kalaṅwan*

ṅka aṙṇnaḥ leṙ taŋ paṅastryānan alun-alun i heŋ bajralepanya ratna,
salwa anīla awaṅuntuṙ pinakasabha-sabhā saŋ watĕk yadw-asewa,ꦉ
kaywanya aneka tejanya ri kĕñaṙ i sĕnö niŋ maṇik bhūṣaṇa abhra,
lagy-aṅde saṅśaya n wwantĕna rawi manusup nāgata iŋ rāhuwimba*

hīṅanya n sāri niŋ rājya tiki hana rikaŋ dwārawaty-adwitīya,
laṅgĕŋ kapwa iki rāmyanya tuwi paḍa mahāmūlya kālanya makweḥ,
mambö gandhanya lumra aŋ asĕp asawaŋ aket mrik hrĕbuk tūt hawan göŋ,
daṙppa ikāŋ atpada anatpada maṅusiṙ inak hetukanya n pĕnuḥ wwaŋ*

maṅkā krĕp niŋ grĕha akaṇṭa sakuwu-sakuwū seriŋ iŋ rājyadhāni,
denya atiṅkaḥ mahantĕn ri lĕbuḥ ika lawan pañcuran wāṇḍira agöŋ,
len tekaŋ bwat salö mwaŋ patani ri tĕpi niŋ māṙgga ramya apapuṇyan,
muṅgwiŋ doḥ paṅhyaṅan śela tuwi katulajĕg caṇḍi kapwa apucak mās*

lwaḥ saṅkeŋ jro kaḍatwan hĕniŋ i bañu nika adrĕs hilīnya aṅgaluntaŋ,
tañjuŋ wūṅw-a asana aśoka surabhi kamuniŋ muṅgwi piṅgiṙ nikaŋ lwaḥ,
siṅgroŋ-siṅgroŋ ikā rantunan iŋ iwak ariŋ lālana aliṇḍuṅan wwad,
kĕmbaŋ laywan kahily-aṅduluṙ anak-anakan keṭaka aṅumbaŋ-umbaŋ*

ndātan dwa n tan bĕsuṙ taŋ wwaŋ umulat irikā nyāsa makweḥ tinonton,
lyan tekaŋ lakwa-lakwan para ratu n umarĕk mwaŋ watĕk yodhamantrī,
saṅkĕp saŋ wrĕṣṇi-wīṙ-a andhaka saha panĕṅĕṙ cūḍaratna pradīpta,
pantĕs-pantĕs rare saŋ yadukula winani iŋ praŋ sĕḍĕŋ daṙśśanīya*

sāmpun prāpta atatā riŋ wataṅan alun-alun mantri saŋ nātha krĕṣṇa,
sahya agasyak magoṣṭhy-a awĕtu guyu hana ta abhāwaka amiṇḍa-miṇḍa,
māry-a aśabda ararĕm ḍyam ri wijil ira mahārāja saṅkeŋ kaḍatwan,
kewalya akāra saŋ śrī nrĕpati winulatan-tan wawaŋ yan panāntwa*

nantĕn tapwan masowe haji maṅuliḥ-uliḥ jag ḍatĕŋ saŋ mahāṙṣi,
saṅkeŋ swaṙgga aduluṙ somya sira sama-sama iŋ siddhi sīra n paḍa hyaŋ,
kagyat-gyat saŋ narendra amulati muniwara apan sawaŋ riŋ paṅipyan,
gorawy-atyanta saŋ bhūpati karaṇa nira n tan paṅanti i palaṅka*

nyā pwa aŋ aṙggha atiśobha anupama suci matis muṅgu riŋ kumbha ratna,
yekā sāmpun panuṅsuŋ narapati ri mahāpaṇḍya tuṣṭa prahaṙṣa,
lāwan tekaŋ palaṅka aśayana ya humaḍaŋ saṅgraha i saŋ tapaswī,
rĕp-rĕp-rĕp-rĕp maluṅguḥ muniwara ri tĕlas iŋ maśānti i narendra*

mojaṙ saŋ nātha ḍū bhāgya tĕka muniwara prāpta riŋ deśa śūnya,
hopĕn tekaŋ purī yan gatarasa pinaran tan hana inuṅsiṙ-uṅsir,
maṅke n kambaḥ tĕkap saŋ prawara hana gamantanya maṅgiḥ pawitra,
Āpan saŋ paṇḍita aṅde hayu humilaṅakĕn kleśa niŋ janmabhūmi*

astam rānak mahāpaṇḍya kadi wihikan iŋ swaṙgga yan ton mahāṙṣi,
siṅgiḥ yan bhāgyamanta ṅhulun apa ta kunaŋ kāṙyya riŋ pūṙwwajanma,
nityāśaṅkw-a amaṅun dhaṙmma karika maṅipuk yajñā ṅūny-a ananĕm soŋ,
ndaḥ yeki n rakwa maṅke phala nika ri ḍatĕŋ saŋ paṅĕmpwan para ṅke*

om om-om sājña saŋ śrī nrĕpati kudaŋ ike saṅhulun siddhayogī, 
maṅke n sāmpun katon byakta ri dadi bhagawān weṣṇawa śrī narendra,
sakweḥ saŋ siddhayogīśwara kita śaraṇanya iki muṅgwiŋ swacitta,
aṅhiŋ siḥta n sinādhya aṅlĕpasakĕna sarāt riŋ pada anindyajāti*

ḍū tan maṅkā pwa de saŋ yatiwara maṅucap ri ṅhulun hīnabuddhi,
nantĕn denya ŋ warānugraha maṅudaŋ-ṅudaŋ saŋ mahaṙṣi iŋ kadi ṅwaŋ,
ndañ jātinya n puriḥ saŋ sujana juga maha aṅastawa aṅde prahaṙṣa,
lwiṙ prāpta iŋ brahmaloka ṅwaŋ ahawana wuwus de mahāpaṇḍya mojar*

ndaḥ kṣāntabya ṅhulun toḥ sahuri taña ranak saŋ mahaṙṣi i yatīndra,
ndy-a anuŋ saṅkan paran ndon saṅapa sira ṅaran saŋ yati ṅwaŋ turuŋ wruḥ,
nā liŋ saŋ nātha krĕṣṇa ataña wawaŋ awaraḥ don ira i saŋ narendra,
siṅgiḥ-siṅgiḥ wuwusta i kami laki majara i tiṅka-tiṅkaḥ mahāṙṣi*

ṅūni pwa khyāti saŋ hyaŋ narahari makasādhyā kahaywān ikaŋ rāt,
pūjābhyāsa iŋ widhi bwat krama sira satata amrĕddhyakĕn śiṣyasaṅgha,
nāhan saŋ paṇḍya śiṣya atuha tinuhakĕn iŋ kahyaṅan de bhaṭāra,
śuddhasthāna adhika ndaḥ panĕmu nira mahādhyātmika areḥ pralīna*

ndā-ndā siṅgiḥ pwa ya atyanta halĕp ira huwus pūṙṇna riŋ jñānasandhi,
saṙwwajña mwaŋ tikāŋ aṣṭaguṇa paḍa hana i saŋ rĕsi byaktasiddha,
tĕkwan tekaŋ kamāhātmyan ira sama lawan hyaŋ prajāpaty-anindya,
niṙwighna astu swabhāwa ṅhaṅĕn-aṅĕn i sira n sāmpun iŋ waktraśoca*

nā liŋ saŋ paṇḍya tan len ṅaran ira bhagawān aṅgira atyantawāgmī,
saŋ sākṣāt hyaŋ widhīśabda sakala ṅuniweḥ śāraṇa iŋ ādikāwya,
riŋ kꜽśwaryan tanora amaḍana sira yan iŋ saṙwwayogaprayoga,
śrīy ātmā śuddhabuddhi pratuhu-tuhu kawīndra adi siddhāntaśāstra*

sāmpun teki n waraḥ ni ṅhulun i haji kunaŋ don mahaṙṣi i narendra,
paṅrakṣanta iŋ triloka udasina nira ri saŋ nātha maṅke n para ṅke,
atyanta iŋ bhūṙ bhuwaḥ swaḥ kinawaśakĕn ikaŋ rākṣasa akweḥ prakīṙṇna,
wadwānya iŋ dānawa anāma naraka pĕnuḥ iŋ dik-widik tan pahīṅan*

śīṙṇna ŋ swaṙgga alilaŋ taŋ patapan-apan ikaŋ rākṣasa aṅrampa-rampak,
luṅhā saŋ tāpasa atiṅgal alaradan adoḥ sāri-sāri n tinumpu,
len taŋ wāhwa aṅlawan kapwa mati ginarabag kāsihan ya ŋ daridra,
waṅkaynya aṅlaḥ-laḥ iŋ maṇḍala saha daluwaŋ kaṇḍi-kaṇḍinya kontal*

tīḍak ḍīkötahui
<wikrĕti>:2.
⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

kunaŋ pwa haji tatwa saŋ naraka rĕṅwakĕna tiki tĕkap nareśwara,
bhaṭāra hari padmayoni sira ta aṅucap-ucap ulaḥ iŋ kadigjayan,
tanora liŋ ira amaḍāna ri kaśaktin ira pisaniṅū hana ŋ lĕwiḥ,
ya hetu nira māna kāṙyya nira liŋ nira sahana nikaŋ jagattraya*

sĕḍĕŋ nira magoṣṭhi jag hana ta liṅga maṇik aṅadĕg iŋ pahīṅanan,
dawānya manĕhĕṙ katon dadi sira aṅliŋ apa tiki katon asambhawa,
manaḥ nira wawaŋ tĕka anatapa liṅga wahu mayat ikaŋ taṅan kiwa,
umiṇḍuhuṙ ikaŋ maṇik-sphaṭika-liṅga sadĕdĕg irikā n tiniṅhalan*

kapūhan aṅĕṭĕk bhaṭāra maṅadĕg paḍa maṅayuhi puñcak iŋ maṇik,
samaṅkana tikaŋ maṇik makin umiṇḍuhuṙ amatĕṅaḥ iŋ nabhastala,
ya ta amaṅunakĕn gĕlĕŋ ri sira saŋ rwa mamaribhawa maṅdĕha aṅdĕdĕl,
paḍa aṅgrĕgut añakra tan hana juga amyati warayaŋ ira awaluy-waluy*

kaṅelan asuwe bhaṭāra hari keśawa muwaḥ irika aṅdadak bhawa,
nĕhĕṙ matĕmahan warāha sawukiṙ himawan iki sira anwab iŋ lĕmaḥ,
prayojana katĕmwa buṅkaḥ ikanaŋ maṇik ulaḥ-ulahĕn maran rĕbaḥ,
lĕpas tĕka ri soṙ kaḍāha sira tan palaca-laca wĕkas nikaŋ maṇik*

prajāpati sira atemaḥ manuk uluŋ wĕkas anatap pucak nikaŋ maṇik,
huwus tĕka sira i kaḍāhaka nika i ruhuṙ ika binĕlaḥ nira iŋ hĕlar,
lĕpas pwa sira tan katon wĕkas ikaŋ maṇik aruhuṙ adoḥ samaṙ lĕyĕp,
tuhun bañu niŋ aṙṇnawa anĕḍuni bhūṙ bhuwaḥ inusiṙ apan catuṙmmukha*

kĕbĕk pwa kalĕbū taŋ aṇḍabhuwana aṙṇnawa kadi muwaha ika tuṅgala,
muwaḥ sahana saŋ hyaŋ aṅhyaṅi bhaṭāra hari mari marūpa sūkara,
samantara bhaṭāra wiṣṇu humĕnĕŋ pinĕkul ira juga ŋ jagattraya,
huwus pwa masamādhi pūṙṇna tikaŋ aṇḍabhuwana kadi ṅūni tambayan*

manon ta sira dewatī hyaŋ ikanaŋ lĕmaḥ atiśaya riŋ guṇa ahayu,
sahaṙṣa sira tan dwa sāhasa mamaṅkwakĕn anuculi sandhi niŋ tapiḥ,
kunaŋ pwa sira saŋ kinol nira ya ta akrak anaṅis anulak sira akĕtĕr,
miṅe kawawa mūṙccha melik i bhaṭāra mituturi sira n warāhika*

ilik nira wasundharī mwaŋ iki rāga nira sira bhaṭāra keśawa,
tinūt i paṅiḍam nira iŋ kṣitisuta ŋ rasatala pinakaṅgwan iŋ rare,
lawas nira wasundhara amĕtĕṅakĕn tĕka tahun ika sewu tan kuraŋ,
mijil pwa tanayan bhaṭāra madhusūdhana yatika marūpa dānawa*

prajāpati sira awĕlas maṅanumoda sira tĕhĕṙ aweḥ anugraha,
sira aṅarani riŋ rare si naraka astujaya wijaya liŋ nira aṅgamĕl,
rinatwakĕn ira ika saŋ kṣitisuta pwa makahulun ikaŋ jagattraya,
ri göŋ i siḥ ira ikihĕn kamalayoni karaṇa ni mahīsuta añjaya*

tĕlasnya n inanugrahan ciha-ciha apraṅa juga kaharĕpnya tan waneḥ,
mijil ta ya mara iŋ samudra saha sañjata dinuluṙ ikaŋ balāsura,
manuṅgaŋ iŋ iwak liman wija-wijaḥ saha bala nika rāmya tūt hawan,
hanan jĕnĕk aliṅgiḥ iŋ karaŋ aṅuṅkuli halun i surud nikaŋ bañu*

ry-uliḥnya saka riŋ samudra tadanantara maṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn ta ya apraṅa,
dhaneśwara sira ika liŋnya-ya tĕkāna nagara nira rakwa rampasĕn,
umaṅkat ahawan haṅin saha balanya kumukus aduluṙ mahānala,
tĕka aṅgĕsĕṅi rājya muntab i gĕlĕŋnya tinahĕn ika maṅkin ujwala*

katiṅgal ikanaŋ wimāna maṇipuṣpaka tĕkap ira saŋ dhaneśwara,
ya ta inalap ikaŋ mahīsuta manuṅgaŋ atĕhĕṙ umuliḥ sakeŋ raṇa,
ikāŋ asurasaṅgha ya aṅadĕgakĕn kuṭa ni naraka muṅgu riŋ du lor,
amumpunana paścimottara sadeśa baruṇa kalawan dhanādhipa*

tĕlasnya magawe kuṭa adbhuta samaṅkana marawaśa riŋ tapowana,
nihan tiki nimitta saŋ rĕṣi sama anasi pamahayu saŋ nareśwara,
narendra juga ya antakā niŋ asurādhipa pawĕkas ira hyaŋ a uśwara,
mataŋnya n aṅusiṙ wĕlas ṅhulun i saŋ prabhu tumaḍaha ŋ āśraya i haji*

nahan wuwus i saŋ rĕṣi prawara nārada mawara-waraḥ ri saŋ prabhu,
watĕk rĕṣi kabeḥ sumöŋ ri mukha duhkha nira lumuḥ aṅĕmbĕŋ iŋ mata,
narendra wĕkasan tumuntĕn atiyatna maṅanumata don mahāyati,
mĕhaḥ sira mĕṅĕs wawaŋ wĕtu ni luḥ nira mamarĕṅi luḥ mahāmuni*

maśabda naranātha sis kadi linād hati ni ranak ira mpu maṅrĕṅö,
nihan ṅhulun atoha jīwita rumakṣa sahana-hana riŋ tapowana,
tuhun makasiluṅluṅa ŋ yaśa juga ṅhulun amahayu bhūmimaṇḍala,
anugraha mahāṙṣi ri ṅhulun acaṇḍya ri pagĕha nikaŋ jagaddhita*

nda ya iki sipi bhāgya niŋ tapa sukha ṅhulun inubhaya de nareśwara,
kunaŋ pwa mapa dāya saŋ prabhu mapa iki hiṅĕt-iṅĕt i saŋ narādhipa,
kunĕŋ ri panukū mahīsuta mara iŋ amarapura dumon sureśwara,
kĕnoḥ niki balanya hĕntyakĕna siŋ kawĕkas amaribhūta riŋ wiku*

syapa ika hinutus narādhipa rumakṣa ri para rĕṣi riŋ himālaya,
kapagwakĕna tan hĕlĕm-hĕlĕmĕn āpan awĕdi sira riŋ balāsura,
kṣamākĕna mara iki śabda niŋ aminta śaraṇa kadi tan paṅantyakĕn,
swabhāwa nikaŋ āśraya amicaraṇa aśraya karĕs ika ya aṅgrĕmĕt-grĕmĕt*

ya ta ujaṙ ira saŋ rĕṣi prawara nārada wawaŋ asahuṙ nareśwara,
tatan sigi-sigin kunĕŋ wĕtu ni saṅhulun aṅutusa yogyarakṣakā,
hana iki pinakāgra niŋ swatanaya ika gati niki tĕlas krĕtāyudha,
lumakwa mara riŋ tapowana sumapwana ŋ asura sukĕt niŋ āśrama*

anantara ḍatĕŋ ta sāmba humatuṙ dadi tinuduhakĕn ri saŋ rĕṣi,
sĕḍĕŋ wĕrĕ-wĕrĕḥ katon raras ira n lituhayu ya mawoṙ guṇa adhika,
kapūhan aṅĕṭĕk mahāmuni mulat prasama tĕhĕṙ anaṙkka liŋ ira,
nyama aŋ tapi-tapi iŋ girī rumaras iŋ piṅulahana tumiṅhala i sira*

ri samparan iraŋ watĕk rĕṣi kabeḥ wihikana sira saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
tĕlas pinaripoṣita anarima nāna sira paḍa maśānti saŋ prabhu,
humantuk ahawan tawaŋ sira hana iŋ jalada jĕnĕk aṅöb samaṙ-samar,
hanan kadi wayaŋ katon kinĕliran puti-putiḥ adamaṙ traŋ iŋ rawi*

byatīta gati saŋ watĕk rĕṣi narendra sira tiki gumanti waṙṇnanĕn,
prayojana mahāṙṣi muṅgu ri manaḥ nira yatika hinöm nira aṅdadak,
saŋ uddhawa sira awuwus prabhu kĕnoḥ larisakĕna ŋ upāya de haji,
narendrasuta sāmba maṅkata lawan sakatuduha tumūta rakṣaka*

yadin tan alaha abwata ŋ musuḥ atambĕha hana juga mājara i haji,
watĕk yadu waneḥ muwaḥ tumuluṅa i nrĕpasuta tumuluy riŋ āśrama,
kahinya n akĕḍik mara ika bala niŋ naraka paḍa mareŋ kadewatan,
alaḥnya niyatanya haywa kapalaŋ palĕkasa nira saŋ nrĕpātmaja*

kunaŋ hala nikiŋ hĕlĕm-hĕlĕma de narapati maṅupāya riŋ musuḥ,
hilaŋ yaśa narendra saŋ yati paḍa asasaran alaradan mareŋ waneḥ,
ikaŋ musuḥ agöŋ ya donya tĕmahan milaṅakĕn i śarīra saŋ prabhu,
apuy sumĕlap iŋ hatĕp ṅaran ikā hĕnĕṅakĕna gatinya de haji*

nihan paṅupamanya rakwa hana ta wwaŋ asawa-sawaḥ iŋ lĕmaḥ rĕnĕk,
saniścaya ta ya iŋ parinya yan ahaywa maraṇa tuwi tan hana aṅapa,
hana pwa ri lĕmĕḥ nika amatuna hetu ni dukut i sawaḥ nika aruhur,
alit wĕtu nikaŋ pari n karahaban waliṅi ya hala niŋ palĕḥ-palĕḥ*

prakāśa mara kīṙtti saŋ prabhu tĕlas pinakasuluḥ ikaŋ prajāhita,
wulan-wulan iraŋ mahājana tanora lumĕwihana śobhita abuṅaḥ,
katon kalĕwihan rika anukhani saṅka ri wĕtu nikaŋ ambĕk uttama,
prihĕn tĕmĕn ikaŋ karakṣan ika de nrĕpati makaphala aŋ jagaddhita*

rĕsĕp rasa ni śabda rakryan apatiḥ pinatiḥ ira narendra riŋ naya,
wĕtunya ŋ upapatti yukti ya ta mukhya niŋ ayu niŋ upāya de haji,
manaḥ prawarawīra haṙṣa rumĕṅö wacana nira saŋ uddhawa iŋ sabhā,
hatuṙ salaga kāṅinan kapanasan sumĕkaṙ i tĕka niŋ hudan wĕṅi*

wawaŋ nrĕpati krĕṣṇa mantuk i dalĕm nagara ri parahasyan iŋ daṅū,
narendrasuta sāmba sāmpun aśila i harĕp ira pinapak wineḥ sĕpaḥ,
tĕñuḥ twas ira śīṙṇna rakwa dadi luḥ drawa ri mata nira n parambĕhan,
panampĕta nira n taṅis mara-maraḥ nrĕpasuta riy asiḥ nira aṅrĕsĕp*

tuhanku bapa tan sake lalis iki ṅhulun umutus i māsku riŋ bhaya,
asiḥku ri kita iki haywa ta kita analaḥ-iḍĕp i sabuddhya ni ṅhulun,
prasiddha hurip i ṅhulun kita mataŋnya kapan awĕnaṅa aku niṣṭhura,
kadigjayan ike katönku ri wĕkaṅkw-i saŋ anulus anĕmwa kaprabhun*

kita pwa hinarĕp-harĕpku śaraṇaṅkw-amagĕhakĕna dhaṙmma ni ṅhulun,
t-akīṙtti t-aṅusiṙ guṇa adhika tuhanku laki t-aṅipuk ambĕk iŋ jagat,
ameta kajanapriyan ta kita wuṅsu hawana ni ḍatĕŋ nikaŋ hayu,
nihan ṅhulun acaṇḍya māsku saphala aṅusira pagĕha niŋ jagaddhita*

lana amala-malaṙ ṅhulun bapa manĕmwa phala niŋ awĕka adi śaktimān,
tan āri masamādhi riŋ rahina riŋ wĕṅi saha japa dhīra subrata,
kita iki saŋ iniṣṭi niŋ twas i yayaḥta laki kĕkĕsakĕnta riŋ hati,
wĕlas larapan iŋ siḥ i ṅwaŋ awĕka apunagi maharĕp iŋ tĕka iŋ paran*

pajātyan ira saŋ makānak adhimukhya pituhun iŋ anak maran sukha,
kaduhkhan ira yan katona patita ŋ tanaya nira calānana iŋ sarāt,
kaduṙyyaśan ikaŋ maputra wiparīta kawĕdi nika yan pamīḍana,
halib halĕp ira anaka pratitabhakti magĕlĕm anĕnĕbw-amet guṇa*

hana iki pawaraḥ nira adipuruṣa aminĕkĕti riŋ ulaḥ mwaŋ iŋ gati,
yateka kinĕkĕsku riŋ twas abuṅaḥ makasuluḥ iŋ amet prayojana,
kapaṅgihan ikaŋ janottama wiśeṣa katĕwasa tĕkapnya tan hilaŋ,
maṇik-maṇik iŋ aṅgĕgö kira-kira aṅalahakĕna pataṇḍĕg iŋ musuḥ*

wĕka pwa saŋ aṅuṅsi haywa ni yayaḥ hyun ika ya ta kayuktyan iŋ wĕka,
gawe niŋ atuha pwa nitya gawayĕn ya makalarapana twaŋ iŋ bapa,
kadaŋ sukha tĕkapnya rakwa hiniḍĕpnya wariṅin i samīpa niŋ hĕnū,
dudū pamuji niŋ sarāt ri saguṇanya saphala pinalaṙ paṅöbana*

kalīṅa niŋ ujaṙ ku māsku saphala ṅwaŋ awĕka guṇawān sulakṣaṇa,
ikaŋ phala ri yajña sātus apitowi tan amaḍa kasoṙ ya de nikā,
putus niŋ atibhāgyamanta sira saŋ pinituhu niŋ anak mapet hayu,
mataŋnya kamituhwa haywa ta manaḥta cala yaśani ta ṅhulun tuhan*

<jagaddhita>:3.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

nā liŋ saŋ naranātha mojaṙ i narendratanaya mamanis wuwus nira,
saŋ sāmba adara tan sahuṙ tuhun anĕmbaḥ amuhun iki rakwa maṅkata,
maṅkin sök hati saŋ narendra mamĕlas ry-anak ira wahu-wahwa maṅkana,
de niŋ siḥ pinĕgat mataŋnya n umilī bañu ni mata nira n hawan pipi*

ṅkāna i jro nagara iki saŋ nrĕpasuta amuhuna tumama kaṙwwa pawwahan,
dewī jāmbawatī wawaŋ sira kataṅgama ri tĕka nareśwarātmaja,
haṙṣa anantwa paran ta kāṙyya ni wĕkaṅku mapa kita diṅaryan aṅlawad,
maṅke n prāpta kita i ṅhulun kadi hañaṙ dinadak apa tikaŋ prayojana*

siṅgiḥ liŋ ra bibi i ṅhulun bibi haji inutus ira naranātha maṅkata,
ndān ṅkāna iŋ himawāntapaṙwwata tĕhĕṙ paramarĕṣi sira ika rakṣanĕn,
agya iki ṅhulun induŋ oliha yaśa anĕmuha kawijayan ṅwaŋ iŋ raṇa,
denya asaṅwa pati ṅwaŋ amrihakĕn iŋ nrĕpati pamuhaka iŋ hutaŋ hurip*

ndān amwīta lumampaha ṅwaŋ ibu hetu maṅubhayahita ambĕk i ṅhulun,
haywa aśoka pajātyan iŋ pinakaputra panuluyana dhaṙmma niŋ yayaḥ,
ṅhiŋ pintaṅkw-i panambĕhanta pawĕkas-wĕkas aṅinakana i twas i ṅhulun,
praŋ kahyunkw-ibu len kasiṅhan iŋ ayun pakahawan iy asiḥ nareśwara*

Ūḍū maṅkana kapwa māsku tak aweḥ ṅhulun i kita lumakwa mapraṅa,
ewĕḥ riŋ giṇa śūra riŋ raṇa ṅaranya kahali-halin i ṅhulun tuhan,
Āpan maṙmma dahat ra reṇa ni wĕkaṅku mapa ta wĕnaṅanta taṅgwana,
t-aṅhera pwa huwus wĕkaṅku kita haywa mamituhu ri saŋ nareśwara*

wruḥ ta ṅwaŋ manaha aṅgagap manaḥ i saŋ narapati tan asiḥ nira i ṅhulun,
maṅke wyakti ni tan harĕp nira nihan ta kita bapa kinon mareŋ musuḥ,
sis milw-a anaku tan sinanmata narendra kita bapa makebu ri ṅhulun,
Āpan ṅūni riris nira i ṅhulun agöŋ ḍumawuḥ ika tumus tĕka iŋ kita*

tan maṅka iki n ade manampĕtana kāṙyya paṅutus ira saŋ nareśwara,
Ājñā niŋ guru teki tan dadi linaṅghanan ibu paṅatīta ri ṅhulun,
yadyan mātya sadenya kapwa saha bhakti ri haji makasoṅa ni ṅhulun,
bhāgyan-yan mahurip siwil palaṙ anĕmwa wibhawa siḥ i saŋ hyaŋ i ṅhulun*

saŋ kṣepanya lumampaha ṅhulun ameta hawana niŋ akīṙttya riŋ jagat,
tan saṅkeŋ pamihaŋ sahuṙkkw-i kita cihna niŋ aguṇa kasiṅhawikraman,
jāti kṣatriya tan panoliha kadaŋ kula bapa bibi yāwat iŋ raṇa,
kastutyan kajayan lawan sukha nikaŋ bhuwana kaharĕp i ṅwaŋ amriha*

om putra apa liṅanya reṇa ni wĕkaṅku pasayut ika tan wĕnaŋ kĕdö,
ndā sāmpun mapa ta ujaraṅku ri kita anaku hali-halinaṅku niŋ wĕka,
nāhan taŋ paṅanugrahaṅkw-i tanayan mami kawaca maṇiknya bhāswara,
lāwan bhūṣana saṙwwaratna jayaśatru ta kita bapa denya riŋ raṇa*

dewī maṙmma sira i narendrasuta sāmba kinawacan ira iki hinyasan,
sakweḥ niŋ maṇibhūṣaṇa aṙjja kinĕnākĕn ira tĕhĕṙ i saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
tuṣṭa ambĕk nira saŋ narendradayitā mulati ŋ anak umaṅkata apraṅa,
cĕt mogha asemu rĕs tikaŋ twas anahā ŋ pati karaṇa ni luḥ nira umijil*

lamlam tan pawalĕṙ halĕp nrĕpatiputra sawaŋ ira tawaŋ tĕṅaḥ wĕṅi,
abhra awā maṅĕḍap maṇik nira sawintaŋ apupul i hiriŋ nikaŋ laṅit,
len taŋ hintĕn ira iŋ kapö kumĕñaṙ aṅgyat akilat ahulap tiniṅhalan,
sākṣād handaru teja niŋ kawaca bhāswara lagi tinahā n panunwana*

ry-aṅkat saŋ nrĕpaputra saṅka ri dalĕm nagara dinuluṙ iŋ hulat maliŋ,
līlā tañ jriḥ i paṅhaḍaŋ niŋ akire turida nira n aliṇḍuṅañ crĕmin,
tan seṅĕḥ rinĕbut riŋ ambĕk iŋ akūŋ karĕsĕpana makoliha i sira,
maṙmma aṅde kĕtĕṙ iŋ twas asriŋ awaluy liriŋ ira yan anambaṅi ŋ liriŋ*

ceṭī kāṙwwa tuhan maha aṅucap-ucap turida nika ri saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
muṅgwi i saṇḍiŋ ikaŋ hawan ri haliwat nrĕpasuta sahaja amirĕṅwakĕn,
liŋnya antĕnku lĕwös laṅö saŋ asawaŋ wulan araras anūkṣmakĕn lulut,
rāmya ṅwaŋ tumuta aṅduluṙ kadi wulañjaṙ aṅirim aṅĕnoḥ sumaṇḍiṅa*

saŋ luṅha asiha de tuhanku bapa tiṅhali gati niŋ akūŋ kĕna iŋ unĕŋ,
toliḥ griŋnya kakiṅkiṅan karakĕtan siḥ aṅusapi ri luḥnya meḥ tibā,
haywa anĕṅgaḥ iwĕḥ sinambat iŋ apinta śayana tuluṅĕnta riŋ jinĕm,
tambānanta tĕmĕn tiki n lara matanya kalilipĕn i māsku tan lipur*

tustus niŋ madhu sāri niŋ kusuma saŋ ḍinawuhan i manaḥta yak maṅö,
nitya awastu manis nira analaga riŋ mukha tĕlas apĕnĕd sinukṣukan,
alwaŋ kūŋ raras iŋ manumbĕṙ ahawañ jaruman ahurusan maweḥ ṭikā,
maṅke ṅwaŋ turida alara unĕŋ iki hetu niŋ awaraḥ akon tumiṅhala*

nāntĕn teki hajöŋnya kāri riŋ asaṅwa kuŋ umulat i tapwan iŋ gati,
yan muṅgwiŋ kakawin manisnya pinakāntya mamutusi tĕkap iŋ aṅrĕṅö,
kepwan rūmnya yan iŋ puḍak dadi hana iŋ karas ahawan i tuṅtuŋ iŋ tanaḥ,
rāhasya abhaya niŋ rasanya saphala arasana tamakĕna iŋ pasaṅgaman*

nāhan liŋnya waneḥ dudū saŋ aṅaraŋ sumĕmu-sĕmu rĕṅūnya yan liriŋ,
riṅraŋ haṙṣa rimaŋ-rimaŋnya n alara awiṅit aṅĕsaḥ awaṙṇna kasrĕpan,
maṙmmanya n paturū ya ta anamara lĕŋlĕŋ arurub asana ahulĕs gaḍuŋ,
kady-a aṅipya mareŋ smarālaya mahĕnwa lĕyĕp i kukus iŋ hrĕbuk miṅiŋ*

wwantĕn bhrānta kĕdö manūtakĕn unĕŋnya karakĕtan aminta sanmata,
tamtam ry-ambĕk ika aṅajap midĕra riŋ wukiṙ amasaha kūŋnya riŋ pasir,
maṅkin lĕŋlĕŋ atön gĕrĕḥ raras i rūmnya n aṅidani laṅö nikaŋ rimaŋ,
jañjan citta niki n tan eṅĕt i sĕkaṙnya tan atutuṙ i luṅsuṙ iŋ gĕluŋ*

akweḥ taŋ paricārika amĕkulakĕn lulut ika ri nareśwarātmaja,
tuṅtuŋ niŋ turidanya rakwa riŋ awaknya sinahaja winiṅkis iŋ laṅö,
len kiṅkiŋ lara kūŋ maṅĕn-haṅĕn ikaŋ rĕṇa pamawan unĕŋ raras hati,
rĕs rūm-rūm i liriŋnya haṙṣa pamalanda nika winawana amatan-matan*

sāmpun prāpta ri heŋ narendratanaya praṇata ri sira saŋ halāyudha,
amwīt maṅkata māṙ manāntwa mawĕlas ri sira tĕhĕṙ aweḥ warāyudha,
ndā tapwan masuwe muwaḥ sira mara i narapati harimūṙtti riŋ sabhā,
ndān amwīta muwaḥ lawan pinĕkĕtan gati nira hana riŋ himālaya*

ndān saŋ śrī nrĕpa krĕṣṇa māṙ hati nira n mulat iŋ anak umaṅkata alaga,
waspa agātra dine hasiḥ nira sinambay anaku liŋ ira aṅgamĕl taṅan,
maṙmma iŋ putra maśabda manda wĕkasan ta manaṅis asĕkĕl nareśwara,
ramya arūm karĕṅö kunĕŋ pĕyĕḥ ikaŋ swara kadi gĕrĕḥ iŋ labuḥ kapat*

ndā putraṅku sudhīrakĕn sapaṅutusku dumamĕlakĕn iŋ prajāhita,
haywa iwĕḥ pinakāśraya ambĕk awilāsa ŋ amalaku parāśraya i kita,
jñāna akas puruṣottamanta makabuddhi nira saŋ adhikārarakṣaka,
matya amatya jayanta tan mupakara iŋ pinahayu nira wīra tan surud*

saŋ śūra pratisāra riŋ raṇa sira apagĕḥ amagĕhi wīraśāsana,
tan pambhagnakĕna iŋ harĕp-harĕp iŋ aty-amalaku śaraṇa atiduhkhita,
siṅgiḥ janma wiśeṣa kapwa sira yogya pinaran inusiṙ niŋ atpada,
tuṅgal-tuṅgala kastawan prakaśita adhipati ṅaran ira ñ jaya iŋ raṇa*

yan bwat kṣatriyadhaṙmma niŋ yadukula akral anuluṅi kahaywan iŋ prajā,
śūra akol lĕṅĕn aṅhalaŋ-halaṅi śatru tĕka tan awĕdi iŋ paraṅmukha,
byaktābyakta kasiṅhan oliḥ anatap śiraḥ iŋ ari kapökan iŋ ratha,
lagy-a aśoca ri luḥ nikaŋ ghariṇi niŋ musuḥ amalaku milwa patyana*

ndaḥ maṅke pwa kinonku n amrihakĕna ŋ para rĕṣi hĕlĕm iŋ himālaya,
haywa ajīwita yadyapi i bhaya mara i kapĕjaha tuwi haywa saṅśaya,
kastutyanta phalanya göṅakĕna de niŋ aṅulati lĕkasta rakṣaka,
yeka kṣatriyadhaṙmma tan dadi surud tumuluṅa ri saduhkha niŋ para*

jīwājīwa ni saŋ mahāpuruṣa donya dadaha ri kahaywan iŋ jagat,
kīṙttyākīṙttya ni saŋ huwus krĕtayaśa amuli-muliha wiśīṙṇna niŋ prajā,
dhaṙmmādhaṙmma ri siŋ pinaṇḍita mahāṙddhika pinakapatīṙthan iŋ sarāt,
putrāputra tumiṙwwa kāṙyya nira saŋ wwaŋ atuha laki yogya tūtakĕn*

yan wwaŋ śakti tan ahyun iŋ yaśa hade kinarajakĕna śakti riŋ para,
maṅkā wwaŋ mapirak yadin kapana tan pamirakana sarāt ya tan padon,
wyaṙtha ŋ kāṙyya-ya tan pakāṙyya hayu tan damĕlakĕna tĕkap mahājana,
tañ jīwān ika jīwa niŋ wimukha riŋ hayu kadi-kadi jīwa niŋ kĕnas*

rwa ikaŋ kāṙyya ri loka yogya gawayĕn kanĕkĕtakĕna yogya daṙśśanan,
nyā ŋ kāṙyya adhiparatra teki riŋ akāṙyya sĕḍĕŋ i kahananya sādhana,
mwaŋ kāṙyya amuhara prasiddha hayu ya ika katĕmu riŋ ihatra don ikā,
kāṙyyā kāṙyyakĕnanta kāṙyya saphala amuhara kasuphalanta riŋ jagat*

saŋ niṣkāṙyya ri saŋ kṣinatriya tanora hinaliwatan i ṅhulun kabeḥ,
lāwan praŋ winuwus katönku ri kawiṣṭi niŋ apuliḥ i tandaŋ iŋ musuḥ,
kady-adyus curiganya kāmbulan amūk tĕhĕṙ amĕjahi śatru riŋ raṇa,
yekā wīṙyya ṅaranya riŋ raṇasabhā muliḥ iniriŋ atampakan śiraḥ*

yatna ikī kita sātiruny-aku gumantyana n asukha maran pwa ya abuṅaḥ,
pöŋ-pöŋ yowana śaktimanta kita saṅhulun anaku lĕwas paṅāśrayan,
śūra iŋ praŋ puriḥ iŋ prawīra tumulad guṇa ni yayaḥ ika agawe sukha,
māry-a aweha kaṅelana iŋ atuha kapwa kahalĕpa nikaŋ tĕka iŋ tĕkan*

wwantĕn śabda niraŋ rĕṣi prawara nārada ri kita rikāna keṅĕti,
tan wwaŋ len kita rakṣakā liŋ ira riŋ himagiri śaraṇā mahāyati,
nāhan taŋ laras uttama atiśaya śakti nika ya ta pawehan i ṅhulun,
om swasthā tanayaṅku māsku jayaśatru ta kita bapa riŋ himālaya*

toḥ t-aṅkat hara pöṅakĕn hayu nikaŋ diwasa makaphalā ŋ kadigjayan,
nāhan liŋ nira nātha krĕṣṇa tumuluy nrĕpasuta n umusap ri jöŋ prabhu,
sāmpun maṅkana śīghra yan wijil i heŋ sira katĕmu tikaŋ balādhika,
muṅgaḥ riŋ ratha raktawaṙṇna sira dāruki pinakasurakṣa niŋ ratha*

wwantĕn daṙśśaniya iŋ raras wwaŋ apaṅus prawala ṅaran ikaŋ kadaŋ haji,
anwam pantĕs amaṅku pawwahan iraŋ nrĕpasuta manulus wicakṣaṇa,
towin wāhu dhanuṙddhara aṅaji kalāghawan ika ri nareśwarātmaja,
nāhan hetu nikā n tumūt aharĕp apraṅa lihatana de nrĕpātmaja*

maṅkat saŋ nrĕpaputra keriṅa sayodha nira paḍa wināni riŋ raṇa,
tan makweḥ dahatĕn limaŋ puluḥ ikaŋ prajurit iṅadhisādhu nītiman,
saṅkĕp denya manuṅgaŋ iŋ ratha sama aṅhalĕpi kinawacan paḍa araras,
tan kantun ta rakeŋ juru dyaḥ aharan sahaja halĕp anuṅgaŋ iŋ ratha*

lampaḥ niŋ ratha rāmya riŋ lĕbuḥ atūt palipiran i harĕp nikaŋ tĕpas,
mambö wāluka denya keriṙ i siriṙ niŋ anila mapulaŋ lawan hrĕbuk,
paṅhrik niŋ kuda waṙṇna masyaŋ umara iŋ acala dumulura i nrĕpātmaja,
grit niŋ cakra nikaŋ ratha asĕmu surak pinarĕṅan i gĕrĕḥ muni i du lor*

māsa pwa ika riris-riris halit awoṙ haṅin anirirakĕn sĕkaṙ lĕwas,
megha abāŋ mahirĕŋ waneḥ asĕmu riṅriŋ anawĕṅi hiriŋ nikaŋ laṅit,
kuntul möṙ aduluṙ ñamut-ñamut awaṙṇna mĕnuṙ aluñut iŋ gĕluŋ lukar,
mandra alon kĕtĕṙ iŋ patĕṙ kadi taṅis niŋ ahayu kawĕkas hana iŋ jinĕm*

luṅhā sāmpun adoḥ huliḥ nrĕpatiputra humaliwat i deśa niŋ pura,
māṙgga agöŋ lĕmaḥ aṅgĕgĕṙ hawan ira agarihul i salĕsĕk nikaŋ watu,
tĕkwan koṅaŋ ikaŋ pasiṙ sabha-sabhān ikaŋ aṅapi laṅö kasaṅhuban,
tuṅhā niŋ paraṅan lĕṅöŋ hana wuruŋ-wuruṅan niŋ atanaḥ kari iŋ śilā*

paṇḍan raṅkaŋ atuntunan ri tĕpi niŋ pasiṙ asira-siran karaŋ liman,
kady-aṅlaṅhuy ariṅgĕkan ri tĕka niŋ bañu pasaŋ amatĕmwakĕn harus,
kĕmbaŋ laywan awoṙ karamkam apulaŋ lagi karawit i roknya karyakan,
aṙjjā gātra nikaŋ puḍak-puḍak acihna kakawin iŋ akūŋ katuṅhapan*

strī wāhw-a adaluwaŋ tigaŋ siki kapaṅgiḥ anamun i parasnya riŋ pilis,
ndan rakwa ika mara aṅirim ri saŋ adihyaŋ amawa ri sakāpti saŋ pĕjaḥ,
tampiŋ siñjuŋ ika araras jinamaṅan sahaja pasaji tiṅhal iŋ mulat,
byaṙ kĕbyaṙ siniriṙ-siriṙ niŋ aṅin edi kadi sĕmi pamiṅkisan puḍak*

olaḥ niŋ  ṙyyak alumba-lumba maṅusiṙ paraŋ atĕpi guhā liwaŋ-liwuŋ,
lwiṙ kuṅkaŋ karĕṅö swaranya jĕmuṙ iŋ paraŋ anaragi mandra kāṅinan,
himpĕṙ hintĕn awoṙ pawal sira-siratnya ri papupul ikaŋ sahiŋ-sahiŋ,
kady-a apet kalaṅön katon uwuṙ-uwuṙ nika karakĕt i duṅhus iŋ karaŋ*

nūsa anuṅgalakĕn laṅö lĕṅĕŋ ika ahyun anarukaha rāmya niŋ pasir,
ndan pakṣa amadanāśrama ika rinĕgĕpnya n aṅusira parantya niŋ maṅö,
rĕp sūkṣma ahaliṅan limut kadi humötakĕn ika ri manaḥ niŋ aṅlĕṅöŋ,
cöt siddhy-a aniluman katon kakĕñaran rawi lĕyĕp ajamaŋ kuwuŋ-kuwuŋ*

ṅkāna iŋ lod hana ta plawā nikaŋ amañciŋ aparahu jukuŋ panuṅgalan,
rūpanya aputiḥ aṅhulap-hulap apan lumarap i larap iŋ wway iŋ tasik,
waṙṇna apiṇḍa manuṅgaŋ iŋ kuda sumĕṅka tumurun i baṅĕt nikaŋ halun,
mumbul pwa ŋ gajamīna kāraṇa nika an paṅĕcĕpuk awĕlaḥ mareŋ tĕpi*

<śikhariṇī>:4.
⏑ – –| – – –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 17

sawaŋ kanyā lwiṙ niŋ pasisiṙ i halintaŋ nrĕpasuta,
lĕṅöŋ waṙṇnanya ahyas mapata-patahan taŋ  ṙyyak alaṅö,
layaṙ niŋ baṇyāga anusu-nusu katon manda tan awās,
limut niŋ wway māwra asĕmu-sĕmu pupuṙ piṅhay i pipi*

huwus luṅha adoḥ saŋ nrĕpasuta tĕka iŋ wanwa masĕnĕt,
alas loṙ kulwan wetan ika marĕnĕb tīṙtha maparĕk,
pucaŋ mwaŋ nyū makrĕp walahaṙ ika tūbanya gumuruḥ,
makĕmpoŋ-kĕmpoŋ taŋ palu daluwaŋ asraŋ masawuran*

tĕṅaḥ ṅwe mantuk taŋ tuha buru paḍa aṅliḥ kapanasan,
rare maṅhwan saṅkeŋ talaga saha kañcuṙ paḍa tĕlĕs,
kaki mpw-aṅhwan goḥ kapwa pijĕṙ anukĕt kāwanan aṅöb,
muliḥ maṙmma amakpak maṅamĕṙ i sapinya n sapi ḍayaŋ*

arāṙyyan saŋ nāthātmaja sakarĕŋ iŋ wāṇḍirataru,
aliṅgiḥ riŋ watw-aṙjja śumayana kāliḥ pamucaṅan,
tinaṅkil de niŋ bhrĕtya nira tan adoḥ rāki sahaja,
tĕka anāntwā maswāgata tĕhĕṙ asucy-a asaji taḍaḥ*

rara anonton-nonton wija-wijaḥ arampak paḍa rara,
girahyāsĕn de saŋ lituhayu magupyan ḍara-ḍaran,
guyunya asriŋ peda n saputi ri kĕmulnya ayat-ayatan,
ade liŋnya n sinyaŋ muliha pijĕṙ ahyun salaḥ iḍĕp*

lumiṅsiṙ saŋ hyaŋ we nrĕpasuta n umaṅkat sira muwaḥ,
matūt rimbaŋ niŋ paṙwwata dinuluṙ iŋ rĕm saha riris,
maṅö de ny-ambö niŋ kusuma tahĕn aṙwwan ḍara-ḍaran,
lĕṅöŋ līla anon luṅluṅan aṅĕliḥ eñjuḥ kapawanan*

bagañjiŋ riñcuŋ sāk lĕwas atuha sāmpun karayapan,
aṅanti i tuṅhā niŋ paraṅan aṅuṅaŋ groŋ wway adalĕm,
kalusyan tambiŋ runtuḥ i hatĕp ika awaṙṇna kawudan,
manambiŋ-nambiŋ lwiṙ mayat alabuha iŋ roŋ ahañutan*

ri himbaŋ-himbaŋ niŋ giriwana hana aśoka marĕnĕb,
i soṙ kĕmbaŋ laywan sĕpaḥ agĕnĕt iŋ watw-aṅalasa,
winaṅwaŋ-waṅwaŋ rantunaniŋ ahañaŋ wāhw-iṅalapan,
paṅādeśā sambat kawĕkas i lawö niŋ puḍak arūm*

hana iki n kaṙwwa istrī wĕḍihan ika ragyan wahu lĕsĕḥ,
rabinya adodot jiṅga sinuhun iki n mesi kapipi,
piliḥ mantuk saṅkeŋ sawuŋ ika rarasnya ajĕnu hijo,
mucap mantunya amwaŋ panaṅis i putunya n pakilayū*

hana wwaŋ pat-pat wijy-aduluṙ apayuŋ tekaŋ i harĕp,
tikaŋ muṅgwi i wuntat mamiku-mikul abwat bari-bari,
piliḥ waṙgga ibu mwaŋ sakari kaminīnta pwa marikā,
ulaḥ ḍaŋ hyaŋ saŋ nāyaka cinaritanya n kapanasan*

trĕbis wiṣṭi lwiṙ niŋ kahawan asamīpa alas alaṅö,
paraŋ groŋ-groŋ-roŋ niŋ juraŋ i hiriṅanya amuwuhi rĕs,
gaḍuŋ moṇḍuŋ mĕṇḍuḥ siluk ika sugandha aṅrarasakĕn,
kapantĕsnya sthānā niŋ amawa tanaḥ kaṙwwa lĕpihan*

arimbit kambaŋ rimbaŋ iŋ acala rūmnya amuwuhi kūŋ,
sahaṙṣa anāntwa ikiŋ prawala ri siraŋ krĕṣṇatanaya,
tuhan rakryan tonton ta raras i kucup niŋ tarahudan,
sawaŋ hastā niŋ stry-a alurus akupik aṅgyat manuduhi*

hyasan ṅgānya ikiŋ paṙwwata ya pinakendaḥ dalan ikā,
kasinya asukṣuk riŋ tapakan apĕnĕd sāmpun arata,
dukut riŋ sĕṅkan lwiṙ lilit agĕnĕt awyaŋ mĕtu wuruŋ,
tuhun kambaŋ laywan paṅisi ni rarasnya n winulatan*

liraŋ ramya ajaṅjaŋ pinanuliṅakĕn de nikaŋ ĕpiŋ,
pakis dadw-ānwam siñjaŋ ika sĕkaṙ iŋ jaṅga manĕḍĕŋ,
mariṅgū-riṅgū kāṅinan aṅucapit ronya maṅawe,
kusuḥ niŋ wwe ri jro juraŋ iki n arĕs ya akĕrĕcĕkan*

taṅeḥ yan waṙṇnan rāmya nika bapa sāmpun kulĕm usĕn,
ndi teka anuŋ yogya n pakulĕmana maṅke n lihatana,
sawātan lāwan pājaran athawa yan wanwa karika,
sakahyun rakryan paṅhinĕpana paḍa arĕmbha niyata*

nahan liŋ rākī saŋ prawala mataña i saŋ nrĕpasuta,
sumĕṅkā rakwa iŋ āśrama manaḥ iraŋ krĕṣṇatanaya,
na hetunya n tan lālana lari nikaŋ syandana kabeḥ,
kalalwan wanwa akweḥ pira-pira kunaŋ pāṙśśwa kahawan*

tumuṅgaŋ śꜽla hyaŋ dinakara sumöŋ manda tan awās,
limut muṅgwīŋ agra araras asĕmu soṅsoŋ dadu bañu,
muni ŋ cuṅgereret lyan ĕpiŋ araras mwaŋ hayam alas,
kidaŋ śīghra amaṅsul mawaraḥ i kaki hyaŋ matamuyan*

kapaṅgiḥ tekaŋ Āśrama rinacana iŋ saṙwwakusuma,
lĕṅöŋ nyāsanya awaṙṇna kula-kula niŋ swaṙgga manurun,
huwus labdhajñāna hyaŋ atuha nimittanya n ahalĕp,
pĕnuḥ makweḥ taŋ śiṣya ra tapa dudū saŋ kili-kili*

kaki hyaŋ kagyāt-gyāt ri ḍatĕŋ ira saŋ krĕṣṇatanaya,
nini hyaŋ kapwa agya agarawalan anonton wahu-wahun,
wijaḥ saŋ tāpa ahyun wruha tĕhĕṙ adan bāhiri mijil,
wawaŋ tiṅhalnya atön linawanan atiṅgal kawiratin*

kunaŋ sakweḥ niŋ bhrĕtya winani paḍa aṅanti ri yawa,
madum ṅgwan kapwa ahuṙ-huran iki n asaṇḍiŋ lwaḥ alaṅö,
hana aṅheṙ-heṙ iŋ bwat kamala maṅĕnĕs yañ jalawura,
marūm lwiṙ saŋ wikw-iŋ tulis arĕja piṇḍa asĕgĕ-sĕgĕḥ*

tĕlas prāpta i jro maṇḍala patamuyan krĕṣṇatanaya,
ndatan kantun rāki prawala ṅuniweḥ rāki sahaja,
mijil kāliḥ strī hyaŋ matuha marĕk aswāgata sira,
arūm de niŋ mojāṙ amuhara sukha aṅimbuhi pĕnĕd*

nda bhāgya aṅlīlā saŋ nrĕpasuta mareŋ śūnya patapan,
paran don prāpta ṅke kita bapa diṅaryan mahas-ahas,
kawuntĕn kapwa asañjata paḍa masimpĕn linihatan,
kasihyun t-a ajaṙ yan kita laki wiśeṣātmaja haji*

malĕs mojaṙ saŋ krĕṣṇatanaya mapet śabdaracana,
kĕnoḥ liŋ saŋ paṇḍya ataña ri kami līlā n mahas-ahas,
kinonkon saŋ śrī bhūpati tiki ranak saŋ yatiwara,
rumakṣa i saŋ muṅgwiŋ himagiri nanā de niŋ asura*

kunĕŋ nyāpan ratrya aṅhinĕpa ta ranak saŋ muniwara,
tamolahkw-iŋ deya amriha tuhun iŋ eñjaŋ lumarisa,
kamāhātmyan saŋ paṇḍita masiha ri twas niŋ umara,
sumewa jñāna hyaŋ matuha śaraṇaṅkw-iŋ kasugatin*

asowe saŋ sāmba awacana sakamantyan kulĕm usĕn,
ikaŋ sandhyā sāmpun marahup asalin bhūṣaṇa sira,
masaŋ we tistis yeka n inaturakĕn pwa ŋ kilaŋ arūm,
muliḥ kāliḥ strī hyaŋ matuha kari tekā nrĕpasuta*

wulan piŋ nĕm riŋ kāṙttika kahatuṙ aṅde turida kūŋ,
sahaṙṣa asyaŋ rowaŋ nini tapi mara aṅdon amĕŋ-amĕŋ,
kunĕŋnya i saŋ sāmba aṅawaśakĕn arĕpnya iŋ hati pinĕm,
uḍū saŋ tāmuy liŋ niki n api kasaṇḍuŋ mapi gigir*

hana ataṇḍak ramya aṅiduṅakĕn unĕŋnya n karakĕtan,
karaśmin saŋ krĕṣṇātmaja rinacana iŋ gīta winuwus,
si tan seṅĕḥ liŋnya ndi n aluluta saŋ kāṙyya luluta,
sawet niŋ göŋ haṙṣa akĕtĕb anĕmu laky-an paṅuruhi*

dudū taŋ kily-a ajoŋ sumalini laranya n paḍa wagĕd,
nahan liŋnya ṅwaŋ teki sihana gati ṅwaŋ mara-mara,
waneḥ liŋnya ṅwaŋ si iki ya lagi tiba iŋ saŋ wahu tĕka,
ndi donya n tak mājaṙ ya si wahu tĕka ndak pĕkul iki*

waneḥ ramya apetpetan aṅĕnĕs apet uṅgwan asĕnĕt,
hana ambĕknya n prāpta iŋ nrĕpasuta maminta akalihana,
mijil timpaŋ-timpaŋ lagi ḍara-ḍaran baddha katiliŋ,
wuwusnya aswī kanya aku haḍaṅi kakuŋ saŋ wahu tĕka*

hana iki n kily-a ajaṅjaŋ anahĕn ulaḥ niŋ kararayan,
sumimbiŋ buddhinya atatasa lumihat riŋ lituhayu,
raras niŋ wwaŋ sawwaŋ cinarita nika iŋ goṣṭhi pinaran,
ahal tībra ajaṙnya aṅrasani puput iŋ kāṙyya tan asiḥ*

kaki hyaŋ ramya agoṣṭhi kalĕṅĕṅan iŋ deśa kayaśan,
anaṇḍaŋ twak muṅgwiŋ sujaŋ apĕnĕd antuk niŋ anasi,
manis niŋ bhāṣa mwaŋ kiduŋ ika samitra araras arūm,
kahĕnti ŋ lek denya aṅhĕla-hĕla lĕṅöŋ niŋ sakalaṅön*

<aśwalalita>:5.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

wuwusĕn ikaŋ bala aṅinĕp i heŋ paḍa aṅinum arāmya-rāmyan aṅiduŋ,
lĕṅĕŋ asuluḥ pĕtuŋ sinib iki n dudū sukha-sukhan ya rakwa sajuru,
balĕman agöŋ panunwan iki n ambayas huraŋ uliḥ nika aṅdadak amet,
bari-bari tambu-tambul iki tan pĕgat jaru-jaruḥ nika awĕtu laṅö*

hana ta ya tuṅgak iŋ wwaŋ aṅinum bĕtaḥ linarikan muwaḥ tan akalib,
titiṙ arĕhak mariṅguhan aṅantuk asriŋ anĕpak pupūnya n aṅucap,
maṅabuk amaḥ praṅĕn wuwus ikā n musap tatu nika i lĕṅĕnya n akihal,
karaṇa nika akrak iŋ paṅinuman ndi tā liŋ ika n aprĕgas riŋ alariḥ*

hana maṅĕnĕs ri soṙ nikaŋ aśoka lālana samitra ya aṅucap-ucap,
kucu-kucu lot ginanti cinucupnya wet nika ri tuṅgal iŋ manaḥ anūt,
sumari magoṣṭhi sewaka nika amalaṙ kahulunan lana atapa-tapan,
hayam-ayamanya lāgi winuwus nika anahura siḥ ri saŋ nrĕpasuta*

hana maṅucap lĕkasnya n awijil pirak saha guyunya kaṙkkaśa pacĕḥ,
liŋ ika mĕṅĕn-mĕṅĕn kawilĕt ambĕk ewĕha lawan turuŋ tama rusit,
hana kagiṇaṅku yan pagĕha de ni keñ juru kacidra den kawĕkasan,
amawa tulis rahadyan aku yan paṅĕṇḍĕka ri donku siddha manahur*

yatika tĕwĕknya deñ juru sira amrĕpa iry-aku wulat nika asuma habot,
miṅay ikahĕn sinĕṅgaḥ amiraḥ ḍaḍanya sinapaṅku tan panahuri,
cinulu-culuḥku maṅkin abutĕŋ  lana aṅucap asiṇḍi liŋnya n amisuḥ,
pinihanan i ṅhulun pwa satĕṅaḥ cakĕt mĕtu guyunya māri marĕṅū*

malĕs awaraḥ ta rowaŋ ika liŋ nika aku bi hañaṙ ḍatĕŋ mamĕŋ-amĕŋ,
amilaṅa wāni donku kahaḍaŋ hana iky-atukaṙ iŋ hawan paḍa wani,
ndan i haliwatkw-anĕṅgaḥ aliwat nika iry-aku tĕhĕṙ ta ya amisu-misuḥ,
tan ubhaya ta aku denya tak alakw-analyani riya anahuṙ tĕlu wĕlas*

nahan ujaṙ iŋ bala aṅucap-ucap dudū taŋ aturū makĕg masahuran,
lawan ika paṅhawinya paḍa tan hana aṅliliṙ apan kaṅelan aḍarat,
tĕhĕṙ anawĕṅyakĕn turuŋ ataṅhi maṅhwab iri lĕt nika asriŋ anitir,
wĕkasan ataṅhy-adandan ahulĕs hiḍĕpnya makĕcap tiki n kapacirit*

tiḍak ḍikĕtāhui
<krĕti>:6.
⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 20

rahina awa waspada patiṅkaḥ i kayu ri sare nikaŋ gĕgĕr,
pacakiṅkuk iŋ bakikuk aṅlawani gaguŋ i piṅgiṙ iŋ juraŋ,
gumarañjaŋ iŋ bañu sakeŋ paruŋ aṅawara kuṅkaŋ iŋ juraŋ,
irikā nini hyaŋ awuṅū dadakan inatag iŋ hayam halas*

naranāthaputra wara sāmba maśila ri harĕp mahāyati,
winaraḥ sira iŋ karaṇa yajña n ulaha niŋ akīṙtti riŋ raṇa,
mwaŋ ikaŋ prayojana niŋ abrata manusup ameta pājaran,
niyatanya tuṅgal inusiṙ hiwag ika mapalenan iŋ hawan*

ri tĕlas nira amuhun umaṅkata lumaku tikaŋ ratha agĕlis,
palapat hañaṙ kajawuhan hawan ira sumare sakeŋ gĕgĕr,
pagagan katon kakĕliran limut awayaŋ ulaḥ nikaŋ pisaŋ,
wwaŋ amet gaṅan lĕṅĕŋ abaṇḍuŋ aṅiduŋ alaṅö lana amacĕḥ*

haraṇan kapaṅgiḥ asawe mawilĕt alĕsu śīṙṇna riŋ wana,
lumale suḍanya marĕk iŋ kalak asĕkaṙ aket lawan karuk,
kucup iŋ sĕkaṙ lĕmaḥ i soṙ asĕmu taji tajĕm sinuṅgakĕn,
kadi mutyahāra kasawuṙ titis i hĕbun i tuṅtuŋ iŋ dukut*

patapan hañaṙ tarukan iŋ kajĕnĕkan amagantakĕn laṅö,
putus iŋ kalaṅwan aṅaliḥ bhramara nika ri sāri niŋ wuṅū,
ḍatĕŋ iŋ riris kadi sinuṅsuŋ i guyu ni sĕkaṙnya riŋ natar,
asĕgĕḥ katon kucup ikaŋ bakuŋ irika maṅañjali iŋ tamuy*

hana bañw-inuttama kapaṅgiḥ apĕnĕd ahĕniŋ sakeŋ wukir,
pinaran patīṙthan ira saŋ sujana tuwi lanā n acaṅkrama,
aḍake bañunya kahalintaṅan awilĕt ikaŋ kataŋ-kataŋ,
watu luṅka-luṅka ri pĕluknya lagi makaparanti niŋ maṅö*

sumiriṙ tikaŋ haṅin alon makin aṅinaki citta niŋ mahas,
amuluŋ-muluŋ hrĕbuk arūm bhramara kadi tĕka apasaṙ-pasar,
rumarab-rarab kadi pupuṙ lutuṙ anamaṙ i gandha niŋ gĕluŋ,
sahaja amahā mituturi ŋ rimaŋ alulut i rūm-rum iŋ pipi*

hana wanwa śuddha sipi rāmya nika janapada atiśobhita,
riŋ anaṙtha nāma niki kaprakaśita paran iŋ wwaŋ aṅlĕṅöŋ,
ri pasiṙnya paṇḍan apuḍak saphala kumasut iŋ karaŋ liman,
adhikāra niŋ kalĕṅĕṅan linayaran iŋ abhāṇḍa bhāṣita*

hujuŋ iŋ karaŋ sumiraŋ iŋ pasisi hawan iŋ aṅhuwus-huwus,
kadi kampira ŋ tirisan iŋ lumaris ahañutan tĕlas hilaŋ,
lwaḥ i tīra tan lumaris iŋ mukha mahiwagakĕn susuk-susuk,
śawa niŋ maṅö saha laras kusuma wĕkas ika anusup-nusup*

anĕḍĕk patiṅhalan ikaŋ jaladhi riŋ anĕka a kasaŋ carik,
tan apujy-anajyakĕn ikaŋ sarasi saha lawan huraŋ tanaḥ,
riŋ awaṙgga rūmnya karikā tan asĕgĕha tĕmĕn pananmata,
riŋ ahimya-himyan iki len kawi paḍa mapasuṅsuṅan hañaŋ*

katĕkāna rāmya riŋ añaṙ palabuhan alaṅö tiniṅhalan,
ri pĕkĕnya kambaḥ asarik racana ni pajajaṙnya len tĕpas,
waruga aruhuṙ paṅuṅaṅañ jinamanikan i luṅgaḥ iŋ gaḍuŋ,
pamalantĕnanya karĕṅö swara ni palu nika aṅiriŋ kiduŋ*

kahatuṙ manis pĕkĕn ika atiśaya sukha ḍatĕŋ nrĕpātmaja,
atihaŋ-tihaŋ tarima ta ikiŋ amalija lulut paḍa ahajöŋ,
amuraḥ liriŋnya tinawākĕn ika ri haliwat nrĕpātmaja,
irikā n katon kupa-kupaŋnya saha jaja sajöŋnya pintanĕn*

masuhun-suhun sĕkaṙ ikaŋ parawan ajaja kūŋnya kaṅlihan,
mawade hayunya ri harĕpnya hañaṅĕn ira saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
mwaŋ apaṅkwa-paṅkwana tĕṅaḥnya maṅusira tĕwas karāsikan,
lalu kāsihanya tuna kūŋnya manaḍaḥ-asiha iŋ kuraŋ wĕlas*

haliwat nira irikaŋ anaṙtha pira-pira kadoḥ nira n huwus,
aṅawindhyapaṙwwata ri pāṙśśwa nika hawan ira amuraŋ-muraŋ,
milu duhkha buddhi nira de ni gatarasa nikā n kuraŋ tahĕn,
kadi melika iki riŋ apan sira mulati tĕgal nika apaḍaŋ*

pakulan-kulan pasanakan kaludan ika sama aṅhapit raras,
rwi sisiṙ pilaŋ rukĕm aṅap lumaru-laru sĕwönya riŋ sapāŋ,
kasine lĕwas kapanasan tĕlas akuniŋ i saṇḍiŋ-iŋ hawan,
aṅalas manis gula gumantuŋ ika tinĕmu niŋ mahas maṅö*

lumalay-lalay galiŋ ika anwam asuluṙ aṅayuḥ tahĕn ragas,
wruḥ ataṅkil iŋ lĕbak ikaŋ mata-mata kuluma aṅuṅaŋ tawaŋ,
kalawan gaḍuŋnya sumĕkaṙ-mĕkaṙ ika kadi pahyas iŋ maṅö,
umaḥ iŋ mabhaṇḍagiṇa paṇḍan ika ri baciṅaḥnya sök pacĕḥ*

lumaris muwaḥ nrĕpasuta i hayunan ira ri madhya niŋ tĕgal,
rĕmĕŋ aṅdadak truḥ awĕlas ri gati nira n aṅölakĕn panas,
pawana aṅiriŋ miriṙ alon maṅatĕrakĕn i saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
gĕrĕḥ aṅhiṅöt-iṅĕti riŋ hawan ika dug aganti riŋ tĕgal*

gunuŋ ojayan wahu katon awuk-awuk aṅawuṙ sakeŋ adoḥ,
kadi kahyaṅan paṅalusan hyaŋ atanu kalaṅönya tan sipi,
aruhuṙ lĕyĕp lwiṙ ilaŋ iŋ jaladhara riŋ anūtakĕn laṅö,
paran iŋ limut gati nika apatitisan iŋ ĕbun sakeŋ tawaŋ*

hiriŋ-iŋ laṅit pili-piliḥ lalayan ira bhaṭāra manmatha,
matulis laṅö ni jaladanya winĕtu-wĕtu niŋ samīraṇa,
i ruhuṙnya teja mawĕnĕs kinĕñarakĕn i polaḥ iŋ kilat,
wukiṙ ojayan kalimutan lĕyĕp asĕmu tulis hañaṙ lutur*

anuluy lari nrĕpatiputra sira wahu sumĕṅka riŋ wukir,
kahiriŋ-hiriŋ lari nikaŋ ratha ri hiriṅan iŋ gĕgĕṙ-gĕgĕr,
irikaŋ juraŋ hana ta wuṅkuk akaramas amaṅkuk iŋ śilā,
kadi tiṅkaḥ iŋ susuḥ aneŋ watu maṅariŋ-ariŋ sakeŋ bañu*

aliwat  nrĕpātmaja riŋ ojayan alaris ikaŋ ratha aga ilis,
aniraŋ ri yātragiri ri imbaŋ ika hawan ira amuraŋ-muraŋ,
agĕlaṙ tikaŋ wrĕṣabha hinwan iriya maduluṙ yathāsukha,
tan awĕdy-anon gaja-turaṅga-ratha paḍa lumakw-arampakan*

lwaḥ ahöt anambak karĕṅö swara gaṅari nikaŋ saraswatī,
kĕna śāpa rakwa karaṇanya n inĕnahakĕn iŋ tĕgal marū,
kawĕlas-harĕp tahĕn ika iŋ tĕpi sana-sini lot hibĕk lĕbū,
kasihan tan asmi hana maṅragasi lĕṅĕŋ aṅantyakĕn jawuḥ*

awiwākṣita ika n alawas nrĕpatanaya lumampaḥ iŋ hĕnu,
ḍatĕŋ iŋ himādri sira n aṙjja mulati lĕṅĕŋ iŋ wanāntara,
patapan katiṅgal alawas kabuyutan ika saṇḍiŋ iŋ hawan,
awiraŋ katonan ikaŋ aṙcca kajĕnĕkan aliṇḍuṅan tahĕn*

tiḍak ḍīkĕtāhui

rāmya panuṅsuŋ iŋ himagiri i nrĕpatisuta paḍa agawe parahita,
tumpyatak iŋ hĕnū yaśa sajinya saha bañu tinuntun iŋ pĕtuŋ aho,

tuṣṭa saŋ āṙyya denya katĕkan-tĕkan ira magiraŋ-giraŋ hati nira*

ṅhel ira saŋ narendrasuta māri sira siniriṙ iŋ samīraṇa mirir,
maṅkat atūt hiriŋ-hiriṅan iŋ giriwana sira lālana alalĕḥ alon,
thāni wiśīṙṇna de ni hala niŋ narakabala tinon iraŋ nrĕpasuta,
wāhu rinambu-rambu waruganya para-paran i tiṅhal iŋ humaliwat*

imbaŋ ikaŋ himācala kidul ya ta pinaran i saŋ narendratanaya,

towin ikaŋ wulan katawĕṅan n paṅaruhuṙ atawĕŋ ghana ataratayan,
dok muni len kĕbĕt-kĕbĕt aganti pawurahan i daryas iŋ kĕpuḥ agöŋ*

maṅkin arĕs tanora mahawan hana ni hawan i lambuŋ iŋ wukiṙ ikā,
śūnya sapaṅhaḍaŋ-haḍaṅan iŋ macan aṅaliŋ-aliŋ kidaŋ humaliwat,
saṙppa nika ahaṅöt-aṅĕt aliṇḍuṅan aniluk i salwaŋ iŋ watu sumoŋ,
daṙppa kawĕs kĕnasnya binurū kumĕtĕṙ anusup iŋ sukĕt kabarasat*

riŋ talunan paran-paran ikaŋ wwaŋ aburuhun anumpuṙ iŋ patalĕsan,
hĕnti winiḥ nikaŋ sawaḥ asat mwaŋ alaŋ-alaŋ i soṙ tinunwan aradin,
tan paṅucap tĕgĕg pitakut iŋ jawa rumĕpa haneŋ sukĕt paḍa kumöl,
ṅhiŋ kukulan tatiŋ muni titiṙ makupik asahuran ndatan hana tĕkā*

dhaṙmma hilaŋ tĕlas kaḍĕḍĕtan kabubak i lalayanya tan kahuniṅa,
mukṣa laṅö-laṅö ni pasabhanya piliḥ umuliḥ iŋ surendrabhawana,
caṇḍi linepa bajra pariśuddha kadi hañaṙ umantuka iŋ śiwapada,
kiñjĕŋ ika ataṅis-taṅisan iŋ wariṅin alara kāri deniŋ alaṅö*

tan hana kapwa pakṣa hayu riŋ jagat i panaput iŋ tamaḥ maṅawaśa,
tan kabĕnĕṙ pradeśa nika de ny-awuṙ-awuṙ ika piṇḍa duṣṭa sagawe,
māṙgga dudū tinūt ndaḥ i mĕnenya tan iṅapa dinohan iŋ wwaŋ asamun,
lwiṙ kalaśa awawan sasahab iŋ wĕṅi kadi manaḥ iŋ durātmaka jugul*

saŋ nrĕpaputra yatna sira de ni pamiḍĕṅĕṙ ira iŋ niśācarabala,
jagratara atihaŋ laras ikaŋ bala tĕlas apasaŋ rathanya tinitaḥ,
tan dwa ḍatĕŋ tikāŋ asura kātara maṅamaḥ-amaḥ lanā n pawurahan,
maṅlayaŋ iŋ nabhastala waneḥ masahuran aṅuhuḥ mapaŋ kadi gĕlap*

kahyun ika aṅrĕwĕk-rĕwĕk asiŋ katĕmu ya tawanĕn ya patyana kunĕŋ,
kagyat umunduṙ awri rumĕṅö hrik i kuda naranāthaputra kadunuŋ,
saṅśaya kapwa ya anaha-nahā paran ikihĕn asambhawa ŋ kuda muni,
liŋnya waneḥ dudū ya kuda niŋ wiku-wiku makuda bwat eṅgal anasar*

taṙkka nikaŋ waneḥ riya turaṅga niŋ aburu katiṅgal iŋ lagi-lagi,
yan tan ikaŋ wiku pwa ya cumaṅkaḥ akuda lumagā lawan kita kunĕŋ,
mojaṙ ikaŋ waneḥ gumagap iŋ hiḍĕp iṅĕt-iṅĕtĕn kalīṅan ikahĕn,
sugyan upāya niŋ wiku mameta śaraṇa nika śūra sāra riŋ ayun*

haywa tatan prayatna haja denta jaḍa-jaḍa ri don i saŋ para rĕṣi,
wiṣṭi tĕmĕn tikaŋ wiku musuḥ wiku wihikan i sandhi niŋ kira-kira,
ṅwaŋ tunaśāstra kewala wagal-wagal agul-agul eṅgal ambĕk agalak,
tan kadi saŋ wiku wruḥ i rusit tutuk ika humĕnĕŋ hatinya kuṭila*

sūkṣma ri don ikaŋ wiku manīti yan inupakara alĕmĕḥ mamalĕsa,
ndan hana kapwa de nika mameta lĕkasana nikaŋ sĕḍĕŋ maribhawa,
dāyaka śakti rakwa winaraḥnya mawĕlas ika dāyakanya matuluŋ,
toḥ niyatanya maṅkana mataŋnya paran iki hañaṙ ḍatĕŋ dudu-dudū*

om tuhu liṅta pāman aku ṅūni winaraḥ iŋ anon ratha adulu-dulur,
wwaŋ paḍa wīrayodha ya wicakṣaṇa lituhayu rakwa mahyas asiga,
byakta tikā ya dāyaka nikaŋ wiku parawaśa kahyaṅan ya rinuraḥ,
duṙjana saŋ watĕk rĕṣi ṅaranya maharĕp i halanta duṙyyaśa wiku*

ndaḥ mapa taŋ huliḥ bapa rare liŋ ika hana ta ya awrĕgas wariṅutĕn,
doḥ yatiku n kita n pamitaha awĕdi-wĕdi kita tan muwaḥ milu-milu,
denya paran kawĕdyana rikiŋ musuḥ aku lawananya mon hyaṅa tuwi,
yan tak utaŋ sugiḥ nira wĕnaŋ muliḥ aku turuŋ oliha aṅjara-jaraḥ*

bhoḥ t-ajĕjĕp muwaḥ paran ikaŋ makuda-kuda nihan waluy kita kabeḥ,
nā ta wuwusnya kapwa ya paḍa aṅijiŋ ahaliṅan iŋ wwit iŋ tahĕn agöŋ,
liṅsiṙ ikaŋ wulan kadi maha anuluhi ri bala saŋ janāṙddanasuta,
hetu nikaŋ balāsura mulat yatika yatiku liŋnya yan paḍa humuŋ*

munduṙ adān ta ya aruḥ-aruhan surak atĕhĕṙ atiṅkaḥ iŋ tĕgal alas,
byakta huwus gĕlaṙnya tumuluy nrĕpatanaya manuṅgaŋ iŋ ratha nira,
bhrĕtya paḍa atihaŋ sama-sama amalĕs anuraka wāhananya tinitaḥ,
saŋ sahaja iki saŋ prawala muṅgwi sana-sini narendraputra maparĕk*

dꜽtyabala agalak lumaga maṅgurumuŋ aharĕp oliha amĕjahana,
mambĕkĕm iŋ śilā hana tĕka aṅalaṅi sahana sañjatanya lumĕpas,
kapwa malĕs ta wadwa nira krĕṣṇasuta tikaŋ anuṅgaŋ iŋ ratha masö,
rākṣasa paṅharĕp kapagut orig alulun aciṅaŋ kawĕs tinĕpĕtan*

len hana rākṣasa aṅusak-asik tĕhĕṙ amawa lipuŋ nika akas aluṅid,
tan dwa tugĕl gulūnya pinanaḥ lawayan ika maṅuṅsiṙ aṅḍik aburū,
krūra tĕkā pwa ya amawa gada akral abutĕŋ anikĕp ratha agahan amūk,
trus kĕna duk ḍaḍanya katibā lumaḥ anibani tiṅhasan dug aluṅid*

parĕŋ asusun ikaŋ wil wīra riŋ praŋ magaṇḍi,
pati pĕcut apĕcut sep de nika anujwakĕn hrū,
pati-pati taŋ aṅumban maṅhawag saṅka riŋ doḥ,
maṅĕnani ri juluk niŋ rowaŋ awrĕg manoliḥ*

sama-sama taŋ aduk dukduk lĕpas de nika aṅduk,
winalĕsan arĕja ales yan tinūt munduṙ-undur,
magalaḥ anĕbaḥ aṅgyat ginyat aṅgyat siliḥ-gyat,
murĕṅaŋ arĕṅaŋ eṅas taŋ maṅonta n kinonta*

ndan ikaŋ aḍaḍap endaḥ muṇḍa kadganya tīkṣṇa,
mayat inayatan eṅa aṅlĕs mulat riŋ tumandaŋ,
wĕdi-wĕdi nika maṅdoḥ tan padon sañjatanya,
wruḥ atika kataraṅgul jriḥ kumöṙ pūḥ liniṇḍiḥ*

nrĕpatanaya maṅajña i bhrĕtya sāmpun yinodha,
bala nira paḍa tahw-iŋ praŋ rupĕk śūra śakti,
akas atiśaya medran riŋ kuda aṅgyat tumandaŋ,
lima ŋ aratha paḍa wruḥ riŋ dhanurwedaśāstra*

ikanaŋ akuda mapraŋ rwaŋ puluḥ kweḥ nika aṅgyat,
kiriwili rinakutnya ŋ wil wicitra iŋ magaṇḍi,
aṅicipiṙ i harĕp niŋ rākṣasa akweḥ pakewĕḥ,
hana ta parĕŋ aniṅhas tĕṅgĕk iŋ śatru maṅsö*

saŋ aratha mamanaḥ tan pāntara asraŋ tumiṇḍiḥ,
makasĕrĕpĕt ikaŋ hrū de nika aganti-ganti,
winalĕsan inirup niŋ rākṣasa atomara akweḥ,
arukĕt awilĕt amraŋ pinraŋ alwaŋ siliḥ-lwaŋ*

nrĕpasuta sira maṅsö mwaŋ watĕk bhrĕtya wīra,

paḍa mamanahakĕn hrū bāṇasampāta diwya,

sinama-sama rinok riŋ tuṅgaṅan tan tinaṅgĕl,

makin ananā ŋ rākṣasabala kepwan,
sakasapuluḥ māti kĕna cinakra,
hana ta pĕgat bāhu nika katimpal,
wahu malayū bāp kaḍawuḥ aṅohan*

parĕŋ asusun sāyudha maṅabehi,
saparan ikaŋ syandana ya tinūtnya,
makakĕrĕpĕk tĕṅgĕk ika cinakra,
makakĕḍĕpĕk tĕṇḍas ika kasiṅsal*

sahasa tĕka aṅduk nrĕpasuta yatna,

winalĕsakĕn yeka mahā kĕna trus*

kadi ta ya megha akilata sihuŋnya,

magĕlaṙ abāp waṅkay iŋ asura ṅke*

hana ya wanabyūha gĕlarĕn i ṅwaŋ,

mati kapisan siŋ kĕna pinanaḥ trus,

makakarasak riŋ sukĕt anusup kweḥ,
ikaŋ ahawan riŋ laṅit alilaŋ mör,
turaḥ ikanaŋ māti kĕna cinakra*

hana ta maṅuṅsiṙ juraŋ asĕnĕt groŋ,

mwaŋ ikaŋ aṅuṅsiṙ juraŋ apulaŋ rwi,
rumĕpa tibā riŋ watu ridaŋ aṅrĕs*

paḍa malayū śeṣa nika matiṅgal,
muliḥ akĕḍik ndan kanin ika makrĕp,
maṅasiḥ-asiḥ lot mamalaku herĕn,
ikaŋ asĕgĕṙ meṅĕt ika paḍa amriḥ*

tĕka ta jurunya apuliḥ adawa agöŋ,
ṅaran ika hīrāṅga sahasa maṅsö,
haṅin ika mādrĕs tuwin aṅalisyus,
kadi pinusus taŋ kayu-kayu denya*

yatika manāntwa i nrĕpasuta sāmba,
liŋ ika paran ko wwaŋ adhama tuccha,
umara-mara ṅke pasabha-sabhaṅku,
niyata pĕjaḥ ko tĕkap i gadāṅku*

sumahuṙ ikā saŋ nrĕpasuta śīghra,
aku śaraṇa i saŋ wiku rinarahmu,
kunaŋ apa pan ko ya pĕjaha deṅku,
papagakĕna ikaŋ himagiri maṅke*

liŋ ira tĕhĕṙ maṅlĕpasakĕn astra,
makasarapat cakra nira mawantaḥ,
paḍa maṅĕne syuḥ taŋ asura denya,
kadi malabuḥ prāṇa kahiḍĕpanya*

ri pĕjaḥ ikaŋ rākṣasa juru maṅke,
makabarasat śeṣa nika paḍa arĕs,
muliḥ akaniñ cihna nika yan apraŋ,

rahina tatas hyaŋ dinakara mabhrā,

hana ta maṅaṅsaṙ manĕhĕṙ asambat,
lawan umulu ususnya lumaḥ umambĕk*

hana ta tugĕl tuṙnya jĕnĕk aluṅguḥ,
maṅarut-arut mulyaṙ ika matanya,
amalaku lūdĕn ta ya gupay aṅliḥ,
karaṇa nika amātyakĕn iŋ awaknya*

hana ta kĕna iŋ hrū mata nika kāliḥ,

lumaku kasaṇḍuŋ titiṙ amurug rwi,

kasihan ikaŋ meḥ pĕjaha kacakra,
tikĕl i pupūnya n kanin ikana trus,
dalĕm i tatunya n ri ḍaḍa manumbĕr,
ininum ike rāḥnya-ya malapa wway*

tahĕn ikanaŋ pāṙśśwa kadi binaṅbaŋ,
makatiritis rāḥ kawĕkas i ronya,
makakuratil taŋ kuṇapa kasaŋsaŋ,
usus awilĕt riŋ paŋ ika gumantuŋ*

ri pucak ikaŋ hori hana kasaṅga,
paru-paru limpā ri caraŋ ika abāŋ,
sahaja dagiŋ mwaŋ hrĕdaya sumampir,
kadi ta manambe riŋ asura māti*

<girisa>:10.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – – –| – – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏓ = 16

nrĕpasuta sira mintaṙ ṅkā saṅkeŋ wana palagan,
dinakara sira māwās rāmya ŋ deśa winulatan,
limut anapihi kaywan keṅkab de niŋ aṅin alon,
hana luru-luruk aṅjraḥ mahw-aṅde lulut iŋ akūŋ*

wwara patapan asimpaṙ miṅkis kāmpiran iŋ unĕŋ,
kukus i patanĕkanya arok mwaŋ megha marawayan,
racana ni paciranya anyāsa aṙjja atulis alaṅö,
yan iŋ amarani kaṇṭa ṅhiŋ prāpta aṅjĕnĕki maṅö*

nrĕpasuta dumunuŋ seriŋ mwaŋ bhrĕtya nira kabeḥ,
kawaca linuputan len taŋ cāpāstra kinĕkĕsan,
lumaku sira mara adyus riŋ sĕñjaŋ suci mahĕniŋ,
ri tĕlas ira matīṙtha amūja iŋ hyaŋ nĕhĕṙ ajapa*

kuda nira winiweka aṅheṙttalya anĕḍuni  paruŋ,
makin atika tinalyan de niŋ tis tan inasĕhan,
umilu tika si dāruky-adyus tan tĕka sakarĕŋ,
apan aṅurutut asriŋ untunya agaṭik akaṭuk*

ri huwus ira mamūjā saŋ sāmba adara humarĕk,
ri sira muniwara asiḥ maṙmma aswāgata masĕgĕḥ,
anaku bapa tan iŋ rāt maṅke n prāpta kita huwus,
uliḥ i pajapa ni ṅwaŋ priḥ rakṣanta kami kabeḥ*

kadi sinipi ganas niŋ dꜽtya ṅke mamarikala,
manikĕp anawan adwa lwiṙ doṣanya pinĕjahan,
kari patapan ikā sāk saŋ wikw-a alaradan adoḥ,
aṅaluṣa tĕmahanya amet uṅgwan manusu-nusup*

nahan ika pawaraḥ saŋ paṇḍya aśabda saha kĕtĕr,
narapatisuta māṙ maṅrĕṅwākĕn pawuwus ira,
tĕhĕṙ aṅupaśamākĕn saŋ krĕṣṇātmaja sumahur,
pala-palarĕn iŋ ambĕk rānak saŋ rĕṣi śaraṇa*

nrĕpatisuta tinamw-iŋ bwat sopācara mahalĕp,
barubi pinakasamsam luṅlūṅañ cinacaṙ ira,
kunaŋ aṅinaki ri twas tiṅhal saŋ muniduhitā,
karaṇa nira matambĕḥ kūŋ tapwan warĕg alulut*

ri tĕlas ira tinamw-i i roṇḍon kāṅinan iŋ aṅin,
akusa-kasikan olaḥ tamtamnya n warĕg aṅĕsaḥ,
nrĕpatanaya sinambe niŋ jriŋ pādapa maṅĕliḥ,
karaṇa nira n anoliḥ de niŋ syuŋ maṅaku kaka*

manuk awurahan asraŋ ṅkāna iŋ ambulu matasak,
nyaŋ arĕbut i paŋ aṅjraḥ mwaŋ rowaŋnya siliḥ-adĕḥ,
ndan anĕṅĕn-aṅiwākĕn wwaḥ niŋ hambawaŋ umaḍam,
lutuŋ akĕmilan oṅsil siŋ roṇḍon piniliḥ ikā*

rusit ikaŋ acala akweḥ priṅganya ajuraŋ apiṅit,
hapi mamaḍĕmi ŋ ampyal priŋnya ŋ nyū makin alupa,
marukĕt awilĕt odwad riŋ kaywan milu kawilĕt,
wruḥ aṅuṭilani rowaŋ buddhinya aṅruhuṙ i hawan*

<aśwalalita>:11.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

hana mata pājaran lĕṅĕŋ amānuṣa inĕmukan iŋ hima araŋ anipis,
aṅaṅaṙ-aṅaṙ katonan i sĕkaṙnya waṙṇna tulis iŋ suji inisisakĕn,
kukus ikaŋ eṙttali iriya marok lawan kukus ikaŋ pahoman alaṅö,
raras i paṅuwwaŋ i mrak ika sinraŋ iŋ wijayaghaṇṭa mandakarĕṅö*

parawan adewatīṙtha kari śiṣya saŋ rĕṣi lĕyĕp hayunya dinĕlö,
mapa kili māṙ manis ya tuhu yañ juruḥ ni madhu niŋ sĕkaṙ piniturun,
paṅawak aros arampiŋ abuṅaḥ tĕṅaḥ nika n awaṙṇna sinwam aṅĕliḥ,
rupit i suśūnya rakwa mapiṅit nimitta nika tan hana amaḍani ya*

raras ika yan haneŋ patiga niŋ patamwan asisig-sisig kinĕmuran,
hana ta maweḥ lulud hana n amīti hāṙyyan anĕmat-nĕmat mwaŋ anĕlaḥ,
aṅapusi puṣpaliṅga saha maṅdanī kusuma waṙṇna daṙbbha tinatā,
apĕnĕd arūm paḍa arĕs umiṅis lumaṇḍĕp i liriŋ nika aṅrĕsi hati*

guru kaki wāhu saṅka riŋ alas lawan tapa-tapa amikul huwi hilus,
suḍa salaya n tinaṅguṅan ikaŋ gaḍuŋ saha gaṅan kinaṇḍut i harĕp,
saŋ aṅayu rāmya lālana hana aṅiduŋ hanan amet jamuṙ syuŋ agĕlar,
sumari mamet liraŋ kaṅĕlihan manambyakĕn amet luŋ iŋ karawila*

nrĕpasuta lālana i suku nikaŋ wukiṙ jĕnĕk i rāmya niŋ sakamatan,
walahaṙ agöŋ inĕntasan ira alaṅö watu sumantĕn aṙjja lumutĕn,
pata-pataḥ iŋ hĕni i tĕpi nika anĕlat kasawuran sĕkaṙ wahu rurū,
susuḥ aduluṙ matuntunan awaṙṇna raśmi ni cĕcĕk-cĕcĕk niŋ araras*

pira ta lawas niraŋ nrĕpatiputra yan tĕka rumakṣa saŋ para rĕṣi,
ya ta sakulĕm sira aṅhinĕp i saŋ rĕṣi irika saghorawa asĕgĕ-sĕgĕḥ,
milu para śiṣya maṙmma ri sira asĕḍĕp hana maweḥ phala asiŋ arasa,
pinakapuriḥ saŋ uttama ghinoṣita n pamarituṣṭa riŋ para nanā*

<wasantatilaka>: 12.
– – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏓ = 14

sāmpun kalaṅlaṅan ikaŋ suku niŋ himādri,
de saŋ narendrasuta sāmba sudhīrajāti,
sakweḥ mahāṙṣi sukha tan hana wighnamātra,
yajña prasiddha ginaway nira dewapūjā*

atyanta tuṣṭa nira saŋ wiku riŋ himādri,
tan dwa aṅrĕṅö turaḥ i dānawaśatru kāri,
hetunya sāhasa muwaḥ rumaraḥ mahāṙṣi,
sabsab paḍanya n umara iŋ wiku tan padoṣa*

luṅhā ta saŋ rĕṣi paḍa aṅhili nora kantun,
Āpan kasampaṙ aradin tinawan waneḥnya,
len maṅlawan mati turaḥnya kawös tinūt tlas,
ṅĕs-ṅösĕn epu manusup maṅusī guha ajro*

maṅkā tikaŋ tapa-tapi prihatin gupa ipuḥ,
tan wriŋ paranya malayū manaṅis masambat,
runtiŋ tapiḥnya daluwaŋnya rujit kasambit,
santĕn ragĕt karagĕt iŋ rwi dumeḥ rarasnya*

mwaŋ saŋ watĕk guru nini iki maṅiṇḍit-iṇḍit,
tan saḥ panucyan ira len tĕnunan pamuswan,
lāwan tikaŋ wusu-wusū lawayan gumantuŋ,
kapwa ika liŋ nira siluṅluṅan iŋ paratra*

abwat kaki mpu burayut mamikul ry-anaknya,
rañcaknya mesi sapuluḥ sasisiḥ tinaṅguŋ,
puṇḍaknya kaṙwwa paḍa mesi wĕgig siliḥ-prĕp,
wadwān ika amĕtĕŋ uwus kalima iŋ pisuswan*

maṅgĕḥ swadhaṙmma nira saŋ macĕpuḥ sinuṇḍaŋ,
kāliḥ pwa ya n taṅan ira uṅsil ikaŋ manuṇḍaŋ,
mogha ika kasrĕk irikaŋ wadara awwaḥ akrĕp,
caṅkĕm nira ika maṅakĕp kabharan kacaṇṭyal*

kañcit ḍatĕŋ nrĕpatiputra lawan bala akweḥ,
kapwa amanaḥ sira lawan bala tan tahĕn twas,
alwaŋ tikaŋ musuḥ aneka rinok paṅohan,
hetunya kaṇḍĕg alayū paṅarĕpnya kondur*

enak ta buddhi nira saŋ rĕṣiśiṣyasaṅgha,
milwa apuliḥ saha patil suligi mwaŋ umban,
dukduk wuluḥ watu pinaṇḍĕmakĕn ya moliḥ,
saŋ mona māri humĕnĕŋ mamisuḥ sira akrak*

saŋ dewagurw-aṅadu śiṣya marĕk manonton,
ambĕk malañciṅan aniṅsĕti baddha ruñcud,
nā liŋ nira apraṅa ta haywa takut hiḍĕpku,
mon ko mamāti kĕna teki musuḥku wāhya*

yan ko makoliha musuhmu mĕna iŋ payuddhan,
ndak gañjaṙ iŋ basahan aṙjja tĕka iŋ jamaŋnya,
yapwan hana aṅgalaḥ amātyani riŋ prawīra,
denya alabhā pinahalĕp hana siṅhĕlanya*

maṅkin ta saŋ tapa-tapa amriḥ arampak apraŋ,
endaḥ samaṇḍala-samaṇḍala paṇṭa-paṇṭan,
guntĕnya saŋ ghalusĕkaṙ pinakādhikāra,
maṅrikwakĕn ta gati saŋ kabayan kaki hyaŋ*

anyāt katon wiku turuŋ wirati iki mapraŋ,
unduṙ wuwus nika tumandaŋ aṅuṇḍa dukduk,
tan wruḥ ta ko ry-aku pinun mun aṅakw-asajña,
liŋnya agarap kasalahan ya masumba-sumbar*

len taŋ waneḥ wiku kapeṅin anon wani iŋ praŋ,
mĕṅgĕp tumūt ndan ahiwaŋ sinurak mara agyaŋ,
denya apraŋ aṅragayaḥ aṅlawani ŋ prawīra,
keṅĕl kĕna iŋ watu wĕhaŋnya rurū bahĕmnya*

anyāt paḍa alwaŋ abutĕŋ marukĕt siliḥ-prĕp,
rambut kasaṇḍuŋ akusut kadudut karĕṅgut,
rodra anahut ya sinahut maluñut siliḥ-tūr,
kapwa aṅgrĕgut muwaḥ akañjaṙ aṅaṅgut-aṅgut*

enak pataṅkĕp ikana aṅlaga riŋ kamantyan,
eṅgal paḍa alwaŋ ananā wiku rākṣasa akweḥ,
maṅsö ta wadwa nira saŋ naranāthaputra,
kapwa aṅawit paḍa mamātyani śatru śakti*

sāmpun lĕpas ni warayaŋ nrĕpaputra sāmba,
tan pāntara anarawata aṅibĕki ŋ payuddhan,
kontap kabĕntaṙ ikanaŋ suraśatru denya,
himpĕṙ śata n tumaji rūpa nikaŋ paḍa uliḥ*

bĕntaṙ bubaṙ mababaran bala rākṣasa alaḥ,
maṅkin wiśīṙṇna hinudan-hudanan warāstra,
waṅkay matip mibab-ibab sawaneḥ katimpal,
waṅkwaŋ pupū hana tugĕl dalĕmanya runtuḥ*

kyāti pralamba tuhan iŋ bala dꜽtyawīra,
yeka apuliḥ mapagi wūk nrĕpaputra sāmba,
muṇḍa uṇḍa śūla nika śakti malaṇḍĕp atwas,
maṅduk narendrasuta tan pañarik linesan*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:13.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

muntab krodha nikaŋ pralamba ri luput saŋ sāmba wīrottama,
hetunya n pamanaḥ maha amaruputi iŋ hrū śakti tan pāntara,
saŋ krĕṣṇātmaja śūra maṅlĕpasakĕn krorāstra sök tan pĕgat,
dhwasta ikaŋ panaḥ iŋ pralamba kasĕsĕb niśśeṣa kasyūḥ hilaŋ*

tan syūḥ yadyan ikaŋ musuḥ lawanana ambĕknya apan alpādhama,
nāhan ta ujaṙ i dāruki iya karĕṅö de saŋ narendrātmaja,
nyā ṅhrū śakti kawodhana astra pamanaḥ saŋ sāmba siṅhākrĕti,
trus limpad hati niŋ pralamba kawĕnaŋ prāṇanya sāmpun hilaŋ*

luṅha arĕs malayū turaḥ-turaḥ ikaŋ dꜽtya umuliḥ riŋ pura,
riŋ pātāla waneḥ paranya mahawan riŋ jro nikaŋ sāgara,
ṅĕs-ṅösĕn winaliŋnya wiṣṇu manurun saŋ sāmba śūra iŋ raṇa,
meṅguŋ buddhi nira atakut maharĕp aṅhily-a apan awrin kawös*

tuṣṭa ambĕk nira saŋ watĕk rĕṣi kabeḥ mantuk mareŋ kahyaṅan,
mwaŋ śiṣya prajurit hulūnya makusut bandhanya siṅsal waneḥ,
len taŋ mājarakĕn waninya makaput caṅkĕmnya de niŋ hidu,
wwantĕñ jriḥ maṅabuk haneŋ wuri yaya anaṅgaḥ ya milwa anuduk*

byātītan gati saŋ watĕk tapa paḍa agoṣṭhi praŋ iŋ maṇḍala,
saŋ krĕṣṇātmaja mintaṙ aṅlarisakĕn lampaḥ nikaŋ syandana,
ramya atūt gĕgĕṙ iŋ wukiṙ gaga-gagā ŋ deśa atatā koṅkulan,
himpĕṙ wastra putiḥ katiṅhalan ikaŋ toya aṅĕbĕk riŋ sawaḥ*

wwantĕn  kahyaṅan uttama iŋ halĕp apūṙwwa atyanta nora aṅhirib,
denya n śobhita kapwa saṙwwa hinĕduk nyāsanya ramya alaṅö,
towy-a amiṅkiṅakĕñ juraŋ tĕḍunan iŋ wwe saṅka riŋ paṙwwata,
gĕntĕṙ niŋ bañu tan pasaṅkya karĕṅö mwaŋ śabda niŋ nīrada*

khyāti iŋ rāt sira wiśwamitra bhagawān muṅgwi irikāŋ kahyaṅan,
tĕkwan rājarĕṣi prasiddha sira mājaṙ dhaṙmma saŋ paṇḍita,
byakta ika atiśaya iŋ kasiddhan adhikāra uttuṅga śuddhāgama,
sākṣāt śiṣya bhaṭāra wiṣṇu manurun saṅkeŋ wadaryāśrama*

tiṅkaḥ rājya patiṅkaḥ iŋ patapan endaḥ de mahaṙṣy-a agĕlar,
maṅkā riŋ pasabhān-sabhān tĕkap ikaŋ śiṣya atata akweḥ marĕk,
sinyaŋ taŋ para śiṣya yan waśariṣa agasyak tanora atuluŋ,
saŋ kily-a araras aṙjja saŋ tapi sĕḍĕŋ lindinya maṅde kĕcap*

cuṇḍuk saŋ naranāthaputra ri siraŋ rājaṙṣi bhakty-a ararĕm,
sambaḥ ya uliḥ-uliḥ nira adara sinuṅsuŋ riŋ śiwāmbha apĕnĕd,
trĕpty-ambĕk nira yan hulūna nira rakwa i saŋ mahāpaṇḍita,
maṅgā tan muliha iŋ purī sira yadin sambeganĕn saŋ rĕṣi*

saŋ śrī rājarĕṣi prahaṙṣa sira siḥ de saŋ narendrātmaja,
mojaṙ liŋ nira bhāgya yan kita ḍataŋ maṅke rikeŋ āśrama,
moliḥ prāṙthana ni ṅhulun yatiku paṅrakṣanta saṅkeŋ musuḥ,
byakta awās kita hetu niŋ mari-mariṅguŋ de nikaŋ rākṣasa*

ndā t-aṅheṙ sakarĕŋ t-arāṙyyan anaku wruḥ ṅwaŋ ri ṅelta alaga,
towin taŋ turaga alapa akuru kuraŋ turw-a apa tan lālana,
tan wwantĕn mari kaŋ katĕmwa tan ikaŋ mās bhoga riŋ kahyaṅan,
mwaŋ siŋ bhūṣaṇa tan hana aṅlawanana i śabdanta yan wruḥ kawi*

<aṅgitahu>:14. 
⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏓ = 11

alawas nrĕpaputra riŋ himādri,
pinakāśraya de niraŋ mahāṙṣi,
bala dꜽtya tatan muṅup kawös jriḥ,
sukha tan sipi saŋ yati n pamūjā*

hana śiṣya mahāṙṣi wiśwamitra,
maṅaran guṇadewa tan hana uli,
wihikan kawi gīta len palambaŋ,
ya ta sānaka de narendraputra*

saparan sira selwan iŋ wanādri,
lĕṅĕŋ iŋ pagagan paran kahāsan,
lalu lampaḥ ira n kaluṅha-luṅhā,
kawawa i kahanan lĕwĕs laṅönya*

irikā ta sira ñ jĕnĕk magoṣṭhi,
rikanaŋ tarukan miriŋ śila alwā,
sĕmi wāhu lĕwas ya ta uṅgwan-uṅgwan,
pakulen ira raśmi niŋ sĕkaṙ mrik*

dinĕlö nira hīṅan iŋ samudra,
ri hiriŋ nikanaŋ laṅit wĕkasnya*

<mattarāga>:15.
– – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 20

saŋ krĕṣṇaputra sira ta ataña iŋ sakamatan ri saŋ rĕṣiputra,
mwaŋ maṇḍala iŋ giriwanāntara krama nikā kabeḥ tinañakĕn,
mājaṙ sira iki guṇadewa toḥ bapa tama ṅhulun tuhu-tuhu,
tan saṅśaya pwa ta manaḥta tiṅhalana rāmya niŋ sakamatan*

nyā ŋ maṇḍala arĕṇĕb agöŋ lawasnya marika n lanā kasiratan,
gaṅgā sakeŋ laṅit ikā n tumampuḥ i samīpakanya maparĕk,
nārāyaṇa pratita saŋ makāśrama sadeśa riŋ sabhuwana,
nāhan ta kāraṇa niki n pawitra parana adidewaśaraṇa*

honya ŋ tapowana ri puñcak iŋ wukiṙ anak samaṙ kalimutan,
mandāra kaywan iŋ alasnya maṅjraḥ asĕkaṙ mapādapa waneḥ,
manda ahĕniŋ lwaḥ ika niṙmmala atis apitowi tus niŋ acala,
himpĕṙ karas juraŋ ika alaṅö paran i saŋ kawīśwara maṅö*

śrī yajñawatya sira saŋ pratiṣṭha pinakādhikāra nipuṇa,
sākṣāt bhaṭāra rawi saŋ paṅajyan iŋ aweda ṅūni karĕṅö,
wākbajrapaṇḍita sira n prawādika wiśeṣa niŋ wruḥ aṅaji,
tāpāya riŋ wiku mawās tĕkap nira tatas riŋ āgamarasa*

rakryan lihat-lihatana ikiŋ āśrama lĕṅöŋ tiniṅgal alawas,
kapwa alaṅö trĕṇalatānya len kayumanis nika awĕnĕs alĕk,
mwaŋ nāgapuṣpa nika rukṣa sinwam iŋ aśoka mambĕt aṅĕliḥ,
kumbaŋ nika aṅrĕŋ anaṅis midĕṙ sawaŋ asambat iŋ saŋ alalis*

tanseŋ halĕp niki rikāna rakwa kadi kendran iŋ kalĕṅĕṅan,
maṅke wiśīṙṇna kasihan kasiḥnya katunan karaśmin iŋ arūm,
lāwan tikaŋ wĕlas-asiḥ lana aṅalaya tansaḥ iŋ kayu sĕnö,
mwaŋ taŋ dwirepha milu kāsihan mabasahan kadut lĕwas awūk*

atyanta rāmya nika tan hilaŋ paḍa madūm rarasnya n alaṅö,
bĕntaṙ sayat watu karaŋnya riŋ pacira kaswab iŋ tahĕn agöŋ,
rĕṅkā ni gopura śiwaknya lot kakasut iŋ wwad iŋ priḥ awilĕt,
syuḥ śīṙṇna maṇḍala nika arĕmuk gula-gulanya mantĕn amanis*

bapranya wuṅkal inukiṙ winimba wanitā winehan añaṅa,
rukṣa apasaḥ kapĕgatan sĕnĕŋnya kaduk iŋ rĕbaḥ tuwi tibā,
tan wriŋ kwananya karikā nimitta ni kucĕmnya lĕŋlĕŋ akusut,
sāmpun mayat lumabuha iŋ paraŋ ri lari niŋ priyanya kasihan*

aṙcca aparan karika ṅūni riŋ watu karaŋ tiniṅkaḥ arĕcĕp,
aṅrĕs kasoṅan iŋ aśoka mĕmbaŋ asawit lata aŋ jriŋ asĕmi,
piṇḍa alara aṅaluṣakĕn ry-awaknya lulurĕn siliḥ-jaga mĕlĕs,
kady-a apupuṙ mukha nika anĕlat kalumutan turuŋ karahupan*

wuṅkal hitĕm patiga niŋ taṭāka riŋ usāna runtuḥ anibā,
len taŋ kari ŋ wwad iŋ aśoka lĕŋlĕŋ asaput pakis dadu mirir,
daṙppa aṅlumuḥ mara śilodakanya tumiba iŋ prĕduŋ-prĕduŋ aroŋ,
waṙṇna akĕcap salaḥ-asa i rarasnya n inatīta maṅkin alaṅö*

śrīdanta len mĕnuṙ awoṙ lawan trĕṇalata aṅayuḥ wuṅa tali,
sakweḥ nikā wĕlas-arĕpnya tībra kasihan tinambaŋ alawas,
aṅhiŋ katiṅhalan ikaŋ walik-haḍĕp ika ahyasan linihatan,
mahyun lawad-lawadĕn iŋ kawipriya kunĕŋ mataŋnya n asĕkar*

tañjuŋ wuṅū surabhi campaka asana marok lawan surataru,
ramya aśilā kumalasā ri soṙnya katiraḥ rumiṅriŋ alaṅö,
paṇḍan lĕṅis rĕbaḥ apan hibĕk gaḍuŋ apiṇḍa tan kahuniṅa,
eman puḍaknya n abuṅaḥ katon kadi wĕtis niŋ adyaḥ aturū*

ndā paṅrĕṅö ra tapa rakryan aṅgĕḥ ika ṅūni rakwa tarukan,
saŋ dhaṙmmadewa sira wiṣṇuputra matapa iriya n panaruka,
saṅke kasiddhyan ira tulya kendran ikahĕn tapowana nira,
himpĕṙ hyaŋ indra sira deniŋ apsara kabeḥ sumewa ri sira*

saŋ yajñawaty-atiśaya iŋ raras kalulut iŋ janāṙddanasuta,
nora aṅhirib hayu nira amanis pituwi katwaŋ iŋ surawadhū,
sakweḥ nikaŋ kusuma kāṅinan musiṙ i rūm nira ika mapupul,
sinwam lanā kaṅĕlihan tumirw-i lĕmĕs iŋ tĕṅaḥ tinapihan*

<mrĕdukomala>:16
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 18

dewī yajñawatī tiniṅgal ira dhaṙmmadewa wĕkasan,
kāri ṅka i patapan tamolaḥ agawe tapabrata ginöŋ,
tan len rakwa sinādhya de nira katĕmwa de saŋ alalis,
saṅke tībra nikaŋ lara unĕŋ irikā n sira alabuḥ apuy*

tapwan māri wuwus niraŋ rĕṣisuta awaraḥ duga-duga,
cĕb ṅöṙ twas nira saŋ narendratanaya aṅrĕṅö kapĕnĕtan,
aṅrĕs citta nira awĕlas tutuṙ i saŋ katiṅgal aturū,
māṙmma mrāt twas ira n tĕñuḥ ri gati saŋ priyā n kasiḥ-arĕp*

tībra akūŋ sira sāmba mohita rinañca niŋ lulut unĕŋ,
ndi pwa ikāna wĕkasta māsku liŋ ira anĕhĕṙ maguliṅan,
tan dwa alĕk lumĕyĕp kapaty-apĕga yat mĕgĕŋ lara nira,
liṇḍu taŋ kusuma akĕtĕṙ prabhawa gĕntĕṙ iŋ patĕṙ alon*

Āśābhūta manastapa prihati teki saŋ rĕṣisuta,
yaṙ ton saŋ naranāthaputra kapĕjaḥ ndatan pakaraṇa,
maṙmmanya aṅgugaḥ epu liŋnya laki t-aṅliliṙ kita bapa,
sowenya n panaṅis kamantyan atutuṙ ta saŋ nrĕpasuta*

enak de nrĕpaputra meṅĕt awĕwĕḥ ta luḥ nira tibā,
masrĕt de niŋ aśabda kewala sĕkĕl nikaŋ hati tĕñuḥ,
sambat-sambat ira ndatan sphuṭa pĕgat-pĕgat saha kĕtĕr,
lwiṙ kumbaŋ maṅisĕp sĕkaṙ swara nira anaṅis katanĕhan*

nāhan liŋ nira he kaka aṙṣitanaya ṅhulun mawaraha,
ṅūni mūla ni janma ni ṅhulun anak bhaṭāra puruṣa,
nitya aṅgöŋ tapa dhaṙmmadewa ṅaran i ṅhulun prakaśita,
tan len yajñawatī prasiddha sisihanku haṙṣa rasika*

ndaḥ yekī patapanku ṅūni paḍa keṅĕtan tahĕn ikā,
mwaŋ tekī wulakanya padyusan i kāsiḥ i ṅhulun ike,
tāmankw-i iki batuṙnya mātra katutuṙ kw-asiŋ sĕkaṙ arūm,
paṅlīlāṅkw-iki paṅhyaṅanku ri tĕlaskw-amuṣpa majapa*

sakweḥ niŋ paricārika apsarawadhū paḍa ahayu rare,
pantĕs bhāwa nikā hana irikaŋ aśoka rambay asĕkar,
yan sore paḍa mamrĕm iŋ grĕhalata akĕmit gati nikā,
dewī muṅgw-irikaŋ jinĕm sira lawan ṅhulun siliḥ-asiḥ*

maṅjanma pwa bhaṭāra keśawa tumūt ṅhulun nda maṅĕnĕs,
tan pamwīt ṅhulun i sira n kari haneŋ tilam saŋ aturū,
tan toliḥ lara niŋ katiṅgal apan aprĕgi ṅwaŋ alayū,
de niŋ nāgata tan kapaṅgiha wĕkas bhaṭāra mahulun*

nāhan teki nimitta ni ṅhulun aṅaryakĕn ri saŋ arūm,
tan saṅkeŋ lalis i ṅhulun-ṅhulun iki pwa bhakti mayayaḥ,
ndan saŋ yajñawatī kunĕŋ salaḥ-iḍĕp manĕṅgaḥ alalis,
maṙmmanya n pamalĕs lara i hati tĕwĕk nika alabuḥ apuy*

<citrawilāpa>:17.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 21

hana ta kunaŋ tĕkapaṅkwa lumipura lulutkw-iri saŋ tĕkasiḥ,
sukha pĕjaha akw-atapa iŋ wukiṙ anusupa tan maluya iŋ nagara,
satĕmahanaṅkwa lawan rasika tuhun apaṅgiha tan kasaha,
saphala tika aku siwin tan uwaha ri gatiṅku n aniṅgalakĕn*

dyaḥ ari nihan ta kakanta lihatana ta kāsihan iŋ kalaran,
hanaṅisi māsku kita araras alaris aweḥ lara kūŋ ri hati,
ndi ta kahananta tuhanku maṅusapana luḥku nihan t-aṅadĕg,
hanawaŋ unĕṅta manambat i kita saŋ anūkṣma pinet ri hati*

ṅkapana manista katĕmwa rari dĕlĕ-dĕlönku rikaŋ kusuma,
wukiṙ aparan ta kunaŋ pamulikana hayunta lĕṅit dahatĕn,
tak arusuha aku yadin lumayarana rarasta yan iŋ pasisi,
mabayaṅana iŋ gagana ṅka turida ni kakanta mamet ri kita*

rumiṅa-riṅa aku ri kambaŋ iŋ asana miṅiŋ ri pipinta rari,
katĕmu ri lūm niŋ aśoka lĕmĕs i panĕpinta maminta hulĕs,
hirĕŋ i laṭinta haneŋ tĕbu hirĕŋ amanis sinĕsĕp-sĕsĕpan,
gĕmuḥ i susunta juga amĕkasi hati nimitta niŋ agriŋ akūŋ*

munisuta maṙmma tĕmĕn sira ri lara narendrasuta aṅawaśa,
irika mataṅguḥ ujaṙ t-adiwasa bapa denta wimūṙccha dahat,
puriḥ ikanaŋ dadi duhkha gati nika mataŋnya n ade hiḍĕpĕn,
lilaŋ i manaḥ nrĕpaputra paṅuṣadha saŋ āṙyya rikaŋ prihatin*

hana laki tatwa nikaŋ dadi ginaway anitya dadinya kabeḥ,
anili-niliḥ wiṣaya ŋ manĕmu sukha bhinukti maweḥ prihati,
prawala nikā saŋ aṅenak-inaki ŋ aniliḥ sukha mogha jĕnĕk,
saŋ anĕmu bhoga ta yan wruha ta sira pinaṇḍita yogya tirun*

lawan ikahĕn tĕmaḥ iŋ wwaŋ akurĕn apasaḥ ta wasāna nikā,
siḥ ika sināhakĕn iŋ pati kalawan inaknya winaṣṭa kabeḥ,
kunaŋ ikanaŋ kari mogha karakĕtan i rāmya niki n kabharan,
ikaŋ alara i tĕka niŋ pati niyata turuŋ wruḥ ikā n maṅaji*

iki paṅucap ra bhujaṅga nira n upaśama i naranāthasuta,
pitutuṙ i saŋ wihikan tiki juga winuwus ra tapanta rĕṅön,
ujaṙ ira saŋ guṇadewa mawaraha ri buddhi narendrasuta,
ya ta maṅĕne hati hetu ni hĕnĕŋ ira sāmba marĕn manaṅis*

sĕḍĕŋ ira sāmba wimohita tĕka ta tilottamā dewawadhū,
acaru sĕkaṙ ya ri cetya ni hawu nira yajñawati i patapan,
atapi-tapiḥ gula gaṇṭi tinulis iŋ ĕmas lusuhan saŋ arūm,
aṅĕmulakĕn suji hantuk i taṅan ira yajñawatī manuji*

kawula nira ŋ nrĕpaputra tumuluy atutuṙ syuḥ ika twas ira,
maṅucapa tan wĕnaṅa i pawaraḥ hana yan eliṅa saŋ sapanĕn,
maṅĕn-aṅĕn ambĕk ira i saŋ ahayu kari de nira riŋ śayana,
karaṇa ni waspa nira anaputi mata mata amuhara amanisi*

wĕkasan anāntwa sira i saŋ amaraduhitā liŋ ira iki nihan,
kaka pu tilottamā tan sinipi puji-pujinta kita atiśaya,
nahan ika liŋ nira saŋ sinapa midĕm-idĕm wruḥ i saŋ manapa,
aṅiriṅi līṅan ira mpu tapa ya ta nimitta nira apihĕnĕŋ*

muwaḥ awuwus ta narendrasuta kaka tilottamā t-a ajarakĕn,
wĕkas iy arinta saŋ apsarapatiduhitā ndi manis rasika,
luwaṙ i taṅanku raras nira n aṅuwahi raśmi nira an pinĕkul,
kita karika aṅĕñĕp iŋ maṇik apuji laṅö ṅwaŋ ike mulata*

<jagaddhita>:18.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

nāhan liŋ nira saŋ narendratanaya anĕhĕṙ amĕpĕṙ i saŋ tilottamā,
kepwan saŋ tinañan manaṅśaya paniṅgala nira muwaha iŋ suputrikā,
ndātan mājara māṙ manaḥnya mawĕlas ri pamalaku ŋ asiḥ nrĕpātmaja,
rañca ambĕk ri hatinya meḥ bĕlaha papraṅan iŋ aṅĕn-aṅĕn siliḥ-dĕhā*

akweḥ siḥnya ri saŋ nrĕpātmaja nimitta ni sahuṙ ika maṙmma haṙṣaja,
siṅgiḥ māti saŋ apsarendraduhita aturun apuy i hilaṅta riŋ tilam,
ndā maṅjanma huwus ri saŋ prabhu riŋ uttaranagara wiśeṣaputrikā,
dewī yajñawatī muwaḥ ṅaran ira an uliḥ i paramayajña de haji*

mogha iki n tĕka mārakaṙmma ni yayaḥ nira tinĕkan ikaŋ mahāsura,
māti pwā sira de niraŋ naraka ṅūni paḍa maṅadu śakti riŋ raṇa,
bela śrī parameśwarī kari ta saŋ narapatiduhitā sĕḍĕŋ rare,
ṅkā saŋ dānawarāja māsiḥ awĕlas mamipili ri salaḥ nrĕpātmajā*

dewī yajñawatī prasiddha pinakānak ira saŋ asurādhipa aṅaku,
riŋ kanyāpuri r-uṅgu de saŋ asurendra rikaŋ alaya ratna len sakhī,
ndan saṅke sira ta ṅhulun laki kinon lumaya-laya ri saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
t-aṅkat-t-elu mare sira ṅhulun anuntunakĕn i kita haywa saṅśaya*

maṅkā śabda tilottamā krama lumampaḥ aduluṙ aṅĕnĕs mareŋ puri,
mwaŋ saŋ sāmba kunĕŋ sira mpu guṇadewa muwaḥ umuliḥ iŋ tapowana,
byātītan hana riŋ hĕnū tucapa saŋ maṇik iŋ ahayu rājakanyakā,
riŋ raṅkaŋ maṇijātirĕṅga sira n aṅliḥ aṅaraŋ inaweśa niŋ smara*

mewĕḥ saŋ wihikan ri buddhi nira mesi turida wahu kabwatan raras,
sūkṣmāsāri wināwan iŋ sasisihan siḥ ira hana tikĕl nikaŋ halis,
maṙmma i santĕn ira ika mahrit inamĕṙ sinaji panĕwĕka i twas iŋ akūŋ,
luñcip niŋ mata dug siṅi iṅid-iṅidan winiṣan iŋ amanis mamātyani*

siṅgiḥ yan sira puṣpamūṙtti katĕṅĕṙ paṅawak ira n añampaka akuniŋ,
māmbö rūm ni gĕluŋ nira ahirĕŋ awaṙṇna maṅunĕŋ akila ariris mĕnur,
luṅsuṙ niŋ pupuṙ aṙjja mātra karakĕt ri wijaŋ araras aṅhrĕbuk lĕwas,
śumrīdanta mĕkaṙ katon waja nira ahidu madhu karikā lanā manis*

rūm niŋ puṣpa laṅö ni sinwam iŋ aśoka piniturun i rāmya niŋ kapat,
kapwa aṅjanma raras narendraduhitā mamanisi madhu niŋ sĕkaṙ miṅiŋ,
sākṣāt śrī ni kalaṅwan iŋ pasisi saṙwwa sĕkaṙ iŋ acala adi niŋ laṅö,
lakṣmī niŋ puḍak aṅdadi i wĕtis ira n lagi pinapag i dèwa niŋ ṭikā*

maṅkā rakwa laris nikaŋ wataŋ aṅāśraya ri jariji saŋ suputrikā,
sinwam niŋ taru nāgapuṣpa n amiraḥ kakaratala rarasnya de nira,
hyaŋ-hyaŋ niŋ salaga akucup mulati sāri ni manis ira tan kĕneŋ lĕwas,
dewī niŋ patapan wawaŋ murakĕnā hayu niki n awiraŋ sinorakĕn*

<sragdharā>:19.
– – –| – ⏑ –| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – –| ⏑ – –| ⏑ – ⏓ = 21

nyā ŋ kĕmbaŋ niŋ wakāta n rakĕt i talapakan soṙ ika i jöŋ suputrī,
kĕmbaŋ niŋ rājasa aṅdohi gisi-gisi tĕwas tan kĕnā rūm pan ajriḥ,
kĕmbaŋ niŋ nāgapuṣpa ahiwaŋ aṅiṅĕt-iṅĕt riŋ kapö ndi n kahopa,
kĕmbaŋ gaṅsal kĕta iriŋ rahat i laṭi nira n rakta somya aṅĕne twas*

osik taŋ puṣpasāry-a aṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn i raras rūm niraŋ rājakanyā,
luṅha aṅilya ṅhrĕbuk de ni wida nira sumāṙ mūṙ ikaŋ campaka amrik,
nda alaḥ taŋ pādapa n kambwan i gĕrĕḥ i lĕmĕs niŋ tĕṅaḥ tan hinambĕn,
luṅlūṅan luŋ nika aṅliḥ wruḥ alĕmĕsan atiṅhal yan ambĕt wruḥ olaḥ*

mambö śrī niŋ kapat śrī narawaraduhita anraŋ laṅö niŋ basanta,
lakṣmī niŋ saṙwwasāry-a amisani raras ira alūŋ i rūm niŋ kalaṅwan,
maṅkin yan koparĕṅga iŋ patĕṙ i manis ira aliṇḍyanā rūm ya lindi,
waṙṇna awaṙṣa amadhu lwiṙ nira n asĕmu lĕyĕp niŋ masa ameghapuṣpa*

waṙṇna ayw-aywan ta puṣpā saracana nika taŋ bhūṣana abhrā maṇiknya,
hintĕn mantĕn rinĕṅga iŋ śaśarudhira tutup keśa himpĕṙ wirāga,
lāwan tekaŋ kilat bāhu kilat awilĕt iŋ bāhu tejanya saśrī,
rap-rap-rap rĕp larap niŋ rum ahulap i mukha aṅambwakĕn söŋ niŋ ūṙṇnā*

siṅgiḥ yan pārijāta ahayu nrĕpaduhita aṙwwan laṅö mwaŋ raras rūm,
sākṣāt lūŋ-lūṅan aṅlūŋ jariji nira n alūŋ mwaŋ lĕmĕs niŋ nakha aṙjja,
aṅjraḥ kĕmbaŋ nira iŋ bhūṣaṇa sĕḍĕŋ araras rūm nira aṅasturi mrik,
nyā ŋ pawwaḥ padmarāga ajraḥ i hati mawiji i mas miraḥ riŋ paṅūcal*

sore sāmpun ḍawuḥ sapta tĕka kaka rĕken kāsi-kāsiḥ suputrī,
pintĕn lĕñjĕp riŋ ambĕk wruḥ aṅapi kalaṅön ya apasajñan sahaṙṣā,
bhaṅginya n poliḥ-oliḥ hatuṙ inamĕṙ ikiŋ sinwam iŋ nāgapuṣpa,
wwantĕn ta induŋ tĕmĕn saŋ paran iŋ aṅĕn-aṅĕn liŋnya n antuk manĕmbaḥ*

ambĕk saŋ rājakanyā winaśa-waśa rĕsĕp siḥ nira i saŋ sahaṙṣā,
Āpan mambö kahambö turida nira pinĕm ndan yaya apet raras rūm,
nāhan pājaṙ nira ndi n kusuma kaka mapet patya māṅuṅsya kumbaŋ,
aṅhiŋ yan wwantĕn iŋ campaka mĕkara sakeŋ nīrada aku n sarāga*

nā liŋ saŋ rājakanyā smita nira tan awās waṙṇna maṅrwa asĕnötan,
maṅkin haṙṣā sahaṙṣa aṅriṅa-riṅa turida aṅgītakĕn kūŋ niŋ onĕŋ,
tan makweḥ aṅladi twas kiduŋ iki n atĕrĕḥ sūkṣmarāga aṅrĕsi twas,
kĕmbĕŋ niŋ luḥ tikĕl niŋ halis ira panuwal saŋ sĕḍĕŋ maprapañca*

sāmpun prāpta iña pahyas nira n apĕnĕd arūm strī walū rājapatnī,
tapwan pānak sama mwaŋ rara pamulu nika anwam susunya akas ahrit,
tan saḥ riŋ rūm kahambö ri pipi pinaraban ya ŋ parab saŋ madihyaŋ,
meṅĕt tañcānatañcā panĕṅĕṙ ira ri saŋ swāmi cihna iŋ kasatyan*

maṙmma ajaṙ dyaḥ tuhan toḥ t-atĕlasana sapiḥ pwa ŋ sĕkaṙ putra-putran,
milwi i saŋ ṅāṙyya nak rakryan apa sira yayaḥta n yayi ṅwaŋ turuŋ wruḥ,
nā liŋnya awaṙṇna kepwan saŋ ahayu tinañānya n midĕm yan paśabda,
wwantĕn riŋ twasku saŋ sūkṣmaturida husirĕn tan sphuṭa aliśya-liśyan*

wruḥ riŋ ceṣṭa amacĕḥ rāga nira ri gati saŋ rājaputrī n kĕna iŋ kūŋ,
Āpan sāmpun maṅambaḥ wuni niŋ amuni haṙṣa awiraŋ yan wruha ikā,
hetunya adandan ahyas hana saji humaḍaŋ mwaŋ sĕkaṙ mrik dinānan,
gundik ramya atatā maṅharĕpakĕn anawuŋ puṣpa niŋ kanyaka aṅjraḥ*

<amarawatī>:20.

hyas bwat amarawaty-aṙjja pinakapahyas narawaraputrī rinacana pinriḥ,

i jro crĕmin ira himpĕṙ smaranagara awak siluman inapyan,

ramya atulis arĕcĕp ta amaṇigrĕhawimba aŋ lĕyĕpakĕnāmbĕk,

{erawati}:21.4

māyā nrĕpaduhita awaṙṇna ratiḥ apet hayw-aniru-niru hyas nira madanastrī*

saŋ śrī nrĕpaduhitā sāmpun alulud amraŋ buṅaḥ ira himpĕṙ kanaka sinaṅliŋ,
wāhw-a asalin atapiḥ raṇḍi tinulis iŋ mās miriṙ amarantĕn mamutuhi santĕn,
luṅgī hayu nira nora amaḍani dudug riŋ laṅit anawaŋ nīrada masĕnö bāŋ,
tuṅgaŋ giri maṅadĕg riŋ nataṙ alaṅö rūpa nira tinoliḥ niŋ aruṇa rāgī*

liŋ niŋ kaka-kaka maṙmma asĕmu-sĕmu haṙṣa aṅucapi hajĕŋ saŋ kadi śaśiwimba,
ndi ŋ wwaŋ rari tan akūṅa i raras ira n anwam yan amali paṅlwaŋ sahaja tumaṅgal,
ramya ahajĕŋ alaṅö ṅwaŋ makasuluha i pūṙṇnama ni kalaṅwan nira makin aśrī,
denya ṅwaŋ awuṅaran kagrahaṇana de niŋ prabhu taruṇa aneka ri tuhan i ṅwaŋ*

nāntĕn kapana hana aṅambila kusuma i jro gahana na yāra is tuwin apulaŋ rwi,
maṅkin wiphala ni rūm śrī nrĕpaduhita aṅdadyakĕna sasiḥ niŋ malara sarāga,
lāwan rari kita sakweḥta marĕk i jöŋ saŋ narawaraputrī lewu kasihanta,
himpĕṙ śaca dadi ni ṅwaŋ lĕwas atuhā meman alĕsĕḥ iŋ sampiran ika donya*

<wisaṙjjita>:22.
