om kaka siṅgiḥ ujaṙtta dalu kasihan i ṅwaŋ alĕḥ piniṅit,
mepu haneŋ nagara asurawarapuri tiṣṭa lanā n kinĕmit,
ṅūni haneŋ pura len ṅhulun iki tinawan mapasaḥ riŋ yayaḥ,
ṅke pwa taya ŋ kulawaṙgga dalihan iŋ amintani han wijila*

Āḥ kapana iki tuwuḥku karakĕtana rāga sinaṅśayakĕn,
dūra karambatana i lulut iŋ apaṅus aṅrĕs aweha raras,
mawwad aluŋ marikiŋ turida wirasa ta pwa lawan sirarā,
mātaŋ akiŋ ṅwaŋ akiṅkiŋ amariṅin akiŋ biṣama n prihawak*

ndā yatiki n karaṇaṅku n apĕga siwuhĕn mulati ŋ kusuma,
tan hana sambatĕn iŋ manaṅis i tĕka niŋ gĕrĕḥ aṅlawadi,
maṅkana yan wĕṅi maṙmma maṅĕsĕsan atis ṅwaŋ anaṅhi jawuḥ,
wwaŋ syapa ta aŋ umaṅöt i hudan iŋ adamaṙ kilat iŋ śayana*

maṙmma dahat wacananta rari tuhu-tuhun taruṇī kasihan,
tan wihikan ṅwaŋ i rāmya niŋ aṭika-ṭikan turuŋ akw-asĕnĕŋ,
nāntĕn iki n paṅucap niŋ atuha rinĕṅöṅkw-alulut rinasan,
rakwa ṅamöṙ amĕkul masalit araras aṅlihaṅi wwaŋ arūm*

waṅśastha lan indrawaṅśa
<upendrabajra>:23.
⏓ – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏓ = 12

nahan wuwus niŋ paricārika aṅucap,
ḍatĕŋ tikaŋ rātri tĕlas ḍawuḥ wwalu,
saŋ hyaŋ wulan sĕnw-irikā n makin mawā,
siliḥ-suluḥ mwaŋ maṇigopura iŋ pura*

meḥ-meḥ tĕkā riŋ pura saŋ tilottamā,
atuntunan mwaŋ nrĕpaputra riŋ hawan,
kepwan ri denya n tumamā mareŋ dalĕm,
apan kulĕm kori tĕlas manaṅkĕbi*

tilottama arĕs kumĕtĕg tikaŋ hati,
akweḥ tikā saṅśaya niŋ swacittaka,
antĕn t-alampaḥ kita saprahāra ri,
humantya reḥ niŋ tumamā mare dalĕm*

kathañcana iki iña niraŋ suputrikā,
saṅke dalĕm rāmya sira amajaŋ wulan,
akweḥ tikaŋ guṇḍik arūm paḍa aṅigĕl,
ya hetu niŋ kori humĕṅha sakṣaṇa*

enak tikā buddhi ri saŋ tilottamā,
maha anamaṙ hamba wicakṣaṇa anilib,
alib siraŋ sāmba parĕŋ tĕka i dalĕm,
riŋ śūnya kāliḥ dumunuŋ ri paṅhapit*

tilottama ajaṙ ta sira i nrĕpātmaja,
t-aṅheṙ bapa ṅke sakarĕŋ t-arāṙyyana,
ṅhulun mamet uṅgwan iraŋ suputrikā,
nā liŋnya luṅhā malipiṙ matūt ahöb*

dewī sira ndaḥ kahatuṙ sĕḍĕŋ sukha,
haneŋ umaḥ ratna maṅölakĕn taṅis,
tilottama iniṣṭi sinambya tan waneḥ,
lawasnya luṅhā tinatā nira iŋ tĕtö*

wilāśa niŋ citta kinubdha de nira,
śoka aṅaraŋ tan katĕṅĕṙ tikaŋ lara,
anūkṣma rāga anilib ambĕk iŋ rimaŋ,
muṅgwi twas aṅhiŋ dadi dhaṙmmadewa ya*

jātismarā janma nira ika ṅūny-awās,
saraśmi niŋ swāmi kacitta de nira,
lulwī sira i twas cala riŋ kisapwana,
yateka kāṅĕn katutuṙ nira i kakuŋ*

maṅke pwa yan tan hana konĕŋ iŋ liriŋ,
yayā tĕka añumbana yan haneŋ jinĕm,
meraŋ tumuṅkul pira yan pajaŋ wulan,
na hetu niŋ hewa tumiṅhala iŋ śaśi*

tilottamā prāpta ri saŋ suputrikā,
maṙmma n pamakpak rari māsku liŋ nikā,
haywa ika deniŋ manaṅis hĕnĕŋ tuhan,
Āpan kapaṅgiḥ dadi dhaṙmmadewa ya*

maṅjanma ri śrī naranātha keśawa,
prasiddha śūra iŋ raṇa śakti nītiman,
saŋ sāmba sajñā nira kaprakāśita,
raras nira aṅde raras iŋ twas iŋ mulat*

kunĕŋ pratiṅkaḥ naranātha keśawa,
wiṣṇw-a anurun lakṣaṇa dewamūṙttika,
pratiṣṭha riŋ dwārawatī sira adhika,
karĕs nikaŋ rākṣasa dꜽtya dānawa*

ndā saŋ narendrātmaja sāmba rakwa ya,
kinon marā riŋ himawān sira apraṅa,
rumakṣa sakweḥ nira saŋ mahārĕṣi,
anwam wruha akīṙtti widagdha śaktimān*

ṅūni pwa saŋ dyaḥku makon umeta ya,
kañcit pwa saŋ krĕṣṇasuta asyaŋ iŋ kami,
matakwan uṅgwanta sira amĕlas harĕp,
nimitta niŋ mājarakĕn hananta ri*

maṅkā ṅhulun mwaŋ sira śīghra maṅkata,
huwus tĕkā ṅke sira māsku liŋ nikā,
nahan sinādhyā tumutuṙ mare kita,
liṅĕn saŋ adyaḥku manuṅsuṅa iŋ guyu*

<prahaṙṣiṇī>:24.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑|  ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏓ = 13

nāhan liŋ surawanita iŋ narendraputrī,
saŋ sāmba aśila ri samīpa saŋ suputrī,
maṙmma aṅholakĕna ri māsku liŋ nira ujar,
kāṅgĕk citta nira liniṅsiran suputrī*

saŋ sāmba akĕcap aṅĕsaḥ mĕhāḥ rinĕṅwan,
kepwan haṙṣa rinirisan rimaŋ prapañca,
yadyastun salaḥ-asa ta aku liŋ nira i twas,
maṙmmanya awaraha maṅiṣṭi ta aku mātya*

tan tuhw-i ika wuwus i saŋ tilottama asyaŋ,
duṣṭa amet kahilaṅa ni ṅwaŋ iŋ puri jro,
Āpan śatru sura kĕta aku riŋ paranku,
siṅgiḥ ṅgānya ya wiṣakānanā ṅaranya*

nāntĕn ta wwaŋ anumata aśraya iŋ hala ṅwaŋ,
siṅgiḥ paṅgilana puriḥ nikaŋ tan āpti,
strī ratna iki tuwi surūpa rājakanyā,
nyāma nya awiraṅa rinĕṅwan iŋ karaśmin*

rūm-rūmĕn rarasana raśmi kūŋ lawan siḥ,
rakryan toḥ śaraṇa nira amanista māsku,
nāntĕn ton rari lara niŋ kĕna iŋ lulut kūŋ,
kahyunkw-a atĕwasa tĕṅaḥta riŋ paturwan*

antĕn yan lawanana siḥku denta māsku,
rāmyaṅku n siliḥ-asiha anawuŋ raras rūm,
raśmī sāturida sarāga tohan i ṅwaŋ,
taṅgap siḥku makasihan ta riŋ puḍak mrik*

saŋ māwak lara niŋ akūŋ kasiḥ niŋ onĕŋ,
aṅde māṙ i hati rĕnaḥta yan tumiṅhal,
ndātan poṣadha ni manista maṅlare twas,
maṅga anumpurakĕna haṙṣa citta ni ṅwaŋ*

saŋ māmbö kusuma miṅiŋ lihat kita antĕn,
hyunkw-a agya anisana ŋ iraṅta maprapañca,
tan māry-ānalaga lĕwas manista māsku,
sārinta ari karaṇa niŋ manatpada aswī*

rakryan dāhana punagiṅku denta māsku,
sādhyaṅkw-a aṅamĕra susunta riŋ paturwan,
maṅke pwa aṅhĕnĕṅakĕn iŋ kakanta māsku,
antĕn dyaḥku juga mapaṅgi-paṅgil elik*

maṅka akaṙṣaṇa nira saŋ narendraputra,
kasyāsiḥ maṅasiḥ-asiḥ maminta kāsiḥ,
dewī kepwan iŋ ulaha awiraŋ tumuṅkul,
mĕṅgĕp taṅlihat anilib liriŋ nira aśrī*

wruḥ pwa ikaŋ suraduhitā ri buddhya dewī,
maṙmmanya awuwus aṅiriŋ manaḥ suputrī,
māskw-i induŋ kapana siraŋ narendraputra,
tan maṙmma asiha ri tuhanku kāṙyya haṙṣa*

tañ jātismara hiḍĕp i ṅhulun ri māsku,
yan tan meṅĕt i sawilāśa dhaṙmmadewa,
tonton ta iki litu-hajöŋ narendraputra,
samplaḥ mwaŋ harisuta saŋ pinet rikāna*

lāwan kosthuba mala cihna niŋ sahaṙṣa,
mrik gandhanya kadi rikāna tan papendaḥ,
yeka aṅde rĕsĕp i hatinta liṅta ṅūni,
ṅkā dewi ika yan atutuṙ midĕm sahaṙṣa*

<wisaṙjjita>:25.

Āḥ kaka haywa kĕdö mirĕsĕpakĕn apet siḥ aminta kasiḥ,
tan wuruŋ aṅlawana i hati marika wuwusta rĕsĕp ri hati,
ṅwaŋ kadi tan rara denta n amĕḍara karaśmi nihan ṅwaŋ awak,
santaḥ anambĕhi siḥta tan amupugana ikiŋ akūŋ tinahā*

māsku tuhankw-ibu haywa hali-halin i buddhi narendrasuta,
cihna nihan kahananta bhaya tuwi tathāpi sira iki mara,
dyaḥ t-asĕgĕḥ tari māskw-akira turida kāṙwwa lulut ri kita,
taṅgap i rūmta raras nira panamuya lindi nikaŋ pamatan*

ndi pwa hunĕṅta pininta ri hati wĕḍarĕnta tuhankw-i sira,
don i rarasnya mara i kita sira naranātha rirista mijil,
wyaṙtha ni rūm i pipinta pasaji-saji māsku mahāpi miṅe,
tansaha jöṅta sinewa niŋ amalaṙ aṅuṅsiṙ acatwa tĕṅaḥ*

ndaḥ si putiḥ si kita aṅucap aku kaka tan wruḥ i saŋ wwaŋ ika,
tan sahura aku muwaḥ ri kata kita maṅel ṅwaŋ ameta sahur,
nāhan ujaṙ nira saŋ narawaraduhita asĕmu haṙṣa nira,
tulya kuḍuŋ-kuḍuŋ iŋ turida sira rĕsĕp ri lulut siḥ ira*

saŋ nrĕpaputra wawaŋ wruḥ i manaḥ ira yajñawatī wĕkasan,
śīghra mamaṅkwakĕn aṅharis-aris saha siḥ rĕsĕp iŋ saŋ arūm,
rĕs nikanaŋ hati māṙ makĕtĕṙ i paṅamöṙ nira riŋ panĕpi,
lwiṙ tan awak marika awak iḍĕp ira rikā n karakĕt ri susu*

ambĕk ira alawas abrata wiṣaya lanā karaha ŋ turida,
tambay ira alabuhan manis iŋ ahayu manwam arūpa ratiḥ,
tan wriŋ aris maṅĕpĕl susu taṅan ira kāṙwwa maṅaŋ tan arĕs,
lāgy-anutul pipi nāsika nira titiṙ oliḥ i luḥ saŋ arūm*

<jagaddhita>:26.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

mojaṙ saŋ nrĕpaputra tiṅhal i kakanta rari baraŋ aṅölakĕn lara,
saŋsāra ṅwaŋ akūŋ kĕna priḥ i wajanta sinawawa ni raśmi niŋ guyu,
māṙ mrāt twasku kanin tĕñuḥ katikĕlan halis ibu tuluṅĕn pwa taṅhulun,
ṅhiŋ jampyaṅkw-i susunta lūŋ ni luṅayanta bĕbĕda ni kakanta riŋ tilam*

dyaḥ saŋ haṙṣa winimba kūŋ piniturun saŋ awak iŋ alaṅö linaṅwakĕn,
rūpanta iŋ madhu piṇḍa lindi ni matanta kadi juruḥ atuṙ gula drawa,
sotan tā dadi niŋ raras hati rarasta mapamulu ṭikā haneŋ puḍak,
sākṣāt sāri ni sāri niŋ kusuma māsku n ariris iŋ awaṙṇna ṣaṭpada*

antĕnkw-a aṅĕn-aṅĕn katĕmwan i kakanta rasana ri sĕḍĕṅku dewatā,
rakryañ citrarathātmaja atuha ri putra lĕṅĕŋ anaruka iŋ himālaya,
aṅkat hyaŋ madhusūdana aṅdadi tumūt aku ri sira tatan waraḥ kita,
hīṅan hyaŋ widhi kapwa hetu ni kakanta rari layat atiṅgal iŋ tilam*

maṅke prāpta kakanta deniŋ utusan sahaja mara humundaṅa i ṅhulun,
wwantĕnkw-i iki manĕmwa haṙṣa sahasa n sinalaḥ-asa manaḥku tan liniŋ,
dwandwan ṅgānya kita i ṅhulun ri gati niŋ pinun alawas atiṅgal iŋ kita,
rakryan piṇḍahi ta aku hetu niŋ aminta kalukunĕn i luḥta riŋ pipi*

doṣaṅkw-i i kita ṅūni maṙmma riraŋ iŋ gati ri kita rikāna riŋ jinĕm,
sāmpun siŋ sapanigrahanta ri manĕḥta yadin apusananta riŋ lulut,
mwaŋ yan kūŋ tuwi milwa kūṅku saphala n palu-palu turidanta ri ṅhulun,
denya aṅisyani rāgahaṙṣa ya wilaŋ damĕl ibu lawas i ṅwaŋ iŋ paran*

rakryan sanmatanĕn kakanta rari tapwa hiniwagan unĕŋnya yaṇ ḍatĕŋ,
wehĕnta n rĕsĕpa ambĕkanta tuhun aṅlawanana kita tiṅhal i ṅhulun,
sāmpun wruḥ ṅwaŋ i saṅśayanta riŋ apa aku tan asiha manuṅgala i kita,
maṙmma aniṅgala riŋ laṅö ṅwaŋ iriya n malalis amĕkasa iŋ karaŋ liman*

saŋ hyaŋ niŋ kalaṅön lihat rari riŋ aṅhyaŋ amalaku kakuŋ hana i kita,
pūjaṅkw-i i sari sāri muṅgwi gĕluṅanta saha sĕkaṙ urā haneŋ tilam,
mwaŋ sambatkw-i paṅastawaṅku hiḍĕpĕnku wacana niŋ akūŋ mapet asiḥ,
rakryan toḥ t-aṅanugraha ika ri kakanta suṅakĕna pininta ni ṅhulun*

ñĕṙ citta nrĕpaputrikā winuwusan rĕṅu-rĕṅu nira tan tĕka i hati,
tuhw-a alūŋ siḥ ira amĕlas-harĕp aron turida siniram iŋ karāsikan,
mampĕḥ rakwa kĕtĕṙ nira aṅdadi lulut sumalaḥ i sira saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
maṙmmā niŋ hyun alūŋ ya leśya nira yan paṅuwahi panulak nira iŋ jaja*

siṅhit-siṅhit ira i hati iki winĕḍaṙ nira liŋ ira ri saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
wruḥ ṅwaŋ ry-ambĕkan iŋ priyambada mĕne pwa puput ika kuraŋ-kuraŋ wĕlas,
nāntĕn ndī wĕnaṅa ŋ sĕkaṙ muwaha riŋ bhramara makalisa iŋ hrĕbuk miṅiŋ,
ndā maṅka aku yadin katiṅgala sumantĕn anĕsĕla śarīra ni ṅhulun*

maṅke kapwa tĕṅaḥ niŋ aṅlalisi raśmi sĕḍĕŋ iŋ anaḍaḥ siḥ iŋ sĕnĕŋ,
wruḥ pwa anāntwa sinanmata iki dadi niŋ sinaṅi-saṅi sinewaka iŋ hiḍĕp,
lwiṙ tan sot rika yan kĕdö rawi phalanya riŋ asuji hinundaŋ iŋ lulut,
ṅhiŋ maṅke sukha mātya bhukti pamĕkas kalara niŋ alaṅö kināryakĕn*

om antĕnku sadenta mojaṙ-ujaṙ aṅlarani hati kakanta tan wiwal,
sāmpun wruḥ ṅwaŋ i suṅsut iŋ kadi kita ahayu manupura rājasa iŋ rimaŋ,
yadyastun śapathāna ta ṅwaŋ ari denta saphala karĕṅö tikaŋ wuwus,
Āpan tan hana śabda niŋ jalada maṅgĕsĕṅana ri kapö niŋ aṅrĕṅö*

ndi n taŋ cātaka nāgata iŋ riris ikaŋ jalada rari sĕḍĕŋnya n aṅlayaŋ,
lāwan ndi n salaga awĕdi iŋ riris i meḥnya sumĕkara kagĕntĕran gĕrĕḥ,
maṅka aku n sinaranta kāsihan apan rinirisan aṅusiṙ kita iŋ jinĕm,
haṙṣa asoṅa karāsikan ṅwaŋ aharĕp riŋ amanis ahudan-hudan madhu*

maṅkin trāsa manaḥku de ni panaḥ iŋ madana mamanasi twas i ṅhulun,
yekā n śīṙṇna manaḥku denya kakĕnan lara turida ni rāga niŋ smara,
maṅke pwa iki kahaṙṣa ni ṅwaŋ i kita ibu kita madĕha kiṅkiŋ i ṅhulun,
aṅhiŋ tamba kanin tapiḥ saput ulĕs palakun i kita haywa t-a atĕṅĕt*

wruḥ riŋ ceṣṭa tilottamā n mijil aleśya n aṅĕyĕha wawaŋ tĕka iŋ natar,
tan señjuḥ rasikā kinon maluy alĕs lumaris apituli n pamet sahur,
saŋ sinwī kawĕkas wiraṅwaŋ aṅĕsaḥ prihati linukaran tapiḥ nira,
miṅsĕṙ-miṅsĕṙ aḍuḥ wuwus nira kinewala kaparĕpĕkan tinītihan*

dewī yajñawatī karāgabhaya riŋ śayana kahilaṅan raras hati,
rĕs-rösĕn prihatin karājasana piŋ rwa n amadanawilāśa riŋ tilam,
tan  ṙyyamban kinisapwakĕn rĕṅĕ-rĕṅön ri wuwus iŋ aṅamöṙ prahāsana,
luḥ lāwan turaḥ iŋ taṅis juga sahuṙ nira hinasi-hasiḥ nrĕpātmaja*

dyaḥ saŋ nāyaka niŋ laṅö waśa waśeṣa kita ri lĕṅĕŋ iŋ pasiṙ wukir,
rūm-rūmta anusaḥ iŋ sĕkaṙ milu tĕṅaḥta mamarawaśa sinwam iŋ tahĕn,
tan laṅgöŋ puriḥ iŋ puḍak kĕtĕṙ anĕmbaḥ i manis i matanta yan laris,
antĕn toḥ diwasa ŋ mata pwa sipata aṅlarani titiṙ inaṅluḥ iŋ manis*

siṅgiḥ yan sugiḥ iŋ manis rari kita agati panarima niŋ madhubrata,
aṅkĕn yan madhumāsa māsku sinahuṙ manis amuhaki sāri niŋ sĕkar,
rob kālanya ḍatĕŋ tasik madhu nimitta nika lĕṅĕŋ adoḥ mapet manis,
maṅke donkw-i kita ṇ ḍatĕŋ rari maha aṅinakana manis iŋ hutaŋ tĕṅaḥ*

yan rekhākĕna riŋ puḍak ṅhulun i paṅlĕṅĕṅan iŋ alaṅö hañaṙ maṅö,
rakryan rowaṅa ni ṅhulun hubhayanĕn sasisihana raras ṭikākĕna,
ramya asaṅwa lulut ṅwaŋ antĕn akĕmul-kĕmula hima ri duṅhus iŋ karaŋ,
yan wwantĕn bhramara aṅlawad yatika sūṅakĕna sararab iŋ hrĕbuk miṅiŋ*

<aśwalalita>:27.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑|⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

nahan ika śabda saŋ nrĕpatiputra haṙṣa turida ajaṙ aṅrĕsĕpakĕn,
hañĕñĕṙ awoṙ manis hinaras iŋ raras hati rĕsĕp ri maṙmma saŋ arūm,
saŋ ahayu māṙ gupe sira ri kapriyambadan i saŋ narendratanaya,
titiṙ akĕcap manĕṅgaḥ ahuyaŋ ya leśya nira n aṅluse tapiḥ ira*

nrĕpaduhita asawaŋ jalada kāṅinan raras ira an lukaṙ gĕluŋ ira,
riris ira rakwa māri siniriṙ  ṙyyasiḥ nira ri saŋ narendratanaya,
gĕrĕḥ i lulut nira iki wĕkasan lawan patĕṙ i kūŋ nira n karakĕtan,
larap i pupuṙ nira akilat awās manambĕṙ i tapiḥ nira an inalapan*

wahu waśa saŋ narendraduhitā n wineḥ sĕpaḥ anaṅgap iŋ tutuk arūm,
pipi nira māṙ miṅiŋ ya panuwal nira aṅinaki citta saŋ nrĕpasuta,
laṭi kumĕñaṙ titiṙ sinĕsĕpan pamöm nira waja n khara aṅani hati,
puji yan asañjata i luṅid ikaŋ halis mukha nira n lana anĕkani siḥ*

wahu paḍa rāmya maṙmma sira kāliḥ aṅrasani rāmya niŋ siliḥ-asiḥ,
sagula sawĕltiḥ iŋ patĕmu yan paṅaṙwwani hulĕs miṅiŋ kinapuran,
aṭika-ṭikan laṅö raras ira i dalĕm jinĕm amukti rāmya niŋ arūm,
patakis ikaŋ kale marahakĕn raras wiphala tan hana aṅawaraṇa*

ri ḍatĕŋ ikaŋ hudan siḥ ira saŋ nrĕpātmaja mawāḥ sukha amarupuhi,
aṅibĕki citta hetu nira sāmba haṙṣa masawaḥ raras pinahayu,
nrĕpasuta tan kara aṅgalĕṅi buddhi yan sumalaha iŋ tilam sĕḍĕŋ akūŋ,
aṅamĕṙ-amöṙ sarāga n añuluḥ-ñuluḥ lulut ira i saŋ adyaḥ araras*

lumĕkas amuṣpa rāga sira riŋ manobhawa saha aprayoga turida,
waṅi-waṅi niŋ pipi i hiḍĕp ira asĕp endaḥ adamaṙ liriŋ saŋ ahayu,
sira-sirat iŋ lawö karaṇa gandha wīja nira mālati i sari gĕluŋ,
caru nira maṙmma haṙṣa winirāga de nira hinaṅsĕ riŋ pakasutan*

madanamahotsawa iki ginawe nira iŋ śayana tan pakāla dinadak,
sumari ya waśya-waśya ni laṅö nira an aṅapi haṙṣa niŋ saturida,
alap-alapan raras gati nira n siliḥ-suwal i gandha niŋ pipi miṅiŋ,
makin awuwuḥ rĕsĕp wĕrĕ-wĕrö dawā sĕmu nira n luse tapiḥ ira*

asari-sari i manis-manis iŋ ojaṙ aṅracana raśmi niŋ siliḥ-asiḥ,
ajĕnu nakhabraṇa aṙjja masĕkaṙ gaḍuŋ sira n arāmya-rāmyan araras,
nrĕpasuta tan kara aṅayari haṙṣa rāga ri saŋ adyaḥ iŋ pakasutan,
hanan inajöŋ lulut nira lana anitiṙ saŋ ahajöŋ siraŋ nrĕpasuta*

rahina tĕlas mijil kĕñaṙ ira hyaŋ aṙkka muni taŋ manuk mawurahan,
sawuṙ i rurū nikaŋ kamuniŋ-iŋ nataṙ siniram iŋ riris-riris alit,
sahana ni ron ikaŋ tahĕn ataṅhi paṅhwab i sĕkaṙ nika abab awaṅi,
milu taŋ aśokapādapa lawan paṅulyat i siriṙ nikāŋ aṅin alon*

tĕka ta tilottama amuṅu ri saŋ haneŋ jinĕm apan sĕḍĕŋ karakĕtan,
ataña ri gatya saŋ tĕlas apaṅgiḥ ekaturida apisan manaḥ akūŋ,
sahuṙ ira saŋ rwa haywa kita saṅśaya i ṅhulun akūŋ ṅwaŋ iŋ satinahā,
apituwi saŋ mahīsuta mareŋ surālaya taṅeḥ umantuka sira*

liŋ ira narendraputra kaka yan tĕkā saŋ asurendra haywa magigu,
aku lawananya tan suruda riŋ kadhīran asiluṅluṅa ŋ purasabhā,
yan alaha ta akw-aṅadwa guṇaśakti de niŋ asura aḥ alök ṅaran ikā,
kaka tumuta ṅhulun pĕjaha liŋ narendraduhitā ri saŋ nrĕpasuta*

prāpta ikaŋ warawanitā kabeḥ manaṅkil,
ndā tan wruḥ ri gati niraŋ narendraputrī,
ṅūny-aṅdoḥ aṅilagi suṅsut iŋ rahadyan,
hetunya amĕŋ-amĕŋ asiŋ paran katurwan*

söŋ saŋ hyaŋ rawi karaṇanya yan pataṅhi,
kapwa agyā lumaku mareŋ taman kabeḥnya,
ṅkāna iŋ pamrĕman ira saŋ narendraputrī,
haṙṣa n ton surawanitā haneŋ surambyan*

mojaṙ ya asĕgĕḥ i siraŋ tilottama aṅliŋ,
agyā prāpta saŋ inipi ipi ta ṅwaŋ onĕŋ,
dewī tan sipi paṅucap nira i lawasta,
nāhan hetu nira dumohakĕn sira i ṅwaŋ*

sakweḥ niŋ marĕk i sira n madoḥ tinuṇḍuŋ,
nāhan hetu niŋ amajaŋ wulan paḍa aṅdoḥ,
maṅke pwa apuhara hane samīpa dewī,
maṙmma agaṙjjita hati ni ṅhulun tumiṅhal*

nāhan liŋnya saha manīs ikā n patakwan,
mājaṙ saŋ tinañan anandhyakĕn sinādhya*

om sāmpun katĕmu siraŋ pinet iniṣṭi,

nāhan liŋ suraduhita awaraḥ prahaṙṣa,

nā liŋnya n paguñĕpan iŋ nataṙ magupyan,
wyaktinya aṅucap amanis lawan guyunya*

nāga agöŋ tĕka mamilĕt narendraputrī,
yeki wyakti nira phalanya śīghra sākṣāt*

nyāŋ māsiḥ sira ri gatiṅku pūṙwwasewa,

bhadrānugraha niyatā niki n sukhanta,
Āpan tan waraṅĕn ikā hawan katĕmwa*

taṅheḥ yañ caritan ujaṙ nikaŋ warastrī,
maṙmma agaṙjjita magiraŋ kabeḥ manaḥnya,
tan toliḥ wuyuṅan iraŋ surendraśatru,
denya agya aṅlayat abĕsuṙ haneŋ kaḍatwan*

ceṣṭākāra ni paricārikā sudewī,
sāmpun kawruhan inĕbaŋ-hĕbaŋ rikaŋ twas*

ndan dewī hana wiraŋ iŋ manaḥ swabhāwa,
tan wriŋ tiṅhalana mĕne yan iŋ parāna,
sotan taŋ hañaṙ asĕnĕŋ tuwin suputrī,
meraŋ riŋ mulat anahā ri līṅa niŋ len*

riŋ raṅkaŋ maṇi rika saŋ rwa yan pasīwo,
muṅgwi jro kacapuri rāmya yan pasaṇḍiŋ,
māyākāra sira katon agātra-gātra,
himpĕṙ madya kinĕkĕs iŋ gĕḍaḥ lumimbak*

ñĕṙ twasnya aṅliriṅi liriŋ narendraputra*

wyātītā gati nikanaŋ sakhī n paḍa apti,

śobha arūm wulat ira haṙṣa saŋ tumiṅhal,
aṅde māṙ i mata manis nira aṅani twas*

wwꜽ muṅgwi i śaśadhararatnakumbha śuddha,

mwaŋ toya iŋ ghaṭa rawikānta ṅöt aṅötnya,

wwaynya awaṙṇna kakĕñaran sĕnö hyaŋ aṙkka,

riŋ nūsa apatani jamuṙ maṇik wiśuddha,

Āpan māsku madanaputrikā hiḍĕpku*

nāhan laṇḍĕp i warayaṅku rakṣakanta*

wuwus ira saŋ narendrasuta maṅkana tĕhĕṙ aṅisapwakĕn saŋ ahayu,
tĕka ta tilottama anuturakĕn saha kaka-kaka saŋ narendraduhitā,
nĕhĕṙ aṅalap sĕkaṙ sumanasa mrĕbuk awaṅi lawan sugandhakusuma,
sĕmi niŋ aśoka nāgakusuma jriŋ uliḥ-uliḥ ikā n paḍa aṅhaturakĕn*

irika ta saŋ sahaṙṣa tĕkasiḥ wagĕd amanis arūm irĕŋ yan awuwus,
anak-anakan sĕkaṙ tĕka hinĕmbanan ika sĕkaṙ iŋ gaḍuŋ sĕḍĕŋ arūm,
liŋ ika ri saŋ narendraduhitā wwaya ta sira tuhan ṅhulun makilayū,
wacana nikā priyambada nira n siliḥ-asiḥ araras manaṅgap aṅamör*

sĕḍĕŋ ira saŋ narendrasuta rāmya yan aṭika-ṭikan mamukti kusuma,

wwaya paricārika aṅajarakĕn ri tĕka nika si dārukī n hana ri heŋ,

bapa pawĕkas mahāṙṣi ri patikta jaga-jaga narendraputra liŋ ira,

nrĕpaduhitā sabhāgya sira yan tumutakĕna bapaṅku haywa ta jĕnĕk*

tuwi tĕka hamba rakryan atihaŋ maṅiriṅakĕna saŋ narendraduhitā,

nrĕpatanaya aṅrĕṅö gĕrĕḥ ikāŋ asurabala manaḥ nira anahĕnana,
kawanin ira awuwuḥ sĕmi kadhīran ira tĕlas aron kamānawibhawan,

kunaŋ ika saŋ narendraduhitā kakĕtĕran awĕdi i surak niŋ asura ,
amĕkuli saŋ narendrasuta sāmba sira saha taṅis gupe kinisapu,

paṅawak ira alĕmĕs yatika māṙ i kapanasan ira aṅrĕṅö suraripu*

nrĕpasuta maṙmma mājari saŋ adyaḥ ibu laku t-uliḥ mare dalĕm umaḥ,
ṅhulun alagā lawan sahana niŋ suraripubala sök maṅĕmbuli puri,
ṅwaŋ ayaśa dhaṙmma niŋ yadukula aṅilaṅakĕna musuḥku riŋ pabharatan,
ṅhiŋ iki panumbasaṅkw-iri kita ari kawanin i kakanta tan hana waneḥ*

mijila kakanta māsku pahawās ta rari raras ikiŋ sĕḍĕŋ kamasihĕn,
ṅwaŋ aṅarĕki i kita ṅwaŋ aṅayuḥ tĕṅaḥ iki rari saṅwa ni ṅwaŋ alaga,

nrĕpaduhita alume winuwusan prihati nira marambahan saha kĕtĕr,
liŋ ira kaka ndi teki parana syapa śaraṇa ri tan hananta masiha,
karaṇa niŋ āpti mātya rumuhun ṅwaŋ i harĕp i kakaṅku tiṅhali nihan,
ujaṙ ira maṅkana atĕhĕṙ aminta curiga nira saŋ narendratanaya*

nrĕpasuta sāmba haṙṣa rumĕṅö sira ri wuwus i saŋ narendraduhitā,
ibu kita māsku liŋ nira tuhankw-iki saŋ ahayu haywa maṅkana kita,
kapana kakanta sora lumaga iŋ suraripu haku śūra śakti riŋ ayun,
lagi-lagi kambulan kasusunan ṅhulun anĕṅaḥ anīṙṇna dānawabala*

mataŋ iki haywa saṅśaya manaḥta rari pisaniṅun ṅhulun yaŋ alaha,
pagĕḥ i kasiṅhan i ṅhulun ika n pagĕhakĕna hara ibu haywa kabharan,
ra kaka tilottamā rari rumowaṅana kita maṅantyakĕn ṅwaŋ alaga,
liŋ ira n aweḥ sĕpaḥ tĕhĕṙ aṅol aṅarĕki ri siraŋ narendraduhitā*

ri wĕtu narendraputra saka riŋ puri ratha nira śīghra sāmpun apasaŋ,
tumuluy anuṅgaŋ iŋ ratha sira akawaca tĕlas asaṅkĕp astra niśita,
bala nira śūra kapwa marĕpat katĕmu sĕḍĕŋ ika agĕlaṙ tan akaḍat,
prawala lawan raken sahaja sāmpun akawaca paḍa aṅgĕgön laras agöŋ*

tucapa tikaŋ musuḥ prasama maṅlĕpasakĕn i panaḥnya tan papĕgatan,
hana malipuŋ tumandaŋ aṅunus baḍama nika sinuṅkĕlaŋ sana-sini,
aṅun-aṅun ahyun oliha ri saŋ nrĕpasuta sahananya ya asira-siran,
aṅasut aṅĕmbul iŋ śara saha aśwa-gajapati marampak atri gumuruḥ*

panaḥ ira saŋ nrĕpātmaja lawan bala nira mĕtu riŋ payuddhan asusun,
mijil asuluŋ-suluŋ panaḥ ikaŋ prawala sahaja kīṙṇna sök winulatan,
kumusuḥ abāyubajra tumulak warayaŋ iŋ asura iŋ nabhastala katūt,
maṅĕnani rākṣasa iŋ gaja maṅohan awurahan agĕntuṙ awri kawaluy*

mĕlĕtuk ikaŋ lĕbū tĕkap iŋ aśwa-ratha-gaja-padāti mosyan asuwe,
kumukus umiṇḍuhuṙ pĕtĕŋ ikaŋ gagana kadi marok lawan kṣititala,
wulaṅun ikaŋ bala asura tatan wruḥ i wĕkas i lawanya kapwa masĕlur,
karaṇa nika aṅawag pati panaḥ-panaḥ i pati mahā lana amahi wĕdi*

<sragdharā>:30.

kālanya n tan katon lwiṙ nikaŋ asurabala atyanta śabdanya ghora,
strī-strī kanya iŋ pura awrĕg mawĕdi giri-girin tan wruḥ iŋ de kabeḥnya,
ceṭī lāwan parigyan kaka-kaka manaṅis pūḥ gĕyuḥ seña rukṣa,
sambat-sambat nikā ṅhiŋ tuhan iki liŋ ikā n kāsihan tan hana apa*

mwaŋ saŋ śrī rājakanyā sira ta katanĕhan māṙ gupe pūḥ karĕs-rĕs,
tan saḥ riŋ hĕmbanan mrĕm kapati makin awū taŋ wwaŋ iŋ jro masambat,
taṅheḥ yadyan sira aṅhera hiḍĕp ira hiña anāgata iŋ duṙbala agöŋ,
heṙ saŋ śrī nātha bhomāsura karaṇa nika umuṙ humĕmban suputrī*

sakweḥ niŋ strī dalĕm tan hana kari ya tumūt makrigan kapwa luṅhā,
ṅkāna iŋ prāgjyotiṣa ikaŋ hinusiṙ ika kabeḥ kwān i saŋ śrī mahīja,
tan waṙṇnan lwiṙnya riŋ māṙgga tĕka ta ya rikaŋ rājya sāmpun sinuṅsuŋ,
tan śobha aṅel tinurwākĕn iki sira hane soṙ ikaŋ pārijāta*

ndā rakryan rājaputrī sira ta wahu katon aṅliliṙ labdhajīwa,
tapwan maṅgĕḥ ry-awak twas nira kĕtĕ-kĕtĕgĕn mwaŋ sumaṅhī tan andĕl,
tiṅhal ndā tan sphuṭāṙtha aṙddha pĕjaha manira n kāmukan luḥ kumĕmbĕŋ,
ndā māwrāt taŋ sahuṙ yan tinañan iṅĕt ira i saŋ marĕk mwaŋ matakwan*

<wiśwalalita>:31.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 17

tĕlas abaṅun ta saŋ prawaraputrika aṅĕsaḥ alök,
waluyana ta ujarĕn praŋ ira saŋ narendratanaya,
amanahakĕn mahāstra waraśakti tan patahĕnan,
alilaŋ ikaŋ lĕbū kaḍĕḍĕtan ta rāḥ niŋ asura*

gajaratha tan pasāra ya cinakra de nrĕpasuta,
makatihalaŋ pwa rĕṅga nika riŋ payuddhan atunaḥ,
śawa nikanaŋ balāsura matimbun iŋ pabharatan,
atumaŋ atap lawan kuda liman pĕjaḥ kakuwuṅan*

tura-turaḥ iŋ balāsura pĕjaḥ ya ta amriḥ alayū,
maṅusiṙ ikaŋ kuṭa i naraka tan panoliḥ i musuḥ,
karaṇa nikā n tinūt hinudanan warāstra niśita,
muliḥ atakut kabeḥ kadi liman tumon mrĕgapati*

nrĕpasuta mantuk iŋ puri hiḍĕp nira n marĕn anūt,
huwus umaluy sira i ratha kaṅelan apraŋ asuwe,
hariṅĕt ira i mukha drawa mareŋ jaja aṙjja tumitis,
husapana saŋ narendraduhitā kakuŋ nira mĕne*

tĕka ta tilottama iki manaṅis manuṅsuŋ i sira,
liŋ ika hilaŋ kasiḥta bapa tan haneŋ puri sira,
iña nira yan malaywakĕn i saŋ maṇik niŋ ahayu,
atĕhĕṙ ahĕmbanan taṅan ikā sira n kasiḥ-arĕp*

lĕwu mara taṅguḥ i ṅwaŋ irikaŋ sakhījana kabeḥ,
kunaŋ apa tā paḍa awĕdi ri saŋ mahīsuta juga,
nahan ika hetu saŋ prawaraputrikā yan inalap,
winawa mare dalĕm sira ri kāla rakryan alaga*

dalu kawĕlas-harĕp nira kawös gupe kakĕtĕran,
kapati ri hĕmbanan sira hinerakĕn kinisapu,
tiritis i luḥ nikaŋ mata tĕhĕṙ tiba i susu nira,
karaṇa nira aṅliliṙ lagi sira ataña i kita laki*

liŋ ira tilottama awaraḥ i saŋ narendratanaya,
irika ta saŋ nrĕpātmaja hilaŋ manaḥ nira lĕṅöŋ,
jĕṅĕṙ asuwe nda tan sahuṙ apan pijĕṙ kahĕnĕṅan,
mĕhaḥ aṅĕsaḥ sira aṅusapi luḥ nira n salaḥ-asa*

<rajanī>:32.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 17

alupa sira n tiba alara sira mwaŋ ikaŋ warayaŋ,
irika kalĕṅgak iŋ ratha sira alara pūḥ kapĕgan,
tatan umiṅĕl sira n kĕḍap apan kasatan ri gulū,
maṅusapi hīs ni lūḥ nira ri lambay ira n tan arĕn*

wĕkasan udāni dhīra sira riŋ kṣaṇa māry-alupa,
inuṣadhan iŋ kamānawibhawan sumaput ri hati,
aṅĕnĕb-ĕnĕb raras hati nira n kamĕna aṅucapa,
tĕhĕṙ aṅucap ri saŋ surawadhū liŋ ira iki nihan*

kaka marĕna anaṅis kita pi haywa dahat prihatin,
ṅhulun umara iŋ kuṭa anĕkana śatru kabeḥ punaha,
saphala yaśaṅku yan hilaṅa rājya nikaŋ naraka,
tan uliha yan turuŋ malap arinta tĕkapku mĕne*

wuwus ira maṅkana anĕhĕṙ umaṅkat adan kawaca,
tĕlas atihaŋ sasañjata sira iŋ ratha nora kari,
rika ta sira ika śīghra maṅĕbak mahawan palapat,
dhwani nika kaṙkkaśa asĕmu patĕṙ maḍarat riŋ ayun*

irika ta nārada anututi saŋ naranāthasuta,
akuyu-kuyū rikāna hariṅĕt nira riŋ wadana,
daluwaŋ ira akusut lukaṙ i bandha nirā katiliŋ,
ginamĕl ira i tĕṅĕn mwaŋ i kiwa ika tĕhĕṙ maṅawe*

aṅuhuḥ akon marāṙyyana sira i naranāthasuta,
wuwus ira kātara asrak apĕḍĕs haliwat ri kapö,
kṣañ. a sira saŋ nrĕpātmaja manoliḥ amaspadakĕn,
wawaŋ atutuṙ sira adara ri saŋ yati yan tumurun*

pataña narendraputra ri mahāmuni  bhakty-ararĕm,
maśila sira iŋ śilātala ri saṇḍiŋ iraŋ sutapa,
mataña sira i prayojana mahāṙṣi makon maluya,
dadi sumahuṙ ta nārada ri saŋ naranāthasuta*

nahan iki donkw-ataṅguḥ i putuṅku rikaŋ sakarĕŋ,
kita manĕkāna śatru paraduṙllabha yan kawaśa,
apituwi jīwitanta ya ta wiṣṭi kasambya mĕne,
tĕhĕṙ ika yan kabhāwa tĕmahanya kasiḥta hilaŋ*

hana kalĕhĕṅta mantuka mareŋ nrĕpa krĕṣṇa muwaḥ,
awaraha yan tĕlas kita rumakṣa mahāṙṣi kabeḥ,
mwaŋ i papasaḥta saŋ narapati iki wĕkasnya jĕmaḥ,
ubhayakĕna iki kāsiḥ i putuṅku mĕne malapa*

pituhu wuwusku potraka waluy juga haywa wihaŋ,
kita guṇamanta śakti lituhayw-anurāga dahat,
ahata kita iŋ awak payuṅa don rasika iŋ bhuwana,
saphala paṅöbana amuhara tuṣṭa niraŋ sujana*

nahan ika śabda saŋ rĕṣi mataṅguḥ akon maluya,
tĕlas apatĕḥ narendrasuta sādhu tutūt winaraḥ,
ndatan awĕdi iŋ musuḥ sira nimitta nira amituhu,
pinakapajātyan iŋ kadi sira aharĕp iŋ wibhawa*

ri waluy ira iŋ hawan rika ta mogha rĕmĕŋ sumaput,
katĕmu tilottamā ri hiriŋ iŋ giripāṙśśwa muwaḥ,
nrĕpasuta sāmba śīghra tumurun saka riŋ śakaṭa,
miṅĕl aṅusap mata anaṅisakĕn lara niŋ mapasaḥ*

ra kaka tilottama apa ta pakoṣadha ni ṅwaŋ akūŋ,
kani-ni hatiṅku tan pahuwusan kakĕnan turida,
karaṇa hinambilan sĕḍĕŋ i siḥku n aṅaṙwwani kūŋ,
tuluŋ aku yan kakiṅkiṅan i rūm saŋ aniṅgalakĕn*

prawala ni sihny-arinta karikā ḍatĕŋ aṅranĕhi,
labuḥ i laṅö karĕŋrĕŋan unĕŋ ṅwaŋ udan siwuhĕn,
lagi kahañut ṅwaŋ iŋ lulut aṅĕntasi wāḥ turida,
aku kawahan drĕs iŋ lara lumaṅhuy i saŋ tĕkasiḥ*

kaka pu tilottama apa ta wĕkas ni yarinta lĕlĕḥ,
ri sĕḍĕŋ ika inalap niŋ iña duṙyyaśa tan wriŋ asiḥ,
niyata pasambatanya ri tĕkāṅkw-amara anuluṅa,
luwaṙ i tayaṅkw-anūt ripu nimitta nika n kawaśa*

aṅawaśa kūṅku tan patahĕnan linipuṙ-lipuran,
bari-bari kapwa ya amituturi ṅwaŋ aweḥ kalaṅön,
sahana-hana iŋ wukiṙ kadi maha amuṅu citta rimaŋ,
taru kusuma agawe ry-unĕŋ iŋ onĕŋ i rūm saŋ arūm*

Āḥ dyaḥ saŋ maṇik iŋ ahayu hinayu-hayu niŋ ahayu hananta aśrī,
rūpanta ahyas anawaŋ asana nisana nagara sanagarī raṅsī,
rūm niŋ kāṙttika piniturun iŋ atanu karika rari rarasta aṅrĕs,

<nawahaṙṣa>:35.

lipurĕnta laraṅku bĕsuṙ aku linaṅwakĕn iŋ prihati,
siwuhĕn riŋ aniṅgali turida dinohan i kāsiḥ ikā,
rinasaṅkw-i ñamut-ñamut aṅuyaṅi ŋ ambĕk iŋ onĕŋ akūŋ,

<basantatilaka>:36.
– – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏓ = 14

mantuk ta saŋ nrĕpatiputra sakeŋ himādri,
moliḥ wiyoga lara niŋ mapasaḥ paḍa asiḥ,
śoka prapañca matawan-tawan iŋ lara unĕŋ,
lāgy-a aṅĕsaḥ mulati mambĕt i sinwam iŋ jriŋ*

tan  ṙyyamban iŋ hawan aniṅhali deśa rāmya,
maṅkin maṅö sira tumon iŋ aśoka mĕmbaŋ,
tañjuŋ mĕnuṙ surabhi campaka puṣpa maṅjraḥ,
lwiṙ gandha niŋ gĕluŋ aṅimbuhi kūŋ niŋ onĕŋ*

paṇḍan lĕṅöŋ ri tĕpi niŋ padamāṙgga mĕmbaŋ,
lumrā hrĕbuknya siniriṙ niŋ aṅin tan adrĕs,
moghanya kāmpiṙ iy awak naranāthaputra,
himpĕṙ pupuṙ tumulaṙ aṙjja katon ri bāhu*

tan waṙṇnanĕn lawas ira iŋ wanadeśamāṙgga,
sāmpun tĕka iŋ nagara śīghra sira n tama i jro,
kañcit narendra hana jāmbawatī pwa saṇḍiŋ,
maṅlālana iry-unĕŋ ira i nrĕpaputra sāmba*

prāpta pwa sāmba magiraŋ sira kaṙwwa mojar,
om om tuhanku laki liŋ nira yan sinĕmbaḥ,
atyanta tuṣṭa nira jāmbawatī prahaṙṣa,
ry-antuk panuṅsuṅan ira i naranāthaputra*

saśrī narendra sira sambhrama riŋ swacitta,
ry-ākāra saŋ nrĕpatiputra wiyogaduhkha,
lāwan tikaŋ jaja nakhāṅkita manda-manda,
towin samaṙ kajuruhan ragĕt iŋ kĕna iŋ hrū*

<indrabajra>:37.
– – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏓ = 11

saŋ śrī narāṙyya ata pacĕḥ kapūhan,
de saŋ suputra alara rāga māśa,
nāhan tikā hetu nira n patakwan,
ṅkā liŋ nira n tiṅhali dāruki ikā*

mojaṙ tikānaŋ tinañan tan adwā,
byakta agriŋ onĕŋ naranāthaputra,
sambandha rānak naranātha mastrī,
kanyā praśasta hayu rājaputrī*

wwantĕn surastrī jaruman suputrī,
ya ikā n umundaŋ nrĕpaputra ṅūni,
śīghra n lumampaḥ maṅĕnĕs paḍa anis,
prāpta iŋ pura añidra silib nikaŋ wwaŋ*

wwantĕn taman saŋ kṣitija atirāmya,
kanyāpuri ikī panĕlaḥnya waṙtta,
ndā ṅkā ta rānak haji yan papaṅgiḥ,
lāwan siraŋ yajñawatī paḍa asiḥ*

nora ikihĕn saṅśaya niŋ swacitta,
Āpan tĕlas kālahan iŋ swaśatru,
sakweḥ mahaṙṣi iŋ himawanta tuṣṭa,
nā hetu rānak nrĕpati pwa ṅīccha*

tapwan salek ṅūni sira n papaṅgiḥ,
mogha n dine niŋ widhi duhkharāga,
saŋ nāthaputra n tinĕkan sira iŋ praŋ,
wuntat nira apraŋ hinalap suputrī*

prāgjyotiṣeka n pamawan suputrī,
yekā n linakwan tumuluy tĕkā ṅkā,
kañcit pwa saŋ nārada ṅūny-ataṅguḥ,
nā hetu rānak nrĕpati iki mantuk*

na ujaṙ ni dāruky-awaraḥ prayatna,
saŋ nātha kāścaṙyya manaḥ sahaṙṣa,
len krodhabahni i hati saŋ narendra,
muntab murub winwaṅan iŋ swaśatru*

agyā mijil saŋ naranātha krĕṣṇa,
ṅkāna iŋ sudhaṙmmā sira yañ cumuṇḍuk,
sakweḥ nikaŋ wīra kabeḥ manaṅkil,
astām tikā saŋ yaduwīra-wrĕṣṇi*

sāmantarāja atata nora kantun,
kapwa atata atūt krama riŋ paliṅgiḥ,
Āpan sira śrī baladewa mukhya,
saṅgwan lawan saŋ naranātha krĕṣṇa*

kañcit ḍatĕŋ citraratha iŋ narendra,
gandhaṙwwarāja ika wiriñciputra,
sāmpun maliṅgiḥ pwa riŋ āsana aṙjja,
sākṣāt bhaṭāra indra halĕp nira hyaŋ*

saŋ nātha maswāgata śīghra maṅliŋ,
bhāgyā karun sanmata saŋ paṅĕmpwan,
māra anumoda aṅlawad iŋ kadi ṅwaŋ,
dhaṙmmādhikārāṇa maweḥ sukha agöŋ*

maṅke tĕkanta iŋ yaduwīrasaṅgha,
aṅde prahaṙṣa amuwuhi i kasiṅhan,
siṅhākrĕtinta iŋ raṇa hetu tan lyan,
Āpan swabhāwanta tinūt ikaŋ rāt*

śāstrajña wedajña kita adhikāra,
tatwajña sampūṙṇna krĕtopadeśa,
lāwan wiśeṣanta riŋ indraloka,
gandhaṙwwarājā kita yukti pūjān*

prāptanta ri ṅwaŋ yadu śuddhabuddhi,
kāweśa de niŋ guṇamātra māmbĕk,
siṅgiḥ kita aṅde sĕkaṙ iŋ twas i ṅwaŋ,
himpĕṙ wulan mwaŋ kumuda amaṅun śrī*

yapwan pirak mās maṇirājya yogya,
meman mare saŋ krĕta yan kapaṅgiḥ,
aṅhiŋ taŋ ewĕḥ rikanaŋ dadi wwaŋ,
tan len katĕmwanta wiśiṣṭasādhu*

nā liŋ nira n saŋ prabhu padmanābha,
gandhaṙwwarāja n sumahuṙ widagdha,
ḍo wastu sambhāwana de narendra,
yā na ujaṙ i ṅwaŋ wiguṇa alpakāya*

atyanta maṅde sukha niŋ kadi ṅwaŋ,
sojaṙ mahārāja waraprasāda,
lwiṙ teja niŋ sītakara awa pūṙṇna,
rāmya n paweḥ tuṣṭa magöŋ rika iŋ rāt*

sākṣāt narendra amaralokanātha,
Āpan samitra pwa lawan hyaŋ indra,
sambandha saŋ hyaŋ śatayajña motus,
maṅke ṅhulun yan tumama i narendra*

tan len aminta aśraya don surendra,
ri śrī mahārāja juga amalaṙ siḥ,
Āpan tĕlas kabwatan iŋ raṇāṅga,
apraŋ lawan saŋ naraka anĕkāni*

sakweḥ nikaŋ hyaŋ paḍa tan pasāra,
saṅkĕp sira iŋ sañjata wāhanādi,
nora aṅgarit riŋ musuḥ aṅgakāra,
luṅhā lumiṅsiṙ tinĕkān paḍa arĕs*

Ꜽrāwaṇā wāhana saŋ hyaŋ indra,
mātaṅga śūra iŋ raṇa lāgi-lāgi,
maṅke n lagī wāhana saŋ mahīja,
tan sāra ta n pānulalay rika iŋ praŋ*

bajra adhikārāstra nira iŋ mahendra,
atyanta riŋ kās kadi hīrabajra,
mogha ika māpĕs maṅĕne mahīja,
leśyanya n unduṙ ya wajanya tĕmpak*

hyaŋ śakra sakrodha ri saŋ mahīja,
yeka an tumandaŋ capala amrĕp asriŋ,
kedĕṙ sira agriŋ winalĕs kalĕṅhĕr,
sewu mata wyaṙtha pĕtĕŋ panonya*

śīghra hyaŋ agny-a apuliḥ iŋ hyaŋ indra,
prodbhūta mumbul saha dhūmaketu,
kapwa aṅasut saŋ kṣitija iŋ raṇāṅga,
heman paḍĕm swaŋ kabalik tinisnya*

maṅkā sira hyaŋ yama kaṙwwa ḍaṇḍa,
madwandwa lāwan kṣitija aṅadu kral,
saŋ hyaŋ yama aḍaṇḍa ri bhūmiputra,
ṅkā ŋ ḍaṇḍa wibhrāmya katon kawaṅsul*

saŋ hyaŋ nirity-a atahĕn iŋ kamantyan,
rodra aṅagĕm riŋ muśalāstra hīra,
pakṣa akral aṅhalwakĕna iŋ mahīja,
wahw-a aṅayat yaṙ kabalik ginantaŋ*

sotan sira hyaŋ baruṇa alaḥ aṅrĕs,

iti maṅkana ata pawaraḥ saŋ uddhawa,
ri siraŋ nareśwara wawaŋ sira n sahur,
tuhu tan kasaṅśayakĕnanta maṅkata,
ika saŋ watĕk yadu sayogya maṅkata*

niśaṭha ulmuka adi nikanaŋ lumampaha,
kalawan ta satyaka si sāmba śāraṇa,
irikaŋ tigaŋ wĕṅi wĕkas ya maṅkata,
saha kośa wāhana padāti saṅgĕpan*

ri tĕlas narendra maṅutus lumampaha,
umuliḥ sira iŋ pura huwus tĕka i dalĕm,
para taṇḍa rakryan umuliḥ sakeŋ sabhā,
ṅuniweḥ watĕk ratu kabeḥ samāṅjuru*

sira saŋ sĕḍĕŋ winidhi maṅkata alaga,

kadi siṅha niṙbhaya muliḥ sakeŋ sabhā*

i ḍatĕŋ nira iŋ kuwu nira n kasowaṅan,

juru-jurw-adandan ahutaŋ-hutaŋ waneḥ,

aṅalap tareki milu piŋ pitu umidĕr,
aṅĕliḥ mutaḥ tahi kaṅelan aṅdĕlĕg*

inalap nikā raṅin ika asrama iŋ lĕbuḥ,

amupuḥ rabinya sahasa agawe pirak*

ajuruḥ manis ni liriŋ iŋ mata amanis,

waliwis hana iriya maha aṅisis hĕlar*

para rājaputra haliwat sakeŋ nadī,
giripāṙśśwa kīṙṇna kahawan tĕkap nira,
riŋ abhīruthāni kahalintaṅan huwus,
ri tĕlasnya wiṣṭi ya paṅĕntal-ĕntalan*

iŋ marustanī tĕgal adoḥ kuraŋ bañu,
ya ta kāmbaḥ awyaŋ ikanaŋ dukut lĕpas,
kumukus lĕbūnya dumudug tĕka iŋ laṅit,
kadi ta aṅusiṙ bañu mareŋ payodhara*

i kurapradeśa kahawan kathañcana,
hana jahnawī lwaḥ ika saṅka riŋ laṅit,
śuci niṙmmala atiśaya tis nika adalĕm,
alaṅö tĕpinya hibĕkan sĕkaṙ miṅiŋ*

sira saŋ watĕk yadu sahaṙṣa lālana,
kalaṅön linolyan i sagandha niŋ sĕkar,
sukha de ni hīs ni sirat iŋ  ṙyyak ombakan,
sahaja amrĕta arasana tis nikaŋ haṅin*

tumurun matīṙtha sira saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
lara ṅel ṅĕliḥ nira hilaŋ samāntara,
pariśuddha citta nira niṙmmala abuṅaḥ,
pinakaswabhāwa saŋ atīṙtha riŋ śuci*

ri tĕlas nira adyus irika alaris muwaḥ,
irikaŋ halas ri tĕpi niŋ mahānadī,
makiris tikaŋ tahĕn arok lawan latā,
lwiṙ awāhwa-wāhwan ulaḥ an siliḥ-kayuḥ*

mrak i tuṅgak iŋ kayu manis manuṅgilis,
alaṅö tĕkap ni kĕlab iŋ dhwaja akilat,
maṅigĕl ḍĕṅö paḍahi saŋ watĕk yadu,
wĕkasan manawwaŋ irikā lwiṙ ambahan*

tumayuŋ tikaŋ liraŋ i piṅgiṙ iŋ juraŋ,
mabĕbĕd gaḍuŋ kapaṅĕliḥ tiniṅhalan,
apuji n pĕtuŋ yaya pinaṇḍi riŋ halas,
kadi tan wruhĕn rahayu kabwatan raras*

maṅunĕŋ wuṅū ta n alayū nya kāsihan,
hanamun kabeḥnya paḍa tan hana asĕkar,
i karinya ṅūni n inatīta niŋ laṅö,
karaṇanya hewa mari ta asuhun sĕkar*

ry-uttarakośala iki kahawan tĕkap yadukula,
rāmya nika apitowi saha bhāwabhoga sulabhā,
wwaŋ nika daṙśśanīya paḍa sahya suśrama katon,
rāmya sabhā pĕkĕnya malĕbā lĕbuḥnya matĕpas*

mwaŋ ri sawaḥnya rāmya mahijo bañunya tan arĕn,
ṭok uni niŋ taluktak alaṅö lana amuhara kūŋ,
wwaŋ ri waruŋ-waruŋnya maṅiduŋ makaṅsi kukulan,
riŋ talunanya taŋ kidaŋ anĕmpu-nĕmpuhi tahĕn*

kubwan ika ajawā hana jaguŋ mahā n sinalisir,
kaṇḍuyuhan pacaṙnya sulasiḥnya mĕmbaŋ anĕḍĕŋ,
tyuŋ wakatalnya len karawilanya mawwaḥ asigar,
lwiṙnya maweḥ sukha aṅinaki citta saŋ yadu kabeḥ*

lwaḥ sarayū kapaṅgiḥ adalĕm bañunya mahĕniŋ,
sāmpun inĕntasan ya parituṣṭa taŋ bala kabeḥ,
yapwan anekawiṣṭi nika hetu niŋ wwaŋ awĕdi,
lwiṙ manaḥ iŋ durātma kahananya mogha n ahiheŋ*

jro ni latĕknya lāgi paran iŋ warak yan aguyaŋ,
gaṅgĕŋ ikā n katūt ri suku niŋ kĕbo wana maköm,
laṅliŋ ikā hana i sihuŋ ikaŋ warāha makipū,
mwaŋ kalamĕñja guṇḍa karawit rikaŋ rwi lĕmahĕn*

tañ caritan kulĕm ya makula iŋ hawan sira huwus,
doḥ ni paran kunaŋ pira-pira ŋ purī ya kahawan,
tan wuwusĕn tikaŋ gunuŋ alas tĕgal-tĕgal agal,
rāmya nikaŋ hĕnū tan ucapĕn sakambaḥ alaṅö*

riŋ wĕkasan katon ta pucak iŋ himālayagiri,
kaywan ika ahawūk ry-alas-alasnya de nikaŋ ĕbun,
ṅkāna ta saŋ watĕk yadu maṅañjali i sĕkaṙ urā,
kapwa ri jöŋ bhaṭāra puruṣottama atwaŋ ararĕm*

pāṙśśwa nikaŋ himādri hana ta lwaḥ ūtagahana,
kokta ṅaranya ya uṅgwan ira keśawa an sĕḍĕŋ aköm,
śuddha pawitra tūs niŋ acala pwa niṙmmala atīs,
tūban ikā lĕṅöŋ tumĕḍun iŋ paraŋ paruŋ aroŋ*

prāpta-ta saŋ watĕk yadu rikaŋ himālayagiri,
rāmya marāṙyya-rāṙyyan irikaŋ śilā kumalasa,
haṙṣa tumiṅhal iŋ sĕkaṙ aneka tan palĕwasan,
gaṙjjita yan sinuṅsuŋ iŋ aṅin mawoṙ hrĕbuk arūm*

sāmpun ira n marāṙyyan arahup ta ya n laku muwaḥ,
śīghra sira aṅaloṙ i suku niŋ himālayagiri,
maṅkin awās pradeśa nikanaŋ musuḥ tĕkap ira,
tulya payodhara ika pakatiṇḍu-tiṇḍu kakare*

duṙgga nikaŋ musuḥ ya katĕkan tĕkap yadubala,
sakṣaṇa tan pahīṅan i sukĕt wukiṙnya maruhur,
priṅga nikaŋ juraŋ pinakalālanā nikaŋ alas,
nista nikā n wiśīṙṇna yan inambaḥ iŋ kuda liman*

duṙbala taŋ pradeśa kahawan tĕkapyadukula,
paṙwwata maṅlunaŋ hadĕg ikaŋ kayunya mananā,
lwaḥnya juraŋnya sāmpun aratā lawan tĕgal arok,
asru tikaŋ lĕbū mĕtu tinūb nikaŋ haliwawar*

piṅgiṙ ikaŋ samudra hana paṙwwata aruhuṙ agöŋ,
kīṙṇna tikāŋ aśoka surabhi iriya anĕḍĕŋ atöb,
heman i sinwam iŋ kayu hibĕk lĕbū tan inalap,
de nira saŋ watĕk yadukula apan aprĕgi sira*

riŋ tadanantara krama ḍatĕŋ ta saŋ yadu kabeḥ,
wanwa nikaŋ musuḥ paḍa wuruŋ ya siŋ sakatĕmu,
nyāpan ika aṅhilī wwaŋ ika nāgata iŋ yadukula,
drĕwya katiṅgal iŋ lĕbuḥ aneka tan kahuniṅa*

kāla niraŋ watĕk yadu ḍatĕŋ hyaŋ aṙkka makucĕm,
meḥ tumibā pitu pwa mabhawaḥ ta saŋ yadu kabeḥ,
yatna sira aṅĕmit sabala tan wineḥ mapasaha,
bañcana niŋ musuḥ ya tinahā mamoṙ aṅimura*

thāni katiṅgal adbhuta halĕpnya towi n alaṅö,
mwaŋ parimaṇḍalanya pira yojananya ta kunaŋ,
ya ika pakuwwa-kuwwan ira saŋ watĕk yadu kabeḥ,
lwiṙ siluman kaḍatwan ikahĕn gatinya wĕkasan*

wrĕtta niraŋ watĕk yadu ḍatĕŋ prakāśa karĕṅö,
strī rikanaŋ kuṭa ika paḍa maṅrĕṅö kakĕtĕran,
pāḥ prihatin ri tan hana nikaŋ sĕnĕŋnya manukū,
sambat ika anaṅis lawan anaknya māsiḥ-asihan*

Āḥ anak i ṅhulun ndi ta parāna niŋ masusupan,
towi bapanta tan hana mapa ulahaṅkwa tanaku,
henaka ta ṅhulun pĕjaha saṅka riŋ kahañaṅa,
ṅhiŋ śawa ni ṅhulun tĕmun ikaŋ bapanta n umuliḥ*

mwaŋ paricārikā hana sukhanya duhkha sawaneḥ,
kahyun ikaŋ waneḥ tawanĕn iŋ prawīra lalita,
kelik ikaŋ waneḥ dadaha niŋ brata aywa mahala,
meman awaknya liŋnya ṅuniweḥ yadin kahamiṣa*

aṅgĕḥ ikaŋ bala akĕmit i rājya saŋ kṣitisuta,
kepwan ataṅgu-taṅguḥ anatā walaŋ-walaŋ adoḥ,
len ikanaŋ mamet kira-kira apupul-pupul ahöm,
tan wruḥ i dāya niŋ lumawana ŋ watĕk yadu ḍatĕŋ*

saŋ nrĕpaputrikā sira ta maṅrĕṅö yadu ḍatĕŋ,
tuṣṭa manaḥ nira n milu saŋ āṙyya sāmba marike,
tan huniṅan ri pawrĕg ikanaŋ wwaŋ iŋ kuṭa kabeḥ,
ṅhiŋ ta tilottamā pinakarowaŋ iŋ maguṇita*

hetu nira n pakona lulut iŋ priyā nira tĕmĕn,
puṣpawatī ṅaranya yatika inutus jarumana,
wruḥ sawuwus prahāsana pĕnĕd riŋ ambĕk aradin,
apsaraputrikā gati ni saṅhulun surawadhū*

tanmaya na anilib wwaŋ asĕluṙ tĕlas layat adoḥ,
riŋ gagana ikihĕn hawan ikā ndatan kasuwayan,
saŋ nrĕpaputra sāmba kadunuŋ katanduk alaris,
śīghra tĕka iŋ lĕmaḥ tĕka manĕmbaḥ iŋ nrĕpasuta*

nihan ta bapa hetu ni ṅhulun anĕmbaḥ inutus anĕkākĕna ŋ karas,

tuwin rari wiyoga ṅūni papasaḥta laki sira turuŋ kĕna iŋ turū,

ikaŋ gagana manda wintaŋ ika maṅkin awuwuḥ awuwuṙ tiniṅhalan,

samaṅkana ta saŋ watĕk yadubala amwaŋ apuy i surup iŋ niśākara,

ikaŋ lalayan adbhuta ikanaŋ anak niŋ acala himawān inadwakĕn*

dhwasta ŋ śūla tikĕl kĕna tinuju*

krodha ikaŋ muraputra ri niśaṭha,
kapwa anambuti pāśa nika masö,
yeka n sep tinugĕl tali nikahĕn,
kānin kapwa gulūnya kĕna panaḥ*

wwaŋ sānaknya waneḥ sĕḍĕŋ apuliḥ,
dhīra asĕṅhit i saŋ niśaṭha kabeḥ,
makrak sāhasa kapwa mawa tĕwĕk,
pakṣanya uliha kaṙṣanatanaya*

ambĕknya apraṅa mogha rinuhunan,
bāhunya i tĕṅĕnan pĕgat apasaḥ,
anyāt dꜽtya tugĕl ri wĕtĕŋ ikā,
deniŋ hrū niraŋ ulmuka tan arĕn*

hĕnti ikaŋ hana riŋ kṣiti pinanaḥ,
de saŋ satyaka sāmba sira n amūk,
wadwā niŋ mura śīṙṇna mati matap,
syuḥ mwaŋ wāhana riŋ raṇa magĕlar*

tandaŋ niŋ mura riŋ nrĕpatanaya,
göŋ krodhanya mĕlĕg ri liman ikā,
ambĕknya uliha saŋ nrĕpatisuta,
pāśāstranya-ya ta akilat awilĕt*

paṅheṙ koŋ rĕbi liŋnya wahu mayat,
sep tĕṅgĕknya cinakra kapisanan,
mātaṅganya punaḥ ya kinurubut,
pat pādanya pĕgat kĕna pinanaḥ*

māti pwa ŋ mura māwrĕg asasaran,
ṅkā taŋ dꜽtyabala awĕdi malayū,
māwrī taŋ hana riŋ gaganatala,
luṅha amet parananya lĕṅit adoḥ*

kālanya alaḥ ikāŋ asura murud,
paṅheṙ liŋnya nĕhĕṙ milu malayū,
ṅkā hrūnya ika tibā tan inulatan,
akweḥ dꜽtya jurunya mati kĕna*

konduṙ mūṙ aṅusiṙ kuṭa ya tinūt,
len ṅĕs-ṅösĕn amet lĕkas apuliḥ,
ndātan sāra kĕna iŋ panaḥ akĕdal,
luṅha arĕs ya kabeḥ layat alayū*

awrĕg taŋ sakuṭa awurahan awū,
towin ṅ-ānala ya inapuy umurub,
muntab kadbhuta tulya gunuŋ apuy,
lumrā ŋ dhūma sawaŋ tahĕn aṅadĕg*

sāmpun śīṙṇna tikaŋ kuṭa katunu,
akweḥ strī kabĕnĕm saha tanaya,
kanya akweḥ katawan hana dinudut,
kasyāsiḥ kumĕtĕṙ tĕhĕṙ anaṅis*

yan bwat saŋ yadu tan hana manawan,
yāwat strī laraṅan hinaliwatan,
Āpan tulya bibi ika hiḍĕp ikā,
göŋ-göṅĕn ri kasādhun ira juga*

Āsiŋ drĕwya haneŋ pura niyata,
mās ratnādi tĕlas larut inalap,
wadwā saŋ yaduwīra paḍa sarat,
de niŋ kweḥnya tikaŋ jara-jarahan*

wwantĕn ta anĕmu puṇḍutan agiraŋ,
pindĕk wiṅkiṙ isinya kacaŋ irĕŋ,
maṙmmanya n rinubuŋ ginuyu-guyu,
yā liŋnya n sinurak malĕs anurak*

saŋ nāthātmaja sāmba sira ḍatĕŋ,
mwaŋ wadwā nira sāyudha maṅiriŋ,
riŋ kanyābhawana iki paran ira,
agyā yan mulata i ŋ nrĕpaduhitā*

prāpta iŋ jro nagarī nrĕpatanaya,
tan wwantĕn sira saŋ nrĕpaduhitā,
kepwan teka manaḥ nira kumĕtĕr,
de niŋ siḥ marikā bara tinahā*

ṅkāna iŋ raṅkaŋ ĕmās ta paran ira,
uṅgwan yajñawati ika lagi-lagi,
mogha pwa n taya saŋ nrĕpaduhitā,
ya aṅde saṅśaya saŋ nrĕpatanaya*

nāhan liŋ nira yan panaha-nahā,
yan mātya iki sira ikana kalalaḥ,
nyāma nya ika katĕmwa śawa nira,
ṅke riŋ ratnapalaṅka rurubana*

yadyastun rasikā wruha ri wuwus,
byakta anuṅsuṅa liṅku tan asuwe,
maṅke tan hana ta ikihĕn awaraḥ,
hetuṅkwa apĕga tan wruḥ iŋ ulaha*

nāhan liŋ nira saŋ nrĕpatanaya,
prāptā puṣpawatī manuduhakĕn,
ry-uṅgwan yajñawatī yan asusupan,
saŋ sāmba ika sira agiraŋ umara*

ṅkā saŋ yajñawatī katĕmu lume,
muṅgwiŋ paṅkwan iraŋ surawanitā,
śoka aśā humiḍĕp nrĕpatanaya,
heṙ-herĕn mrĕmakĕn ri lara nira*

śīghra aṅliŋ tika saŋ suraduhitā,
haṙṣa anantwa ri saŋ nrĕpatisuta,
śabda awoṙ panaṅisnya ya ta giraŋ,
kagyat yajñawatī wawaŋ amĕkul*

luḥ saŋ yajñawatī tĕhĕṙ umilī,
kadya aswāgata riŋ nrĕpatanaya,
wruḥ saŋ sāmba mamakpak aṅusapi,
maṙmma ahĕmban i saŋ nrĕpaduhitā*

sāmpun yajñawatī sira hinalap,
akweḥ ceṭi tumūt milu katawan,
agyā mantuka sāmba tĕka ri heŋ,
ndan ri swaṙgga paran suraduhitā*

mantuk saŋ yadu śīghra tan akaḍat,
sakweḥ niŋ bala tuṣṭa wija-wijaḥ,
ramya atūt suku niŋ wukiṙ alaṅö,
piṅgiṙ niŋ pasiṙ aṙjja linihatan*

kāry-a adoḥ tikanaŋ pura wĕkasan,
tapwan māri kukusnya winulatan,
lwiṙ hyaŋ niŋ nagara aṅadĕg aṅure,
śoka aśa akilayū ri yadukula*

<widyutkara>:44.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏓ = 25

poṙyyaŋ garyaŋ araŋ kayunya wilutan pilaŋ anakan arok lawan kutu-kutu,
śuṣka adoḥ bañu tūt hawanya karikil gumaway i lĕsu niŋ watĕk yadubala,
saŋ hyaŋ we tumiliŋ sĕḍĕŋ panas ira aṅhuyaṅi riŋ ayunan dinohan iŋ aṅin,
mātra ŋ rĕm humalintaŋ aṅhĕla-hĕla wruḥ apuji riŋ atūt gĕgĕṙ halibabĕn*

lampaḥ niŋ gajawāhana aṙddha makaḍat kaṅĕlihan iki luhya tan pawĕlĕgan,
de niŋ bwat nikanaŋ maṇik jarahan iŋ ripu winawan ikā ri rĕṅga nikahĕn,
len taŋ syandana kabwatan rajata kañcana karaṇa nikā n malon tan asarag,
göŋ līlā n paduluṙ-duluṙ hanan apet hawan anusu-nusuṙ maha anasa-nasar*

ambĕk saŋ para rājaputra hana monĕŋ i kuwu nira hetu niŋ parigĕlis,
sotanya alawas iŋ paran kapana yan tan aṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn iŋ priyā mabuhaya,
tapwan saḥ kadi wimba muṅgu ri manaḥ nira saŋ ahayu kāri riŋ pakasutan,
söŋ-söŋ haṙṣa nira i saŋ adyaḥ ira tan winawa-wawa nira ahañaŋ sĕḍĕŋ arūm*

ṅkāna i saṇḍiŋ ikaŋ gunuŋ ri magadha iki kahawan atiduṙgga-duṙgga mabhaya,
khyāti iŋ rāt jarasandha saŋ prabhu rikā musuḥ ira naranātha krĕṣṇa malawas,
hetunya n paḍa yatna saŋ yadu kabeḥ rahina wĕṅi lumampaḥ iŋ tĕgal alas,
yodhā tan hana lālana aṅinak-inak lumaku parigĕlis tĕhĕṙ maṅalawaŋ*

sāmpun rātri tĕkā ŋ pĕtĕŋnya sumahab ri sahana nikanaŋ pradeśa kahawan,
Āstām taŋ turaga alapa alara kaṅelan apituwi kuraŋ turū ya maṅalas,
hetunya an ajĕjĕṙ ta lampaḥ ikanaŋ bala kaṅĕlihan epu luhya wĕkasan,
maṅlampw-a aṅadipīra maṅrĕrĕba ta ṅwaŋ ujaṙ ika paḍa aṅucap makulĕma*

hetunya n pakulĕm paḍa iki maturū satĕka-tĕka nikā ndatan pawulatan,
salwā niŋ palapat hibĕk tĕkap ikaŋ bala ṅuni-ṅuni damyan iŋ sawaḥ asat,
mātaṅganya lawan kudanya yatika atri mawurahan agĕnturan ywa karĕṅö,
Āpan lwiṙ jalada anurun saha riwutnya dinuluṙ i gĕlapnya tan papĕgatan*

indrābajra lan upendrābajra 
<upastitha>:45.
⏓ – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏓ = 11

byatīta māmrĕm yadu-wrĕṣṇiwīra,
rikā ta saŋ śrī jarasandha kojar,
sakrodha takwa iŋ yadu-wrĕṣṇiwīra,
swabhāwa niŋ duṣṭa kaṭuṅkabuddhi*

saṅkĕp huwus mwaŋ bala duṣṭacitta,
aṅāhalas pakṣa ṅulā hijo ya,
wadwā nika aneka padāti makweḥ,
wĕḍuŋ pamūk mwaŋ kuḍuwak sikĕpnya*

lukan pwa yan tan mĕjaha i musuḥnya,
hetunya n otus ri kudanya luṅhā,
wawaŋ maluy dūta nika atiśīghra,
i paṅhinĕp saŋ yadu-wrĕṣṇiwīra*

ṅkā maṅkat aśrī jarasandha maglis,
lawan balanya ika watĕk durātmā,
sāmpun ḍatĕŋ lampaḥ ika iŋ alas göŋ,
ndātan hana aśabda kabeḥ śinikṣan*

tan maṙmma sowe magadheśwara ṅkā,
tuṣṭa ika yan ton yaduyodha māmrĕm,
rikā n tumandaŋ tumuluy sakeŋ doḥ,
tĕka aṅgalaḥ len manĕwĕk mamöki*

māwrĕg ta mabyūran ikaŋ watĕk praŋ,
ti ibrāharip yan tinĕwĕk maṅantuk,
akweḥ maṅohan tinujaḥ śinūla,
lawan kĕna iŋ duk wulaṅun kinonta*

wogan kacuṇḍuk nrĕpaputra sāmba,
wadwā nira awrĕg tinĕwök an āwū,
wawaŋ si dāruky-awuṅū prayatna,
maṅaṅgal-aṅgal makuyap matanya*

wawaŋ maṅambil ri kudanya śīghra,
adan pasaŋ ya agul-agul prayatna,
pinraŋ pwa yan duṙbala liŋnya kagyat,
lumumpat amriḥ sumusup mareŋ rwi*

rikā pwa saŋ sāmba wawaŋ mataṅhi,
tĕhĕṙ sira agya anusupa iŋ alas göŋ,
yeka apasaŋ syandana sāmpun eṅgal,
śīghra n panuṅgaŋ saha nāthaputrī*

dewī sira arĕs kumĕtĕg tikaŋ twas,
tan saḥ mĕkul saŋ nrĕpaputra sāmba,
tĕhĕṙ sumuṅkĕm sira pūḥ kawĕswös,
gupe kalĕswan humĕnĕŋ sināntwa*

saŋ sāmba kepwan pinĕkul sudewī,
tĕhĕṙ sira agĕgwan apus niŋ aśwa,
kewran sira i tan hana niŋ wwaŋ amrĕg,
na hetu niŋ tan kawĕnaŋ mayodha*

tandaŋ nikā saŋ jarasandha śīghra,
manuṅgaŋ iŋ sāmaja tan tahĕn twas,
wadwā nira akweḥ ya maṅambuli ṅkā,
maṅduk ta ya iŋ tomara len triśūla*

samaṅkana ikā nrĕpaputra sāmba,
tañ jriḥ winūk de magadheśwara anūt,
sakrodha teka awak ira n kĕna iŋ hrū,
atyanta riŋ lāghawa suśrama iŋ praŋ*

saṅka gĕlisnya ika dumuk lipuŋnya,
lāwan panaḥnya atiśaya adrĕs akweḥ,
kĕna ika hastā nrĕpaputra denya,
prāyanya moliḥ ta maṅambuli ṅkā*

sāmpun kanin hasta narendraputra,
alwaŋ tika ambĕk nira saṅśaya arĕs,
hetunya ya aṅgĕgwani hasta śīghra,
muñcaṙ tikaŋ rāḥ sumirat ri dewī*

glāna pwa saŋ sāmba kanin kĕna iŋ hrū,
samaṅkana ikaŋ kuda yan palaywan,
ri tan wĕnaŋ saŋ nrĕpaputra maṅhrĕt,
ya kāraṇanya n saparanya luṅhā*

prāpta irikaŋ uttarakola sāmpun,
manūt hawan hetu nikā n matanduk,
eñjiŋ pwa mūlanya tĕka iŋ tĕṅaḥ ṅwe,
nĕhĕṙ tan ora iki mameta pāda*

ikaŋ ratha atyanta lakunya mādrĕs,
ikeŋ alas duṙgga maluṅka-luṅka,
ṅkā ta n katĕṅhān kahiriŋ ya kaṇḍĕg,
tuṅgal cucul cakra nika n kasiṅsal*

ndan saŋ narendrātmaja tībra mūṙccha,
tibā lawan saŋ naranāthaputrī,
ṅkāna iŋ hawan duṙgga panas lĕbūnya,
umrĕm paḍa aṅliḥ sira kāsihan ta*

dewī kamantyan mabaṅun wimūṙccha,
musap narendrātmaja śokacitta,
hanan pamakpak manaṅis masambat,
kaka aku toliḥ ṅwaŋ ujaṙ sudewī*

<udgatawisama>:46.
⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 20

⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏓ = 13

ri pasambat-sambat ira saŋ narawaraduhita aswara apĕyĕḥ,
Āḥ kaka lihat iy arinta tuhan,
kasihan ṅhulun kawĕkasa iŋ alas bhaya*

kaka t-aṅliliṙ t-usapi luḥku pahayu gĕluŋ i ṅhulun lukar,
ḍū humĕnĕŋ iki kita amrĕm alök,
t-aṅucap tuhanku sahuri pwa ta ṅhulun*

ndi culuḥta ṅūni n aṅisapwakĕn aṅarĕki yan paweḥ sĕpaḥ,
siḥta namu-namu pinetku hilaŋ,
tali haṙṣa śīṙṇna pinĕgat ni kūŋ lara*

ri hanaṅku ṅūni karaṇanta kawĕnaŋ inusiṙ nikaŋ musuḥ,
Āḥ nihan aku kaka maṙmma rĕsun,
ya hinūṙ ta mātya sapadi ṅhulun kĕna*

hilaŋ ambĕk i ṅhulun anon hilaŋ i kĕtĕ-kĕtĕgta riŋ jaja,
swāmi t-awuṅu t-abaṅun ta tuhan,
diwasa ŋ mata amrĕm akĕkĕs-kĕkĕs manis*

pawajanta ṅūni ya rumājasani maṅalap ambĕk i ṅhulun,
wruḥ tiki pamuji pijĕṙkkw-anaṅis,
sariris ri lambay i manĕḥta kārikā*

ndi manis-manis ni wacananta n anuculi ri sandhi niŋ tapiḥ,
duhkha puhara ni sukhanta maṅel,
guyu ni ṅhulun karika ya abalik taṅis*

pinalaṙ-palaṙ ku tulusa asiha kita ri gatiṅku kāsihan,
Āḥ wiphala ni pasuṅaṅkwa hurip,
t-aṅusiṙ tuwuḥta rinawas nikaŋ widhi*

bapa reṇa ni ṅhulun ikāna lalu lalis ira n paṅāryakĕn,
maṅkana ta kita muwaḥ tan asiḥ,
yaŋ atiṅgal i ṅhulun ika iŋ wanāntara*

ndi nikaŋ pradeśa kahananta wana gahana wiṣṭi tan sipi,
tan hana kula kadaŋ aṅlawada,
mulata i laraṅku kalawan kita priya*

ndya taŋ enaka aṅhiŋ aku milwa pĕjaha ri pĕjaḥta tan waneḥ,
herĕn aku tuhan anūta hĕnū,
kaka tuntunĕn ṅwaŋ irikaŋ wwat eṅguṅan*

<waṅśastha>:47.
⏑ – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏓ = 12

nihan tikaŋ śwāna wana aharĕp śawa,
hane samīpanta mulat hana aṅhalup,
humerakĕn patya ni taṅhuluñ juga,
mataŋnya tān intaṙ aweḥ lara i ṅhulun*

tuwin kulĕm hyaŋ rawi manda yan kĕñar,
miraḥ nira awaṙṇna kaninta yan tinon,
umaṅkin alwaŋ sumurup samaṅkana,
pĕtĕŋ tikaŋ rāt kadi buddhi ni ṅhulun*

ahāḥ kamu ṅhyaŋ daśalokapālaka,
kĕmit ṅhulun haywa sabhāra wismrĕti,
tĕhĕṙ tuluŋ saŋ nrĕpaputra kāsihan,
palaṙ-palaṙ ṅwaŋ malĕsa iŋ paṅaṙccana*

kita hyaŋ iŋ lwaḥ t-aṅanugraha i ṅhulun,
prasiddha reṇaṅku kita asiha i ṅhulun,
warāmrĕta iki n palakuṅku tan waneḥ,
apan panambā ri siraŋ nrĕpātmaja*

bhaṭāra saŋ hyaŋ nikanaŋ wanāntara,
lawan watĕk hyaŋ sahana iŋ jagat kabeḥ,
asiḥ ta ri ṅwaŋ sĕnĕŋ i ṅhulun tuluŋ,
hurip gĕlis kapwa ya pinta ni ṅhulun*

nihan ta sambat nrĕpaputrika anaṅis,
tatan wruḥ iŋ de kapĕgan lana amĕhaḥ,
mĕlĕs tika abaŋ mĕlĕk iŋ mata amiraḥ,
sawaŋ turaḥ niŋ hawu-haww-aweḥ raras*

ikāŋ alas milw-atahĕn-tahĕn lara,
wuluḥ riyā tan pahatī lana aṅĕsaḥ,
miṅĕl pucaŋnya n wahu waṙṇna kemĕṅan,
wase nikā nitya taṅisnya tan pĕgat*

ri kāla saŋ yajñawatī wimūṙcchita,
hana iki wikw-a amawa toya riŋ ghaṭa,
sakeŋ patīṙthan maṅaran tapowana,
mulat ri saŋ sāmba rujit kĕna iŋ panaḥ*

tĕñuḥ tikā citta nira mpu kāsihan,
wawaŋ manāntwa i naranāthaputrikā,
paran kita induṅku kapaṅgiḥ iŋ bhaya,
lawan sĕnĕŋ meḥ pĕjaha asakit kanin*

narendraputrī sumahuṙ sira adara,
bapa mpu siṅgiḥ taña saŋ yati i ṅhulun,
sĕḍĕŋ wiwal tan pamisiṅgiḥ iŋ bapa,
ya hetu niŋ mūṙ ahañaŋ mareŋ wukir*

amet ṅgwan aṅdoḥ mara tan kinawruhan,
asiŋ ḍusun śūnya tĕlas kalaṅlaṅan,
sawet niŋ göŋ niŋ siḥ akālihan lulut,
ṅhulun lawan swāmi manuṅgal iŋ hurip*

kunaŋ ta ya n mogha kawighnan iŋ hawan,
anĕmwakĕñ cora lumampaḥ iŋ kulĕm,
ikaŋ maliŋ sāhasika aṅduk aṅgalaḥ,
sĕnĕŋ ranak hyaŋ kaki wāni maṅlawan*

ṅhulun manumpĕt manusup mareŋ sukĕt,
nimitta niŋ tan kĕna de nikaŋ maliŋ,
kĕna pwa ta swāmi ranak mahāyati,
ya hetu niŋ duṣṭa muliḥ paḍa adulur*

mijil ranak hyaŋ kaki saṅka riŋ sukĕt,
rikā n kapaṅgiḥ priya ni ṅhulun pĕjaḥ,
tibā ni luḥ ni ṅhulun aṅdyusi ŋ sĕnĕŋ,
ya hetu niŋ somya kĕcap mata aṅdĕlö*

nahan ta liśya nrĕpaputrika awaraḥ,
mahaṙṣy-amakpak sira maṅrĕṅö wuwus,
uḍūḥ katuhwan kawĕlas-harĕp dahat,
kita ibu lāwan priya maṅrĕsi i hati*

na śabda saŋ paṇḍita māṙ manaḥ nira,
tĕhĕṙ sira aṅdyus ri siraŋ nrĕpātmaja,
saha prayoga amrĕta jīwarakṣaṇa,
nĕhĕṙ minantran sthiti de mahāyati*

tĕlas narendrātmaja dinyus aṅlilir,
aminta toya apan asat gulū nira,
wineḥ i ron iŋ tĕmu de suputrikā,
umaṅkin enak wĕkasan manaḥ nira*

<wiśwalalita>:48.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 17

nrĕpaduhita agiraŋ sira ri paṅliliṙ nrĕpasuta,
maṅupaśama i mahāṙṣi pukulun tasön kasihana,
yaśana ranak mahāyati n awāndhawa irikaŋ alas,
kasihana rakṣanĕn tulusa de mahāmuni masiḥ*

wuwus ira saŋ narendraduhitā ri saŋ yatiwara,
ya ta karĕṅö tĕkap nrĕpatiputra māṙ mrat awĕlas,
karaṇa narendraputra matahĕn lara amarupuhi,
aharĕp amaṙṣukha aṅinakana i manaḥ saŋ ahayu*

ri tĕlas ira abaṅun mulat anāntwa riŋ rĕṣiwara,
kadi sinĕkaṙ tikaŋ hati tumon ri saŋ yatiwara,
warakaraṇa swadhaṙmma nira ri ṅhulun kasiḥ-arĕp,
tuhu-tuhu dewatātmaka mahāṙṣi siddhi winuwus*

tumulusa tan kapālaṅa ta siḥ ni saŋ muniwara,
riŋ agati kāsihan wawa riŋ aśrama hyaŋ atuha,
yatiwara sanmatan tika n umuṅsira i pada nira,
anaḍaha sewa rānak amalaṙ warāmrĕta nira*

nihan ika śabda saŋ nrĕpasuta i mahāmuni sira,
sahuṙ ira saŋ mahāṙṣi tija bhāgya yan kita mara,
ujaṙ ira maṅkana krama madĕg ta saŋ nrĕpasuta,
lumaku maṅiñcut-iñcut anasaṙ kadi wwaŋ awĕrö*

nrĕpasuta māṙ gupa iki n umĕhaḥ ywa mĕṅgaḥ aṅĕliḥ,
hanan aṅadĕg kaṅelan irikā n tinuntun inamör,
nrĕpaduhitā manundaŋ anĕhĕṙ mamakpak anaṅis,
pira kari sāra niŋ sĕmi panumbaka iŋ kayu sare*

pira ta kunaŋ suwenya ri hawan ta meḥ sira tibā,
i harĕp ikaŋ tapowana marāṙyyan iŋ watu magöŋ,
humĕnĕb-ĕnĕb kaṅelan ira yeka raḥ nira mijil,
wĕkasan udhāni maṅkata muwaḥ maṅiṅkin atĕkĕn*

tĕka ta sira i dalĕm ri patapan mahāṙṣi wĕkasan,
ri huwus ira ñ jinampyan aturū sinaṅhulun atis,
manaḥ ira śuddha yan pamiṣaya i prajāpati tĕpĕt,
puriḥ ira saŋ mahāpuruṣa tan bara amrĕta turū*

hali-hali saŋ narendraduhitā ri saŋ nrĕpasuta,
inusap-usap nira iki mukha saŋ priya aṅḍik awĕnĕs,
bari-bari saṅśaya i pĕjaha saŋ narendratanaya,
karaṇa nira n pataṅhi manĕhĕṙ sira aṅrahinakĕn*

<mrĕdukomala>:49.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 18

taṅheḥ yañ caritan lawas nira piraŋ kulĕm sira huwus,
tamba asiŋ tamatan hana amarasi roga saŋ katanĕhan,
rūm saŋ yajñawatī juga aṅinaki citta saŋ nrĕpasuta,
tambiṙyyan haṅĕt iŋ payodhara haṅöt-aṅöt nira n atis*

eñjiŋ saŋ nrĕpaputra yaṙ warahakĕn taŋ ipyan ahayu,
ṅkāna i yajñawatī huwus nira maśoca liŋ nira nihan,
rakryan rakwa tinonku mabrata mawastra piṅhay amawar,
ṅwaŋ rakwa iki hane samīpa niy ariṅku tansaḥ aparĕk*

ndā ṅkāna i pasabhān pwa yajña nira saŋ watĕk rĕṣi kabeḥ,
saŋ hyaŋ bahni murub ywa rakwa sira tan padhūma maṅadĕg,
saṅkeŋ agni mijil bhaṭāra puruṣottama awak aṅadĕg,
sākṣāt dèwa catuṙbbhuja aparimita iŋ salakṣaṇa sira*

Ātmā rakwa paweḥ nira inĕnaḥ ira i jajaṅkw-i wĕkasan,
paṅheṙ ṅke ri si sāmba liŋ nira ri saŋ winehakĕn ira,
antaṙllīna sira iŋ kamantyan aku kāna de nira sukha,
byaktanya aku waras hiḍĕpku ya mataŋnya haywa kalaran*

nāntĕn prāwala ni ṅhulun rari lawan kita ikana hĕlĕm,
ṅkāna iŋ dwārawatī mahotsawa yateki deṅku gawayĕn,
mwaŋ pūjā ri bhaṭāra keśawa wiṣeṣa mukhya gĕlarĕn,
caṇḍi i śāla ta deṅku saŋ nrĕpati krĕṣṇa rāmawijaya*

nāhan liŋ nira saŋ narendratanaya i narendraduhitā,
dewī yajñawatī prahaṙṣa nira tulya kāṙttika ḍatĕŋ,
śoka i twas nira wāhu māri siniram nikaŋ sukha magöŋ,
saṅkeŋ tuṣṭa marambĕhan wĕtu ni luḥ nira ika ri mata*

ndā tapwan masuwe sira amarahakĕn sulakṣaṇa nira,
yekā n prāpta mahāṙṣi maṅhaturakĕn śiwāmbha ri sira,
mwaŋ tambā nira toya wāhu pinutĕṙ saha akaṙ ikahĕn,
wwantĕn ta alwaŋ ikaŋ lara i nrĕpasuta awuwuḥ waras ira*

hrĕt niŋ lakṣaṇa len samāhita mahaṙṣy-asaṅgĕm anuluŋ,
hetunya an amigas-migas ta sira saŋ narendratanaya,
luṅhā ŋ kāla saṅaŋ kulĕm sira haneŋ tapowana huwus,
santoṣa anacaṙ antuk iŋ tapa-tapa anasi mwaŋ acukil*

wadwā saŋ nrĕpaputra sāmba tadanantara krama ḍatĕŋ,
lāwan ta ika si dāruki prawala len ta rāki sahaja,
haṙṣa awwat panaṅis nikaŋ bala tuhanku liŋnya magiraŋ,
luḥnya adrĕs humilī ya rakwa pamasĕḥnya jöŋ nrĕpasuta*

mojaṙ saŋ nrĕpaputra he kaka pu dāruki ndak ataña,
ndi ika saŋ niśatha ahurip kari saŋ ulmuka ndi kawĕkas,
mwaŋ saŋ satyaka śāraṇa pwa hamĕṅān ira ikana kabeḥ,
mwaŋ hetunta hurip tĕkap nikanaŋ aṅrĕwĕk waraḥ aku*

nāhan takwan i saŋ nrĕpātmaja si dāruki wruḥ asahur,
sojaṙ saŋ naranāthaputra bapa śāśwatā sira kabeḥ,
Āpan tan hana śīṙṇna saŋ niśaṭha satyaka ahayu sira,
mwaŋ saŋ śāraṇa len saŋ ulmuka tĕka ika wadwa sawaneḥ*

sambandhanya nihan parĕŋ sira kapat manek ratha nira,
maṅkat saṅka rikaŋ paturwan ira saṅgata amapagakĕn,
kapwa añakra ri wadwa paṅharĕp ikaŋ musuḥ sĕḍĕŋ amūk,
lwiṙ guntuṙ mapagut matampuḥ i tĕṅaḥ tikaŋ gajapati*

paṅhrūk niŋ wani len paṅohan ikanaŋ sĕḍĕŋ kakuwuṅan,
enak taŋ laga lūd pĕtĕŋ jĕmuṙ ikaŋ siliḥ-praŋ arukĕt,
śabda ndi iku ya ta iku ya iku karĕṅö humuŋ mawurahan,
makweḥ taŋ lwaŋ ikaŋ musuḥ pinĕgatan winūk tinĕṅahan*

wadwā saŋ magadhendra kāpĕsan alaḥ kabeḥnya malayū,
kapwa atiṅgal amet huripnya wĕkasan musi irikaŋ alas,
kepwan saŋ magadhādirāja ginĕlis cinakra pinanaḥ,
hetunya n pamĕlĕg limanya n alayū tĕlas kakaninan*

wwantĕn ta anak iraŋ narendra magadhādinātha kawĕnaŋ,
khyāti iŋ rāt maṅaran pratīpa kasikĕp binandhan atĕhĕr,
sāmpun maṅkana saŋ nrĕpātmaja kapat mare kita bapa,
śoka ika prihatin kabeḥ sira ri tan katonta mahurip*

ṅkā n tiṅhal sira ri ṅhulun bapa paḍa awĕlas mara sira,
maṙmma ajampyan iri ṅhulun hana maweḥ sĕpaḥ sira waneḥ,
prāpta ikaŋ inutus nira aṅlayata len wĕkasta wĕkasan,
yekā n kapwa muliḥ matiṅgal i manĕḥta kāri malara*

ndan mogha iki hana awĕlas ri gati ni ṅhulun kasiḥ-arĕp,
wikw-a asiḥ pasĕnötan i ṅhulun amet hurip masusupan,
tamba akaṙ biṣa rakwa ya iki panuluŋ nira n pamarasi,
hetunya n tĕka ta ṅhulun bapa ri jöṅta masyaŋ umuliḥ*

mwaŋ wadwanta hane yawa aturaḥ ikaŋ pĕjaḥ wahu ḍatĕŋ,
t-aṅkat haywa jĕnĕk ta saŋ nrĕpasuta iŋ tapowana bapa,
Āpan saŋ magadhādhipa iṅut-iṅutĕn kĕna anak ikahĕn,
utsāha i kita rakwa dhīra maharĕp sira apulihana*

nāhan liŋnya si dāruki i sira narendraputra winaraḥ,
mamwīt rakwa narāṙyya sāmba ri siraŋ mahāṙṣi wĕkasan,
minta ŋ pratyadhirakṣaṇa iki pinĕkul tĕkap yatiwara,
mwaŋ mrĕtyuñjaya hetu niŋ jaya rikaŋ raṇāṅgana hĕlĕm*

mantuk saŋ nrĕpaputra sāmba mahawan ratha adrĕs alaris,
tan waṙṇnan sira riŋ hĕnū pira kunaŋ lawas nira huwus,
prāpta iŋ dwārawatī mapaŋ kadi hudan hañaṙ tĕka nira,
nāhan hetu nikaŋ manuṅsuŋ asuluŋ-suluŋ paḍa mijil*

sāmpun prāpta iŋ dwārawatī saŋ nrĕpaputra,
enak ta ambĕk saŋ yadu-wrĕṣṇy-andhakawīra,
sakweḥ niŋ paṅhotsawa sāmpun ta kabhukti,

<indrabajra>:51.

mandĕl ta saŋ kimpuruṣādirāja,
yekā n pahĕmhĕm naranātha krĕṣṇa,
mukhya i paluṅguḥ nrĕpati druma ikā,
lāwan sira ikiŋ basudewa nātha*

siṅgiḥ narendra atuha tūt krama areḥ,
sāmpun tumūt śrī baladewa nātha,
soṅgwan lawan śrī naranātha krĕṣṇa,
ri i soṙ nira ikaŋ yaduwīra śūra*

ṅka irīka n uṅgwan para mantri mukhya,
kapwa atata atūt krama riŋ paliṅgiḥ,
Āpan wikadrūpa saŋ uddhawa adi,
sākṣāt guru sthāna nira iŋ kawāgmin*

mojaṙ narendra druma sādara alon,
nā liŋ nira ṅke naranātha hopĕn,

yadyan sukhā saŋ prabhu yan tumiṅhal,

wwantĕn pwa len towi yadin tĕkāsiḥ,

tuccha ŋ wwaŋ ahyun walĕs iŋ winehan,

<aṙddhasamacatuṣpati>:54.

ṅuniweḥ sukha niŋ jagat cinitta,

paṅusiṙkkw-iki höb nikuŋ yaśa agöŋ,

nrĕpati krĕṣṇa lawan halāyudha,
makanaryama buddhiy ugrasena,
irikāŋ sādhya sinādhya ni ṅhulun*

sira saŋ baladewa śīghra mojar,
prabhu tan saṅśaya saŋ nareśwara,
yaduwīra matoha jīwitanya,
sumarathyākĕna kāṙyya saŋ prabhu*

sumahuṙ siraŋ ugrasena śīghra,
ya kĕnoḥ śabda narendra ta anaya,
apan aṅhiŋ i dona niŋ samaṅke,
umariwrĕtta ri saŋ maṅāśraya*

aṅucap naranātha keśawāṅsa,
pada yukti ika wuwus nareśwara,
yaduwīra saŋ uddhawa ata mahyun,
ri sapājaṙ naranātha tan salaḥ*

tiḍak ḍīkĕtahui
<krĕti>:55
⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ – = 20

ri tĕlasnya n enak apagĕḥ pwa paṅaku nira saŋ watĕk yadu,
nrĕpati druma pwa sira tuṣṭa manaḥ ira sumöŋ mare hati,
umuliḥ mareŋ kuwu nira aṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn i lĕkas nira apraṅa,
inusap nira awak ira manyus akisut atĕhĕṙ sira aṅgĕtĕm*

i sĕḍĕŋ nira n paḍa sukha nrĕpati sahana saŋ watĕk yadu,
ṅuniweḥ narendra harimūṙtti sira tika kagöṅan iŋ sukha,
ri ḍatĕŋ narendra haji kimpuruṣapati ri saŋ watĕk yadu,
yatikā prakāśakĕna de nira saphala karĕṅwa riŋ musuḥ*

makaleśya ta ŋ mahas acaṅkrama mamarĕkana aŋ ḍusun-ḍusun,
hana paṙwwata iŋ madhura rewataka ṅaran ikā ya lakwana,
inatag tikaŋ yadu kabeḥ saha tanaya sadāra saṅgĕpan,
tĕka riŋ mabhaṇḍagina kapwa paḍa milu ghinoṣitan haji*

sukha kañcit ambĕk ira saŋ tĕlas inarahakĕn paḍa atihaŋ,
pakaronya wastra binĕbĕd-bĕbĕd inapitan iŋ galaḥ miraḥ,
hana len rinaṇḍi tinulisnya harĕp iŋ arĕja asawaŋ tinon,
tiga waṙṇna kahyun ika rājasa sinahaja bāŋ lawan putiḥ*

sakatambay eñjiŋ an umaṅkata narapati tan kalūbana,
adadak tikaŋ wwaŋ i dalĕm nagara wijaḥ akabwatan manis,
yatikā kapantĕsakĕna iŋ sarahi-sarahi n āpti ya inapi,
mwaŋ ikaŋ masiñjaṅa katon atulisa ginawe kinasturi*

kahatuṙ wulan kasapuluḥ sĕḍĕŋ i lĕṅĕŋ ikā madūm laṅö,
paḍa tan hana aṅinak-inak sahana-hana nikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ puri,
raras iŋ lumampaha waneḥ sacinarita nika amajaŋ wulan,
sama haṙṣa rāmya sawilāśa gati nika saraśmi sasmita*

yatika aṅucap sama samitra gumuṇita sakahyun iŋ hati,
rari yadyapin swan ika tĕmpuhakĕna nira saŋ nareśwara,
apiliḥ ṅwaŋ iŋ kaharĕp i ṅhulun awĕdi tumiṅhala iŋ maru,
ṅuniwehkw-amaṅgiha kawalwan aku niyata kāwara iŋ prĕman*

rari yan hana ika sira taṇḍa suṅana paranaṅkwa de haji,
arĕṇaḥ rahadyan i gatinya ta mahuluna denya ri ṅhulun,
wruḥ ika awayuḥ wruḥ anĕkāni sukha tĕhĕṙ aweḥ anaṇḍaṅa,
nda nihañ calanya sanu deṅkw-apiṅit asĕmu tan basa iŋ kadaŋ*

lĕṅĕŋ ambĕk i ṅwaŋ amalaṙ turuŋ agati ri jöŋ nareśwara,
raras iŋ sakĕmbaṅa katon anĕku-nĕku kurĕn maṅasyasiḥ,
sahurip sahaṙṣa paḍa rāmya siliḥ-asiḥ anuṅgal iŋ manaḥ,
witade sadenya n ahila ndan ika warĕg akālihan hulĕs*

<jagaddhita>:56.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

om siṅgiḥ kaka liṅta tan sinipi rāmya niŋ aṅalap uliḥ nikaŋ wulat,
mogha n kaṙwwa kasaŋnya soṅa niŋ aṅuṅsira pasisi mahimyan-imyana,
līla aṅaywa laṅö ṅhulun kaka sapālapana puḍak aṅantya riŋ karaŋ,
raśminya i hrĕbuk iŋ sĕkaṙ dadaha ni ṅhulun anĕṅĕra jaṅga kasturi*

yan botoḥ juḍi tan rahat ṅwaŋ irika alaḥ ajĕjĕp iŋ ujaṙ samaṇḍala,
pantĕs yan humalaŋ mujuṙ pwa ya kaliṇḍĕn i basahan ikā kuraŋ wasĕḥ,
tan paśrīnya maliŋ timaḥ tuwin anĕṅgaḥ awak ika bisa awijil pirak,
yan pastrī ndan uliḥnya mol amurugul tan awĕdi sinapa amalaywakĕn*

yan wwaŋ thānya bisa aṅgalĕŋ manahan iŋ wwaŋ anakĕbi tinuṅgal iŋ prĕman,
prāyanya añ jawuḥ iŋ kulĕm kawawa kelu mamabaki tapiḥ baraŋ gĕlis,
agya atañjĕka liŋ nikā n pinarihāra n agĕlĕm agawe ndatan bĕsur,
nistanya abaḥ-abaḥnya saṅkĕp agĕḍĕg ṅwaŋ i wuluku nika awihiŋ-wihiŋ*

yan kaṙmmā titi mawrat ambĕk ika denya n akas akalibān ikiŋ manaḥ,
solaḥnya aṙddha narajwa sahyana pira aku wĕnaŋ amĕṭika astu siñjaṅa,

om denya n paṅĕsös iriŋ śayana muḍwakĕna jaja nika iŋ payodhara*

nāhan liŋnya tĕhĕṙ paḍa aṅuwusakĕn hyas ahayu raras iŋ paḍa araras,
kapwa areḥ asĕgĕḥ manis lawan ikaŋ tĕṅaḥ aṅĕliḥ amādapa alĕmĕs,
endaḥ rūpa niki n tĕlas masĕkaṙ aṙjja ri pataḥ atitaḥ binĕntĕlö,
māmbö rūmnya sumāṙ nimitta nika kumbaṅĕn alulut i gandha niŋ pipi*

rakryan hĕmpu nikaŋ karaṇḍan agawe paḍa makĕpĕtan iŋ tĕṅaḥ wĕṅi,
pes-pesan satalad-talad pusu-pusuḥ sinama jamuṙ ika akisī-kisi,
calwan sobal-ubal katon iwaka niŋ bĕkĕl inĕnaḥ ika iŋ pakudwanan,
aṅhiŋ taŋ katupaŋ sapaṅgiliṅan aṅhalĕpakĕna taḍaḥ nika iŋ hawan*

byātītan tikanaŋ kulĕm rahina riŋ kamantyan apaḍaŋ,
maṅkat saŋ naranātha makrigan ikaŋ sarājya maṅiriŋ,

<wibhrama>:59.
⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – –| ⏑ ⏓ = 20

tadanantara krama ḍatĕŋ saŋ aṙjjuna lawan subhadra aṅĕnĕs,
tumuluy cumuntĕn i narendra krĕṣṇa baladewa haṙṣa agiraŋ,

awuwuḥ karāmyan ikanaŋ mahotsawa makin halĕpnya asalin,

tuhu taŋ laṅit kadi rinantaga aṙjja jaladanya mabra asinaŋ,
pamatĕs ni teja ni kilat nika anipati riŋ mata aṅde lĕyĕp*

awiwākṣita iki gati niŋ kulĕm hana ta duhkharāga aṅaraŋ,
wahu-wāhu rakwa manahĕn lara aṅĕsaḥ aṅölakĕn kūŋ rimaŋ,

mawuwus ta ceṭi nika māsku toḥ mapa ta hetu niŋ sukṣĕka,
mapa ta inalĕḥ lara mata ṅhulun rari wĕkasnya tan saṅśaya,
uṣadhanya jahya tulisanya tuṅgĕŋ inumi ika baṇḍī sahir,

aparan tikāŋ uṣadha ni ṅhulun t-ajarakĕn ta haywa agigu,
paḍa tan hana anukhakĕna ŋ susuk masihana ŋ prapañce hati*

mapa liṅta māsku kĕna rāga kupwa mapa ta ulahaṅkwa i kita,
aparan ta mūla nika ṅūni toḥ mapa ta rūpa saŋ maṅlare,

<girisa>:60
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – – –| – – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏓ = 16

nihan iki kaka maṅde kiṅkiŋ ni ṅhulun i hati,
prathama ni lari ni ṅwaŋ saṅkeŋ rājya mawukiran,
lĕṅĕŋ aratha paḍa asraŋ ramya atūt palapat ayun,

bapa haji sira muṅgwiŋ wuntat lāwan ibu haji,

salĕsĕk i ratha niŋ wwaŋ akweḥ maṙmma niŋ apasaḥ,

ratha mami makin aṅdoḥ līla atūt alas alaṅö,
asiŋ asĕkaṙ aweḥ kūŋ mwaŋ luṅlūṅan aṅalayan,
hana ta makuda piṅhe lwiṙ hyaŋ manmatha manurun,

pamahiriŋ i larinya aṅinte tiṅhalana mami,
puji n apaṅus ulaḥnya n pantĕs tan hana kakuraŋ,
ṅhulun apimulati ŋ rĕm ndañ cittaṅku mara riya,

sahaja ya maṅagĕm wwaḥ bhāwanya akĕcap ahidu,

wruḥ ika ri manaha ṅwaŋ maṙmmanya n rĕṇa rinasan,

kunaŋ ika si suwaṙṇnī wruḥnya aśabda manahuri,

lagi pinakapaṅalyan tambiṙyyan wruḥ amalĕsi,
basa mataña ṅaranyā rowaŋ ni ṅhulun adulur,

tĕka pawaraḥ ikaŋ wwaŋ putra śrī druma liŋ ikā,
taruṇa kadi kucup niŋ kambaŋ cāmpaka riŋ arūm,
lituhayu sira himpĕṙ hyaŋ-hyaŋ niŋ tarukusuma,
aku rika ta kĕna priḥ de niŋ haṙṣa salaḥ-iḍĕp*

ndan apa kunĕŋ amogha n prāpta ŋ cāra manututi,
pakuda ni bapa hajy-a akon aṅhera ya ri kami,
lumaris ika duluṙnya anoliḥ māṙ ṅhulun asĕkĕl,
lĕwu tan apa tikāŋ luḥ maṅke denya paṅalilip*

tĕka ratha bapa hajy-a atanduk ri ṅhulun adulur,
ibu haji sira maṙmma amakpak n ton ṅhulun anaṅis,
waliŋ ira karikā ṅwaŋ duhkha adoḥ saka ri sira,
karaṇa nira manampil (r)y-uṅgwankw-a aṅusapi ri luḥ*

aku ta kaparĕk aṙddha alök tiṅhalku dudu-dudū,
apan iki duluṙ i ṅwaŋ byakta anuṅgayap i mata,
kami katanĕhan onĕŋ tan wriŋ de kĕna turida,
karakĕtan irikā ṅwaŋ maṅga anūtakĕna lulut*

⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

kamānuṣan ira n saŋ adyaḥ anĕhĕṙ mawacana sahaja amaṅun raras,
tuhanku bapa tan sipi iki pagawenta turida riŋ arūm prapañcika,
tan adwa dinaliḥ maliŋ lulut iki n kita lagi-lagi kesi riŋ jinĕm,

gupe sira hanan lĕṅöŋ ḍinawuhan turida tan atutuṙ pinaṅkwakĕn,
cucul tali tapiḥ nira n lukari puṇḍutan ira n inalapta riŋ jinĕm,
lĕwĕs lara nira n huwus kahilaṅan kararan akusikan sira anaṅis*

<kusumawilasita>:64.
– ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏓ = 21

tan baribin ta riŋ lagi tinakwanan i wĕkas i citta niŋ rimaŋ,
toḥ ta tĕkap ni sādhu paran iŋ turida lalu bisa anĕnötakĕn,
kapwa lawan tatan duga-duga n dinaliḥ aṅalap ambĕk iŋ mulat,
tan sabhara n katona curawāda mara kita tan intaṙ iŋ karas*

riŋ bhramara n katiṅhalana kūṅta bapa yan amagantakĕn sĕkar,
tan huniṅanta riŋ rimaṅa niŋ puji-puji pinalaṙ manuṅgala,
siḥta haneŋ riris hanisi maṅhuyaṅi hati niŋ aṅdĕlö tawaŋ,
hyaŋ wulan ambĕk i ṅwaŋ i kita n kinaharĕpan iwön haneŋ tilam*

saŋ kadi wimba niŋ sĕmi kalahrun aṅĕliḥ alala aṅrĕṅö gĕrĕḥ,
śrī niŋ aśokapuṣpa sira rāgakusuma sira puṣpadewatī,
rūpa nira adhikāra n ahĕle kawĕlas-asiḥ aṅiṣṭi raṅkĕpan,
hyaŋ rati ambĕk i ṅwaŋ i sira n kita madana mapaṅgiha iŋ wukir*

ndan hĕnĕŋ ambwatī hĕnĕṅĕnanta kinalaran apujya tan para,
wyaṙtha dahat pwa donku bapa denta n amihaṅi hinundaŋ i ṅhulun,
tan puriḥ iŋ priyambada kita iki n ulaḥ alalis an kinonĕṅan,
aṅhiŋ ikaŋ wilāpa paṅahat-hat iri kita palaṙ pisiṅgihĕn*

nāhan ujaṙnya saŋ winuwusan wawaŋ anahuri haṙṣaja awuwus,
Āḥ lĕwu kūṅku de ni pawaraḥta ri gati saŋ inimba riŋ manis,
guntuṙ unaŋ ṅhulun kajawuhan turida niŋ araras mara ŋ riris,
syuḥ kahilī hatiṅku kawawa i tĕṅaḥ iŋ ahayu kāmpiṙ iŋ susu*

kepwan i buddhi ni ṅwaŋ aṅiriŋ panarimana riŋ adyaḥ aṅlare,
tan wruḥ i pāmbĕkanya n arusit nĕhĕṙ aṅapusi citta niŋ rimaŋ,
ton mara kūṅkw-i taṅguŋ i lulutnya n amulihi laṅönya riŋ ṭikā,
ṅhiŋ kawiraṅku reṇa nika yan pamasahakĕna haṙṣa ni ṅhulun*

kāla nira ikana anita lawan bibi katĕmu marumpukan sĕkar,
wruḥ ri ḍatĕṅkw-apet silib aminta sakaharĕp ika anĕhĕṙ mulat,
saŋ wri liriŋ nikaŋ rĕsĕp aṅampirakĕn i liriŋ i ṅwaŋ iŋ susu,
Āpti nikā n hĕnĕŋ kanĕban ambĕk adalihan aṅantyakĕn pariḥ*

t-ājarakĕn griŋ i ṅwaŋ i sira alara karakĕtan iŋ payodhara,
lāgy-apanas twas i ṅhulun aṅölakĕn unĕŋ i pamrĕmku riŋ jinĕm,
māṙ manaḥ i ṅhulun hali-halin rasika karaṇa ni ṅhulun maṅö,
tībra kakiṅkiṅan yatika hetu niŋ umarĕk aminta tambana*

maṅkana liŋ nira n ri jaruman saŋ ahayu manilib nĕhĕṙ muliḥ,
moliḥ-uliḥ sĕkaṙ mrik anamaṙ sĕmu sumari ya leśya riŋ mulat,
gaṙjjita saŋ tĕkāsiḥ i ḍatĕŋnya tuhun amuni haṙṣasañcaya,
luḥnya tibā tumiṅhali wilāpa saŋ anĕmu sipat haneŋ mata*

sāmpun iki n kulĕm ḍatĕŋ ikaŋ jaladhara ri hiriŋ nikaŋ laṅit,
kapwa marĕn ririsnya masalin pamirĕsĕp i manaḥ niŋ aṅrĕṅö,
söŋ ni kilatnya manda hana mātra gĕrĕḥ ika tinuṅtuṅan patĕr,
hyaŋ himaraśmi wāhu sumĕŋ aṅḍaḍari sadamaṙ iŋ haneŋ jinĕm*

ndan saŋ aṅölakĕn turida riṅraŋ aṅĕsaḥ apa tan kĕna iŋ turū,
daṙppa tumiṅhal iŋ tawaŋ awaṙṇna gĕluŋ inapi söḥ susup-susup,
mwaŋ buṅaḥ iŋ śaśī lagi paranti ni liriŋ ira n onĕŋ iŋ pipi,
paṅhrĕŋ ikaŋ patĕṙ tinaliṅa iniṅĕtakĕn i wĕkasnya tan humuŋ*

<udgatawisama>:65.
⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 20
