⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏓ = 13

irikā ŋ aśoka saŋ akūŋ karakĕtan alaṅö smarātura,
sinwam aṅĕliḥ inamĕṙ kinayuḥ,
raras iŋ sĕkaṙ mrik inisĕp nirantara*

<śālinī>:66.
– – –| – – ⏑| – – ⏑| – ⏓ = 11

kĕmbaṙ wwahniŋ nyū gaḍiŋ paṇḍak aṙjja,
rakwa aṅde māṙ ywa inusap sāri-sāri,
lāwan hampuk niŋ pupū tan pasiñjaŋ,
aṅrĕs twas māṙ hetu niŋ tan wĕnaŋ sāḥ*

<tanumadhya>:67.
– – ⏑| ⏑ – ⏓ = 6

byātīta gatinya,
riŋ weśma lata aṙjja,
söḥ sāri jinĕmnya,
ramya aṅayu haṙṣa*

saŋ hyaŋ wulan āwa,
māwan sakamantyan,
himpĕṙ mukha niŋ strī,
kanyā tanumadhya*

<jagaddhita>:68.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

wwantĕn strī kinalalwan iŋ jalu maṅanti kajĕjĕpan i haṙṣa niŋ sĕnĕŋ,
sampunya n pamaṅan haṅöt-aṅĕt asaṅkĕpan awĕḍak aṅöt makasturi,
raṇḍy-a aṙjja iki bĕbĕd pupus pisaŋ ikaŋ pasaji-saji bubuk turuŋ lukar,
hetunya n paṅucap laranya ri paḍanya kinawayuḥ aṅantyakĕn prĕman*

sĕmwan siḥ lĕwu pāpa ni ṅwaŋ aniwi i wwaŋ apuji hana ta aṅjajaṙ prĕman,
saŋsāra ṅwaŋ akūŋ harĕp-harĕp aṅanti wĕṅi lagi tumiṅhali ŋ lawaŋ,
yan paṅjanma jĕmaḥ ṅhulun tan aharĕp kawayuhĕn alara aku tan kahur,
astām yan ṅwaŋ aṅambila anaka taha aku kahulunana sewaka iŋ maru*

yadyan raby-atuha aku kāsihana towi patikĕlan ikaŋ sĕmat nĕhĕr,
ṅel-ṅelanku n aṅiṇḍaṅi iŋ maru wineḥ wruha ri hala hayunya kewĕhan,
doṣa iŋ kāṙyya tikīŋ anaṇḍaṅa lĕwiḥ baribin umulat iŋ halis tikĕl,
kasyāsiḥku tiwas lawan duwahagi ṅwaŋ iki n inucap ambĕk iŋ kuraŋ*

tan maṅkā sanu denya baṇḍuṅĕn ikā rwa tĕlu pat i bisā nika arabi,
towin rāmya nihan phalanya tan aṅel ṅwaŋ aniwi sagawe tuluŋ tĕkĕn,
yekā rakwa karaśmin iŋ kinawayuḥ kadi saragi gatinya kuṇḍaṅa,
ndān aṅhiŋ yan anūt sade niŋ amatūtakĕna yan apa sĕmwa tan padon*

ḍū sĕṙbbi iki paran ta rāmya niŋ inambilan iŋ apa n anūta menaka,
yadyan sānaka towi jāti tikĕla ataḥ alis ika kalĕwyan iŋ raras,
haywa asĕmwan anambaha aṅalapa soṙ tan ika karaṇa ni ṅhulun rĕṇa,
wāswāsön ikanaŋ tinuṅgal apuput kadi pakĕcapan iŋ dukut pahit*

tanṅeḥ yañ caritan wilāsa ni manaḥ niŋ anakĕbi kapaṙwwan iŋ prĕman,
luṅhā ŋ rātri tĕlas ḍawuḥ wwalu munī sikatan ika n aniṅgaṙ iŋ hawis,
rāmya ŋ caṅkiluŋ iŋ pĕtuŋ ri marĕn iŋ taḍaḥ-asiḥ anaṅis lawañ cucur,
tĕkyak riŋ kuwuŋ aṅgyat aṅhĕla-hĕla ṅhamalaku wayuha anahā priyā*

wintaŋ saṅśaya sūkṣma mukṣa dinĕlö lĕṅit aṅusiṙ amiṇḍa riŋ tawaŋ,
śeṣanya araŋ awaṙṇna pañjut akuḍuŋ-kuḍuŋ i panaput iŋ lamad-lamad,
saŋ hyaŋ lek asamun kaliṅsiṙ asamaṙ-samaṙ apa tan awās pĕgat-pĕgat,
wwantĕn lot rumakĕt paran kunaŋ ikaŋ kadi tura-turaḥ iŋ mukha awĕnĕs*

<bhujaṅgaprayāta>:69.
⏑ – –| ⏑ – –| ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = 12

lumöŋ teja saŋ hyaŋ rawi iŋ ambara awās,
tuhun kāwaran de nikaŋ nīrada awrā,
rumāgī limut niŋ wukiṙ lwiṙ jinĕm niŋ,
pahömhöman iŋ saṙwwasāry-a aṅajĕŋ rūm*

huwus niŋ ghana iki n kasandhyan laṅönya,
patĕṙnya aṅrĕṅiḥ tan kara asambat aṅras,
kaworan lĕṅĕŋ taŋ tawaŋ de nikā tan,
tĕlas lek nika alök tĕmĕn taṙ pateja*

<prĕthwītala>:70.
⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – –| ⏑ ⏓ = 17

mijil hyaŋ aruṇa ahalĕp wali nira n ghana aṙjja asinaŋ,
ikaŋ limut awaṙṇna-waṙṇna ya nawagraha aṅde raras,
gĕrĕḥ kadi curiŋ binaṇḍuṅan i kuṅkaŋ iŋ groŋ lĕṅöŋ,
patĕṙ kuwuŋ ikaŋ manuk widu tahĕn tan imba aṅigĕl*

tiḍak ḍikĕtahui
<wikrĕti>:71.
⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑|– ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

paḍa arihan ikaŋ tahĕn muni manuk saragi nika ri piṅgiṙ iŋ juraŋ,
liraŋ hana ri pāṙśśwa niŋ wukiṙ ikaŋ katiraḥ asĕmu tāruka alĕsĕḥ,
lawan trĕṇalatā katon awurana iŋ sukha sigi-sigin iŋ luŋ iŋ galiŋ,
sĕkaṙ sinawuŋ iŋ basanta kari hetu ni pataruŋ ikā n paḍa awani*

<śikhariṇī>:72.
⏑ – –| – – –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 17

tĕlas māwan saŋ hyaŋ rawi wija-wijaḥ saŋ yadu kabeḥ,
amet rūm-rūm niŋ rewataka pinaran siŋ sakamatan,
hana amet-met riŋ lwaḥ walahaṙ aduluṙ mwaŋ kasiḥ ikā,
amukti i raśmy-a asiŋ sararas awilāsa akĕla-kĕlan*

pituŋ rātri ikaŋ kāla diwasa tĕlas kaprakaśita,
muliḥ saŋ śrī krĕṣṇa andhakayadukula wrĕṣṇi madulur,
tumūt saŋ pāṙtha apan sira sinarabhāra apraṅa hĕlĕm,
tĕlas prāpta iŋ rājya nda tucapa ta saŋ dānawapati*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍta>:73.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

saŋ bhoma atisaroṣa de ni waraḥ iŋ dꜽtya n wiśīṙṇna iŋ kuṭa,
muntab rakwa panas nikaŋ hati tĕkap saŋ yajñawaty-a ahañaŋ,
nāhan hetu nira n muliḥ saka rikaŋ kendran matiṅgal musuḥ,
agyā n śīghra tĕka iŋ purī katĕmu taŋ rājya atunū lwiṙ gunuŋ*

saŋ bhoma aṅucap iŋ mahodara lihat śīṙṇna ŋ kaḍatwan gĕsĕŋ,
de niŋ yādawa wrĕṣṇi nīca paracidranya anĕkāny-a anilib,
duṣṭā krĕṣṇabala pwa ya aṅhiwagakĕn tan śāsana iŋ kṣatriya,
sotan taŋ basudewaputra matuha iŋ gowrĕnda ṅūnī n rare*

yan wānya ry-aku kenakanya ri hanaṅku n taṅtaṅanya apraṅa,
mon yan motusa minta donĕn aku tan dadya ata tan sambhrama,
maṅke pwā paracidra kaśmala nikā tan dhaṙmmayuddha iŋ musuḥ,
maṅgā tocapĕn iŋ para amawas ikā ṅūni irikaŋ yāwana*

maṅke taŋ druma yan paṅuṅsiṙ irikaŋ krĕṣṇa atakut ri ṅhulun,
bhakti iŋ duṣṭa matiṅgal iŋ sujana dhik ninda aku riŋ maṅkana,
luṅha amet pamarāśrayan syapa tatan krodha i tĕkapnya n tiwas,
Āpan de ni kakö ni buddhi nika hetunya n tan aṅga anuta*

aṅhiŋ ta aṅĕn-aṅĕnku maṅkata dumona i krĕṣṇa tātan waneḥ,
rājya i dwārawatī punaḥ parawaśan sakweḥ nikaŋ maṅjuru,
bwat solaḥ nika taṅgapĕn papagakĕn riŋ praŋ kasiṅhākrĕtin,
tuṇḍanyā makadhaṙmmayuddhan ikanaŋ kahyunkwa yan papraṅa*

nān liŋ saŋ naraka asahuṙ saŋ inajaṙ yukti ika deya apraṅa,
sakweḥ niŋ ratu maṅjuru pwa warahĕn rapwan parĕŋ maṅkata,
maṅkā liŋ nika saŋ mahodara wawaŋ luṅhā tikaŋ cāraka,
śīghra apan mahawan tawaŋ paḍa madrĕs yeka amawa ajñā haji*

ndaḥ waṙṇnan kĕta saŋ watĕk ratu kabeḥ sāṙ sök pĕnuḥ sañjata,
maṅkat saŋ naraka awimāna maṇipuṣpa atyanta śīghra aṅlayaŋ,
sakweḥ niŋ bala dꜽtya rākṣasa kabeḥ kapwa ahawan riŋ laṅit,
Ākāśa aṙddha pĕpĕt bhaṭāra sawitā nisteja sāmpun pĕtĕŋ*

agyā taŋ manapak lĕmaḥ wukiṙ alas dhwasta ŋ tahĕn duṙbala,
guntuṙ taŋ himawān prakampita tikaŋ bhūmy-a atighora ṅhaṅin,
kombak wway nikanaŋ samudra kumĕtug taŋ deśa digmaṇḍala,
utpāta ŋ girisaṅgha puṅgĕl apagut de niŋ watĕk dānawa*

sakweḥ niŋ kahalintaṅan ratu tumūt kapwa aṅiriŋ gadgada,
maṅkin ta imbuḥ ikaŋ watĕk naraka kīṙṇna ŋ rāt pĕnuḥ tan katon,
Āpan mānasa dꜽtya rākṣasa marok tuṅgal sapakṣa atĕguḥ,
yekā n byakta sawaṙgga saŋ naraka matta ikā n paṅuṇḍa ayudha*

saŋ cedi mwaŋ awaṅgarāja magadhendra mwaŋ kaliṅgādhipa,
nāhan mukhya nikaŋ tumūt madadakan maṅkat parĕŋ sāyudha,
tan waṙṇnan ta lawas nira iŋ hawan atīta prāpta riŋ gobraja,
salwā-lwā nikanaŋ palugwan atitip tekaŋ watĕk rākṣasa*

muṅgw-i i puñcak ikā ri gobraja siraŋ bhoma apanas twas nira,
sākṣāt bahni murub tikaŋ mukha mabāŋ tekāŋ awak nīśala,
mawrut-wrut kadi dhūma roma nira mawyaŋ mekĕl-ekĕl katon,
sādhya atakwana dāya saŋ naraka riŋ wrĕṣṇy-a andhaka apan kulĕm*

saŋ cedy-a ataña sājña saŋ prabhu paran ta upāya saŋ bhūpati,
maṅke śatru tĕkāna riŋ kulĕm usön rapwan ya kagyat kabeḥ,
nyāma atiṅgal anak rabinya malayū kewran tikaŋ jro pura,
tunw-i ikaŋ nagara ajaraḥ sahana niŋ ratnādi yeka alapĕn*

luṅhānya n marikā si krĕṣṇa malayū tūtĕn ta de saŋ prabhu,
yadyan sy-a aṙjjuna rowaṅanya saphalanya mātya kaṙwwa inarun,
sāmpun maṅkana hĕntyakĕn bala nikā sāmanta haywa inaris,
aṅhiŋ si druma pañjaran priḥ usirĕn de niŋ watĕk dānawa*

nā liŋ cedipati prayatna ta jarāsandha asahuṙ gadgada,
om siṅgiḥ sawuwusta yukti maṅĕnoḥ ri twas prasiddha ahayu,
ndan maṅka iki kalaḥnya yan kajagana ṅwaŋ maṅrĕwĕk riŋ kulĕm,
kāṅgĕk piŋ rwa tiwas tikaŋ kakaninan ndātan hana ika apuliḥ*

Āpan wyakti nikaŋ musuḥ ya rumĕṅö maṅke ṇ ḍatĕŋ saŋ prabhu,
nyā ŋ pekā matihaŋ mataṅhi ya pajaṙnya ikaŋ pamiṅgiṙ kabeḥ,
towi ikaŋ balasaṅgha ṅel nika turuŋ māry-a alapa aṅlud rapuḥ,
t-aṅheṙ kapwa wiwekanĕn tĕkapa niŋ maṅdon musuḥ nītiman*

ambĕk niŋ wwaŋ aśatru duṙnaya wĕnaŋ sepĕn taŋ alpa iriya,
saŋ wāni i rahina iŋ kulĕm tĕkapa niŋ wwaŋ yan dumona irikā,
ya byakta ika tiwasnya yan taha-tahan pwa ikā hade sāhasa,
Āpan tan rwa ta ya ŋ kabantĕn anĕke ndātan tĕka iŋ don ikā*

saŋ kṣepanya wiwekanĕn juga dĕlönta ambĕk nikaŋ yādawa,
kweḥnya ŋ wwaŋ makĕḍiknya kawruhan awās ta ŋ wwaŋ ya tan prokṣaka,
yapwan bhakti musuḥta bhāgya marika atūta ika tan saṅgrahan,
byakta apan parikas lĕkas nika rĕbut kīṙtti iŋ raṇa priḥ tĕmĕn*

mojaṙ kaṙṇna paranti niŋ naya wĕkas petĕn tĕkap saŋ prabhu,
aṅhiŋ praŋ juga kenakanya waṅunĕn ta asön mabheda adunĕn,
kās niŋ hasta lawan ta laṇḍĕp i tĕwĕkta ikaŋ kawīrabratan,
bhukti ikaŋ phalabhukti mukti t-aṅusiṙ kīṙtty-a adhikāra iŋ prajā*

wyaṙtha ikaŋ naya riŋ mahāprabhawa śakty-a aṅhiŋ lĕkasnya adunĕn,
Āpan dhaṙmma ni saŋ mahāpuruṣa tekaŋ sāhasa ikiŋ musuḥ,
saŋ nātha pwa jagattrayādhipati sākṣāt riŋ krĕtānugraha,
ndi ika amaṅpaṅa śakti saŋ prabhu rikeŋ rāt dèwa towy-a ararĕm*

nāhan liŋ saŋ awaṅgarāja sumahuṙ saŋ bhoma tan kaṙkkaśa,
atyanta ari wuwusta yogya ta rĕṅön de saŋ watĕk kṣatriya,
ṅwaŋ sāmpun krĕtakīṙttya tapwan ajule yan taṙ panītya ŋ lĕkas,
Āpan duṙyyaśanĕn tĕkap niŋ umulat keraŋ yadin tan bisa*

nyā ŋ wwaŋ rūpaka yan mamet iwak iwĕḥ dāyanya yan poliha,
saṅkĕp riŋ paṅalap ta ya apiliḥ uliḥ denya alĕkas moliha,
tadwat maṅkana riŋ giṇa amusuḥ amet dāyā harĕpnya ñ jaya,
tan tūta in panas iŋ hati iki sawalan tan siddhakāṙyya asarag*

ṅ wwaŋ yan śakti halĕp ri śāsana ni kāṙyya wruḥ manīti ŋ musuḥ,
tan saṅkeŋ pĕjaḥ iŋ musuḥ karaṇa ni ŋ wwaŋ yañ jaya iŋ papraṅan,
yan bhakti ika musuḥnya sambhraman ika i sĕmbaḥnya sambeganĕn,
yekā n kīṙtti tĕmĕn ṅaranya ri siraŋ bhūpālakā riŋ jagat*

Āpan buddhi nikā si krĕṣṇa ta turuŋ ta mwa ikihĕn kawruhan,
sugyan wĕdya tumona tapta sumahab kewran puriḥnya akĕḍik,
dūta pwā ya ta kenakanya rumuhun konĕn ta bhaktya i kita,
yan tan bhaktya samaṅkana n lĕkasi tekaŋ dwārawatya apuyi*

saŋ śatruntapa saŋ mahodara marāha i krĕṣṇa haywa agigu,
towekṣa ambĕk ikaŋ watĕk yadu kabeḥ yan bhaktya yan laṅghana,
yapwan bhaktya samaṅkana iriṅakĕnanta ikā lawan si druma,
yan tan bhaktya t-uliḥ tasön tĕka ri don rājyanya sep sāhasan*

ndā tĕmbesuk ikā n lumampaḥ uwusĕn sāri ika sāmpun ḍatĕŋ,
nāhan liŋ nira saŋ mahīsuta luwaṙ sakweḥ nikā saŋ mahöm,
ghora ŋ rākṣasadꜽtyasaṅghabala śabdanya aṅuhuḥ kātara,
cora ika aṅalapa atukaṙ linawanan rĕp ḍyam tikaŋ wruḥ wĕdi*

lumrā duṣṭa nikā n mareŋ wĕṅi paḍa adum deśa kapwa aṅrĕwĕk,
len tekāŋ anĕkāni taṇḍa ri pamiṅgiṙ saŋ watĕk yādawa,
lāwan taŋ garaḍag manumpu wimayā śīṙṇna ika denya alilaŋ,
moliḥ mawwat uliḥnya riŋ tuhan ikaŋ tan poliḥ amriḥ tiwas*

<sandhyakāra>:74.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 22

i sĕḍĕŋ iraŋ mahāsurapati praśasta hana riŋ wukiṙ gobraja,
sahana nikaŋ pamiṅgiṙ ira saŋ watĕk yadu paḍa atĕlas maṅhilī,
karaṇa nikā n paḍa utus ajara i narendra harimūṙtti māpadgata,
rahina kulĕm lumampaḥ utusanya kapwa mahawan turaṅga alayū*

tĕka ta ya riŋ pura amarahakĕn ḍatĕŋ saŋ asurendra bhūmyātmaja,
agarawalan ta saŋ yadu lawan watĕk ratu samaṅjuru prokṣaka,
paḍa matihaŋ sasañjata kabeḥ makādi basudewa nātha druma,
narapatiy ugrasena baladewa saŋ prabhu janāṙddana asaṅgĕpan*

i sĕḍĕŋ i saŋ watĕk yadu mamiṇḍa sañjata ḍatĕŋ ta śatruntapa,
kalawan ikaŋ mahodara haneŋ lĕbuḥ dinuluṙ iŋ sagotra aṅiriŋ,
yatika kapūhan adbhuta tumon ri gopura nikaŋ nagary-a aruhur,
hana n amagantakĕn halĕp ikaŋ purī lawan ikaŋ surendrālaya*

narapati tandwa rakwa wĕgilĕn mahodara lawan kaliṅgādhipa,
tan apa wawaŋ saniścaya sira i prayojana ni dūta saŋ bhūmija,
kathamapi tan kasaṅśaya sira apagĕḥ juga ri buddhi saŋ kṣatriya,
tuhu pinakaswabhāwa nira saŋ mahāpuruṣa riŋ tĕka abhyāgata*

apituwi mantu rakwa gati wabhru de nira narendra śatruntapa,
karaṇa nira n rĕsĕp manaḥ ira atamuy tamuy ira ika tan saṅśaya,
panamuy ira iki bhāra ya mahāsukha aṅinaki yogya riŋ bhūpati,
ya pinakahāra rakwa sahana isi niŋ pasisi paṙwwata aṙjja ahalĕp*

surasa nikaŋ bhinukti saha madya maṙṣukhani de nika amrāyani,
paḍahi kĕta aṅayap swaranika araras lĕṅĕŋ agupyan aṅde sukha,
aṅawat aganti rowaŋ ira wabhru hetu ni kapūhan iŋ rākṣasa,
agĕlis ikaŋ kamantyan aturū ta saŋ pinakadūta tan saṅśaya*

tiḍak ḍikĕtāhui
<dhrĕti>:75.
⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 18

waṅuṇ ḍahina teka saŋ pinakadūta sāmpun arahup,
mabhūṣaṇa mawastra keratilatanta lāka tinulis,
parĕŋ tumama riŋ sabhā nira saŋ ugrasena wĕkasan,
tinon ira ta saŋ watĕk yadu kabeḥ matiṅkaḥ atatā*

kapūhan amĕṅĕn-mĕṅĕn mulat i saŋ watĕk yadukula,
apūṙwwa ri halĕp watĕk yadu kabeḥ prabhāswara katon,
kasĕnwan i kĕñaṙ nikaŋ maṇimaya ika saŋ ratu kabeḥ,
manaḥnya manahā ŋ watĕk hyaŋ apupul saha apsaragaṇa*

hana adi nika saŋ narendra basudewa kantun umahā,
lawan druma sira ariris mulata riŋ mahīsutabala,
kunaŋ sahana saŋ watĕk ratu mahöm atiṅkaḥ atatā,
makādi naranātha krĕṣṇa baladewa dewasakala*

praśasta para rājaputra yaduwīra kapwa marĕpat,
saŋ andhakakulaprawīra milu wrĕṣṇiwīra matatā,
suteja tikanaŋ sabhā tĕkap i teja niŋ maṇimaya,
saŋ aṙjjuna sumĕṅkĕṙ īṅanara tulya bahni dumilaḥ*

ḍatĕŋ pwa ya narendra saŋ pinakadūta saŋ kṣitisuta,
ginorawa wineḥ paṭāraṇa tĕlas maliṅgiḥ ajajar,
ri saṇḍiŋ ira saŋ narendra krĕtadhaṙmma wabhru maśila,
magasyak agiraŋ tĕhĕṙ jitasabhā katon tan atĕgĕg*

<prahaṙṣinī>:76.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏓ = 13

saŋ śatruntapa wihikan riŋ iṅgitajña,
ceṣṭākāra nira kabeḥ tĕlas tinonton,
nāhan hetu nira n aśabda sopacāra,
ṅkāna i bhūpati baladewa keśawāṅśa*

sājñā śrī nrĕpati nimitta niŋ mara ṅke,
Ājñā bhūpati narakādirāja-rāja,
mwaŋ teki n paṅiriŋ iraŋ watĕk narendra,
sāmanta aṅjuru magadhendra cedi kaṙṇna*

sambandhanya paḍa sira an yinuktyan āsiḥ,
kapwa ahyun ri pagĕha saŋ narendra krĕṣṇa,
ndaḥ sāmpun rumuhun ike ṅhulun yan āpti,
ri swasthā yadukula hetu niŋ kinonkon*

ndya asiḥ līṅa haji kĕta i ṅhulun daya iki,
maṅke n prāpta mawaraha iki kopadeyan,
ṅka aswī ta ṅhulun agawe parāṙthadhaṙmma,
Āpan haywa narapati iki sādhya tan len*

yan yogyā hiḍĕpĕn ikaŋ wuwus rasanya,
hopĕn siŋ rahayu nikā n tĕka iŋ narāṙyya,
Āpan tan śrawaṇa madoha riŋ patīṙthan,
śabda lwiṙ tan asiḥ ikaŋ masiḥ nimitta*

saŋ sādhu pwa tuhu wuwus nira n paśabda,
śuddhajñāna sira parāṙthadhaṙmmabuddhi,
kuṣṭa ikaŋ winaraḥ anaṅśaya i kasādhun,
Āpañ citta nika hiḍĕpnya citta niŋ len*

tan maṅkā pwa niyata buddhi saŋ narāṙyya,
towin paṇḍita naranātha tan hana uli,
ndā tan mahyun i hala niŋ para apitowi,
Āpan sāmpun apagĕḥ iŋ kadhaṙmmamūṙttyan*

prādhāna nrĕpati rikeŋ jagat sudhīra,
kaprajñan haji paramāṙtha riŋ wiweka,
lwiṙ tīṙtha ahĕniŋ abuṅaḥ manaḥ narāṙyya,
śuddhā niŋ manaḥ asiḥ iŋ sarāt gatinta*

sākṣāt paṙwwata naranātha riŋ giṇa akās,
lāwan wīṙyya guṇa kaśaktin aprameya,
ndan wwantĕn paḍa-paḍa saŋ narendra śakti,
tan len saŋ ratu maṅutus ṅhulun mara ṅke*

wyaktinya n sama-sama śakti saŋ narāṙyya,
mwaŋ saŋ bhūpati saŋ anāma bhūmiputra,
himpĕṙ sāgara giri saŋ watĕk mahīja,
gambhīra atiśaya sira iŋ mahāprabhāwa*

nistanya n paḍa-paḍa śakti saŋ narendra,
tan mahyun ṅhulun irikāŋ ulaḥ maṅadwa,
śrī krĕṣṇa atiśaya sira iŋ mahāprabhāwa,
timbaŋ-timbaṅa magadhendra riŋ kaśaktin*

siṅhit saŋ narapati de nikaŋ prabhāwa,
citta aṅintarakĕn i saŋ narendra krĕṣṇa,
nistanya amuhara riraŋ ni saŋ narāṙyya,
aṅhiŋ laṅgĕṅa niŋ anak juga ŋ cinitta*

lāwan saŋ prabhu baladewa śaktimanta,
himpĕṙ-himpĕra kalawan ta cedirāja,
saŋ pāṙtha adhikaguṇamanta wīraśakti,
taṇḍiŋ kaṙṇna hana lĕwiḥ tuhun tan akweḥ*

hīṅanya n paḍa gati saŋ narāṙyya riŋ praŋ,
yogya n mitra nika ri saŋ watĕk mahīja,
haywa aṅdohi pakadaṅan ri cedirāja,
bwat meṅa ŋ sukha ṅuniweḥ tikaŋ swajīwa*

atyanta ŋ phala ri narendra yan samitra,
swasthā niŋ madhura ri gobraja awanehan,
nityā niŋ wrĕṣabha sukhā lawan saŋ ahwan,
gopāla apagĕha tan intara i palĕmbwan*

akweḥ kīṙtti haji ri gobrajā rikāna,
aṅde kiṅkiŋ i madhura alawas dinohan,
heman tan wara-warahĕn tikaŋ yaśa agöŋ,
de saŋ nātha karaṇa niŋ makon samitra*

mwaŋ gopāla lulut i saŋ narendra krĕṣṇa,
rakwa ikā n kapihutaṅan paṅan rikāna,
towi pwa ŋ nrĕpa tinuluŋ sake hyaŋ indra,
riŋ gowaṙddhanagiri ṅūni yan rinakṣa*

maṅke yan hana pinalakw-i saŋ narendra,
ṅkāna i saŋ magadhapati irikaŋ pamitran,
siddhanya iki tan asuwe manūtana asiḥ,
ndā nyā saṅhulun iki sopanā narendra*

Āpan byakta magadhanātha rakwa mitra,
sāsiŋ pintanĕn ika saṅhulun kasiddha,
yadyan kimpuruṣapurī winehakĕnya,
saŋ nātha druma muliha iŋ swarājya tuṣṭa*

tan len hetu nika patūta saŋ narendra,
mwaŋ sakweḥ nira ratu sewaka i mahīja,
henak taŋ bhuwana sukha ŋ jagat subhīkṣa,
nora ŋ wighna maraṇa tan hana irikaŋ rāt*

tan saṅkeŋ wĕdi nika saṅhulun samitra,
nöb niŋ buddhi mara tinūt nika awijil siḥ,
krodha i citta pinaḍĕman waneḥ wināśa,
yekā n dhīra ṅaran ikā n makambĕk ekā*

nyā taŋ duhkha winiparīta de nikaŋ len,
kewalya apagĕḥ i kadhīran iŋ swacitta,
tan mahyun mamalĕsa yan tĕka anahāsa,
prajñā rakwa ṅaran ira n prasiddha dhīra*

wwaŋ pwa anūtakĕn i manaḥnya duṙwiweka,
göŋ krodhā maṅucapakĕn wikalpamātra,
tan dwa alaḥ lĕkas ika riŋ swakāṙyya meman,
yekā n mūḍha hala nikaŋ wwaŋ alpamitra*

nyā ŋ wwaŋ śakti juga kuraŋ wiweka yukti,
yan polaḥ sahasa tan eraŋ iŋ kināṙyya,
ya pwa ikā capala ṅaranya tan wruḥ iŋ rāt,
akweḥ māti pinati pāpa niŋ tumiṅhal*

śakti i mitra wĕnaŋ ika atuluŋ kaduhkhan,
maṅga atoha pati rumakṣa riŋ pamitran,
saŋ kṣepanya hana lĕwiḥ nikaŋ swamitra,
de saŋ wruḥ karaṇa nira n harĕp samitra*

lāwan teki muwaḥ anuŋ rĕṅön narendra,
an saŋ nātha ri magadha atiduhkhabhāra,
de ny-a anak nira tinawan ry-anak narendra,
niṙdoṣa amĕŋ-amĕŋ ulaḥ kawālaśīlan*

luṅha aṅlālana mara riŋ wanāntara adoḥ,
ndā līla aburu-buru rakwa yañ cinidra,
nāhan hetu magadhanātha yan masĕṅhit,
ry-a anak saŋ narapati haywa tan prayatna*

len prāgjyotiṣanagara alilaŋ katunwan,
de ny-a anak haji wiparīta duṣṭabuddhi,
wruḥ ṅwaŋ yan kaharĕpa saŋ narendraputra,
jātinya n raray anasaṙ sakeŋ suśīla*

ndaḥ yekā n puhara nikaŋ watĕk mahīja,
an saŋ nātha tan umaraḥ ṅ anak ri śīla,
saŋ sādhw-a apituwi katūt tĕkap nikaŋ len,
yan byaktā humĕnĕŋ anon ulaḥ wimāṙgga*

saŋ nātha anak atiśaya i wĕgig nikeŋ rāt,
nyāma ikā hala tumibā mare narāṙyya,
yan tan wwantĕn upaśama iŋ watĕk ratu ṅkā,
ṅkāna i saŋ ratu saŋ apakṣa bhūmiputra*

aṅhiŋ kapwa yan akĕnoha de narendra,
mitran de nrĕpati siraŋ watĕk ratu ṅkā,
towin maṅkana kaharĕp niraŋ narendra,
tan len saŋ kṣitija jagattrayekawīra*

.  saŋ śatruntapa maṅkana ujaṙ ira saŋ gada apyak asahur,
om siṅgiḥ sawuwus narendra tuhu yukti riŋ kadi kita,
nora wwaŋ hiḍĕp i ṅhulun maḍana buddhi saŋ narapati,
prajñanta iku kapuṅguṅan bisa tiwas wuwusta rinĕṅö*

tan maṅkā pwa ya denta mojaṙ ajule kita n wruḥ awuwus,

Āpan prāṙthana ni ṅhulun yadukula n para iŋ ripukula*

ndā śabda i gaganāntarāla karĕṅö lana ajaya-jaya,

nāhan liŋ saŋ gada akras rasanya,
ṅkāna i saŋ dūta śatruntapākhya,
atyanta iŋ kaṙṇnaśūla aṅlare twas,
hrū mwaŋ gaṇḍy-a aṅĕne tuṙ paḍanya*

tan doṣā saŋ gada apan turuŋ wruḥ*

Āpan mitra ṅhulun de narendra,

nāhan ta ya ujaṙ niraŋ ugrasena,
śatruntapa asĕṅhit ikaŋ mukha abāŋ,
dhīra aṅĕnĕb twas nira bahnitulya,
uśwāsa mādrĕs kumĕtĕṙ sira ujar*

Āḥ saŋ narendra ahuka tan pahīṅan,
de niŋ maśabda aṅlarani ŋ kadi ṅwaŋ,
ndā tan panaṅgĕl manaḥ iŋ samaṅke,
heman wayahta atuha buddhi mūḍha*

pora adhama ambĕkta lĕwiḥ kaṭuṅka,
denta pwa met puṇya taman mara asiḥ,
tan buddhi niŋ sādhu wiweka riŋ rāt,
tuccha iŋ sabhā de ni kaduṙyyaśanta*

sojaṙtta tekaŋ pawaraḥ kadibyan,
solaḥta tekaŋ pawaraḥ ta śīla,
tiṅhalta tekaŋ pawaraḥ kaduṣṭan,
nora ŋ kasādhun karatun ta meman*

caṅkyak wĕnaṅta ujaṙ aninda-ninda,
dusprajña towin kita hīnaśakti,
sampe rikaŋ wruḥ kita hīnabuddhi,
tan yogya riŋ gāgak aṅalpa haṅsa*

mojaṙ wawaŋ śry-a ahuka sādara alon,
saŋ nātha śatruntapa haywa maṅkā,
denta awuwus duṙyyaśa rājadūta,
mlecchaswabhāwa aṅucap iŋ kadi ṅwaŋ*

atyanta yuktinya wuwuskw-i ṅūni,
saṅke pamitran karaṇaṅkw-ataṅgĕḥ,
swasthanta de niŋ pitutuṙ ku tan len,
tan saṅśayanta ṅwaŋ iki n hiḍĕpku*

maṅke pwa sandeha kita i wuwusku,
ṅwaŋ ywa ika paścatparita n panonta,
buddhinta tātan papamitran aṅdoḥ,
siṅgiḥ manaḥ niŋ paḍa bhadrakāpi*

nāhan panonkw-i iki  kaduṙyyaśanta,
an bhūmi saŋ wabhru ya ta inalapta,
lāwan lĕmaḥ saŋ krĕtadhaṙmma kālap,
sāmpun lĕmaḥ saŋ gada tanpa śeṣa*

mitranta towi ika kabeḥ rikāna,
wandhyā tĕkap niŋ pamitra tĕkapta,
Āstām tikaŋ len inalap lĕmaḥnya,
wwat niŋ marĕk riŋ naraka atiduṣṭa*

prāgjyotiṣādi ikaŋ anāṙyyadeśa,
yekā n karĕṅw-a awiwatāra tuṅka,
sakweḥ nika asyandana kapwa ninda,
Āpan tanora pwa ya waṙṇnabheda*

ṅkāna iṣṭa niŋ strī paḍa tan karakṣa,
cora swabhāwanya makambĕk-ambĕk,
wwāgan tan uṅgwi i nagari iŋ udeśa,
pan mogha duhkhanta kapaṙwwan iŋ strī*

nāhan ta liŋ śry-a ahuka göŋ wirodha,
sāmpun hinaywan yadu-wrĕṣṇiwīra,
krodha aṅkas-aṅkas ta mahodara ujar,
śabda atĕrĕḥ tulya gĕrĕḥ gumĕntĕr*

Ꜽ saŋ narendra ahuka haywa madwa,
denta awuwus tan wuwus iŋ sinādhu,
tan swaŋ ratu wrĕddha kita alpaśīla,
siṅgiḥ kaṭuṅka adhipa hīnabuddhi*

saŋ nātha śatruntapa sādhubuddhi,
pājaṙ nira i saŋ yadu-wrĕṣṇiwīra,
mogha ikihĕn yañ cinalan tĕkapta,
swāgöŋ krĕtinta iku dumeḥ ta māna*

byakta ika pājaṙ niŋ aji praśasta,
an rwa ikanaŋ tan sahasāna petĕn,
wwaŋ māna riŋ paṇḍita śāstrahīna,
yekā n paḍa mwaŋ paśu tulya saṙppa*

pratyeka niŋ wwaŋ humiḍĕp ry-awaknya,
śaktiprawīra aku lĕwiḥ ya liŋnya,
tan wruḥ ta yan sora tĕkap nikaŋ len,
mānanya hetunya n aṅalpa riŋ len*

yan wwaŋ sinewa wruha ta iŋ manewa,
sojaṙ nikaŋ sewaka tañ calāna,
Āyogya yogyanya n ade tan aṅgon,
rapwan lanā nīti nika awaraḥ siḥ*

wwaŋ mūḍha dāgha iŋ sukha tan pamitra,
ndi ikā n panĕmwa ŋ sukhabhāra riŋ rāt,
tĕkwan tan ārĕmburi don ikaŋ len,
tan yogya sewan ṅuniweḥ parāna*

saŋ nātha maṅke tan atĕn samitra,
lāwan watĕk bhūmija śūraśakti,
dūrantara ikaŋ karatunta nitya,
yan tan kita aminta rinakṣan i ṅwaŋ*

Ājñā nira śry-a asuradꜽtyanātha,
muṅgwi hyaŋ indra alaḥ anūt prabhakti,
yekā n tĕka an uṅgu ri saŋ narendra,
donanya maṅrakṣa rikaŋ swarājya*

yogyanta cihnanya yadin prabhaktya,
wwantĕn purī nātha kasi inalapta,
yekā n tikā n sūṅakĕnanta śīghra,
saŋ nātha śatruntapa sopananta*

nya anak jarāsandha ṅaran pratīpa,
mwaŋ tekanaŋ strī katawan rikāna,
haywa akalib sambahakĕn kabeḥnya,
ndak ton wiśīṙṇnanta mĕne walātĕn*

henak tikā strīnta kabeḥ sapawwat,
paṅhĕlya rapwan kita tan kahĕntya,
Āpan hana ŋ śāstra ri loka maṅke,
saṙwwapraṇī sādara māṙddhanāta*

yadyan kita asowaya tan pasūṅa,
meṅgal kĕta ŋ daṇḍawadha i kita asru,
Āpan siraŋ bhoma sira antakanta,
tambā ndi tekaŋ tulakĕnta mrĕtyu*

saŋ wabhru mojaṙ tumuluy manambut,
dhik hāḥ haḍā kaśmala dūta pāpa,
denya awuwus tan wuwus iŋ kinonkon,
jambat patiḥ jañjan ujaṙmu duṣṭa*

ndi ikaŋ mahīputra wĕnaŋ tumiṅhal,
ri śrī upendra atiśaya iŋ kaśaktin,
yāwat wĕnaŋ saŋ naraka n tumĕṅhā,
tāwat rĕmĕk syuḥ dinĕdĕl mukhanya*

yadyan kaḍatwan ya tĕka iŋ lĕmaḥnya,
salwānya sakweḥnya tĕka iŋ gunuŋnya,
saṅgan ta de śrī nrĕpa krĕṣṇa dadya,
himpĕṙnya gowaṙddhana riŋ maḍaṅhan*

sakwehmu tekaŋ baladꜽtyasaṅgha,
hĕnti ika de śrī baladewanātha,
bĕntaṙ bubaṙ lwiṙ yamunā gatinya,
de niŋ wulukw-a akas agöŋ malaṇḍĕp*

Ꜽ koŋ kaṭuṅka adhama dūta tiṙyyak,
tan ton taṅankw-a antakatulya teki,
tonton uripmu n tĕkanaṅkwa hasta,
yan yogya mātyānana dūta tuccha*

Āḥ dhā kawiḥnya ŋ ratu wabhru mojar,
dūrantara iki n tuhu hanta rota,
tan wruḥ ta ko yan si mahodara aku,
priḥ ndak hamūk yan tuhu ko prawīra*

maṅke yadin patyana ko rĕbutku,
nora anuluŋ ko sy-ana taṅgalĕṅkwa,
tañ cakra taŋ cakra hiḍĕpku denta,
taṙ wĕdya de niŋ hala sañjataṅku*

nāhan ta ya ujaṙnya mahodara apyak,
lāgy-a anĕpak bhūmi musus taṅanya,
krodha ika saŋ yādawa-wrĕṣṇiwīra,
tan dwa aṅgrĕgut kapwa paḍa aṅagĕm prĕp*

saŋ satyaka agyā n paṅadĕg tumandaŋ,
saŋ sāmba maṅsö tumuluy mataṅguḥ,
Ꜽ haywa maṅka amĕjahi ŋ kinonkon,
sugyan kita aṅambaha śāsananta*

yekān tumiṅhal si mahodara ujar,
cehāhaḥ āḥ toḥ mabutĕŋ kabehmu,
nā liŋnya mamrĕp saka hīrabajra,
horag tĕka ikaŋ wataṅan tĕkapnya*

śīghra aṅadĕg krodha tĕhĕṙnya mojar,
saŋ wrĕṣṇi tiṅhal muliha aku maṅke,
Ꜽ satyaka bwat lari tūt lariṅku,
yan wāni ko ndak tĕlĕsik cĕṅĕlmu*

nā liŋnya luṅha adrĕs ike larinya,
lāwan kaliṅgādhipa taṙ panoliḥ,
tan waṙṇnanĕn lampaḥ ikā n paḍa agyā,
prāpta iŋ mahīputra sĕḍĕŋ tinaṅkil*

mojaṙ ta ya i saŋ kṣitisūta śīghra,
an waṅla saŋ yādawa śatrubhūta,
saŋ bhoma sakrodha wawaŋ kabāṅan,
maṅgĕḥ tĕhĕṙ maṅgĕtĕm aṅgakāra*

<bhadralalita>:80.

wĕkasan maśabda sira hāḥ kapūhan aku de nikaŋ yadukula,
ri wĕnaŋnya maṅkana wuwusnya tan mawĕdi mātya deṅku ya kabeḥ,
syapa teka yogya lawanaṅkwa krĕṣṇa baladewa wiṣṭya kĕpĕla,
ṅuniweḥ tikaŋ ratu makādi pāṙtha ramĕsĕnkwa tulya kuluban*

aku kāṙwwa hasta mubura i puranya tak arowaṅa aṅhapuyana,
gulanaṅku rāḥnya ripu ni ṅhulun rahatanaṅkwa riŋ karatala,
kalawan ya deṅku śiraḥ iŋ musuḥ rĕmĕk utĕknya santĕna nikā,
saphalanya ku n warĕga kīṙttya moha maharĕp yaśa iŋ pabharatan*

na wuwus mahāsurapati prakāśa sumahuṙ ta cedi ri sira,
prabhu yogya maṅkat asĕn aṙddha sāmpun arĕpat watĕk ratu kabeḥ,
hana paṙwwata atiśaya rāmya rewataka ya uṅsirĕn saŋ ahulun,
sĕsĕpĕn kaḍatwan ikanaŋ watĕk yadu mataŋnya haywa wiluma*

atha maṅkana ujaṙ ira cedi maṅkat ika saŋ mahāsurapati,
kalawan watĕk ratu makādi cedi magadhendra kaṙṇna tumuluy,
gumuruḥ prakampita humuŋ ri gobraja tĕkap nikaŋ surak awū,
kĕtug iŋ mahotpata mawantaḥ adbhuta binaṇḍuṅan gajapati*

alilaŋ tikaŋ sakahawan wanādri matĕmaḥ tĕgal parawaśa,
giri windhyapāṙśśwa nikahĕn lĕbūnya kumukus tinūb nikaŋ aṅin,
kṣitiputra muṅgu rikanaŋ wimāna hana riŋ nabhastala sira,
iniriŋ nikāŋ asura yakṣa rākṣasa piśāca nāga wĕki sök*

tadanantara krama ḍatĕŋ sira atiśaya ghūṙṇnita iŋ giriwana,
irika aŋ arewataka r-uṅgu saŋ kṣitisuta atigaṙwwa masiga,
kumupak humuŋ prakaṭa śabda niŋ balagaṇa aśwa lakṣa niyuta,
saka loṙ kidul paṅuhuḥ iŋ balāsura sĕḍĕŋ haneŋ awaŋ-awaŋ*

tuwi koṭi-koṭi niyutā gaja aśwa ratha riŋ mahītala sĕsök,
ikanaŋ haneŋ gagana tanpa saṅkhya gumuruḥ marok jaladhara,
pakilat ni teja ni sihuŋ nikāŋ asura rākṣasa aṅarab-arab,
kadi waṙṣa bahni dumilaḥ katonan i dilaḥ nikaŋ mata mabāŋ*

irikā n paḍa awrĕg ikanaŋ wwaŋ īŋ asura duṙbala awri malayū,
malupā ry-anak-rabi nika apasaḥ pijĕṙ amet hurip masusupan,
sinĕsĕb waneḥ pinaṅan iŋ piśāca ya turaḥ-turaḥnya tinawan,
ikanaŋ mamoṙ ya maṅusi i kawanwan anaṅis maminta hinurip*

paḍa śīṙṇna wanwa nira saŋ watĕk yadu tĕlas tinunwan aradin,
tĕka sewu thāni pinupuḥ sakambaḥ apaḍaŋ tĕlas parawaśa,
ikana iŋ huruŋnya ya liniṇḍihan kahibĕkan kawāhan asura,
kadi raṅraṅan kapĕnuhan wĕrĕḥ tĕkap ikaŋ dhwaja aputiḥ atap*

<waṅśapatrapatita>:81.
– ⏑ ⏑ | - ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 16

kāla niraŋ mahīsuta ḍatĕŋ prasama saha bala,
gaṙjjita saŋ watĕk yadu mapak sama mapagakĕna,
hetu nira atihaŋ haṅun-aṅun wahu-wahu tinĕkan,
sañjata rakwa suṅsuṅakĕna iŋ ripu tĕka sahasa*

kweḥ nira saŋ watĕk ratu sahāya paḍa sira hana,
śālya wirāṭa len drupada rukmanarapatisuta,
bāhlika somadatta paḍa śakti gati nira kabeḥ,
saŋ nrĕpa winda sānak anuwinda tahu ta malaga*

saŋ naranātha wabhru krĕtadhaṙmma paḍa sira hana,
tuṣṭa kabeḥ tĕlas pinaribhoga sira saha bala,
de nira saŋ narendra harimūṙtti masĕgĕḥ akadaŋ,
riŋ tadanantara aṅuliḥ-uliḥ ta sira riŋ ulaha*

saŋ nrĕpa śālya mojaṙ apa dāya narapati huwus,
byakta ḍatĕŋ musuḥ nrĕpati haywa juga palĕ-palĕḥ,
saṅgatanĕn papag prasamanĕn sakahana nikahĕn,
yeka nihan phalanya katuluŋ wiṣaya haji kabeḥ*

yan masuwe tuluŋ nrĕpati wiṣṭi biṣama nikahĕn,
ṅel niŋ atambaka alaḥ alajĕṙ lĕṅĕn apuli-puliḥ,
ambĕk ikā ndya saŋ prabhu dĕlön tĕka ta wawarĕṅöḥ,
sugyan anambaha iŋ musuḥ alĕḥ mawĕdi sinahasan*

saŋ naranātha śālya na wuwus nira maṅarahakĕn,
mojaṙ ikā nrĕpa drupada haywa haji raga-ragan,
petĕn upāya niŋ wwaŋ anuŋ oliha musuḥ agalak,
yan baraṅa aprayoga kĕna ḍaṇḍa biṣama kahala*

de nika saŋ krĕta aṙtha rikanaŋ samara tuladana,
śakti wineḥ rumowaṅana ḍaṇḍa nira lĕkasana,
yatna sira i tibā ni tĕwĕk iŋ ripu yan amalĕsa,
suśrama lāghawa n panĕmu cidra mamisani musuḥ*

wwaŋ pwa ya śakti kewala kaśaktin ika pada n adun,
tan wruḥ i cidra niŋ para pijĕṙ guragaḍa malaga,
tañ jriḥ inambulan lwat ika rakwa paṅayaya nikā,
māti kĕna iŋ gutuk pwa ya tĕmaḥnya wani-wani pitik*

wwaŋ tinĕkan prayatnani tĕkap niŋ amapaga musuḥ,
minta sahāya siddha pinalaṙ-palaṙ iŋ alĕkasa,
haywa tatan prayatna bala saŋ nrĕpati wulatana,
byakta kĕḍik nikaŋ bala mataŋnya n aṅiṅĕt-iṅĕta*

nāhan ujaṙ niraŋ drupada bāhlika sira sumahur,
sājña haji ndya ta uliha nikaŋ tinĕkan akabĕta,
wiṣṭi tikāŋ anak rabi yadin makaliba tinĕkan,
ṅhiŋ ta mapag ḍatĕŋ pati hurip saphala tan awiraŋ*

kweḥ nikanaŋ musuḥ tan ika taṅgĕlĕn iŋ amapaga,
yan kagiriŋ pisan-pisaniṅun ya hana mapuliha,
wūk ta sakeŋ wurinya caturaṅga saka ri hiriṅan,
nyāma ratunya kāri mapuliḥ kucupi ta ya rĕbut*

saŋ nrĕpa somadatta sumahuṙ taha tan iku bisa,
antyakĕna ata sāhasa nikaŋ musuḥ amasukana,
sāmpun ikā ṇ ḍatĕŋ tĕhĕṙ anunwani maṅamaḥ-amaḥ,
gyāt ya pisan t-atuṅkĕbana wūk prasama saha bala*

nyāta nika alayū kahala tūt wuri nika susuni,
ton ta patoṙnya duṙbala nikā ya mari macatura,
kāsrĕka de nikaŋ kuda liman ya marĕbuta tawan,
māti ya kedĕkan ta tĕkap iŋ gajapati maṅuliŋ*

mojaṙ ikā saŋ aṙjjuna hade biṣama dahat ikā,
ambĕk ikaŋ musuḥ mulata riŋ humĕnĕṅa tinĕkan,
byakta tĕpĕt ndatan kajagana pwa ya mamarĕpĕki,
wiṣṭi tĕmĕn praŋ iŋ wwaŋ atahĕn-tahĕna tĕlas alaḥ*

rañca manaḥ niŋ apraṅa manoliḥ i wuri niyata,
kepwana de ny-anak rabi nikā n prajurit alĕkasa,
rigrig i rowaŋ iŋ wwaŋ alaga alaḥ awĕdi maṅaliḥ,
haywa hinerakĕñ juga tĕkap niŋ amusuḥ agalak*

maṅkata rakwa mon karuhunan ṅwaŋ amapagakĕna,
maṅkana liŋ saŋ aṙjjuna mapakṣa mijila tumuluy,
śrī naranātha krĕṣṇa mawuwus rari diwasa kita,
sāhasa tan taha ambĕka ni rowaŋ iŋ aṅiṅĕt-iṅĕt*

tiṅkaḥ i saŋ krĕtāṙtha rikanaŋ sama-sama mapagĕḥ,
taṅgwana niŋ prawīra sira saŋ wruha rikaŋ alĕkas,
sandhi ni de niŋ apraŋ awilĕt warahakĕna nira,
tolihĕn iŋ wineḥ guṇa mamiṅkisa musuḥ asusun*

yan ruhuna pwa ta apraṅa sakeŋ raray amaragaṅa,
yadyapin oliha iki n aphala apa tan ulaha nikā,
piṅrwa tiwas kasambya ni huripnya biṣama rinĕbut,
nora ya meman-eman i pati i pati-pati tumĕḍun*

yeka ta kāri hetu nika saŋ wani tan iman-iman,
yan pakadoñ jayā nira rikaŋ praŋ aṅiriṅi naya,
wīra rare-rara ika pinakālas ira kahilaṅan,
rodra katon kasiṅhan ira n aṅdĕmaki musuḥ ira*

niṙ kawiwekan iŋ daṅu kĕta ikaŋ ulaḥ iŋ alaga,
ambĕk i rowaŋ iŋ wwaŋ ikanaŋ paḍa wawarĕṅĕnĕn,
byūha wineḥ mata ika pasaṅĕn wruha ta ri hiriṅan,
tañ jriḥ i wūk nikaŋ ripukula apagĕḥ ulaḥ-ulahĕn*

tĕkwan ikā hade karuhuna aṅlĕkasi kita rari,
tambay iŋ eñjiŋ iṅwaŋ iki maṅkata parĕŋ apisan,
towi kulĕm ḍatĕŋ tuhun adandana ta sira kabeḥ,
ndā si gaṇākumāra ya matuṅgwa kuwu gati nikā*

Āḥ pwa gaṇākumāra tanayaṅku kita makĕmita,
mwaŋ bala wāhananta ya ta dum paḍa maparĕpata,
haywa tatan prayatna rahina iŋ kulĕm ika midĕra,
denya haṅĕt-haṅĕt gati nikaŋ nagara kadi daṅū*

bhāra nikaŋ musuḥ ya tinahāṅkw-aṅapuyana kuwu,
rākṣasa duṣṭadūta ya niśācara mamĕṅi-mĕṅi,
dānawadꜽtya sūkṣma ni lĕkasnya yan akira-kira,
len hana bañcananya-ya ta kawruhi satĕmaḥ ikā*

haywa manaṅgaḥ alpa ri gawenta kawĕkas iŋ umaḥ,
bhāra tĕmĕn kĕta ŋ sinarabhāra makĕmita kuwu,
sādhu huwus kapaṙccaya kaśaktin ira tika lĕwiḥ,
nyāta mataŋnya yogya kita kantuna pagĕhakĕna*

sāmpun ira aṅutus matĕlasan ta para ratu mahöm,
kapwa mare pakuwwan ika taṇḍa nira ya winaraḥ,
saŋ naranātha saŋ pininaṅan sira kinasĕgĕhan,
kīṙṇna haneŋ tĕgal bala nira akuwu-kuwu sahana*

taṇḍa niraŋ watĕk ratu paḍa atihaŋ asira-siran,
ghūṙṇnita tan pasaṅkya karĕṅö tabĕ-tabĕhan ikā,
len ta saŋ asrama iŋ lĕbuḥ aḍeŋ hulun ika sabatĕk,
ri hyun ikā n katiṅhalana kapwa mawuwuḥ adĕmak*

tan sipi de nira amahayu sañjata paḍa mahalĕp,
riŋ sajuru prawīra saka sātus akaraḥ akaluŋ,
len ikana alĕṅĕn bapaŋ asiṅhĕl aṅatus-atusi,
rohan ika iŋ lĕbuḥ pamĕdi maṅrĕpĕhi lawan ikā*

mwaŋ hana taṇḍa mākrĕp irika aṅulaḥ aṅiṅĕt-iṅĕt,
ndā krĕpana akĕkĕḥ ta n aharĕp mahuluna makuwu,
ṅhiŋ ya barat ginöṅakĕn ika iŋ hĕlĕm ulaḥ agalak,
tan pakasoṙ yan iŋ lĕbuḥ asāra rĕbuta palagan*

wāhu mapañji-pañji karika amalaṙ apamĕgĕta,
sañjata kaṙwwa tuṅgul alĕsĕḥ miṅĕṙ aduluṙ aḍeŋ,
bhāwa nikā n umunduṙ i tĕlasnya mapuliḥ abaṅĕt,
yaṙ mapiliḥ wuwusnya ri patuṅgul ika ciṅa-ciṅaḥ*

rāmya para prawīra saŋ anaṇḍaŋ akaraḥ akaluŋ,
len asipiŋ-sipiŋ kuniŋ arampak arĕja malayū,
mwaŋ hinatak sisiṙ sakala söḥ kagurilap ahulap,
wadwa haji ika cihna niki yan krĕtayaśa riŋ ayun*

tan wulat iŋ hawan salaḥ ulat mulat i saŋ aṅuṅaŋ,
mogha tibā kasĕmsĕm amiraḥ mukha nika sinurak*

ambuluṅanya gaṅśa kadi ghaṇṭa humuŋ awurahan*

sampunya n paṅinum nikaŋ bala kabeḥ yaya aŋ pura humuŋ,

göṅgöṅĕn ta manaḥ para prajurit ahyun apraŋ alawas,

Āstām saŋ rĕṣi-śꜽwa-sogata makādi ḍaŋ hyaŋ ajapa*

saŋ lāgi inucap iŋ katuṅtaṅan i kīṙtti riŋ raṇasabhā*

<gadyakāra>:83.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ –  ⏑| –  ⏑ ⏑|  ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 29

ri tĕlas ira an mijil sahana saŋ watĕk yadu lawan watĕk ratu humuŋ tikaŋ bala kabeḥ,
pĕnuḥ irikaŋ tĕgal gahana gahwara alas alilaŋ wiśīṙṇna tĕkap iŋ ratha akuda liman,
tuhu kadi megha riŋ kapitu kāṅinan winulatan pĕtĕŋ dhwaja nira akilat kĕlab ikā,
paḍahi lawan taroñji murawa apratidhwani kĕtug ni kĕṇḍaŋ iŋ aroha ghora gumuruḥ*

salĕsĕk i lampaḥ iŋ balasamūha tan papĕgatan sakeŋ purasabhā pwa tan paligaran,

iṅut-iṅutĕn lana inubatakĕn cucuk ni pikulanya meḥ anukak an kacuṇḍuk iŋ wuri*

hana ta makuṇḍaŋ aṇḍarat i tuṇḍasāra mapĕṅiŋ ri kuṇḍaŋ ika tan pakālib apulut,

rasika kaṅelan āpan amikul bĕkĕlnya kalasanya hambuluṅan awrat abwat anĕtĕl,

{gadyakāra}:86.4

sumĕlaŋ aṅodwad iŋ rabi nikā n kumat kabaranaŋ burat-burat abaŋ wĕtĕŋnya n agĕḍe yateka sagĕnuk*

tiḍak ḍikĕtahui
<dhrĕti>:84.

luṅhā ŋ lampaḥ saŋ yadu saṅke dwārawatī śīghra paḍa agyā,
kāwit-kāwit saŋ rĕṣi durwāśa ika cumuṇḍuk nrĕpa krĕṣṇa,
rukṣa akurw-a aṅel alapā mantuk sira saṅkeŋ śiwatīṙtha,
siddhāsiddha ŋ wāk śapatha iṅgal yan mapĕṅiŋ towi kuraŋ twas*

wruḥ pwa śrī krĕṣṇa i bhagawān durwāśa sira n paṇḍitasiddhi,
agyā-gyā-gyā yan tumurun saṅkeŋ ratha sāmpun ta manambaḥ,
enak pwa wruḥ saŋ rĕṣi yan trĕpti ika kabhaktin haji ri twas,
menak ta ambĕk niścaya mājaṙ sāṙjjawa somya arūm aśabda*

hehe saŋ bhumyādhipati ndaḥ wehi kami i kahyun ikiŋ twas,
alpa ṅhiŋ tekaŋ labuhan donkw-i i kita lāwan baladewa,
kahyunkw-a antukta aṅliwĕt āpan śuddha pawitra amrĕta sākṣāt,
ndaḥ ṅkāna i rājyanta tika anuŋ yogya kami n wehana denta*

nāhan liŋ saŋ paṇḍya ta kady-a apet karaṇa i saŋ naranātha,
śrī krĕṣṇa anaṅkṣepa ri sojaṙ saŋ rĕṣi śīghra aṅanumoda,
bhāgya n wwantĕn ry-antusa saŋ paṇḍya amuhara aŋ trĕpti ri citta,
ndā santabya agöŋ kĕta rānak saŋ yati herĕn samuhūṙtta*

pun pāṙthā pun rukma tikaŋ konĕn pun anārathyakĕna praŋ,
nāhan liŋ saŋ bhūpati krĕṣṇa aminta ri saŋ paṇḍita herĕn,
sāmpun luṅha ikaŋ pakudan maṅhundaṅa pāṙtha nrĕpa rukma,
śīghra prāpta ikā sira kāliḥ śrī nrĕpa krĕṣṇa ata manantwa*

<bhadralalita>:85.
⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 21

hari ni ṅhulun daki saŋ aṙjjuna ṅwaŋ awĕkas-wĕkas pwa ri kita,
kalawan ta saŋ nrĕpati rukma rakṣa nikanaŋ watĕk yadubala,
kita kāṙwwa sāra śaraṇā nikaŋ praŋ aku mantuka iŋ swanagara,
sira saŋ mahāṙṣi sira ta ikihĕn labuhana aṅhuwus brata nira*

liŋ ira anĕhĕṙ muliḥ atīta teki sira saŋ narendra wĕkasan,
sira saŋ watĕk ratu kabeḥ mareŋ pabharatan paḍa ahyun ayaśa,
ikanaŋ bala prakaṭa kātara amalaku śatru rākṣasabala,
alapa apraŋ abrata kasiṅhan agya malawas maṅanti labuhan*

kaparĕk samīpa ni pakuwwa-kuwwan ikanaŋ musuḥ wahu katon,
irikāŋ arewataka sök tĕka iŋ suku-sukunya tan paligaran,
mwaŋ ikaŋ haneŋ alas agöŋ lawan wiṣamawanwa tan kawulatan,
pasamūhan iŋ dhwani nikaŋ liman kuda ya tan pasaṅkhya gumuruḥ*

sira saŋ dhanañjaya lawan siraŋ nrĕpati rukma dāya gĕlara,
makarānana ika winaṅun kramanya sira kāṙwwa muṅgu ri tĕṅaḥ,
makawaktra saŋ yadukulaprawīra pinakādi sāmba niśaṭha,
mwaŋ ike saŋ ulmuka lawan ta satyaka sudhīra śāraṇa waneḥ*

nrĕpati druma mwaŋ ika saŋ narendra basudewa muṅgu ri wuri,
nrĕpa śālya len drupada bāhlika agra ri tĕṅĕn suṅut gati nira,
nrĕpa winda lāwan anuwinda saŋ prabhu wirāṭanātha ri kiwa,

ri tĕlasnya n enak apagĕḥ pratiṅkaḥ i gĕlaṙ niraŋ yadu kabeḥ,
sira saŋ mahīsuta tĕlas tumiṅhal atigaṙwwa sahya masiga,
amusus taṅan tan ari maṅgĕtĕm tĕkap ikaŋ kamānawibhawan,
aharĕp makoliha ri saŋ narendra harimūṙtti tan hana waneḥ*

winaraḥ sira i taya narendra krĕṣṇa baladewa de niŋ utusan,
yatikā n wiwal manaḥ ira awiśeṣa ri siraŋ watĕk yadu mijil,
maṅĕsaḥ lanā mulati laṇḍĕp iŋ lipuŋ amoghaśakti hinawin,
mwaŋ ikaŋ gada awĕsi satal pinañjĕṙ aṅadĕg tiniṅhalan ira*

nrĕpa cedi kaṙṇna magadhendra saŋ winidhi de mahāsurapati,
mijila irikaŋ samara maṅlagāna ri siraŋ watĕk yadu ḍatĕŋ,
iriṅĕn tĕkap niŋ asuraprawīra paṅarĕp nikaŋ praŋ irikā,
pinakādhikāra para taṇḍa saŋ kṣitisuta atiśakti suyaśa*

ri wijil nira aṙyya magadha apaḍa ahalĕp anuṅgaŋ iŋ gajapati,
tĕka sewu taŋ liman agöŋ hane wuri tĕlas kabeḥ makawaca,
turaga apipit piraŋ iwū wwaŋ iŋ ratha magöŋ arampak atatā,
bala pādarakṣaka pĕnuḥ wajanya mahulap tĕwĕknya lumarap*

milu teka saŋ ratu samāṅjuru prasama tan hana ika makutis,
paḍa ta ahalĕp halĕp i saŋ prawīra maratha ika len aturaga,
papupul ni sañjata nikaŋ samaṅkana wutaḥnya tan papĕgatan,
kadi wāḥ gunuŋ saha watunya śīghra gumuluŋ tĕka iŋ pabharatan*

milu dꜽtya yakṣa tĕka riŋ niśācara piśāca nāga ya tumūt,
apa tan pasaṅkhya saha wāhananya paḍa ta ahalĕp lĕwi-lĕwiḥ,
pakatap-katap ni tĕṅĕranya bāŋ hana putiḥ kuniŋ mwaŋ ahirĕŋ,
kadi megha sontĕn i surup bhaṭāra rawi rūpa niŋ dhwaja kabeḥ*

ri tĕṅaḥ ta ya uṅgwan ira saŋ narendra magadhādhirāja pinupul,

kadi ta aruḥ iŋ jaladhi riŋ gunuŋ karaŋ i piṅgiṙ adrĕs aṅarus*

tadanantara krama ḍatĕŋ ta cedipati tulya sāgara pasaŋ,
amasuk juluk-juluk ikaŋ bala akraḥ akaraŋ limanya maruhur,

amaḍĕm ḍarat hyu mulat iŋ pratiṅkaḥ i gĕlaṙ nikaŋ bala kabeḥ*

pagĕlaṙ niraŋ nrĕpati kaṙṇna duṙggama lawan samānta nrĕpati,
kadi paṙwwata alas atahĕn wana akrĕp aṅadĕg lĕyĕp winulatan,

saŋ awaṅgarāja sira moŋ siriŋ galak ira ahyun oliha musuḥ*

ikanaŋ prawīra bala dꜽtya yā karalawaktra raktawadana,
nayaśālya duṙṇnaya tarakṣa senawiṣama mwaŋ apratihata,
paḍa śaktiwīra tahu ta alaga iŋ samara ṅūni riŋ lagi-lagi,
kawĕdi i surālaya lana amikāra sira saŋ watĕk hyaŋ alara*

hana yakṣa śūra tinahā ṅaranya bahukīṙtti sādhanawaśa,
subala prajamba suwana pradhāna rĕṇabhit subaddha guṇawān,
wigakaṙṇna sāma bahukaṙṇnaka aruḥ-aruhan kabeḥ wija-wijaḥ,
kadi ta awĕrö sahana saŋ watĕk drawinabhuk marorawa humuŋ*

tuhan iŋ niśācarabala aṅiriŋ ri sira saŋ narendra katiga,

si sumolilambu ya parĕŋ mijil paḍa manuṅgaŋ iŋ liman agöŋ*

bala nāga mukhya nika si prasikta si sudhāṅgana ika biniṣa,
makanātha ŋ adrawalika prasiddha ya musuḥ saŋ aṙjjuna tĕmĕn,

milu taŋ piśācabala durwrĕtākhya wigatākṣa kakṣawirama,

si jitāṅgabhaṅgaka śiraghnabuddhi si wiwaṙjjakaṙmma wiratha,

kalayāwanendrasuta muṅgu loṙ kadi limut pĕtĕŋ tiniṅalan,

humarĕp ri saŋ nrĕpati windarāja panihuŋ gatinya tinitaḥ,

bala dꜽtya rowaŋ ika śakti saŋ karalawaktra raktawadana,

saha yakṣa sādhanawana prajamba suwana pradhāna winani,
saha rākṣasa adi nikana prajaṅga mahiṣāṅga siṅhawadana*

waranāga śakti si sudhāṅgana apratihata adĕmöŋ awak ikā,
tĕṅĕran wĕlaŋ-wĕlaŋ awoṙ hijo bala nika aṅdĕlĕs lari nikā,
tahu ta agawe sawa biṣa aṅluwuk lawan ulaḥ nikā n amiḍuḍak,
nda gulūnya n apraŋ awilĕt lana amiṣani śatru tulya sirarā*

ikanaŋ piśācabala mukhya kākṣawirama trikāyawipata,
kalawan si satwa si kulakṣaya atitaḥ i puṅkuran gati nikā,
panihuŋ kiwa atĕhĕṙ ikā kabeḥnya humarĕp maṅulwan agĕlar,
nrĕpa winda lāwan anuwinda bhūpati sira ika mukhya kaharĕp*

caturaṅga niŋ bala samaṅkana ika pira saṅkhya-saṅkhya nikahĕn,
humĕnĕŋ paḍa amapadĕṅan maṅanti tinĕkān paḍa anaha-nahā,
kadi sāgara sthiti tatan hana aṅin ika tulya niŋ bala kabeḥ*

tucapa ŋ sihuŋ kidul apūṙwwa tulya jalada aṅhĕmu hudan arĕs,
lumarap krĕtāla nika waṙṇna widyut awilĕt lawan layu-layu,
sarapuŋnya saŋ nrĕpa hiraṇyanābha kalawan kaliṅganrĕpati,
sasamāntabhrĕtya caturaṅga lakṣa niyuta ŋ gajendra turaga*

irikā ta dꜽtya pinatiḥ prawīra balamantri mukhya-ya kabeḥ,

saha wāhananya gaja sewu sowaŋ ika len rathāśwa niyuta,
saha pādarakṣaka nikā sahasra śatakoṭi tan patagihan*

pinakesi yakṣabala saŋ pradhāna rĕṇabhit guṇa asama-sama,
yatika ahalĕp-halĕpan iŋ prawīra makaluŋ karaḥ kawayakaḥ,

lumarap katonan ika waṙṇna wintaŋ aṅaliḥ parĕŋ larap ikā*

kalawan ta nāga maṅaran prasikta pinakādi saṅkĕp atitaḥ,
mwaŋ ikaŋ piśācabala piṇḍa sāyuta tĕkeŋ swawāhana nikā,

humarĕp ta kulwan atitaḥ kabeḥnya n umarĕp ri bāhlikapati,

i sĕḍĕŋ ikaŋ watĕk naraka wāspada i rĕpat ikaŋ watĕk yadubala,

hana kĕna duk waneḥ kĕna panaḥ kagaṇḍi kagalaḥ waneḥ wahu tibā,
hana sinĕsĕb pinökan inarug lawan tika galaḥnya tan kapulihan,
papan apagut dudū taŋ anuduk suduknya kapĕluk pupug maṅĕnani,
makakurucuk cucuk ni galaḥ iŋ prawīra kumucup tumandaŋ anucuk*

wahu tumĕḍun waneḥ kinurubut mapakṣa muruda atakut kinurutug,
lalu kaduhuŋ manaḥnya-ya katuṇḍuŋ epu mulat iŋ lawan sĕḍĕŋ amūk,
lupa kumĕtig hatinya katutug ḍaḍanya kataraṅgul eṅas aṅaḍuḥ,
uḍuḥ ibu liŋ nikā n kaliwatan panaḥ wĕkasan aṅḍuhuŋ kĕna dinuk*

aciṅaŋ ikaŋ tumiṅhali lawanya sāhasa tumandaŋ amraŋ anacaḥ,
mulat i wuri i palaywana nikā n kawuntwan atakut ywa tan wriŋ ulaha,
kaparĕpĕkan pwa ya aṅlalu manaḥnya mātya karaṇanya yan mrĕm awĕdi,
ri wulat ikā n wuruŋ lawan ika anuruŋ cakĕt agasyak ojaṙ aṅabuk*

hanan arawis ya ta akalis anon lawan kadi pinis hatinya rumaras,
lagi mariṅas kawĕs kawĕnĕsan manon tĕṅĕran iŋ musuḥnya n umasö,
rumaras arĕs hanan maṅĕsĕsan lana aṅgĕgĕs amoṙ iŋ aṅhawin adoḥ,
karaṇa nikā n atis tan inaris-haris rawis ika aradin dinudutan*

hana tikana a bapaŋ-bapaŋ abāŋ papanya tinaha apa tan wani dahat,
ḍaḍap ikahĕn kinonakĕn ikā n palaywakĕna de ni paṅhawin ikā,
apitaña ta i raṅinya katĕkān ulaḥ pati pĕṅöŋ maha aṅuman-uman,
dalihan ikā malaywani ḍaḍap malayw-akipit eṅas amriḥ anikus*

mapuliḥ ikaŋ prawīra mapuput-puput praŋ ika kapwa moliḥ amaḍĕm,
sakatĕmu de nika ababaran āwrĕg orig alulun winūk sinusupan,
kuḍuwak ikā miraḥ paḍa kasaŋsaṅan gajiḥ awaṙṇna rumbaḥ amiraḥ,
wiga pagawenya raṇḍa magawe wulañjaṙ agawe rare huwuḥ-uwuḥ*

sĕḍĕŋ arurĕk praŋ iŋ balapadāti len kuda siliḥ-sĕsĕb paḍa wani,
ratha malawan ratha aratha-rathan paḍa aṅlwaŋ ika sewu sowaŋ atugur,
mĕlĕtuk ikaŋ lĕbū saha samīraṇa adrĕs aduluṙ halisyus amusus,
karaṇa nikaŋ tĕgal pabharatan pĕtĕŋ jĕmuṙ ikaŋ prawīra malaga*

<bhramarawilasita>:87.
– – –| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 11

maṅkin maṅgĕḥ pĕtĕŋ ikaŋ alaga,
tan wriŋ rowaŋ sahana-hana nikā,
tĕṅran ndātan hana juga katĕṅĕr,
gĕṇḍiŋ roñji prasama mawurahan*

sakweḥ saŋ nātha sumahab i harĕp,
maṅkā sāmantri nira saha liman,
lāwan muṅgwiŋ ratha mamawa laras,
akweḥ tekaŋ gajaratha maṅiriŋ*

yekā n tandaŋ mamanaḥ anakiti,
māyākāra n tinuju nira kĕna,
mwaŋ kontā tomara nira lumĕpas,
samya anumbak suligi mamisani*

wet niŋ kweḥnya ŋ kĕna kadi rinujak,
mwaŋ waṅkay niŋ gajaturaga pĕjaḥ,
sumyuk rāḥnya adrĕs sumirat aniram,
himpĕṙ waṙṣa aṅapitu mawawahan*

mampĕḥ taŋ wāluka mari kumukus,
māwās tekaŋ raṇasabha wĕkasan,
sakweḥ saŋ māti ya ta winulatan,
lāwan taŋ sāgara rudhira śaran*

byakta awās taŋ palagan atiśaya,
bhāwanya alaḥ malĕs aṅalahakĕn,
an saŋ wīra alwaŋ ika kasakitan,
munduṙ sāmpun kalĕpas inusuṅan*

akweḥ śūra iŋ gaja ratha kawĕnaŋ,
mwaŋ wadwā sārathi nika mapupul,
rĕmpak taŋ syandana turaga pĕjaḥ,
mwaŋ hastī rowaŋ ika maguliṅan*

tatkālanya n wahu mapahidĕṅan,
aṇḍĕḥ niŋ dꜽtyabala paḍa masö,
lāwan tĕṅranya saha kuda liman,
lwiṙnya n tan paṅgalĕŋ aṅiwuŋ amūk*

praŋ bwat dꜽtya agul-agul lagi kĕna,
maṅgā mātya aṅusiṙ amapulihan,
munduṙ tekaŋ yadubala ri harĕp,
muṅsi ṅkāna i nrĕpati tuhan ikā*

saŋ somādatta kahala kadunuŋ,
konduṙ wadwā nira yatika tinūt,
rĕmpak tekaŋ ratha hana kabalik,
dantīnya inanti wuri niŋ alayū*

saŋ nātha aṅheṙ maṅadĕg aṅililan,
līlā riŋ syandana mamawa laras,
tandaŋ niŋ śatru ri sira kumucup,
ndātan kewran twas ira kinucupan*

yekā n śīghra aṅayati laras ira,
sumyuk tampuḥ ni śarawara nira,
tan wyaṙtha uliḥ ripu mati kapisan,
makweḥ ta lwaŋ ni musuḥ ira pĕjaḥ*

maṅsö tekaŋ bala maṅusiṙ amūk,
sakweḥ niŋ wīra maliman umasö,
saŋ yodha asyandana paḍa lumurug,
len taŋ muṅgwī gaja turaga masö*

konduṙ kombak tikaŋ asurabala,
mwaŋ wadwā saŋ magadhapati murud,
akweḥ lwaŋ niŋ gajaturaga pĕjaḥ,
kīṙṇna n kātiṅgal ika kasulayaḥ*

kapwa ŋ yakṣa adhika mamawa laras,
saŋ śaṙmma mwaŋ subala susamana,
maṅsö saŋ dhaṙmmajita saha bala,
yeka arampak parĕŋ apuliḥ amūk*

milwi ikaŋ dꜽtya maliman umasö,
mantrī saŋ duṙṇnaya parĕŋ apuliḥ,
seriŋ saŋ mānawiṣama sahasa,
wadwānya awāhana-turaga-liman*

sakweḥ niŋ rākṣasa muwaḥ apuliḥ,
maṅsö mwaŋ rowaŋ ika saha liman,
len tekaŋ senawiṣama mamawa,
kāliḥ mwaŋ waktrawikaṭa pinatiḥ*

nāhan lwiṙ niŋ narakabala masö,
kapwa amraŋ sāhasa hana manuhuk,
maṅduk maṅḍaṇḍa hana mamugari,
konta aṅonta iriya pamati musuḥ*

wadwā saŋ soma kahala kalulun,
kedran kewran kĕli-kĕlin inusi,
tan dwa atiṅgal gaja-turaga-ratha,
wīra kweḥ māti tuwi kapugutan*

maṅkin saŋ nātha sira kinucupan,
tañ jriḥ pinriḥ mamalĕsi mamanaḥ,
tandwa akweḥ lwaŋ nikaŋ asurabala,
de saŋ nātha amĕnuhi śarawara*

pat mantry-a aṅḍĕṇḍa narapati kĕna,
lāwan rāmanya bala tĕluŋ iwu,
maṅkin maṅduk tika parĕŋ umasö,
kāliḥ mwaŋ mānawiṣama mamurĕk*

<waṅśapatrapatita>:88.
– ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 17

saŋ nrĕpa somadatta mamanaḥ mamarĕpĕki musuḥ,
tĕṅgĕk i duṙṇnaya inaraḥ-araḥ nira pinatitisan,
hrū nira ŋ aṙddhacandra lumĕpas murub aṅarab-arab,
bhinna tibā ta tĕṇḍas i si duṙṇnaya saha lawayan*

krodha tikā n si mānawiṣama aṅlĕpasi śarawara,
śaṙmma parĕŋ lawan subala siṅhawadana mamanaḥ,
kapwa paḍa amanaḥ maraḥ-araḥ ḍaḍa patakuraṅan,
hrūnya sawaŋ suluŋ-suluŋ anon damaṙ aṅarab-arab*

saŋ yaduwīra satyaka wideha sira ta matuluŋ,
śobhana sādanāntaka sunīti niśaṭha gumuluŋ,
hrū nira tulya waṙṣa tumiba aṅĕnani suraripu,
śabda ni tambaŋ iŋ laras apiṇḍa gĕrĕḥ asahuran*

śīghra pĕjaḥ si mānawiṣama mwaŋ ika si subala,
maṙmma tibā sake ratha si-siṅhawadana tinuhuk,
maṅkin alaḥ tikaŋ musuḥ abāp lwaŋ ika piraŋ iwu,
len ikanaŋ turaṅga gaja tulya gunuŋ anak ahöm*

paṅlurug iŋ watĕk yadukula prasama saha ratha,
saŋ drupadātmaja pwa ri kiwan kicaka ri tĕṅĕnan,
saŋ nrĕpa winda lāwan anuwinda saha bala mamūk,
kapwa paḍa amanaḥ sira maha aṅhudani śarawara*

maṅkin alaḥ rĕbaḥ sahana niŋ magadhabala larut,
kweḥ nira saŋ watĕk ratu sama aṅjuru kapatĕṅahan,
dānawa dꜽtya rākṣasa sama apuliḥ asĕkuŋ amūk,
tomara bhindiwāla pinakāyudha nika lumĕpas*

maṅlayaŋ iŋ nabhastala waneḥ taŋ asura sumahab,
kīṙṇna paḍa aṅhudan-hudani sañjata tĕhĕṙ asurak,
duṙbala taŋ watĕk yadubala awrĕg alara kapusus,
len ikanaŋ pĕjaḥ piraŋ atus mwaŋ ikanaŋ alara*

saŋ nrĕpa winda malwaŋ ananā bala nira katĕtĕḥ,
bhrĕtya patiḥ nirā saŋ anuwinda mati kapugutan,
śīṙṇna wināḥ gunuŋ ginuluṅan tikaŋ i kiwa tinūb,
saŋ drupadātmaja i kiwa lawan bala nira kalulun*

satyaka saŋ wideha niśaṭha apagĕḥ apuliḥ amūk,
dhīra sira amanaḥ panaḥ ira ika maṅĕnani musuḥ,
saŋ kicaka agada awĕsi tumandaŋ atĕhĕṙ amupuḥ,
lwiṙ kadi siṅha kātara mamatyani gajaḥ agalak*

saŋ drupadātmaja aṅlĕpasakĕn sira śara niśita,
saŋ nrĕpa winda lāwan anuwinda ta parĕŋ amanaḥ,
hetu nikaŋ musuḥ kahala śīṙṇna saha bala larut,
duṙbala tan hana apuliḥ apan paḍa kumĕtĕṙ arĕs*

yeka larut rĕbaḥ kasulayaḥ tikaŋ asurabala,
tan dwa kalaḥ matimbun atilaṙ śakaṭa kawayakaḥ,
kadga gadā panaḥ saha galaḥnya-ya ta katihalaŋ,
hetu ni duṙggama i tĕgal ayomaya-maya wĕkasan*

śeṣa nikaŋ haneŋ laṅit ika anrik alulunan adoḥ,
muṅsiṙ amiṇḍa riŋ jaladhara swara nika gumuruḥ,
kandĕl ikaŋ pĕtĕŋ karaṇa niŋ dinakara makucĕm,
krūra nika aṅuhuḥ riris agantya śarawara tibā*

saŋ yaduwīra sakṣaṇa sira anĕraṅi śarawara,
bāyu mahāpracaṇḍa pamanaḥ nira mawaja kilat,
kabwaŋ ikaŋ musuḥ kawalikut ratha nika kawalik,
len ikanaŋ tibā mati katiṇḍihan i gajaḥ ikā*

kāla nikaŋ watĕk narakayodhagaṇa kasakitan,
yakṣa piśāca māti saka sewu pisan aguliṅan,
rākṣasa tan pasaṅkhya kawĕnaŋ kasulayaḥ agĕlar,
dꜽtya pira iŋ atus pĕjaḥ amūk paḍa ya pinugutan*

saŋ nrĕpa cedi kaṙṇna mapuliḥ saha bala sumahab,
tĕkwan ikaŋ watĕk ratu paḍa aṅiriṅi sira n amūk,
kapwa masö parĕŋ saha bala amapagi yadukula,
lwiṙ hinatĕp tikaŋ gagana de ni warayaŋ ira sök*

kaṇḍĕg ikaŋ watĕk yadubala apituwi tĕlas aṅel,
tan pamalĕs ginaṇḍi ginalaḥ pwa sinusunan amūk,
sāk ni gajāśwa tuṅgaṅan ikā pĕjaḥ inatus-atus,
śeṣa nikaŋ paratra kahala aṅĕliḥ umurud alon*

kaṙṇna sira aṅhudan-hudanakĕn śarawara niśita,
mwaŋ nrĕpa cedi sök panaḥ ira amĕnuhi pabharatan,
sāhasa tan tahĕn twas aṅusiṙ saha bala gumuluŋ,
tan wighata iŋ patĕmpuḥ i panaḥ yadukula ri sira*

tan salaya ŋ kuda nrĕpati cedi ratha nira n agöŋ,
sārathi sāra sapta tikanaŋ kuda ni ratha nira,
hetu niraŋ rwa mādrĕs aṅusiṙ saha ratha kumucup,
sāyaka saŋ rwa tan pĕgat anīṙṇnakĕn i yadukula*

saŋ yawanendraputra tumuluŋ kumucup i hiriṅan,
kweḥ nika sātus ewu pamanaḥ nira matitip atap,
kapwa ṅusi iri saŋ nrĕpa wirāṭa kicaka sahasa,
tan panahā bhaya iŋ raṇa maṅĕmbuli bala nira sök*

duṙggama taŋ tĕgal tĕkap ikaŋ pĕjaḥ alaga matap,
mwaŋ ratha sök lawan kuda limanya mati maguliṅan,
sañjata niŋ bala agĕlaṙ arok saha śawa makatap,
lwā ni tĕgal nika asĕmu gunuŋ kunapa winulatan*

nista nikāna ya n tan iniwĕḥ tĕkap ikaŋ alaga,
dhīra ni saŋ prawīra juga nitya paḍa wijaḥ amūk,
waṅkay atap tinindakan i saŋ malaga siliḥ-usī,
rodra paḍa aṅhĕbak malaga riŋ rudhira macacaban*

śīghra kaliṅgarāja kumucup saha ratha gumuluŋ,
nātha hiraṇyanābha saha bhrĕtya sira parĕŋ amūk,
hrū nira taṙ pĕgat juga sakeŋ laras ira masulam,
tulya suluŋ-suluŋ mijil anon rawi wahu kumĕñar*

bhrĕtya narendra śālya kadunuŋ prasama tan atakut,
tan dwa masö hamūk sumahab aṅrĕbahi gajaratha,
niṙbhaya tan panaṅgĕl i pamūk nikana siliḥ-arug,
tan hana tan sudhīra sahananya wija-wijaḥ amūk*

wīrabalā hiraṇyapati taṙ wuruŋ amati musuḥ,
maṅkana bhrĕtya saŋ nrĕpati śālya malĕs amĕjahi,
kādbhuta niŋ bala apraŋ arukĕt mĕjahi-pinĕjahan,
len ikanaŋ mamöki kawalĕs pwa mati kapugutan*

tan dwa musuḥnya sāhasa tĕka amraŋ anuduk anuhuk,
hetu nikā n patĕmpuḥ apagut praŋ ika siliḥ-irup,
gut-gutĕn aṅgalaḥ waja galaḥnya kadi ginaluga,
bāŋ ni tĕwĕk nika aṅuwus amöki kadi cinaraṇa*

papraŋ ikaŋ prawīra mapapan matĕmu paḍa papan,
cek ni curik niŋ amraŋ aṅĕne curik ikaŋ anuduk,
ṅös gĕdĕbug tibā cĕṅĕl ikaŋ katuju gulu nika,
lĕs muriṅas maluy kaŋ awĕdi iŋ pati daliḥ anasar*

teg dhwani niŋ papan kĕna gutuk hana tikĕl arĕmuk,
teg kĕrĕtog gĕḍog walulaŋ alwat alĕyĕ sinuduk,
bog kaguliŋ tibā taŋ awĕdi iŋ galaḥ awilĕt anūb,
Öḥ liŋ ikaŋ maṅohan inarug ḍaḍa nika tarawaŋ*

Āḥ pwa hujaṙ nikaŋ kĕna tuhuk ḍaḍa nika tinujaḥ,
Āḥ pawuwuḥ wuwusnya n awuwuḥ wani nikaŋ alaga,
maḥ cĕṅĕlamwa liŋ nika riŋ amriḥ amĕḍaŋ umayat,
maḥ ta sahut gilut wuwus ika anikĕp aciṅa-ciṅaḥ*

bhrĕtya hiraṇyanābha kapusus makĕtĕṙ alulunan,
tan hana tan pasāra kaguluŋ-guluŋ atahĕṙ amūk,
sāmaja len turaṅga humuŋ aṅhrik amĕpĕki kapö,
gĕntĕṙ i kĕṇḍaŋ iŋ sĕḍĕŋ arok praŋ ika kakĕrĕtug*

enak i raṅkit iŋ praŋ awilĕt prajurit adu wani,
taṅkĕp i pādarakṣaka nikaŋ gajaratha marukĕt,
tandaŋ ikaŋ manuṅgaŋ irikā ta maṅucupi musuḥ,
tomara sañjatanya lumĕpas parĕŋ asusun anūb*

maṅkat ikaŋ ratha atĕhĕṙ arampak anusuni kuda,
tan wiphala prayoga saŋ anuṅgaŋ anuhuk amanaḥ,
len taŋ asañjata ŋ krĕtala bindhiwala mapulihan,
saŋ hana riŋ liman paḍa widagdha tan amali bhaya*

kāla nikaŋ praŋ osyan asuwe matuguṙ i hiriṅan,
maṇḍĕg ikaŋ piśācabala yakṣa saha gajaratha,
dꜽtya niśācara aṅhala-hala agul-agul adu kihal,
hetu ni wadwa saŋ nrĕpati śālya kahala wĕkasan*

māwrĕg i wuntat awri bala madrapati kakĕtĕran,
bĕntaṙ alaḥ bubaṙ binuru kapwa rĕbaḥ arĕs adoḥ,
saŋ drupada adirāja makukud bala nira kadunuŋ,
bāhlika māri bahli caturaṅga nira macatura*

śīghra hiraṇyanābha maṅayat laras aṅaraḥ-araḥ,
ṅhiŋ nrĕpa śālya kapwa dinunuŋ saha bala lumurug,
tan hana tan tumūt sahana saŋ ratu marĕk i sira,
kapwa parĕŋ pisan sira n amāḥ gunuŋ awijaḥ amūk*

ghūṙṇnita taŋ surak saha lawan murawa paḍa humuŋ,
paṅrĕguŋ iŋ gaja ṅhrik i turaṅga ni ratha niŋ alaḥ,
ghoṙ huni niŋ gubaṙ humuŋ agĕnturan akĕrĕtugan,
tulya gĕrĕḥ swaranya gumuruḥ kadi gĕlap ataruŋ*

dhīra narendra śālya maṅadĕg mayat i laras agöŋ,
hrū nira kātara ujwala manīṙṇna ripukulabala,
maṅkin aneka tampuḥ i panaḥ nira malĕsi musuḥ,
rākṣasa dꜽtya dānawa piśāca mati tĕkap ira*

bāhlikanātha len drupadarāja sira sinahasa,
tan hinĕbaŋ-hĕbaŋ tinĕpĕtan bala nira kabalik,
tan hana ta apuliḥ kapalupuy gupu-gupurĕn arĕs,
tan wuwusĕn tikaŋ pĕjaḥ aneka saha kuda liman*

maṅkin alaḥ ta saŋ ratu watĕk yadu bubaṙ i harĕp,
bhrĕtya nira ananā linĕpasan śarawara niśita,
siŋ mapuliḥ pĕjaḥ karika yan mati pinarĕbutan,
hetu nika aluyuk lĕlĕḥ aṅel asukĕṙ alaradan*

saŋ kicaka aṅadĕg saha gada awĕsi ginĕgĕ nira,
krodha tumandaŋ aṅhala-hala aṅubat-abit amupuḥ,
alwaŋ aneka taŋ yawananāthasutabala winūk,
sāk śakaṭanya sīṙṇna gaja wāhana nika pinupuḥ*

saŋ yawanendraputra mapuliḥ rumĕbut i kicaka,
lwiṙ kararaṅga sānak apupul sama-sama maṅasut,
tomara konta sāyaka nika aparimita lumĕpas,
lwiṙ sukĕt iŋ halisyus umidĕṙ kumĕtĕṙ aputĕran*

krodha ta saŋ wirāṭapati muṅgwi liman ira masö,
hrū nira tulya waṙṣa tumiba iŋ yawanapatisuta,
tampuḥ ikaŋ gada awĕsi tĕkap kicaka parĕŋ amūk,
moliḥ amatyanī yawananāthasuta saha bala*

śeṣa nikaŋ pĕjaḥ ya ta masĕṅhit apuliḥ amanaḥ,
len hana maṅduk iŋ niśita śakti mamĕnĕri musuḥ,
mwaŋ hana ta agada awĕsi mupuḥ kicaka paḍa mamūk,
kapwa siliḥ-pupuḥ paḍa ta māyudha magada-gadān*

saŋ drupadātmaja ika hinirup ta sira kinucupan,
ṅkā nrĕpa śālya len ratu samānta parĕŋ amulihi,
towi sira ika saŋ drupadarāja tumuluy atuluŋ,
mwaŋ bala riŋ rathāśwa kumucup saha liman agalak*

saŋ nrĕpa śālya maṅlĕpasakĕn panaḥ ira masulam,
krora sakeŋ samādhi śara pūṙṇna yatika kumutug,
mwaŋ drupadādirāja maṅayat laras ira n amanaḥ,
hrū saha bāyubajra gumuruḥ ya ta pamanaḥ ira*

tan dwa tikāŋ piśāca kalulun kawĕnaŋ ika pĕjaḥ,
len ikanaŋ minantran awĕdi iŋ paśupatiwacana,
yakṣa pĕjaḥ pira iŋ puluḥ aneka juru nika pĕjaḥ,
mukṣa minantran astra malayū ta turaḥ ika kawĕs*

saŋ nrĕpa cedi taṙ wĕnaŋ arĕs ry-alaḥ ikaŋ i kiwa,
kaṙṇna sira aṅgĕgĕṙ ry-alaḥ ikaŋ panĕṅĕn ira gĕlar,
kewala dhīra kapwa sira kaṙwwa mapagĕḥ i tĕṅaḥ,
śūra maha aratha aṅusiṙ amūk ri yadukula sira*

lwiṙ hinatĕp tikaŋ gagana de ni śarawara sĕsök,
wuntu pĕtĕŋ tikaŋ pabharatan maya-maya wĕkasan,
duṙbala taŋ watĕk yadubala alwaŋ aṅatusi pĕjaḥ,
śakti niraŋ rwa kātara sawaŋ dahana maṅaraman*

towi narendra saŋ magadhanātha manusuni pamūk,
kapwa samāntarāja nrĕpa maṅjuru paḍa tumitiḥ,
hetu ni saŋ rwa maṅkin asiga aṅalahakĕn i tĕṅaḥ,
siŋ kaharĕp tĕkap nira wiśīṙṇna saha gajaratha*

konduṙ alaḥ rĕbaḥ yadubala amriḥ agĕlis alayū,
lwiṙ pinasaŋ pwa sañjata nikaŋ mati makacaraṅaḥ,
de ni wĕdinya riŋ pati nimitta nika pati purug,
tyāga nikā n paṅunduri juraŋ katĕmu siliḥ-idĕk*

satyaka saŋ wideha kalulun winĕgilan i bala,
saŋ niśaṭha pwa kāsrĕk irikaŋ gajaratha malayū,
hetu nira n tumūt murud amet kira-kira wĕkasan,
mwaŋ yaduwīra rowaŋ ira munduṙ akikib inusī*

sewu pisan lĕpas ni warayaŋ dinakaratanaya,
mwaŋ śarasaṅgha saŋ nrĕpati cedi saka saṅaŋ atus,
tan wuwusĕn panaḥ para watĕk ratu makacaracab,
len ikaŋ amraŋ aṅduk anuhuk pamaja haji wijaḥ*

bĕntaṙ ikaŋ watĕk yadubala rwaŋ iwu pĕjaḥ amūk,
len ika taŋ gajāśwa kawĕnaŋ muwaḥ anana sakit,
siŋ mapuliḥ pĕjaḥ yatika hetu nika giri-girin,
tan mawĕdi ika kālapana denya harĕpa huripa*

śīghra dhanañjaya ajaṙ i narendrasuta yadukula,
ndaḥ sahananta wīra t-aṅusiṙ yaśa saphala tirun,
haywa tatan pakāṙyya ri gatā parahita riŋ ayun,
ya iku lawan ṅaranya nrĕpa cedi dinakarasuta*

bhoḥ ta t-tamukti bhukti phalabhukti tĕwas iŋ alaga,
priḥ bĕnĕṙ iŋ swamāṙgga niŋ anĕmwa pada sukha magöŋ,
ṅkā n marikā sawaŋ tĕnuŋ iŋ apraŋ alaḥ amĕnaṅa,
ṅhiŋ si kaśūran uttama ṅaranya dadaḥ iŋ ahurip*

heman i denta tiṅgalakĕna ŋ yaśa maṅusira len,
hāt niŋ ajīwa kāraṇa niŋ amriḥ anusupa hade,
yan bwat ikaŋ hurip dadi hilaŋ ya kinatĕṅĕtakĕn,
yan hinaran-haran wruḥ atĕguḥ juga ri saŋ aharan*

dhaṙmmawiśeṣa riŋ kadi kita wruḥ atapa matĕguḥ,
an tan umuṅkura i tĕka nikaŋ ripu parĕŋ umasö,
kīṙtti ni saŋ prawīra tika ya astuti ni musuḥ ira,
tan wiphala pwa mamriḥ ayaśa iŋ jagat inatiśaya*

donta mijil mareŋ samarakāṙyya magawaya yaśa,
don ikanaŋ warāstra ginĕgönta paṅalaha musuḥ,
wyaṙthan ikaŋ hiḍĕpta ri sĕḍĕŋnya malĕmĕḥ alaga,
yeka n awās tiwas kita dinuṙyyaśa nikaŋ umulat*

<sragdharā>:89.

nān liŋ saŋ pāṙtha malwī sahana-hana nikā saŋ watĕk wīrayodha,
enak taŋ praŋ siliḥ-lwaŋ ratu puluṅan abāp māti de niŋ warāstra,
saŋ kaṙṇna mwaŋ siraŋ cedi tan ari sumawuṙ hrū nira akweḥ tumĕmpuḥ,
nānā waṅkay nikaŋ wīra mamapagi sira syuḥ tĕkeŋ kuñjarāśwa*

maṅkā saŋ pāṙtha gumrit ratha nira gumuluŋ mwaŋ siraŋ nātha rukma,
lāwan saŋ śrī narendra druma nrĕpa basudewa aswaŋ amriḥ paḍa agyā,
saŋ sāmba mwaŋ gada adrĕs laku ni ratha nira n tan tahĕn twas tumandaŋ,
sākṣāt siṅhākrĕti ṅkā mulat i rawisuta mwaŋ mahārāja cedi*

gut-gūtĕn saŋ watĕk rotagaṇa mapagakĕn paṅharĕp cedirāja,
kāṇḍĕg wadwā niraŋ sūṙyyatanaya pinagut konduṙ epĕḥ kaṅelan,
maṅkin bĕntaṙ tan aṅgĕḥ pwa pinanaḥ inirup śīṙṇna kolāhala awrĕg,
mātya atiṇḍiḥ tĕkap niŋ śarawara rumujak hrū niraŋ pāṇḍuputra*

saŋ sāmba hrū nira aneka lumĕpas asulam mwaŋ panaḥ saŋ gada anūb,
maṅkā sakweḥ niraŋ yādawakula mamanaḥ riŋ mahāstra atitīkṣna,
mwaŋ sāmānta aṅduluṙ paṅrĕguŋ i gajaḥ ikā n matta medanya mādrĕs,
wadwā peka asurak paṅhrik i kuda nika saŋ wīra maṅsö tĕka amraŋ*

yeka alaḥ śīṙṇna kombak ginuluṅan inirup saŋ watĕk bhūmiputra,
mātya atiṇḍiḥ matap mwaŋ gajaratha matumaŋ duṙggama iŋ yodhabhūmi,
len peka atiṅgal iŋ sañjata makacaraṅaḥ lwiṙ trĕna akrĕp karĕs-rĕs,
maṙmmanya n lwiṙ ni saŋ wīra malaga sinapiḥ de nikaŋ rāḥ maṅĕmbĕŋ*

maṅsö saŋ kaṙṇna siṅhākrĕti mamapagakĕn wūk mahārāja rukma,
lāwan saŋ cedi gumrit ratha nira n umasö maṅdunuŋ pāṇḍuputra,
kapwa amĕṇṭaŋ laras hrū nira paḍa lumĕpas kātara anekarūpa,
molaḥ moliḥ ya māliḥ muwaḥ aṅusiṙ uliḥ riŋ watĕk yādawa awrĕg*

ṅkā saŋ pāṙtha amanaḥ hrū nira n amarawaśa iŋ śatru sakrodha riŋ praŋ,
rĕmpak yodha irikaŋ cedi kahala pinanaḥ syuḥ tĕka iŋ wāhananya,
krodha ambĕk cedirāja amalĕs amanahakĕn bāṇa saṅhārarājā,
muntab lwiṙ bahni tejanya mapanas ahulap riŋ laṅit mrĕtyutulya*

krora ṅhrū nāgadaṅṣṭrā pinanahakĕn iraŋ pāṙtha sāmpun krĕtāṙtha,
himpĕṙnya uśwāsa niŋ pāśa juga wijil ikaŋ bahni saṅke liḍaḥnya,
wāgyutpāta prahāra atiśaya duluṙ ikaŋ śabda ghora adrĕs osyan,
dhwasta ŋ saṅhārarājā tĕkap ika n agĕsĕŋ śīṙṇna bhasmy-alpasāra*

Āscāṙyya ambĕk niraŋ cedi mulat i hilaŋ iŋ bāṇa saṅhārarāja,
hetunya ŋ rudrabāṇottama linĕpasakĕn de nira atyanta riŋ kweḥ,
nitya asaṅkhya anu saṅke laras ira n umilī lwiṙ waḥ iŋ māghamāsa,
yekā n sāṙ sök pĕnuḥ riŋ samara kahibĕkan mwaŋ taŋ ākāśadeśa*

prodbhūta krūra nārāyaṇa pamalĕs iraŋ pāṇḍuputra aprameya,
kapwa awantaḥ siliḥ-tūb makakĕrĕcĕk arok mwaŋ panaḥ cedirāja,
saṅke drĕṣṇya aniwāṙyya amĕnuhi pabharatan wuntw-iŋ ākāśa denya,
Āpan tambis pĕtĕŋ taŋ diwasa kasaputan wimba saŋ hyaŋ pataṅga*

hrū saŋ cedy-a aṅĕne bāhu surapatisuta ndan sisip tampuḥ iŋ hrū,
hrū saŋ pāṙtha aṅĕne cedipati katuluyan taŋ ratha asāk sasaknya,
ndā tan wruḥ saŋ rwa yan kapwa kakaninan alaḥ daṙppa de niŋ kadhīran,
göŋ-göṅĕn ton prabhāwa prasama kawigaran de ni göŋ niŋ kaśaktin*

tan mampĕḥ tampuḥ iŋ bāṇa nika raris ira adwandwayuddha iŋ raṇāṅga,
himpĕṙ-himpĕṙ katon śakti nira paḍa widagdha iŋ dhanurwedaśāstra,
śīṙṇna asiŋ muṅgwi saṇḍiŋ nira kahawa hilaŋ bhrĕtya saŋ cedirāja,
aṅhiŋ hrū cedinātha aṅĕnani ḍaḍa nikiŋ sārathī pāṇḍuputra*

munduṙ saŋ pāṇḍuputra nda tucapa sira saŋ rukma rādheya mapraŋ,
wwaŋ daṙppa iŋ praŋ paḍa amet kira-kira putus iŋ praŋ siliḥ-wūk siliḥ-duk,
moghanya akweḥ tikaŋ sañjata linĕpasakĕn de nira asiŋ kasambut,
siṅlaṙ saŋ kāliḥ apraŋ parĕk aparĕpĕkan tan kacidra ñ cinidra*

kapwa anambut panaḥ tan wawaŋ amanaḥ anūb hrū nira akrĕp lĕpasnya,
puṅgĕl tekaŋ laras kaṙwwa ya karaṇa nira n pāṅunus candrahāsa,
śīghra araṅkit sawaŋ megha matĕmu ri tĕṅaḥ dhīra tan paṅrasa aṅel,
ujwāla ika n tĕgĕg lwiṙ kilat awilĕtan aṅde hulap niŋ tumiṅhal*

saŋ rukma an sep kanin kapraŋ i ḍaḍa humilī rāḥ nira adrĕs tan ampĕt,
maṅsö saŋ satyaka apakṣa tumuluṅa murud kaṙṇna sāmpun kaṅelan,
aṅhiŋ saŋ nātha rukma inalap ira wĕkasan yatna munduṙ sira alon,
ghĕk grit ghĕk lampaḥ iŋ syandana nira manapak waṅkay iŋ sāmajāśwa*

saŋ ulmuka atyanta gĕlĕŋ nira umasö,
laras nira akas warayaŋ nira aluṅid,
wawaŋ tikā sy-adrawalīka maṅlaga,
siliḥ-panaḥ kapwa widagdha riŋ panaḥ*

kĕna asakit sy-adrawalīka mūṙcchita,
rikaŋ kṣaṇa ataṅgal udhāni lāghawa,

musi i ratha sy-adrawalīka sāhasa,
mupuḥ ḍaḍa sy-adrawalīka cūṙṇnita*

nanā ta wadwā śarabha aradin pĕjaḥ*

<rajanī>:91.

śarabha tĕlas pĕjaḥ tĕkap iraŋ suratha iŋ samara,
yatika gĕlĕŋ narendra śiśupāla rikaŋ suratha,
amanahakĕn śarāgni kumutug murub iŋ gagana,
kadi sinaṅā ṅhyaŋ op kapanasan mahuyaŋ-hayiṅan*

rika suratha n prayatna malĕsi ŋ baruṇāstra sira,
bañu mĕtu saṅka riŋ laras apūṙwwa hilīnya magöŋ,
maṅawaŋ-awaŋ sawaŋ suranadī gumuruḥ karĕṅö,
amaḍĕmi sañjatānala hilaŋ malilaŋ wĕkasan*

muwaḥ amanaḥ ta cedipati riŋ śara bajramaya,
maputiḥ akās wajanya kadi hīra katon dumilaḥ,
wahu maṅayat laras drumasuta aṙddha kasep katuju,
tumakisakĕn dhanuḥ nira tikĕl kakĕnan ri taṅan*

rika n aṅalap lipuŋ sira masö mamurĕk rumakĕt,

nihan iki sopananta muliha iŋ yamaloka mĕne,
na liŋ ira tan dwa maṅduk aṅĕne hulu cedipati*

makin awuwuḥ gĕlĕŋ nrĕpati cedi malĕs mamanaḥ,
warayaŋ ira aṙddhacandra maṅĕna ika gulū ni musuḥ*

saha śara bāyubajra maduluṙ paḍa a ya ṅĕnani,
druma sira kātisan gumigil āṅĕsĕsan kumĕtĕr*

dadi sira maṅlage nrĕpati cedi pinaṅpaŋ ira,

kumusuḥ awoṙ halisyus amusus bala cedipati,
hana ta mahograsāyaka nira ika muwaḥ lumĕpas,

amarĕpĕki ŋ musuḥ mamatitis ta sira n pamanaḥ*

linĕpasakĕn ta de nira murub rikanaŋ gagana,
kĕna kapisan saŋ āṙyya śiśupāla bĕlaḥ ri ḍaḍa*

asiga tiniṅhalan sira n apañ jaramanta katon,

<indrawaṅśa>:92.

sāmpun pĕjaḥ saŋ nrĕpa cedi riŋ raṇa,
maṅlaḥ sira i rĕṅga nikaŋ ratha aruhur,
kārun lawan sārathi len ikaŋ kuda,
aṅhiŋ turaḥ niŋ bala duṙbala alayū*

kagyat saŋ aṙkkātmaja gadgada aṅadĕg,
nton ta ika saŋ cedi mati iŋ raṇāṅgana,
trĕṣṇā nira amitra ya ta amaṅun lara,
maṙmma awĕlas hetu ni kĕmbĕŋ iŋ mata*

eṅgal marĕn śoka sira ika sakṣaṇa,
göŋ niŋ kadhīran maṅaweśakĕn wawaŋ,
maṅsö sira i saŋ basudewa sāhasa,
lāwan ri saŋ kimpuruṣendra cuṇḍukĕn*

maṅkin marĕk saŋ rawiputra riŋ ratha,
yaṙ ton siraŋ rwa alara de nira n pĕjaḥ,
śīghra aṅunus kadga nira prabhāswara,
sep saŋ druma n kapraŋ i rĕṅga niŋ ratha*

lumpat niraŋ kaṙṇna sake swawāhana,
muṅsi i sira śrī basudewa tan waneḥ,
agyā sira apakṣa manampila iŋ ratha,
kagyat cinakra amalĕs amraŋ iŋ tĕwĕk*

māti pwa saŋ rwa asiga kaṙṇna yan katon,
līla aṅadĕg riŋ śakaṭa aṅgĕgön laras,
saŋ sāmba sakrodha tĕhĕṙ sira umasö,
tujw-i i panaḥ saŋ rawiputra lāghawa*

saŋ kaṙṇna śīghra n paṅayat laras nira,
hrū nāgapāśa n tumihaŋ tĕkap nira,
sāmpun lĕpas kātara bhīṣaṇa umaṅaŋ,
śabdanya tan pāntara riŋ nabhastala*

kālanya muṅgwiŋ gaganāntara aṅlayaŋ,
saŋ sāmba sāmpun lumĕpas panaḥ nira,
hrū wꜽnateyāstra mahogra śaktimān,
yeka amaṅan hrū nrĕpa kaṙṇna riŋ laṅit*

saŋ kaṙṇna maṅkin sira tan tahĕn hati,
kālogradaṅṣṭrā lumĕpas tĕkap nira,
saŋ sāmba yatna amanahi ŋ mahāśara,
mrĕtyuñjayāstrādhipa nāma kātara*

śabdanya ghora iŋ gagana atighūṙṇnita,
hrū kaṙṇna puṅgĕl katakis tiba iŋ lĕmaḥ,
sakrodha rādheya sira amanaḥ muwaḥ,
riŋ candrawimbāṙddhaśara prabhāswara*

sāmpun lĕpas bhīṣaṇa tulya handaru,
sāmba prawīra wruḥ i tampuḥ iŋ panaḥ,
mĕṇḍĕk sira anaṅgulakĕn laras nira,
puṅgĕl ta laṅkap nira paṙwwa riŋ taṅan*

śīghra aṅalap cakra wawaŋ sira amalĕs,
puṅgĕl dhanuḥ saŋ rawiputra de nira,
maṅsö sira añakra muwaḥ ndatan surud,
tĕṅgĕk niraŋ kaṙṇna cinakra niṙbhaya*

krodha ika saŋ sāmba ri kaṙṇna tan kanin,
nā hetu niŋ mambil ikaŋ gadā n asö,
yeka amupuḥ syandana kaṙṇna riŋ gadā,
kārun lawan sārathi māti de nira*

saŋ kaṙṇna śīghra n tumĕḍun sakeŋ ratha,
tañ jriḥ tĕhĕṙ sambutakĕn gadā nira,
yekā n paḍa adwandwa gadāyudha irikā,
lāwan siraŋ sāmba siliḥ-pupuḥ sira*

kapwa aṅiriŋ cidra widagdha riŋ sikĕp,
ndātan hana asoṙ paḍa śakti suśrama,
siddhaṙṣy-anonton hana riŋ nabhastala,
mahyā humuŋ śabda nira n paṅadwakĕn*

saŋ sāmba mogha n kasikĕp gadā nira,
de saŋ nrĕpa aṙkkātmaja riŋ taṅan kiwā,
hasta i tĕṅĕn sūṙyyasuta amupuḥ musuḥ,
ṅkāna iŋ hujuŋ bāhu niraŋ nrĕpātmaja*

māṙ bāhu saŋ sāmba tĕṅĕn kĕna iŋ gadā,
hetunya siṅsal ta gadā nira i taṅan,
mūṙcchā sira i sakṣaṇa de nikaŋ lara,
ṅka amriḥ sira ataṅgal udhāni dhāraka*

de niŋ kadhīran matahĕn sira atutur,
yekā n amūk prĕp nrĕpa kaṙṇna riŋ kiwān,
rādheya rĕmpū ta śiraḥ nira apasaḥ,
maṅlaḥ tiba i saṇḍiŋ ikaŋ swawāhana*

saŋ kaṙṇna sāmpun pĕjaḥ iŋ raṇāṅgana,
wadwā nira awrĕg saha wāhana alayū,
saŋ sāmba sāmpun winawa iŋ ratha aruhur,
aṅga amiraḥ dinyus i rāḥ pataṅgaja*

kālanya māwrĕg tikanaŋ bala alayū,
maṅsö jarāsandha lawan samāṅjuru,
atyanta riŋ kweḥ tuwi tumpĕkan kabeḥ,
himpĕṙ gunuŋ rug saha wāḥ mahajwala*

<madanalalitā>:93.
– – –| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – – –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏓ = 16

maṅkat saŋ yādawa saha lawan wrĕṣṇyāndaka kabeḥ,
sāmanta mwaŋ bala kadi tasik rob kādrĕsan aṅin,
sakweḥ niŋ sāmaja ratha kuda lwiṙ duṙggama karaŋ,
saŋ wīra aṅkĕn hyu pinakarayāta praŋnya mamati*

enak taŋ praŋ matĕmu ri tĕṅaḥ malwaŋ piraŋ iwu,
maṅkin mātimbun akatap atip taŋ sāmaja pĕjaḥ,
maṅkā taŋ syandana hana ta rimpĕk len hana rĕmuk,
membuḥnya n duṙgga pinakasukĕtnya ikaŋ raṇasabhā*

akweḥ sāmanta mati kĕna riŋ kontā n kakuwuṅan,
mwaŋ tekaŋ māti kĕna pinanaḥ trus twasnya katibā,
Āstām taŋ pekabala matumaŋ waṅkaynya tinapak,
rodra ŋ wīra alaga pakatĕkĕnya akadga niśita*

yeka aṅsö saŋ narapati hiraṇyānābha nipuṇa,
muṅgwiŋ hastī n kinawacan awaṙṇna apuy winulatan,
hrū tan pānta iri laras ira kapwa lwiṙ latu-latu,
dhwastā taṅyādawabala gĕsöŋ de niŋ panas ikā*

maṅkat saŋ wabhru mapagi hiraṇya adrĕs ratha nira,
hrū tīkṣṇa atyanta pamanaḥ ira lwiṙ wintaŋ aṅaliḥ,
kādbhūta awoṙ kilat awilĕt aṅde rĕs niŋ umulat,
tĕmpuḥnya anīṙṇna makuṭa hiraṇya asyuḥ katariwal*

mūṙcchālök towin alara hiraṇya apan kakaninan,
krodha n tandaŋ liman ika musi i saŋ wabhru kumucup,
yatna śrī wabhru mamanaḥ hiraṇya mwaŋ gajaḥ ira,
cek ceŋ tampuḥ ni warayaŋ ira i hastī n kinawacan*

maṅkin krodha ŋ liman aṅuliŋ adrĕs tandaŋ ikahĕn,
ambĕknya ahyun maṅulĕṅa ri saŋ wabhru n pamurugul,
saŋ wabhru wruḥ tumuluy umurud mwaŋ syandana nira,
ahyā taŋ śatrubala ha-ha hāḥ liŋnya aṅguyu-guyu*

krodha ambĕk saŋ gada mamulihi i saŋ wabhru malayū,
śīghra amĕṇṭaŋ laras ira lĕpas mwaŋ hrū nira wawaŋ,
limpad tĕṇḍas ni gajaḥ i hiraṇya apaṙwwa ya bĕlaḥ,
śabdanya n paṅrĕguŋ awurahan munduṙ ya wulaṅun*

sāmpun māti pwa ya kadi gunuŋ rug ghūṙṇnita humuŋ,
yekā n lumpat narapati hiraṇya ataṅgal aṅadĕg,
muṇḍa uṇḍa i śūla niśita murub paṅduk nira lĕpas,
yatna atā saŋ gada mamalĕs iŋ kontā mamisani*

sāmpun māti ika nrĕpati hiraṇya trus ḍaḍa nira,
yeka aṅsö saŋ magadhapati muṅgwi i sāmajapati,
atyanta hrū nira kadi ta waṙṣa adrĕs lĕpas ikā,
lāwan taŋ bāyu duluṙ ika wagyūtpāta makilat*

hrū saṅhārāstra pamalĕs iraŋ krĕṣṇātmaja wawaŋ,
mwaŋ bāyw-ākās kadi hira dahat drĕṣṇya amaluyakĕn,
kedĕṙ hrū saŋ magadhapati denya alaḥ maṅadu kās,
tĕmpuḥnya i saŋ magadhapati kedĕṙ sāmaja nira*

tambis māti ika nrĕpati jarāsandha n katuluyan,
yan tan dhīra atĕguḥ atutura iŋ rudrasmrĕti sira,
yekā ta hrū nira ta ya mahāśakti n lĕpasakĕn,
henak de saŋ narapati mahādhyāna aṅlĕpasakĕn*

yatna wruḥ saŋ gada linĕpasan mĕṇḍĕk juga sira,
nyā ṅhrū bajrojwala walĕs ira atyanta i katatakut,
rūpanya n pañcamukha wipula akās lwiṙ gunuŋ anak,
rĕñcĕm syuḥ denya gaja magadhendra agĕm kapisanan*

<prĕthwītala>:94.
⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 18

lumumpat ika saŋ narendra magadhādhirāja tumuluy,
sumambut irikaŋ gada awĕsi mupuḥ ri saŋ gada sira,
siraŋ gada luput kunĕŋ ratha nira ika śīṙṇna kapupuḥ,
gada awĕsi muwaḥ sinambut ira yan tĕḍun sira wawaŋ*

rikā ta magadhendra daṙppa mamupuḥ ri saŋ gada sira,
luput pwa sira saŋ gada ika pinupuḥ malĕs ta ya mupuḥ,
paḍa aṅiriṅi cidra saŋ rwa masuwe siliḥ-palu sira,
maṅadwakĕn awū watĕk ratu tumon ri saŋ rwa malaga*

kacidra kapupuḥ lĕṅĕn magadharāja tañ jriḥ atahĕn,
wicitra mamalĕs ḍumaṇḍa ḍaḍa saŋ gada ika tumuluy,
pataṅgul ikanaŋ gada atikĕl apaṙwwa kaṙwwa ri taṅan,
ya hetu nira saŋ rwa kapwa maṅalap krĕtāla wĕkasan*

mapālaga mapatrayuddha sira kapwa siṅlaṙ akalis,
siliḥ-praŋ asĕluṙ widagdha matakis ri paṅlaga nira,
amogha magadhendra yan kĕḍap i soway an kamadĕlön,
kasep kĕna gulū nira iŋ kṣaṇa pĕgat pĕjaḥ kapisanan*

<daṇḍaka>:95.1:1
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [– ⏑ –]×58 = 180

atha ri pĕjaḥ iraŋ jarāsandha māwrĕg watĕk bhoma bĕntaṙ numānanya bhagna n paḍa alaḥ rĕbaḥ kolaḥ-olaḥ winahwaḥ nana arĕs kawöswös kagöman minohan rinok tan pasāra n matiṅgal galaḥ paṇḍi gaṇḍinya lāwan ḍaḍapnya n parok tuṅgal aṅrimpĕd iŋ pekayodha n tiba aṅaṅgal-aṅgal jumoṅkoŋ jumaṅkaḥ sukunya n lanā kedĕkan de ni rowaŋnya meḥ mātya yan patyakĕn tekana aṅganya maṅheṙ amoṙ iŋ śawa amet urip kāsihan ya amĕgöŋ prāṇa maṅlimbaŋ iŋ rāḥ kumambaŋ kahilyan śawa amogha mārambakan komba-kāmbaḥ ya de niŋ liman saŋ watĕk wrĕṣṇiwīra aṅusī saŋ watĕk bhūmija,

{daṇḍaka}:95.1:2
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [– ⏑ –]×59 = 183

gaja ratha mari wrĕg lĕgĕg māṇḍĕg-aṇḍĕg hana aṅrĕgrĕg opĕk pĕpĕk yan sĕsĕk de ni waṅkay nikaŋ sāmaja mwaŋ ratha syuḥ rĕmök lwiṙ gunuŋ sĕṅkan ewĕḥ sukĕt duṙgga niŋ papraṅan priṅga maṅde lĕmĕḥ niŋ bala aṅel sumĕṅka apitowin baya i kadga niŋ māti tīkṣṇa n karĕsrĕs katon tulya suṅga a pipit kākrĕcĕk yan kasaṇḍuŋ dudū ta aṅĕne jöŋ hanan trus tugĕl maṅrĕpa ikaŋ kĕna mwaŋ hana aṅlaḥ mulū twasnya saṅkeŋ ḍaḍanya n kĕna iŋ bhindiwāla u-mulu usus nika ikaŋ kasambit wĕtĕŋnya i luṅid niŋ lipuŋ tīkṣṇa makweḥ piraŋ lakṣa kedĕk tĕkap niŋ gajaḥ syandana mwaŋ kuda aṅlūd maṅambaḥ wuwuḥ niŋ pĕjaḥ len tinon,

kawĕlas-arĕp ikaŋ tinūt niŋ lawanya n katon kokalañ jĕmpariŋ koñakan riŋ tuhuk pinraŋ iŋ candrahāsa amibab saṇḍaṅanya n manaṇḍaŋ mrukuṅkuŋ ri lampaḥ nika aṅuṅgut-uṅgut lana aṅuṇḍuk-uṇḍuk dinūk riŋ tuhuk len ikaŋ trus kĕna iŋ tomara mwaŋ winūk pinraŋ amriḥ-mriḥ iŋ jīwitanya n palaywan kalakwan katuṇḍuŋ kahaṇḍĕm katiṇḍĕs kalaṇḍĕs matiṇḍiḥ matimbun matumpuk matambak tuluŋnyā sinambyā manambya anaṅis tan hana asiḥ tumoliḥ gatinya n tĕka ika lawanya n parĕŋ ya aparö māri mādrĕs larinya alara ariñ-ca-riñcuŋ ri pañcuṙ ni rāḥnya n kucuṙ kāraṇanya n paṅohan humuŋ,
