taku-takutĕn ikaŋ watĕk rākṣasa mwaŋ watĕk yakṣa lāwan piśāca aduluṙ nāgaśeṣa alaḥ oliḥ lara alök lanā lwiṙnya maṅboṅlwat alwa ambĕk-ambĕk kaninya n lana aṅĕmbak-ĕmbak mibab yan babak len ri lambuŋ nika aṅambĕk-ambĕk tĕka iŋ ambĕkanya n tan imbā taṅanya anukup tañ cukup tan kacumpwan kacuk-cak ta rāḥnya n lumuñcat lumiñcak tumindak tĕkap niŋ hawan luṅka-luṅka n hibĕk waṅkay iŋ tuṅgaṅan kāraṇanya n paḍa aṅĕṅgaḥ-ĕṅgaḥ masambat bapa mwaŋ bibi mwaŋ ri putranya putrīnya maṅkin ta ya aṅĕmbiḥ-ĕmbiḥ tibā luḥnya mādrĕs tan ampĕt nimittanya maṅkin taṅisnya aṇḍahuŋ*

<daṇḍaka>:95.2:1
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [– ⏑ –]×47 = 147

kahala kawalayaḥ luyuk śeṣa niŋ māti muṅsiṙ pakuwwanya rewātaka arampak iŋ pāṙśśwa len taŋ tibā riŋ juraŋ bhrĕtya saŋ śrī jarāsandha sāmpun pĕjaḥ kāsihan ya anusup riŋ sukĕt mwaŋ guha inuṅsi nistanya tan mātya de niŋ watĕk yādawa anūt sudhīrātara ika anujaḥ riŋ tuhuk mamraŋ iŋ bhindiwāla ama-naḥ tan pĕgat hrūnya kontānya tan pāntara atĕmpuḥ aṅde takutnya ŋ watĕk bhoma yeka arĕbut māṙgga ri priṅga sĕṅkan sĕsök sök siliḥ-tiṇḍiḥ aṅrĕs manaḥ niŋ tumon ya inusi,

{daṇḍaka}:95.2:3
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [– ⏑ –]×48 = 150

agarawalan ikaŋ watĕk dꜽtya muṅgwiŋ kuda atuṅgw-i saŋ bhoma kagyat ḍĕṅö hūŋ nikaŋ wrĕṣṇiyodha aṅuhuḥ kātara lwiṙ gĕrĕḥ niŋ catussāgara i kāla niŋ bāyusaṅhāra yeka amaṅun krodha niŋ dꜽtyasaṅgha aṅadĕg sāyudha n ton ikaŋ cedisena alayū mwaŋ jarāsandhasenā lawan kaṙṇnasena aduluṙ tan panātha apitowin tika amājaṙ i śrī mahādꜽtyarājā tĕlas māti saŋ mitra katrīṇi yekā n kabāṅan tika awak nira asĕṅhit iŋ wrĕṣṇiwīra andhaka atyanta muntab panas niŋ hati,

{daṇḍaka}:95.2:4
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [– ⏑ –]×50 = 156

karaṇa saŋ asurādhipa anuṅgaŋ iŋ puṣpakā ya umasö mwaŋ tikaŋ dꜽtya-saṅgha amanek wāhananya aṅrĕgĕp sañjatanya aṅlayaŋ riŋ laṅit kabwaṅan megha de ny-aṅin iŋ wāhana adrĕs katon lwiṙ ghana iŋ māghamāsa atri ghora n gumĕntĕṙ suraknya i ruhuṙ lwiṙ nikā meghanāda ika tambis pĕtĕŋ ṅganya tan wwantĕna ŋ bhūṣaṇa mwaŋ warāstra aprameyaprabhā bhāswara anekarūpa akilat mwaŋ larap niŋ krĕtāla atitīkṣṇa n krĕbĕt niŋ dhwajanya ahulap māsnya tan papramāṇa i ruhuṙ lwiṙnya tāraṅgana i kāla niŋ madhyarātri iŋ sarāt,

{daṇḍaka}:95.2:2
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [– ⏑ –]×50 = 156

kala-kala hulap iŋ wiyat ṅ-āmarāśatrunātha iŋ wimāna asigā ṅka aṅadĕg niṙbhaya i śabda niŋ wrĕṣṇiwīra andhaka asampay iŋ rākṣasa apan mahāśakti gambhīrawīṙyya n watĕk praŋ krĕtākrĕtya riŋ yuddhakāṙyya adhikāra iŋ kaśūran kadhīran lana akīṙtti ṅūni iŋ raṇa asiŋ musuḥ de nika arĕs dumeḥ göŋnya hĕṅkāra saŋ bhoma bhaṅga aṅgakāra aṅgĕgö kābhimānan mahā niṙbhaya i saŋ watĕk wrĕṣṇi hamham sira aśatru saŋ hyaŋ mahendra apĕs opĕk dinon tan pasāra ika kāṅĕn tĕkap saŋ mahādānawa ambĕknya siṅhākrĕti*

<daṇḍaka>:95.3:1
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [– ⏑ –]×60 = 186

paṅamaḥ-amaḥ ikaŋ watĕk dꜽtyayodha aṅlayaŋ sañjatanya a hulap lwiṙ hĕlaŋ yan tĕka amraŋ mamaṇḍĕm śiraḥ niŋ mahāwīra śatrunya meww-īwu yekā n pamaṇḍĕmnya riŋ wrĕṣṇiwīra agrayodha pwa taŋ dꜽtya töka anikĕp tuṅgaṅan mwaŋ gajaḥ syandana asiŋ kasambut panimbat nika i saŋ yadubhrĕtya len rākṣasa aṅambaḥ iŋ waṅkay iŋ wīra len taŋ manĕmpal manampil pupū hasta paṅduk nikā mwaŋ panĕmpuḥ nika aṅgyat sakeŋ byoma rodra akaluŋ twas paḍa abāŋ ḍaḍanya asawit wuṅsilan limpa sāmpun rinantay nika i hasta maṅkin karĕsrĕs mĕlĕs rāḥ nika awaṙṇna kĕmbaŋ riŋ ākāśa mabhra asawaŋ megha riŋ kālasandhya amiraḥ,

{daṇḍaka}:95.3:2
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [– ⏑ –]×56 = 174

aṅamuk ika waneḥ paṅan waṅkay iŋ wīra matta aṅinum rāḥ warĕg kādbhuta abherawa akrak gumantya awĕrö yan pamuṅgĕl gulū niŋ lawan doyan aṅlaṅga rāḥ niŋ trinādi iŋ huwus mātya ya atyanta ghora apan akweḥ dudū taŋ haneŋ bhūmi bhūta aṅgakāra anĕpaḥ maṅsa maṅsö masĕṅhit sumambut musuḥnya ikapi ndān tujaḥ deñcacaḥ cūṙṇna saŋsāra denya n kĕna ndan pirul dan kumis len ikaŋ dꜽtya moha aṅamūk dan dinūk dan gutuk riŋ watu ndan pupuḥ den wunuḥ len tinalyan rinantaynya pan den dudut denya kady-a amatĕk den wawa iŋ ambara agantuṅan denya tan māti kapwa anaṅis,

{daṇḍaka}:95.3:3
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [– ⏑ –]×51 = 159

yadukulabala tañ jriḥ alwaŋ malĕs maṅlwaṅi iŋ rākṣasa aneka tekaŋ pĕjaḥ len ikaŋ ndan gutuk riŋ cĕṅĕl mwaŋ pupū ndan tĕṅaḥ riŋ lĕṅĕn kaṙwwa ḍaṇḍa n ḍumaṇḍa ŋ watĕk dānawa anidra māmraŋ maṅontā n kinontā siliḥ-duk siliḥ-sob siliḥ-cĕṅkaḥ akral tanora aharĕp munduṙ alwat paḍa alwat hana am-waḥ tikā tan patĕṇḍas kawandhanya kapwa ataruŋ leñ cĕṅĕlnya asahut riŋ lĕmaḥ rodra lambe nika abāŋ mibĕk rāḥ piraŋ lakṣa taŋ wīra maṅka adbhuta awak mahābhūta rūpanya sākṣāt prawīra uttama atyanta rodra adbhuta aṅiṇḍarat,

{daṇḍaka}:95.3:3
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [– ⏑ –]×58 = 180

śawa makatĕlĕbuk tibā paṅharĕp niŋ watĕk dꜽtya maṅsö ri saŋ wrĕṣṇiyodhā tatan dwa ŋ ratha syuḥ rĕmĕk de ni tĕmpuḥ ni waṅkay nikaŋ sāmaja apan sawaŋ waṙṣa śꜽla anana adrĕs tibā riŋ watĕk yādawa awrĕg sĕḍĕŋ duṙbala akweḥ pĕjaḥ de ni kontā n linesan ḍawuḥnya awuwuḥ śūla dukduk lawan samby-aṅembuḥ manaḥnya ŋ watĕk rākṣasa iŋ bhūtala amūk-winūk mamraŋ aṅrok-rinok rodra tekaŋ mulu ususnya denya aṅdudut yeka baṇḍut nikeŋ rowaŋ adwandwayuddha amurĕk yan kabaṇḍut siliḥ-kris siliḥ-māti ka aṙwwa iŋ raṇāŋ-ga ika mogha n sinuṅsuŋ niŋ apsary-arūm tuṅgalan ndan rĕbut śīghra māmprĕp muwaḥ*

<śāṙddūlawikrīdita>:96.
– – –|⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

kālanya n marurĕk tikaŋ praŋ asuwe malwaŋ lĕwiḥ sāyuta,
yekā n konduṙ ikaŋ watĕk yadubala akweḥ māti de niŋ panaḥ,
saŋsārā marikā n sinambut ikanaŋ dꜽtya atĕhĕṙ maṅlayaŋ,
rĕmpū syuḥ tinibākĕn iŋ watu rĕmök mwaŋ tĕṇḍas iŋ tuṅgaṅan*

mwaŋ tekaŋ magajaḥ sinambut apuyĕŋ lāwan gajaḥnya inuyĕŋ,
ṅkāna i rowaŋ ikā n winantiṅakĕn iŋ dꜽtya n pagantya aṅalap,
mātī wwaŋ tikanaŋ pamantiŋ an arok taṇḍasnya sāmpun rĕmök,
rĕñcĕm tekaŋ anuṅgaŋ osyan inadunya i rĕṅga niŋ sāmaja*

sakweḥ niŋ bala dꜽtya rodra maṅalap danti inadunya iŋ laṅit,
saṅkĕp bhāwa nika akaruŋ-karuṅan anyat taŋ  maṅadwa a walaŋ,
lāwan taŋ kadi minda de nika maṅadw-i i tampuḥ iŋ sāmaja,
māti mwaŋ gaja paṅgutuk nika ri saŋ yadw-a arĕmuk siŋ kĕna*

akweḥ saŋ yadu māti denya katibān lāwan ratha syuḥ rĕmök,
maṅkin māwrĕg i wuntat awri malayū yan ton sahab niŋ musuḥ,
rĕmpak byūha nira ikanaŋ makarawaktra apan supitnya aradin,
ratw-a abāp mati tan pasāra kawĕnaŋ de niŋ watĕk dānawa*

saŋ rukma aṙjjuna sāmba satyaka sudhīra aṅheṙ dhanuḥ ywa inayat,
śīghra hrū nira yaṙ lĕpas paḍa parĕŋ moliḥ musuḥ rākṣasa,
alwaŋ sewu nĕmaŋ puluḥ pisan ikaŋ dꜽtya aṅlayaŋ riŋ laṅit,
wāhw-a araŋ ri gĕlis niraŋ pat amanaḥ teja hyaŋ aṙkka anĕlat*

maṅkin ta alwaŋ anekadānawa pĕjaḥ mwaŋ wāhananya n tibā,
rowaŋnya n katibān rihĕk hana tikĕl jeṅkel dudū taŋ pĕñĕt,
towin satyaka sāmba maṅlawan ikaŋ dꜽtya ahawan riŋ lĕmaḥ,
hetunya alwaŋ aneka lakṣa niyuta pwa ŋ dꜽtya len rākṣasa*

maṇḍĕg taŋ yaduyodha māri malayū malwī waneḥ riŋ raṇa,
yeka aṅsö nika saŋ mahodara manuṅgaŋ riŋ liman syandana,
saŋ rukmā dinunuŋnya śīghra kumucup tan paṅgalĕŋ sāhasa,
krūranya n pamutĕṙ gadā nika satal göŋnya aṅĕpöṙ yan katon*

tandaŋnya n pamupuḥ ratha nrĕpati rukma syuḥ tĕka iŋ sārathi,
saŋ rukma n tumuluy lumumpat aṅunus patrĕm si tīkṣṇaprabhā,
aṅsö niŋ liman iŋ mahodara kasep kapraŋ gaḍiŋnya apasaḥ,
maṅkin krodha mahodara amurĕkakĕn hastinya pan den wĕlĕg*

muṅgwī hasti nika atriśūla maluṅid paṅduknya sāmpun lĕpas,
trus limpad hati saŋ narādhipati rukmā denya tan kāwaran,
mahyā rākṣasa yan paṅadwakĕn awū taŋ dꜽtya saṅkeŋ laṅit,
hetunya n sumahab muwaḥ paḍa masö muṅsī surendrātmaja*

wadwānya ŋ bala rākṣasa ika makapaṅhañjuṙ nika aṅĕmbuli,
hamham buddhi nikā n tumon kanin iraŋ pāṙtha atĕṅaḥ tan bisa,
liŋnya aṅhel tuwi yan kanin wuwus ikā sambya aṅasut sāhasa,
kontā tomara sañjatanya lumĕpas bāṇanya tan pāntara*

saŋ pāṙtha n rinĕbut pĕnuḥ panaḥ ira iŋ ākāśa digmaṇḍala,
sakweḥ ny-āyudha niŋ musuḥ kapalupuy puṅgĕl kawaṅsul waneḥ,
tātan pāntara de nira aṅlĕpasakĕn hrū śakti kapwa aṅĕne,
dhwasta ŋ rākṣasa siŋ masö kĕna tugĕl tĕṇḍasnya sāmpun tibā*

anyāt rākṣasa dꜽtya tan pasuku len bāhunya sāmpun hilaŋ,
len taŋ kukṣi nikā pĕgat hana bĕlaḥ twasnya apasaḥ riŋ ḍaḍa,
sākṣāt waṙṣa taŋ antra limpa rudhiranya ŋ papraṅan kādbhuta,
awwaḥ mastaka ya agĕlaṙ kunapa niŋ dꜽtyā tiba agĕnturan*

maṅsö saŋ naraka i saŋ aṙjjuna manuṅgaŋ riŋ wimāna akilā,
śīghra apan prihawak makoliha hurip saŋ pāṙtha nā liŋ nira,
tandaŋ saŋ nrĕpaputra sāmba mamupuḥ lambuŋ nikaŋ puṣpaka,
pok rĕg ghoŋ dhwani niŋ wimāna pinupuḥ de saŋ narendrātmaja*

rĕg-rĕg kāṇḍĕg ikaŋ wimāna makihū lambuŋ nika apan tikĕl,
tambis kedĕṙ ikāna sinrĕŋ inusiṙ de jambawatyātmaja,
molaḥ saŋ naraka i punuknya kaguliŋ kāntĕp tibā riŋ lĕmaḥ,
śīghra awuṅw-aṅalap gadā nira satal rodra aṅalimpuŋ katon*

tandaŋ saŋ kṣitija i narendratanaya krodha aṅuhuḥ kātara,
Ꜽ koŋ nīca lihat wĕkasmu n ahurip yeki iŋ gadā yatna ko,
nāhan liŋ nira tan dwa yaṙ pupuhakĕn tekaŋ gadā bhīṣaṇa,
yekā n māti lawan si dāruki parĕŋ saŋ sāmba riŋ sakṣaṇa*

sāmpun māti narendraputra tumuluy saŋ pāṙtha maṅsö sira,
krodha i saŋ naraka aṅayat laras ikaŋ gāṇḍewa pūṙwwa awĕlū,
hrū śakty-a akas agöŋ mayomaya lĕpas de saŋ surendrātmaja,
tampuḥnya n paṅĕne wimāna gumuruḥ sākṣāt garantaŋ humuŋ*

rĕmpak rĕṅga nikaŋ wimāna pinanaḥ kārun tikĕl mwaŋ dhwaja,
sāmpun śīṙṇna pĕgat maṇiknya katibā maṅlaḥ rikaŋ bhūtala,
maṅkin krodha mahīsuta adrĕs umasö muṅsi i surendrātmaja,
puṅgĕl taŋ kapiketu kādrĕsan aṅin de niŋ wimāna n tĕḍun*

lāwan bahni mijil saṅke taṅan iraŋ bhoma atirodra n kutug,
lwiṙ dhūma n sumarambaḥ iŋ raṇatala atyanta iŋ karĕsrĕs katon,
sākṣātnya n waḍawānala aṅalad-alad hagya amaṅan ywa iŋ lĕmaḥ,
maṅkin wrĕddha tĕka aṅgĕsöŋ ratha niraŋ pāṇḍwātmaja i sakṣaṇa*

saŋ pāṙtha ika tatan wikāra maṅayat gāṇḍewa dhīra aṅadĕg,
ṅkā n brahmāstraśarāgni de nira lĕpas tīkṣṇa agra riŋ bhīṣaṇa,
himpĕṙ sūṙyya ri kāla niŋ pralaya tejanya apanas kātara,
śabdanya iŋ gaganāntarāla kumupak sākṣāt gĕlap sāyuta*

tampuḥnya iŋ ḍaḍa saŋ mahīja kumĕtug limpad tanĕmnya adalĕm,
mūṙcchā saŋ naraka asakit sira tiba alĕṇḍö rikaŋ puṣpaka,
ndātan māti sira n hana ŋ wijayamālāpuṣpa saṅkeŋ ibu,
nāhan hetu nira aṅliliṙ dawut ikaŋ hrū śakty-ataṅgal muwaḥ*

tapwan māri hilī nikaŋ rudhira maṅsö dꜽtya mahyuñ jaya,
yekā n sambut ikaŋ lipuŋ makaṅaran sy-a amogha tīkṣṇa ujwala,
tejanya n pinutĕṙ pĕnuḥ kilat ikā jyotṣṇa aduluṙ waṅkawa,
bāyw-a adrĕs kumusuḥ lawañ jalada kedĕṙ ghūṙṇnita agĕnturan*

sampunya n lumĕpas ndatan dwa maṅĕne trus twas niraŋ phalguṇa,
mahyā taŋ bala dꜽtya dānawa humuŋ mwaŋ rākṣasa aṅadwakĕn,
saŋ bhomāsura mantuk iŋ kuwu muwaḥ mwaŋ bhrĕtyaśeṣa aṅiriŋ,
byātītan tinuluŋ kaśakti nira hetunya n hilaŋ taŋ lara*

<wikrĕti>:97.
⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

kunaŋ saŋ amarendraputra lumaḥ iŋ raṇa kasihan ira agilaŋ-gilaŋ,
hibĕk rudhira taŋ ḍaḍa drawa tĕkeŋ mukha makuṭa kabeḥ kasĕmburan,
lawan paṭa nira amiraḥ kadi rinaṇḍi rumakĕt iy awak nira umĕlĕs,
tĕkeŋ kawaca hīrabajra kadi ta atĕmaha pawal apan katon abāŋ*

lĕyĕp ni mata saŋ dhanañjaya sawaŋ rawi katawĕṅan iŋ lamad-lamad,
ikaŋ gĕluŋ asāk mĕlĕs karudhiran kadi jalada rinĕṅga riŋ kilat,
halĕp ni mukha nisprabha asĕmu kucĕm kadi ta laṅit i kāla niŋ damar,
aśeṣa manis iŋ mata asĕmu guladrawa raḥ ira ri tuṅtuŋ iŋ halis*

<mālāwādi>:98.
⏑⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 27

i pĕjaḥ saŋ aṙjjuna humuŋ tikaŋ bhuwana ghūṙṇnita ŋ jaladhi mombakan mawalikan,
kumĕtug tikaŋ widik awaṅkawa asaliwĕran taṭitnya tan arĕn gĕlap masahuran,
gumiwaŋ mahītala śila adri kampita rubuḥ pucaknya humabĕt rĕbaḥ tahĕn ikā,
hyaŋ anantabhoga calitāgra hogaḥ asuwe dhumāraṇa ri polaḥ i kṣititala*

kapĕgan katonan ikanaŋ jagattri pĕpĕk iŋ lĕbū tĕka lawan hudan hawu mĕlĕk,
tuwi tan pateja ri surup bhaṭāra rawi diṅmukha amrĕm akucĕm wirūpa mawĕnĕs,
panaṅis nikaŋ gĕrĕḥ asaṅghani i jaladhi tan papāntara humuŋ swaranya gumuruḥ,
kĕtĕṙ iŋ patĕṙ tan arĕn iŋ digantara karĕṅw-awaṙṇna sĕsĕgĕn lana aṅisĕk-isĕk*

<waṅśastha>:99.
⏑ – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏓ = 12

atītanĕn saŋ nrĕpaputra phalguṇa,
kunaŋ watĕk yādawaśeṣa duṙbala,
paḍa alara aśā kawĕkas wimūṙcchita,
pĕtĕŋ nikaŋ twas kadi riŋ tĕṅaḥ wĕṅi*

wirāṭarāja drupada atiduhkhita,
ra somadatta prihatin sira aputĕk,
ri taṇ ḍatĕŋ bhūpati keśawa iŋ raṇa,
na hetu niŋ motus amĕṅyakĕn laku*

kunaŋ ta saŋ śrī harimūṙttibhūpati,
tĕlas mamūja i labuhan mahāyati,
umaṅkat āgyā ḍatĕṅa ahawan kulĕm,
haneŋ hawan mwaŋ sira saŋ halāyudha*

tatas tikaŋ rātri mawā ta sakṣaṇa,
ḍatĕŋ ta konkonan iraŋ watĕk ratu,
wawaŋ manĕmbaḥ ri siraŋ halāyudha,
lawan ri saŋ śrī harimūṙttibhūpati*

paḍa awaraḥ ywa i gati saŋ dhanañjaya,
ya hetu saŋ śrī nrĕpa keśawa alaris,
tan antyakĕn sampuna niŋ waraḥ sira,
tuhun drĕs iŋ lampaḥ ira ahawan ratha*

samaṅkana ikaŋ bala dꜽtya rākṣasa,
wawaŋ sumuṅsuŋ lumaga i nareśwara,
pĕnuḥ ta dꜽtya iŋ gaganāntara atĕtĕl,
tĕkeŋ lĕmaḥ sök hibĕkan bala asura*

larap nikaŋ kañcana ratna bhūṣana,
lawan kĕñaṙ niŋ kawaca ayudha akilat,
liman lawan syandana wāji wāhana,
amānuṣa atyanta halĕpnya bhāswara*

katon sakeŋ doḥ pwa ya de nareśwara,
rĕpatnya tindaknya maṅuṇḍa sañjata,
sihuŋ nika akās maluṅid paḍa asalit,
matanya malwa adbhuta kātara ujwala*

masö ta saŋ śrī nrĕpa krĕṣṇa sāhasa,
lawan sira śrī baladewa sāyudha,
ikaŋ watĕk dꜽtya haneŋ nabhastala,
cinakra niśśeṣa tĕkap janāṙddana*

śawanya himpĕṙ hudan adrĕs adbhuta,
haṅinya tan pāntara wagyut ujwala,
gĕlap ni śabdanya humuŋ tĕkeŋ lĕmaḥ,
gajāśwa tulya wwaḥ ika asusun tibā*

ikaŋ watĕk dꜽtya haneŋ mahītala,
ya ta inasö bhrĕtya narendra keśawa,
rathanya makweḥ saha pādarakṣaka,
rinoknya wadwā baladewa riŋ gajaḥ*

nanā ta wadwā baladewa kāmbulan,
rikā n tumandaŋ tumuluy halāyudha,
saha krĕp iŋ sāmaja wrĕddhawāhana,
tĕka amupuḥ riŋ muśalāstra sāhasa*

aneka ta lwaŋ nikanaŋ bala asura,
dudū tikaŋ māti cinakra tan pira,
śawanya tulya aṅkura sāk amaṙwwata,
hilī ni rāḥnya adrĕs awaṙṇna wāḥ gunuŋ*

rikā n masö saŋ mapatiḥ mahodara,
manuṅgaŋ iŋ syandana sāmaja agalak,
sahab ni wadwānya paḍa agajaḥ kabeḥ,
asĕṅhit aṅduk mamanaḥ maṅĕmbuli*

pĕtĕŋ pĕpĕt bhrĕtya nikaŋ mahodara,
riwut katonanya saha adhwaja ahirĕŋ,
sawaŋ rawi śrī baladewa kāmbulan,
mahāprabhāwa n pamupuḥ bala asura*

marĕn kuniŋ waṙṇna niraŋ halāyudha,
tĕkap ni rāḥ niŋ ripu māti de nira,
tĕkeŋ halu mwaŋ wuluku pwa ya amiraḥ,
lawan ratha awaṙṇna hañaṙ cināraṇa*

parĕŋ pamūk niŋ balawīra sök sĕsök,
paḍa ahawan wāhana sāha sāmaja,
alaḥ tikaŋ rākṣasa pādarakṣaka,
rinok minohan linawan siliḥ-sĕsĕb*

mahodara asĕṅhit i saŋ halāyudha,
tumandaŋ amraŋ baḍamanya pāt ḍĕpa,
tinaṅkis iŋ laṅgala de halāyudha,
sinep dinuk riŋ halu ghora yan tibā*

tĕlas pĕjaḥ saŋ mapatiḥ mahodara,
masö tikaŋ dꜽtya muwaḥ maṅĕmbuli,
narendra krĕṣṇa ika winūknya sāhasa,
pĕnuḥ tikaŋ bhūmi tĕkeŋ nabhastala*

prabhāswara atyanta halĕpnya riŋ laṅit,
dukūla wastranya waneḥ prabha asinaŋ,
maṇik nika abhrā kawacanya kañcana,
kadi pwa wintaŋ yan i kāla niŋ tilĕm*

lĕpas ni kontānya panaḥnya tan pĕgat,
aneka denya aṅhudani i warāyudha,
hanan harĕp mamraŋ amogha yan katon,
wulatnya meṅas tumuluy maliṇḍuṅan*

masö ta saŋ śrī nrĕpa keśawa iŋ musuḥ,
mañakra tan pāntara riŋ bala asura,
ikaŋ watĕk rākṣasa dꜽtya dānawa,
kadi pwa ya inuṇḍuḥ abāp tiba iŋ lĕmaḥ*

hanan tugĕl tūṙnya wĕtĕŋnya len gulū,
ri bāhu sĕmpal sasisiḥ lawañ cĕṅĕl,
hanan śiwak paṙwwa parĕŋ tiba apisan,
waneḥ sawaŋ rumbaḥ abāŋ kasamburat*

huwus hilaŋ taŋ bala dꜽtya riŋ laṅit,
tuluy lumampaḥ naranātha keśawa,
lawan tika śrī baladewa hop glisan,
tĕkap nira agyā mulata i saŋ aṙjjuna*

<upendrabajra>:100.
⏑ – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏓ = 11

katon taŋ utpāta riwut praduṙgga,
kĕtug nikaŋ loṙ kidul iŋ digānta,
samaṅkana ŋ dāruki yan paśabda,
ri pāduka śrī nrĕpa padmanābha*

narāṙyya santabya patik narendra,
mucap mahotpāta ḍatĕŋ rikeŋ rāt,
ndatan sakeŋ bhīta kĕta ŋ maśabda,
ri pamriha śrī naranātha donya*

kunĕŋ patik śrī naranātha hopĕn,
mucap kaśaktin prĕthiwīsuta iŋ rāt,
ikaŋ wimāna atiśaya iŋ prabhāwa,
nimitta saŋ bhoma jaya iŋ triloka*

wwaya ikahĕn śꜽla maṇik nira agöŋ,
makambaṅan riŋ gaganāntarāla,
hĕlaṙ nikā n tulya sayojana alwā,
ya ta uṅgwan iŋ strī tawan aprameya*

kunaŋ pratijñā nira saŋ mahīja,
tatan pamuktya ŋ wararājakanyā,
ya tan huwus rakwa jaya iŋ narendra,
kadhīran iŋ bhoma duwĕg wiwākṣan*

hana ika kĕmbaŋ wijaya ika rakwa,
paweḥ bhaṭārī prĕthiwi i mahīja,
yadin paratrā kṣitija i raṇāṅga,
ya tan hilaŋ kĕmbaŋ ika ahurip ya*

ya ta ikahĕn keṅĕta saŋ narendra,
wiwākṣitan dāya niŋ aṅlagāna,
nahan liŋ iŋ dāruki saprayatna,
umodha saŋ śrī nrĕpa padmanābha*

ḍatĕŋ ta saŋ nātha rikaŋ pakuwwan,
rikā n kapaṅguḥ yadu-wrĕṣṇi māti,
kunaŋ pwa saŋ satyaka duhkha moruk,
marĕk ri saŋ bhūpati śīghra mojar*

sira awaraḥ ry-uṅgwan iraŋ kirīṭi,
wawaŋ matanduk tumuluy narendra,
katon ta saŋ pāṙtha rujit kĕna iŋ hrū,
lawan tikaŋ twas tarawaŋ kĕna iŋ duk*

samaṅkana śrī nrĕpa padmanābha,
mĕkul ri saŋ pāṙtha nĕhĕṙ masambat,
hariṅku tiṅhal ri si krĕṣṇa pāpa,
tatan wĕnaŋ rakṣaka niŋ swawaṙgga*

nihan kita antĕn pĕjaḥ iŋ raṇāṅga,
ṅhulun ikā hetu niki n tatan len,
asiḥta ri ṅwaŋ karaṇanta māmriḥ,
lukan pwa yan māti lĕwĕs laraṅku*

<prĕthwītala>:101.
⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – –| ⏑ ⏓ = 17

nahan wuwus ira n musap mukha ni saŋ narendrātmaja,
dhanañjaya sira atahĕn mulati saŋ narendra anaṅis,
ndatan mara hilaŋ tĕmĕn kĕtĕ-kĕtĕg nira i sakṣaṇa,
parĕŋ mwaŋ i hilaŋ ni citta naranātha krĕṣṇa alara*

sĕḍĕŋ nrĕpati krĕṣṇa mūṙcchita ḍatĕŋ siraŋ durwaśa,
wawaŋ praṇata saŋ narāṙyya maṅusap ri jöŋ saŋ yati,
samaṅkana mahāṙṣi yan paṅupasāntwa saŋ bhūpati,
wuwus nira krĕtāṙthadhaṙmma pitutuṙ waraḥ siḥ tĕmĕn*

narendra diwasa ŋ wimūṙcchita puriḥ nikaŋ wwaŋ pĕjaḥ,
wruhanta rikanaŋ carācara ninitya tekā kabeḥ,
bhaṭāra tumitaḥ ta haywa ta kita pramāda irikā,
ikaŋ pati wiśeṣamāṙgga marikā n gatinya n hana*

kalīṅan ika haywa saŋ prabhu wimoha de niŋ lara,
tamomaya dahat manaḥ tatan ulaḥ niŋ aṅrakṣa rāt,
rajahsahitasatwabuddhi rikanā gĕgön de haji,
phalanya-ya wĕnaŋ sumiddhakĕna kāṙyya saŋ bhūpati*

kunaŋ pwa haji don mami i kita nihan hana anugraha,
paweha ri narendra maṅhuripana irikā saŋ pĕjaḥ,
tuhun sasiki rakwa ya uliha nika i saliŋ saŋ prabhu,
si sāmba karikā ya ta iki basudewa yan phālguṇa*

ndya ta iku kaharĕpta haywa masuwe waraḥta ṅhulun,
nahan wacana saŋ mahāṙṣi sumahuṙ ta saŋ bhūpati,
kĕnoḥ wacana saŋ mahāmuni pawehana anugraha,
kunaŋ pwa kadi kepwan i ṅhulun apan paḍa aṅde wĕlas*

siḥ i ṅwaŋ akadaŋ ya kölakĕna de ranak saŋ yati,
dhanañjaya huwus hana anak ipun uttama aṅgantyani,
narendra basudewa sāmpun atuha awĕka akweḥ tĕmĕn,
si sāmba pukulun sade nipun apan punaŋ wwaŋ sanak*

kunaŋ pwa ŋ amaṅun lara i hati ranak mahaṙṣy-a awĕlas,
nrĕpa druma pĕjaḥ mamet śaraṇa ri ṅhulun kāsihan,
ya hetu niŋ aminta sanmata mahāṙṣi ri pwaṅkulun,
anugrahana jīwita ahuripa de mahāpaṇḍita*

<mrĕdukomala>:102.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 18

nāhan śabda narendra krĕṣṇa sumahuṙ ta saŋ rĕṣiwara,
siṅgiḥ sādhu nareśwara aharĕp i dhaṙmma saŋ mamawa rāt,
swasty-astu prabhu saŋ paṅāśrayana niŋ triloka tulusa,
niṙwighna ajayaśatru saŋ narapati irikaŋ pabharatan*

lāwan pājaran i ṅhulun ri haji haywa wismrĕti kita,
an sākṣāt naranātha wiṣṇu sakalātmaka aparimita,
śaktinta ika sake kasiddhyan iy awakta tan hana waneḥ,
māyākāra tikaŋ śarīra paramāṙthadewata kita*

nistanyan kita mānuṣākrĕti yayañ jaya iŋ kṣitisuta,
Āpan siḥ mami hetu saŋ prabhu manĕmwa śakty-atiśaya,
yoga adhyātmika sādhananta saha buddhi sattwa mahĕniŋ,
astu śrī naranātha siddhi sakala n pamaṅgiha yaśa*

sāmpun saŋ paramaṙṣi mājaṙ i narendra māsiḥ awĕlas,
antaṙllīna sira iŋ kamantyan aṅadĕg ta saŋ narapati,
muṅgaḥ riŋ ratha śīghra maṅkat iniriŋ nikaŋ bala kabeḥ,
mwaŋ saŋ śrī baladewa satyaka tumūt hane wuri nira*

maṅkat saŋ naranātha krĕṣṇa rumĕṅö ta saŋ kṣitisuta,
sāmpun muṅgw-irikaŋ wimāna maṇipuṣpaka asiga sira,
maṅkat mwaŋ bala dꜽtya-dānawa sĕsök lakunya mariwĕg,
prāpta iŋ papraṅan adbhuta ŋ bala humuŋ maraṅkit alaga*

tandaŋ śrī baladewa sāhasa mupuḥ mahāsurabala,
mwaŋ saŋ satyaka śālya len drupada saŋ wirāṭanrĕpati,
kapwa aganti sira amanaḥ karaṇa niŋ bala asura nanā,
aṇḍĕḥ niŋ bala dꜽtya-dānawa malĕs ta ya amarawaśa*

henak taŋ praŋ arok siliḥ-sĕsĕb aneka wīra kawĕnaŋ,
paṅhrik niŋ kuda wāhana mwaŋ ika śabda niŋ kakuwuṅan,
yekā n lot karĕṅö lawan patakis iŋ gada asriŋ apalu,
kontā tomara kakrĕcik saha kĕtug nikaŋ pamugari*

gĕṇḍiŋ goŋ gubaṙ apratidhwani sahasra bhinna karĕṅö,
kālanya ŋ praŋ arok masö ta si nisunda dꜽtya pinatiḥ,
toḥ jīwa amrihakĕn ri saŋ naraka lāgy-akīṙtti riŋ ayun,
ndā hetunya kinon tĕkap saŋ asureśwara amriḥ ayaśa*

maṅkat mwaŋ bala wāhananya sakasewu mukhya winani,
muṅsi i saŋ nrĕpa śālya sāhasa masiṅhanāda gumuruḥ,
wadwā saŋ nrĕpa śālya yatna mamanaḥ riŋ astra niśita,
meṅas taŋ paṅarĕp manoliḥ i wuri n panon lawan amūk*

goŋ-goŋ-goŋ muni goŋ nareśwara kumon swabhrĕtya malaga,
aṅkat niŋ gajawrĕnda tuṅgaṅan i wuntat iŋ ratha tumūt,
kapwa atampuḥ arok tikaŋ bala siliḥ-praŋ osyan asuwe,
tan pānta i waratomara aṙddha tumitiḥ sawaŋ hudan agöŋ*

sakweḥ niŋ bala saŋ nisunda n umasö mamūk tan atakut,
kontā kadga gadā tuhuk pinakasañjatanya sawaneḥ,
len teka aṅalaŋ iŋ śilā sakuruṅan ta ya n katihalaŋ,
dantī syandana tuṅgaṅan mati tĕkapnya tan hana bisa*

awrĕg bhrĕtya narendra madrapati tan pasāra wĕkasan,
nāhan hetu narendra yatna malaga aṅayat laras agöŋ,
hrū bajrāśani śuṣka sewu lumĕpas pisan tĕka pira,
śīṙṇna syuḥ bala dꜽtya denya saha wāhananya kawĕnaŋ*

yekā n tandaŋ ikaŋ nisunda mamanaḥ ri saŋ narapati,
hrūnya aneka ya ta aṅĕne dhwaja narendra puṅgĕl apasaḥ,
lāwan sārathi māti denya kadrĕsan panaḥ narapati,
maṅkin sāhasa saŋ nisunda mamĕḍĕk maha amarĕpĕki*

hetunya n paṅalap ri tomara nikā prabhāswara katon,
prāyanya aṅduk asep lĕṅĕnya pinanaḥ tĕkap narapati,
wāhw-a anambut ikaŋ kiwanya pinanaḥ muwaḥ rinuhunan,
sāmpun tĕṅgĕk ikā n pĕgat hulu nika aṅlayaŋ kadi hĕlaŋ*

ambĕknya apulihan ta lāwan ika saŋ narendra wĕkasan,
hetunya n tumĕḍun sakeŋ gagana göŋ swaranya karĕṅö,
wruḥ saŋ nātha mahā prayatna maṅalap swaḍaṇḍa tumuluy,
tampuḥnya iŋ śiraḥ iŋ nisunda kumĕpok mukhanya pinupuḥ*

sāmpun māti nisunda maṅkin abutĕŋ ta saŋ kṣitisuta,
wwantĕn dꜽtya ṅaranya pañcajana śakti lāgi paṅalaḥ,
len saṅke rikanaŋ si pañcajana māti riŋ jalanidhi,
krūra akral tahu ta aṅlawan hyaŋ irikā n kinon apuliha*

muṅgwiŋ sāmaja pat gaḍiŋnya kadi paṙwwata alaku-laku,
tandaŋnya i baladewa śūla rinĕgĕpnya kātara murub,
lāwan bahni murub sakeŋ mata nikā lana alatu-latu,
śīṙṇna ikaŋ bala rohiṇīsuta gĕsĕŋ waneḥ kapanasan*

tandaŋ saŋ baladewa laṅgala minuṣṭi de nira masö,
muṅgwi i syandana śīghra yaṙ putĕrakĕn ta sañjata nira,
krūra akrak maṅuhuḥ si pañcajana heṙ lihat jaga-jaga,
liŋnya n paṅduk aṅadwakĕn mati ya liŋnya yan panudiṅi*

yatna śrī baladewa yaṙ takisakĕn ta laṅgala nira,
puṅgĕl śūla nikā si pañcajana bhagna kontal atĕhĕr,
nāhan hetu nikaŋ si pañcajana mĕtta maṅduk amuwaḥ,
tan poliḥ tinakis muwaḥ tikĕl apaṙwwa tan pajamuga*

ambĕk niṙbhaya dꜽtya pañcajana mamriha amulihana,
kagyat yan ginayuṙ gulūnya kapuliṙ pĕjaḥ kapisanan,
hetunya awrĕg ikaŋ bala asura sahāya maṅkin alayū,
muṅsiṙ saŋ kṣitija aruhun-ruhunan atri māty-alulunan*

<aparāntikā>:103.
⏑ ⏑ –| – ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 11

si hayagrīwa wawaŋ ta ya apuliḥ,
tan aṅiṣṭi i paṅutus mahīsuta,
ri harĕpnya aṅrahatāna riŋ tuhan,
karaṇanya n prihawak ta ya umasö*

kadunuŋ satyaka de nika umasö,
pinanaḥnya iŋ śara bāṇa sāyaka,
mamalĕs pwā mamanaḥ ta satyaka,
śarasampāta lĕwiḥ panaḥ nira*

katulak bāṇa nika asurādhipa,
hana kedĕṙ kawaluy waneḥ puhĕr,
si hayagrīwa makin magöŋ galak,
umalap hrūnya sutīkṣṇa śaktiman*

tinujunya ika gulū ni satyaka,
patitisnya amatitis tĕlas katon,
lumĕpas hrūnya sĕḍĕŋ haneŋ laṅit,
sinawat de ni panaḥ ni satyaka*

irikā satyaka sāhasa amalĕs,
mamanaḥ riŋ niśitāṙddhacandrama,
si hayagrīwa gulū nika apĕgat,
lumaḥ iŋ syandana kaṙwwa sārathi*

<aśwalalita>:104.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

ri pĕjaḥ ikā n hana iky-asuradānawa apuliḥ anuṅgaŋ iŋ ratha magöŋ,
ṅaran ika tāra lāgi paṅalaḥ watĕk hyaŋ ika ṅūni riŋ daṅu-daṅū,
saha bala yeka tan dwa tumitiḥ lumiṇḍiḥ irikaŋ watĕk yadubala,
pinapagakĕn tĕkap nrĕpatiy ugrasena paḍa śakti tan hana kasor*

narapatiy ugrasena mamanaḥ riŋ agniśara caṇḍabāyusahita,
pinapagakĕn riŋ aṙṇnawarasa atighora gumuruḥ tĕkeŋ awaŋ-awaŋ,
paḍĕm ikaŋ agnisāyaka muwaḥ narendra mamanaḥ muwaḥ linawanan,
salĕkas ira ikihĕn wiphala hetu saŋ nrĕpati dhꜽṙyya dhāraka masö*

kunĕŋ irikā n si tāra masiga dyaya n mulati saŋ narendra mabutĕŋ,
rumĕgĕp i tomaranya manĕhĕṙ marĕk tudiṅi teka saŋ narapati,
lihat i taṅanku liŋnya tumuluy narendra maṅalap krĕtāla wĕkasan,
paḍa maparĕk dinuk nrĕpati tan kĕna amalĕs sira amraŋ oliḥ i gulū*

<mrĕdukomala>:105.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 18

mātī tāra sarodra saŋ kṣitisuta umasö sira wawaŋ,
śīṙṇna ikaŋ bala paṅharĕp nrĕpati keśawāṅśa pinanaḥ,
śīghra śrī nrĕpa krĕṣṇa maṅlĕpasakĕn śarottama sira,
dhwasta ŋ dānawa-dꜽtya de nira sapaṅharĕp kṣitisuta*

yekā n sāhasa saŋ mahīsuta haneŋ wimāna magĕlis,
cĕt muṅgwiŋ wuri cĕt haneŋ harĕp amet i cidra caliriŋ,
yatna śrī naranātha keśawa haneŋ ratha akuliliṅan,
Ādrĕs tan katĕṅĕṙ lĕkas nira ri madhya niŋ raṇasabhā*

krodha ambĕk naraka akrak iŋ gagana kātara aṅamaḥ-amaḥ,
nāhan hetu nira n tĕka aṅabĕnakĕn si puṣpaka sira,
puṅgĕl tanda narendra krĕṣṇa matahĕn tibā katariwal,
luṅhā saŋ kṣitija aṅlayaŋ muwaḥ amiṇḍa riŋ jaladhara*

śrī krĕṣṇa atiśaya iŋ gĕlĕŋ mayatakĕn panaḥ nira muwaḥ,
nyā ŋ nārāyaṇabāṇa mrĕtyuradhana ika de nira lĕpas,
wagyūtpāta halisyus adbhuta duluṙnya kātara dahat,
tan wyaṙtha n paṅĕne laras kṣitija śīṙṇna puṅgĕl i taṅan*

kombul kedĕṙ ikaŋ wimāna kahiriŋ tĕkap niŋ anila,
maṅkin tan hinĕbaŋ-hĕbaŋ ta ya cinakra de narapati,
himpĕṙ handaru sewu tulya ni tatal-tatalnya sumawur,
gĕntĕṙ yan tumibā prakampa gumiwaŋ tikaŋ kṣititala*

śīṙṇna ikaŋ maṇipuṣpaka ndan ika saŋ mahīja mahurip,
Āpan tan tumuluy cinakra sira de narendra sakarĕŋ,
towin kambaŋ ira ikanaŋ wijayamālapuṣpa tinahā,
saṅke hyaŋ prĕthiwī paweḥ nira bhaṭāra wiṣṇu ri sira*

saṅketanya rikāna de nira tĕlas prakāśa karĕṅö,
tan pāmātyana siŋ mahāyudha tumampuha iŋ kṣitisuta,
nāhan hetu narendra krĕṣṇa sira taṙ wawaŋ raga-ragan,
Āpañ jāti nira n krĕtajña mawiweka yan palĕkasa*

<bhadralalita>:106.
⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 21

ri sĕḍĕŋ mahīsuta hilaŋ wimāna nira niṙbhaya aṅawaŋ-awaŋ,
maṅagĕm sy-amogha sira dug pracaṇḍa pinutĕṙ nira aṅarab-arab,
tumĕḍun sakeŋ gagana ghūṙṇnita aṅamaḥ-amaḥ sira aṅaraḥ-araḥ,
lumĕpas lipuŋ nira sakeŋ taṅan murub awaṙṇna sūṙyya maṅaliḥ*

saha bāyubajra kumutug dudū ṅhaliwawaṙ lĕbū lĕwu pĕtĕŋ,
lĕpas saṅka riŋ kṣitisuta aṅasut nrĕpati krĕṣṇa len bala kabeḥ,
naranātha krĕṣṇa tumuluy sira aṅlĕpasi cakra tan papĕgatan,
sumĕsĕb sy-amogha tugĕl iŋ nabhastala wiśīṙṇna tan patĕmahan*

ikanaŋ pĕtĕŋ juga ya tan marĕn tumutup iŋ raṇāṅganasabhā,
yatika bhramanta paḍa tan katon sahana niŋ prawīra malaga,
ṅhiŋ ikaŋ liman turaga maṅhrik atry-awurahan ya nitya karĕṅö,
kalawan krĕcik ni tĕwĕk iŋ mayodha matakis lawan waja galaḥ*

awĕlas narendra harimūṙtti kāraṇa nira asamādhi wĕkasan,
irika atriwikrama bhaṭāra krĕṣṇa sira wiṣṇu rodra sakala,
aruhuṙ dudug sira tĕka irikaŋ paramasatyaloka tumuluy,
ikanaŋ ḍaḍa atiśaya riŋ lwa māṅuhabi loka saŋ hyaŋ i ruhur*

tuwi sewu tĕṇḍas ira kapwa ta atrinayana i satĕṇḍas umurub,
asalit sihuŋ nira kunaŋ tutuk nira guhā paḍanya n umaṅaŋ,
mwaŋ ikaŋ taṅan pituŋ iwu prakīṙṇna maṅagĕm warāyudha kabeḥ,
kadi meru kĕmbaṙ ikanaŋ sukū rwa mawĕki ŋ mahītala pĕpĕk*

ḍĕṅĕn iŋ triloka tumatiŋ haneŋ wulu nira ahirĕŋ kadi sĕmut,
hana yan paṅaṙwwani waneḥ dudū taŋ aṅatĕlwani ŋ wulu siki,
saha sañjatanya bahĕluŋ ladiŋ paḍa masumpahan saha wĕḍuŋ,
mawĕḍak-wĕḍak rudhira bhīṣaṇa asawit usus tĕkeŋ paru-paru*

sumĕnö tikaŋ makuṭa sewu bhāskara sahasra tulya mapupul,
mwaŋ ikaŋ maṇik rwaŋ iwu kuṇḍala atiśaya bhāswaranya n umurub,
dilaḥ iŋ sihuŋ pataŋ iwu mwaŋ astra kadi bahni tīkṣṇa lumarap,
karaṇanya māwa wĕkasan tikaŋ pabharatan katon taŋ alaga*

bala dꜽtyadānawa pĕjaḥ piraŋ puluḥ atus ya kedĕk apĕñĕt,
saha wāhananya gaja koṭi-koṭi milu māti kedĕkan apil,
ikanaŋ haneŋ gagana konduṙ āwrĕg alulun katuṇḍuŋ iŋ awak,
muririŋ kagĕm kĕna ḍinĕṇḍa riŋ ḍĕṅĕn awū cinakra ginadā*

ri sĕḍĕŋ bhaṭāra hari matriwikrama ḍataŋ ta sañjata nira,
maṅaran si nandaka si pañcajanya kalawan gadā sama dulur,
ṅuniweḥ ta saŋ garuḍa śīghra kapwa sawawa i bhaṭāra yan agöŋ,
paḍa sewu taŋ harĕp akīṙttya maṅrahatana iŋ bhaṭāra humarĕk*

umulat pwa saŋ naraka yan triwikrama bhaṭāra wiṣṇu sakala,
yatikā n saroṣa tumuluy triwikrama muwaḥ sira aruhuṙ agöŋ,
kadi paṙwwata atumaŋ ikaŋ hawak winilĕt iŋ ghana akilat arĕs,
mwaŋ ikaŋ sphuliṣṭatikara umijil saka rikaŋ sihuŋ pat aghaṣa*

tumuluy sira aṅalap ikaŋ gada awĕsi sayojana ujwala katon,
pamupuḥ nira iŋ sira bhaṭāra wiṣṇu wiphala n kasaṅga ri taṅan,
amupuḥ muwaḥ tinakis iŋ gada awĕsi makādhikāra riŋ agöŋ,
tĕka riŋ diganta karĕṅö dhwaninya kadi rūga ŋ aṇḍabhuwana*

kṣitiputra dhīra maṅagĕm prĕp adbhuta ri göŋnya paṙwwatasama,
sahasa amrĕp aṅhala-hala irikaŋ ḍaḍa bhaṭāra tuṅgĕŋ atĕguḥ,
dhwani niŋ gĕlap śatasahasrakoṭi pakaśabda niŋ prĕp anitir,
paḍa saṅśaya ṅhyaŋ anahā waliŋnya rubuha ŋ laṅit mawurahan*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:107.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| – –  ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

gutgūtĕn ta bhaṭāra wiṣṇu mamalĕs mamrĕp ri saŋ bhūmija,
göŋ niŋ prĕp nira merutulya maṅĕne tĕṇḍas ni bhūmyātmaja,
yekā n kontal ikaŋ maṇikmakuṭa saŋ bhoma irikaŋ sāgara,
tampuḥ niŋ śatakoṭi handaru tibā tulyanya ghora akĕtug*

lumpat saŋ garuḍa aṅalap wijayamālāpuṣpa saŋ bhūmija,
wāhw-a aṅambil ikā n prayatna naraka amraŋ wꜽnateya iŋ tĕwĕk,
yeka apaṙwwa bĕlaḥ śiwak ḍaḍa ni saŋ pakṣīndra rāḥ lwiṙ hudan,
eṅgal mampĕt apan sira amrĕtamaya atyanta iŋ kasiddhan sira*

sāmpun kālap ikaŋ sĕkaṙ wijayamālā de kagendra aṅlayaŋ,
maṅsö hyaŋ hari śīghra yan sikĕp ikā saŋ bhoma siṅhākrĕti,
sātus hasta nira amrĕp aṅhala-hala iŋ taṇḍas niraŋ bhūmija,
rĕmpū syuḥ mapasewu de nira śiraḥ saŋ dꜽtyarājā n pĕjaḥ*

sāmpun māti mahīja waṅkay ira meḥ-meḥ yan tibā riŋ lĕmaḥ,
kontal riŋ wĕkasan tinampik i hĕlaṙ saŋ wꜽnateya abaṅĕt,
ṅkāna i madhya nikaŋ samudra tumibā kagyat hyaŋ iŋ sāgara,
eṅgal yan tĕka riŋ rasātala ri paṅkwan śrī prĕthiwy-a anaṅis*

<jagaddhita>:108.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

byātītan mati saŋ mahīsuta kunaŋ tura-turaḥ ikanaŋ balāsura,
aṅboṅlot asĕnötan iŋ jaladhi nāgata ri sira bhaṭāra keśawa,
len tekaŋ maṅusiṙ gunuŋ gahana gahwara paraṅan arĕs magantuṅan,
saŋsāra ŋ kanin aṅlaḥ amriḥ atĕkĕn kawĕlas-arĕp aṅaṅsaṙ iŋ juraŋ*

maṅkat śrī baladewa maṅraraḥ anūt ṅ-asura kuwu-kuwunya sāk punaḥ,
ṅkā yan paṅgiḥ ikaŋ gunuŋ maṇik akambaṅan atiśaya kādbhuta ahĕlar,
akweḥ wrĕkṣa-latanya ratnamaya jaṅga nika kanaka mĕmbaŋ iŋ liraŋ,
mwaŋ groŋ-groŋ ni juraŋ-juraŋnya humiriŋ watu karaŋ i hiriŋnya komala*

strīratna aṙjja hana irikaŋ maṇimaya asĕmu maṇik inurā kasamburat,
raśminya n paṅurꜽ gĕluŋnya kadi nīlajalada mata komala amanis,
sĕṅsöŋ niŋ miraḥ iŋ laṭī kakĕñaran dinakara maṇibhāswara ahulap,
rūpanya aniru hintĕn esi dinĕlö raras i hajĕŋ ikā n pacendrika*

wwantĕn ta alihaṅan karaŋ pracala piṇḍa tulis inapi dèwa niŋ pĕṭa,
waṙṇnanya akuniŋ anwam iŋ pamulu wimba ni sĕkaṙ iŋ aśoka cāmpaka,
himpĕṙ pādapa rekha-rekha ni tĕṅaḥnya winuri-wuri niŋ tapiḥ suji,
lindinya n tinĕtĕs hajöŋnya ri matā winulatakĕn i raśmi niŋ sipat*

paṇḍan lĕŋlĕŋ i duṅhus iŋ watu karaŋ sphaṭika kinasut iŋ hima anipis,
jaṅganya asĕkaṙ aṅjraḥ aṅjamanika anisiḥ akataraḥ aṙjja kāṅinan,
ṅkā wwantĕn wanita amaṅun lĕṅĕŋ amaṅku wĕtis aṅĕliḥ aṅligā tĕṅaḥ,
waṙṇna hyaŋ-hyaṅan iŋ ṭikā kajĕnĕkan lĕyĕp alĕbu-lĕbū hrĕbuk miṅiŋ*

kālap taŋ giriratna de haladhara akĕmitan awĕdi riŋ jaruḥ-jaruḥ,
mwaŋ taŋ komala hagraśeṣa nira saŋ kṣititanaya madum-dum iŋ bala,
eṅgal prāpta huwus haneŋ kuwu muwaḥ nda tucapa ta bhaṭāra keśawa,
māha iŋ göŋ kadi wuntwa taŋ bhuwana de nira rawi sumurup sake taṅan*

hyaŋ brahmā sira śīghra yaṇ ḍatĕŋ anĕmbaḥ ararĕm i bhaṭāra keśawa,
bhakty-a aṅastuti liŋ nira n prabhu wiśeṣa kita waśawasitwa bhūpati,
utpatti-sthiti-līṇa niŋ bhuwana kāraṇa nika kita n ādidewatā,
bhokta iŋ bhogya kita atmaśuddha puruṣottama kita paramāṙtha kewala*

yan riŋ sandhi katatwan iŋ praṇawadewa kita makaśarīra ŋ akṣara,
lit niŋ sūtra subaddhabandhana binandha kita paramatatwa duṙlabha,
yan riŋ jyotiṣatantra tan hana waneḥ kita sipat i katĕmwan iŋ pinet,
saŋ kṣepanya wiśeṣa riŋ tiga bhaṭāra paramaśiwa n iṣṭidewatā*

nyā ŋ loka ahyun i tatwa ni hyaŋ iŋ apa n wruha ri gati bhaṭāra yan wibhuḥ,
prajñā yan pamasaŋ samāhita tathāpi wiṣaya nika tan tĕke kita,
saŋ yogīśwara towi tan wĕnaŋ ataṙkka ri kita humĕnĕŋ kuraŋ hiḍĕp,
pūjā dhyāna samādhi dhaṙmma pitutuṙ panalimuṙ ira riŋ kapaṇḍitan*

sāmpun maṅkana liŋ prajāpati maṅastuti tĕka sira dewatā kabeḥ,
bhakty-a ahyun mulata i bhaṭāra madhusūdana paḍa mararĕm krĕtāñjali,
saŋ hyaŋ śakra haneŋ gajendra saha bhūṣaṇa nira kumĕñaṙ mawaṅkawa,
himpĕṙnya ŋ kanaka akilat kasuluhan dinakara makin ujwalaprabha*

<sragdharā>:109.
– – –| – ⏑ –| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – –| ⏑ – –| ⏑ – ⏓ = 21

prāpta hyaŋ dwādaśāditya saha ratha sira ndātan atyanta tīkṣṇa,
sākṣāt wālāṙkka ramya amuhara sukha sira i saŋ watĕk hyaŋ sumaṇḍiŋ,
lāwan saŋ hyaŋ dhanendra ahalĕp acĕpuk agöŋ somya muṅgwiŋ palaṅka,
abhra awaṙṇna aṇḍĕp-ĕṇḍĕp kilat ahulap ikaŋ bhūṣaṇa akweḥ maṇiknya*

maṅkat saŋ hyaŋ yama anuṅgaṅi mahiṣa nira adrĕs halintaŋ nira iŋ rĕm,
tansaḥ taŋ ḍaṇḍa muṅgwiŋ taṅan ira panitinya ŋ watĕk pāpakaṙmma,
prāpta i saṇḍiŋ bhaṭāra iśwara paḍa magiraŋ n ton ikaŋ waṅkay akweḥ,
Āpan membuḥ dĕmak rakwa sira ciha-ciha apan sira pretarāja*

saŋ hyaŋ toyādhipaty-a amuwaḥ aciha-ciha anuṅgaŋ iŋ haṅśa śuddha,
waṙṇna alun kāṅinan drĕs ni lari nira sakeŋ doḥ maṅuṅsiṙ bhaṭāra,
saŋ hyaŋ  ṙyyak rob sukha i śīṙṇna musuḥ ira sawaŋ joŋ asāt riŋ karaŋ göŋ,
ndātan māry-a aṅgĕtĕm rakwa sira kamakara n ton pĕjaḥ saŋ mahīja*

<prĕthwītala>:110.
⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – –| ⏑ ⏓ = 17

bhaṭāra parameśwara adhipati saŋ watĕk dewatā,
ḍatĕŋ sira lawan gaṇañjaya kumāra tan saḥ tumūt,
maśānti ri bhaṭāra wiṣṇu sira tuṣṭa haṙṣa agiraŋ,
wuwus nira manohara ajaya-jaya aṅgĕlaṙ śāntika*

huwus paḍa ḍatĕŋ pwa saŋ hyaŋ atata asraṅa aṅastuti,
watĕk rĕṣi humūŋ maweda kadi śabda niŋ nīrada,
samaṅkana bhaṭāra wiṣṇu sukha de watĕk dewatā,
nimitta nira yan panāntwa ri bhaṭāra dhātā sira*

nahan liŋ ira he wiriñci kita māsiha iŋ rāt kabeḥ,
watĕk hyaŋ ika rakṣanĕnta ṅuniweḥ tikā saŋ rĕṣi,
apan kita bapa ibu niŋ sakalaloka kaṙttā kita,
mataŋnya hayu niŋ jagat juga yatanya tan liṅgara*

tĕlas mara hilaŋ si bhoma ya kalĕṅka niŋ rāt kabeḥ,
tĕwĕk nika kahaywan iŋ bhuwana deṅku tan popama,
kita ikana nimitta niŋ tĕhĕra taŋ jagat śāśwata,
marapwan iki tuṣṭa saŋ rĕṣi lawan watĕk dewatā*

sadrĕwya nikanaŋ watĕk hyaŋ inalap nikaŋ bhūmija,
yateka muliha ika deṅku manĕhĕṙ tika atūt krama,
kitā tikanaŋ eṅĕta i krama nikā kita aniṅkaha,
apan mapipika swabhāwa nikaŋ ahyun iŋ drĕwya len*

nahan ta wuwus i ṅhulun ri sira saŋ watĕk hyaŋ kabeḥ,
kita atika nimitta niŋ sakalawaṙṇna tan saṅkara,
tĕhĕṙ kita matūta nitya gawayĕn tikāŋ aṙccaṇa,
marapwan ika tuṣṭa taŋ bhuwanaloka bhakti i kita*

wuwusku hiḍĕpĕn ta haywa ta kita pramāda iŋ hayu,
yatanya kita pagwana apagĕha riŋ kadewabratan,
tumĕmwa phala niŋ kasiddhyan atĕhĕṙ musuḥ tan hana,
ṅhulun muwaḥ ajanma mānuṣa rikaŋ jagat rakṣakā*

tiḍak ḍikĕtahui
<śloka>:111.

na liŋ bhaṭāra hyaŋ wiṣṇu,
ri sakweḥ para dewatā,
saŋ watĕk hyaŋ kabeḥ tuṣṭa,
maśānti mwaŋ maṅastuti*

ri tĕlas watĕk dewatā,
mantuk riŋ swaṙgga lālana,
rĕp hyaŋ wiṣṇu muwaḥ krĕṣṇa,
somya apañ citta niṙmmala*

saŋ hyaŋ śakra wawaŋ malwī,
mare śrī krĕṣṇa haṙṣaja,
muṅgwiŋ wāhana mātaṅga,
iniriŋ niŋ warāpsara*

wawaŋ mojaṙ sira anāntwa,
he saŋ nātha lihat prabhu,
bhārā don mami yan prāpta,
maweha anugraha i kita*

nān liŋ saŋ hyaŋ śakra mojar,
narendra atyanta iŋ gaṙjjita,
dewanātha mahādibya,
sanmata asiha ri ṅhulun*

nihan ta anugraha saŋ hyaŋ,
ri ṅhulun tulusa asiha,
saŋ watĕk ratu saŋ hantu,
kapwa wehĕnta jīwita*

narendra druma kasyasiḥ,
pĕjaḥ mwaŋ putra riŋ raṇa,
amet śaraṇa tan poliḥ,
ya aṅde māṙ i twas i ṅhulun*

yadu-wrĕsṇy-andhaka adinya,
lāwan saŋ pininaŋ māti,
sāmānta pratisāmānta,
huripĕn de sureśwara*

bhrĕtya putra kadaŋ waṙgga,
saŋ watĕk ratu kāsihan,
pĕjaḥ tan tĕkan iŋ mrĕtyu,
yatikā huripĕn muwaḥ*

cedi kaṙṇna jarāsandha,
byakta iki n musuḥ i ṅhulun,
tathāpi huripĕn saŋ hyaŋ,
towin kadaŋ ikā tĕhĕr*

paritrāṇa akrĕtadhaṙmma,
winiśeṣa ri saŋ prabhu,
śatru towin paritrāṇan,
marapwan mari duṙjana*

ya tā liŋ śrī mahārāja,
sumahuṙ hyaŋ surapati,
prabhu toḥ haywa sandeha,
astu kahyunta dadyā ya*

sāmpun mojaṙ bhaṭārendra,
rĕp dhyāyī sira niścala,
tĕka aŋ amrĕta riŋ kuṇḍi,
paniram nira riŋ pĕjaḥ*

tan asowe dahat saŋ hyaŋ,
mahurip saŋ watĕk ratu,
tĕka riŋ śatru siŋ yogya,
labdhajīwa tĕkeŋ bala*

<jagaddhita>:112.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

waṙṇnan ta ulaḥ i saŋ watĕk ratu sama ahurip agarawalan sira awuṅū,
ndā tapwan matutuṙ dahat warurutĕn tĕhĕṙ aṅusap-usap mata apĕḍe,
kāścaṙyyan mulati ŋ pĕjaḥ rudhirasāgara giri śawa niŋ gajaḥ kuda,
nāhan hetu nira n saniścaya ri papraŋ ira paḍa sudhīra riŋ raṇa*

kapwa apakṣa manambut āyudha muwaḥ saha-sahana manuṅgaŋ iŋ ratha,
saŋ hyaŋ śakra mataṅgu-taṅguḥ amatūtakĕn apitutuṙ iŋ patuṅgalan,
nāhan kāraṇa saŋ watĕk ratu paḍa amituturi sawaraḥ sureśwara,
ramya arok wĕkasan tuhun hana wiraŋ nira sahana watĕk mahīsuta*

<bhadralalita>:113.
⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 21

ri tĕlas watĕk ratu paḍa ahurip sukha narendra krĕṣṇa magiraŋ,
kadi riŋ paṅipyan ika rakwa paṅhiḍĕp ira irikaŋ mati kabeḥ,
paripūṙṇna haṙṣa nira tulya waṙṣa paniram prapañca ri manaḥ,
ndan ikā sukha i hati nira n tumiṅhal iŋ anak suputra salisu*

surarāja mamwit anĕhĕṙ muliḥ sira n umūṙ tĕkeŋ surapada,
awiwākṣitan sira kunaŋ pwa saŋ ratu kabeḥ sira iki caritan,
naranātha krĕṣṇa sira gorawa asĕgĕḥ i saŋ watĕk kṣitisuta,
pinakaswabhāwa nira saŋ mahāpuruṣa toyarekha n agĕlĕŋ*

nrĕpa cedi kaṙṇna magadhendra śālya pinakādi sāmpun arĕpat,
ubhaya n pinintakasihan mareŋ pura narendra krĕṣṇa sakarĕŋ,
yadu-wrĕṣṇinātha nrĕpa śālya len drupada bāhlikādi mapupul,
maśilā sama aduluṙ i saŋ narendra harimūṙtti tan hana waneḥ*

basudewa kimpuruṣanātha tan sipi giraŋ nira n marajaya,
sĕmu niŋ lihat ciha-ciha n tumiṅhal i narendra cedi maparĕk,
upacāra sambhrama nira akadaŋ pahula yan tĕlas parabhawa,
paḍa lampaḥ iŋ hati wiwal kinubdha nira lokika iniriŋ ira*

<mrĕdukomala>:114.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 18

mantuk saŋ naranātha krĕṣṇa maduluṙ lawan para ratu,
rājya iŋ dwārawatī tinaṇḍas ira tan kara aṅhinak-inak,
tan waṙṇnan sira riŋ hĕnū mwaŋ ikanaŋ bala ajĕmuṙ arok,
Āpan tulya pasaŋ surud laku nira n sakeŋ pabharatan*

maṅkā ŋ paṙwwata ratna rāmya mahawan tawaŋ mibĕṙ alon,
lāwan saŋ garuḍa aduluṙ milu sudaṙśśana aṅhiriṅakĕn,
līla asoŋ jalada anipis kakĕñaran maṇīndra sumĕnö,
tumraŋ teja nika awilĕt-wilĕt awoṙ haneŋ jaladhara*

<jagaddhita>:115.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

ndaḥ waṙṇnan gati niŋ bala alara ri mitra nika pĕjaḥ anūtakĕn tuhan,
lāwan wāhw-aniluṅluṅi i kadaŋ ikā nĕhĕṙ aṅusapi luḥnya tan pĕgat,
len taŋ māti kakā nikāna paḍa kāsrĕpan amĕkasi luḥ lawan sĕrĕḥ,
kapwa asoŋ prihatin ry-uliḥnya hana kāry-amuri-muri taṅisnya tan humūŋ*

<mrĕdukomala>:116.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 18

strī belā kapapag maṅiṣṭy-akalihan sinuṇḍaŋ awĕnĕs,
ceṭinya anaṅis iŋ wurinya piliḥ amwaŋ amriḥ amalar,
tan seṅĕḥ tinuhan-tuhan pijĕṙ asambat iŋ priya nikā,
liŋnya aṅhiŋ kaka heṙ ṅhulun wuwus ikā n sumĕṅka tumurun*

len maṅhĕmban anaknya patrĕm inagöm nikā n saha sĕrĕḥ,
tan pahyas gĕluṅan mure tapiḥ ikā banantĕn alĕsĕḥ,
maṙmma amakpak anak nika amalaku suswana aṙddha kasatan,
tan trĕṣṇa i wĕka kepwan aṅhaṅĕn-aṅĕn sĕnĕŋnya kasihan*

taṅheḥ yañ caritan laranya tucapa ika saŋ prabhu kabeḥ,
prāpta iŋ dwārawatī sĕḍĕŋ pinaripoṣita iŋ sukha sira,
sakweḥ niŋ surabhogabhāra panamuy bhinukti surasa,
astam taŋ maṇi rājayogya sama yogya riŋ kadi sira*

saŋ cedi mwaŋ awaṅganātha magadhendra śālya caritan,
maṅgĕḥ mitra kadaŋ narendra harimūṙtti rāmya wĕkasan,
Āpan tan mapuji ñ jayā nrĕpati krĕṣṇa hetu niŋ asiḥ,
sāmpun tuṣṭa kabeḥ tĕkeŋ balasahāya wastra masalin*

rwā ŋ we rwā ŋ wĕṅi yan winuṙṣita muliḥ mareŋ swanagara,
sakweḥ saŋ pininaŋ muwaḥ sira muliḥ kabeḥ paḍa sukha,
hetunya n paripūṙṇna kīṙtti nira nātha krĕṣṇa mapagĕḥ,
pinras riŋ kajanapriyan tuwi paṅöban iŋ sabhuwana*

<wiśwalalita>:117.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 17

aparimita iŋ sukha asama-sama iŋ watĕk yadu kabeḥ,
maṅinum agoṣṭhy-amukti phala niŋ jaya iŋ raṇasabhā,
irika narendra krĕṣṇa baladewa pāṙtha manitaḥ,
ri sĕnaha saŋ prawīra ginuṇa iŋ tĕgal dinĕmakan*

sira para rājaputra dinadaṙ dĕmak nira kabeḥ,
makawiṣaya irikaŋ wiṣaya niŋ musuḥ tĕlas alaḥ,
sama-sama sewu kāṭi nira sowaŋ iŋ sawiṣaya,
uliḥ iŋ atoḥ ri jīwita nira amriḥ iŋ pabharatan*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:118.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

saŋ nāthātmaja sāmba sāmpun arĕṇaḥ tekaŋ dĕmak de haji,
an prāgjyotiṣa rakwa punpunan ira ndātan hana anĕmpila,
mās rwaŋ lakṣa kaṭi n kapaṅguhan ira aṅkĕn māsa lek nohanĕn,
hīṅanya n kalĕwiḥ phala śrama nira asāra iŋ raṇa atoḥ bhaya*

saŋ nātha druma mantuk iŋ swanagara imbuḥ wanwa riŋ yāwana,
bĕṅkat-bĕṅkat ira ahawan ratha mure rambut nira ika aputiḥ,
yapwan putra nira ika saŋ suratha kāly-a apan wineḥ putrikā,
de śrī krĕṣṇa tĕlas paḍa asiliḥ-asiḥ rāgapriya aṅgöŋ smara*

ry-antuk saŋ garuḍa aduluṙ sira lawan saŋ pañcajanya aṅlayaŋ,
mwaŋ saŋ komudikī sudaṙśśaṇa parĕŋ mwaŋ nandaka anraŋ kilat,
prāpta iŋ wiṣṇupada ndatīta-ta kabeḥ saŋ nātha krĕṣṇa ajarĕn,
sākṣāt wīṙyya nira n prakāśa karĕṅö riŋ dik-widik niścala*

nāhan hetu niŋ aśwamedha ginawe riŋ dwārawaty-a adhika,
de saŋ śrī basudewa kaprakaśita iŋ rāt mwaŋ watĕk dewatā,
söḥ taŋ ratna suwaṙṇna ratnawanitā n paṅgorawa iŋ brāhmaṇa,
maṅdadyākĕna haywan iŋ bhuwana sākṣāt ri indraloka anurun*

strī kanya ahayu ratnarājaduhita anwam pat hajöṅya anulus,
antuk niŋ mamarājaya nrĕpati krĕṣṇa amukti tātan waneḥ,
ramya awaṙṇna tinuṅgal iŋ jinĕm arūm haṙṣa n saraśmi iŋ tilĕm,
Āpan de ni kawiṣṇumūṙttin ira saŋ nātha n wĕnaŋ wyāpaka*

ndan saŋ śrī warawīṙyya rukma krĕtadhaṙmmādi pralabdha iŋ sukha,
kapwa amukti sakāpti niŋ manaḥ anūt dhaṙmma apagĕḥ riŋ hayu,
swasthā niŋ bala rāmya tan hana sasaṙ saṅka irikaŋ śāsana,
Āstām saŋ caturāśrama atata manūt śāstra ahawan riŋ pada*
